## **129: Moving Through the Forest and the Mermaid Princess**

**AN:** This chapter is part of the Elgant Theocracy arc.

---

“Sorry, but we didn’t get any particularly useful information.”

After wiping out the Granz Kingdom soldiers who had been disguised as bandits, I used Portal to warp to the moving carriage and reported the results to everyone.

Since we couldn’t exactly take an outside-the-forest route to go subjugate the bandits this time, I had the maids prepare six carriages identical to the one we were riding in.

Each of those carriages had a Portal installed inside, and maids dressed as knights stationed at the mansion would warp in one after another.

After the maids overturned the numerical disadvantage, all I had to do was step out of the carriage and give the order to annihilate them. A very simple job.

“After that, we captured a high-ranking soldier and ended up tor… interrogating him, but…”

“I’m really bothered by how casually you slipped in that ‘tor’ just now…”

“I interrogated him.”

Mio’s retort was ignored.

“Ah, so that’s one of those things we shouldn’t comment on.”

“It was quite unsettling, indeed.”

Sera, who was accompanying me in knight attire, adds her own clarification?.

Apparently, the Granz Kingdom soldiers, including their unit commander, had not been told the true objective of the operation, so there was very little useful information.

This attack was ordered by the upper echelons of the Granz Kingdom, and its objectives were the capture of Queen Sakuya and the assassination of the knight Gene.

No matter how strong Gene might be, they apparently judged that with a force of one hundred, they could overwhelm him, take his lord Sakuya hostage, and then kill him.

They were also planning to slaughter all other companions and burn everything down to destroy the evidence.

With only this information, the true aim of the Granz Kingdom leadership remains unclear.

“Master. Granz Kingdom soldiers were also found along alternate routes from the former Eldia Kingdom and the Castal Kingdom toward the Elgant Theocracy. They have already been eliminated, but there was no significant difference in the information they possessed.”

It seems the Granz Kingdom does not believe in putting everything on a single bet.

Vega reported that Granz Kingdom bandit soldiers were found at three other routes leading to the Elgant Theocracy. Naturally, the maids eliminated them, but there was no new information.

After going to such lengths, they still didn’t station any soldiers along the forest route.

A lack of imagination, indeed.

“Well, we don’t know the Granz Kingdom’s objective, but there is one thing that’s become clear.”

After all this, it’s fair to say it outright.

“That the Granz Kingdom has made an enemy.”

“The war with Eldia just finally settled down too…”

Sakuya groans, pressing her temples.

No, it’s not like I intend to start a war. Managing enclaved territories is a pain, after all…

The matter of the Granz Kingdom isn’t something that requires immediate action, so let’s leave it at that for now.

While I was dealing with the Granz Kingdom’s bandit soldiers, the carriage had already entered the forest.

Even within the forest, there are roads wide enough for carriages. They’re not paved, of course, but they’re not so bad that horses can’t travel them.

Since this is monster territory, monsters attack normally, but the maid knights eliminate them before they can get close, so the carriages suffer no damage.

Without stopping the carriage, maid knights with bows shoot down monsters from atop the carriage, or maid magic knights freeze them to death (fire would be dangerous in a forest, so ice magic causes the least collateral damage).

Since we’re in a forest, the monsters are mostly beasts, insects, and plant types as usual.

“Mio, aren’t you joining in?”

I ask Mio, the only archer in our party.

With her bow that has Auto-Tracking, we could easily make it her solo stage.

“Ah, well. Mio-chan is in the maid role, so I shouldn’t be shooting arrows outside, right?”

“True. In that case, only Sera and I could fight.”

Only Sera and I are dressed as knights, after all.

A little girl in maid clothes stealing the show would be strange if you think about it normally. (A very belated realization.)

“What will you do, Sera?”

“I will refrain as well. The maid knights are extremely enthusiastic about being able to accompany you, Master. It would be cruel to interfere.”

This journey is unusual in that we’ve brought along a large number of subordinates outside the main party.

Naturally, all of them are yellow, and they were extremely, extremely, extremely, extremely, extremely excited about traveling with me.

According to the head maid, she really did repeat “extremely” five times.

“Then I guess we’ll let the maids handle things while we relax for a while. Though, working nonstop would get tiring…”

“Oh, Lucea mentioned it. Apparently, they secretly rotate the maid knights during each break. Since everyone has their faces hidden like you, Oniichan, the ministers probably won’t notice.”

According to Sakuya, the maid knights switch out frequently, so there’s no need to worry. In a sense, the high-ranking officials who stay in the carriage the whole time have it harder.

“Could it be that the Castal dignitaries have it the hardest of all…?”

“They’re the only ones truly stuck riding the carriage the entire time.”

Sakuya and I can return via Portal if we want, but the dignitaries who don’t know about our powers have no such option.

Among all the companions on this journey, the dignitaries are undoubtedly the most unfortunate.

“At least let’s make sure they get good food… Mio, please.”

“Okay. I’ll add dessert even though it wasn’t originally planned.”

Even knowing how capable the guards are, forcing the dignitaries to travel through monster territory with minimal escort and stay on carriages nonstop, they deserve at least that much service.

《Dora wants some too!》

“Of course. I’ll give it to everyone, so don’t worry.”

《Yay!》

That evening’s dessert was pudding made with generous amounts of harpy eggs.

The screams coming from the dignitaries carriage were probably not my imagination.

And so, two days passed.

While I feel bad for the dignitaries stuck in the carriage, we (including Sakuya) sometimes secretly returned to my mansion via Portal to rest.

The maid knights handle all the monsters along the way, so we really have nothing to do.

Being in the forest, it’s also hard to enjoy the scenery.

Even so, we still spend about half the day riding in the carriage.

“Looks like we’ll be out of the forest the day after tomorrow. Weren’t we supposed to take about a week?”

We’ve already passed the halfway point, so it looks like we’ll exit the forest the day after tomorrow.

Since I was told it would take a week, it feels a bit fast.

“Oniichan, it’s simple. Normally, when monsters attack, you stop the carriage, right? No one exterminates them from a distance without stopping.”

“Ah, so fewer stops means faster travel. Makes sense.”

The “one week” estimate assumed stopping to fight monsters.

No wonder the calculations were off.

“Is there any problem with arriving early?”

“No, it’s fine. This isn’t your Portal, so travel times fluctuating is normal. Guest accommodations should already be prepared.”

“Then we can do some sightseeing if we arrive early.”

If we remove the knight equipment, we can sightsee normally.

Even I don’t plan to sightsee in knight armor.

“I’d prefer you stay quiet if possible. Whenever Oniichan moves, things tend to escalate. If you say it’s just sightseeing, what are the odds it ends at that?”

“Not zero?”

“Zero.”

“I think it’s zero…”

《Zero!》

“No comment, please.”

With the exception of Maria’s silence, the verdict was unanimously zero percent.

Sorry, Maria, but I agree with zero.

“Fine. I’ll try to behave.”

At the very least, I’ll avoid sticking my nose into trouble.

“That’s all I ask. Just enough restraint so the summit can start safely, okay?”

“Sakuya-chan thinks the summit might collapse just from Master sightseeing…”

“But Mio-chan, if Oniichan got serious, even a major power or two would topple, right?”

“They would… Actually, didn’t one major power fall recently?”

That fallen country, of course, is the Kingdom of Eldia.

“Hey, even I wouldn’t destroy a country just because I had a bad experience while sightseeing.”

“…Even if it’s noble-related trouble?”

Mio asks cautiously.

The Elgant Theocracy, a theocracy worshipping a goddess. Yeah, noble-related trouble seems likely.

“Of course. I’d retaliate against the noble in question, but I wouldn’t hold the whole country responsible. I decided to destroy Eldia because they tried to harm Castal and Estea, my family.”

“When you put it that way, it’s true. Before that, you hated Eldia but weren’t serious about destroying it.”

I thought about it a few times, though.

If I were to destroy a country, it would be because they collectively targeted my family or became a clear enemy.

I don’t think I’d destroy a country over a minor noble dispute… I think.

“What do I do? I’m worried about Oniichan’s actions, but I’m happy to be treated as family…”

Sakuya’s expression melts into a grin.

“Anyway! Unless something extreme happens, I won’t take on a country. You can rest easy.”

“So if something extreme happens, you will…”

“To Master, that’s just another day.”

Mio. I’ve only taken on a country once, and that was Eldia.

…We’ll ignore the time I punched royalty (twins) in the Izumo Wa Kingdom’s royal castle and enslaved them.

No one saw it, so it’s fine. Everyone who did was enslaved…

That afternoon, while we were relaxing in the carriage after eating, Vega made a report.

“Master. A rare monster inhabits this forest. What shall we do?”

“Let’s see…”

I check the map as Vega indicates.

If Vega (Alta) calls it rare, it really must be.

Mermaid (Rare)

LV1

\<Singing LV7> \<Aquatic LV2> \<Diving LV2> \<Transformation LV2> \<Enthralling Voice LV10> \<Mermaid Princess LV >

Notes: A monster with a human upper body and fish lower body.

\<Enthralling Voice>

Mermaid-exclusive. Charms those who hear the song. Duration varies by skill level. At LV1, lasts one hour after the song ends.

\<Mermaid Princess>

Greatly increases stats underwater. Grants absolute command over weaker beings underwater.

A mermaid with terrifyingly powerful skills was living in a forest lake.

“Master. This was discovered when maids were dispatched to Eldia territory, but we left it alone since we were passing through the forest. I judged it suitable as a way to pass the time during carriage travel.”

“You understand me a little too well, don’t you?”

To be honest, I was getting bored of the carriage journey.

The scenery doesn’t change much, and even returning to the mansion doesn’t allow much activity.

“Master. I am honored by your praise.”

Oh, that counts as praise…

Well, since Alta (Vega) went to the trouble, let’s tame the mermaid.

She doesn’t seem evil, and taming is better than killing. Mermaid Princess is clearly a racial skill…

I could probably use it if I absorbed her, but I don’t want to use a skill with “Princess” in the name.

“This girl really is a princess…”

《Dora is the big sister!》

Mio and Dora, who were also looking at the map, make completely different comments, and I realize something.

I was viewing her in monster display mode, but if I switch to human display mode, I see something else.

Name: –

Gender: Female

Age: 3

Race: Mermaid

Title: Mermaid Princess

Skills:

Technical

\<Singing LV7>

Physical

\<Aquatic LV2> \<Diving LV2>

Other

\<Transformation LV2> \<Enthralling Voice LV10> \<Mermaid Princess LV >

I see. It does change the impression a bit.

Well, I’m still taming her.

There are many things I’m curious about, and I want to ask her after taming.

Like “Why is a princess here?” or “Are there other mermaids?”

“Alright, I’m going to tame her.”

“I figured you’d say that.”

“I thought so too…”

Not just Sera and Sakura, but Mio and Dora nod as well.

Do you all understand my patterns too well?

“Jin-sama, I will accompany you.”

Maria’s behavior pattern is also as usual.

Including my behavior, is this all just a template?

《Dora’s coming too!》

“Oh, Dora-chan’s coming? Then I guess Mio-chan will come too.”

“What about Sera and Sakura?”

Since Dora and Mio are coming, I ask Sera and Sakura as well.

Before they can answer, Sakuya steps forward.

“You’re not asking me?”

“I can’t exactly take you along, Sakuya. Stay in the carriage.”

“That’s so unfair…”

Seeing Sakuya slump, Sakura speaks up.

“I’ll stay with Sakuya-chan… If everyone leaves, she’ll be alone…”

“Master. I will remain as well.”

Sakura and Vega will stay.

“Then I shall remain for guard duty.”

“Alright. Sera, I’m counting on you.”

“Leave it to me.”

Leaving Sakura, Sera, Sakuya, and Vega behind, we head toward the mermaid.

We secretly slip out of the moving carriage using Warp and run through the forest.

Of course, I removed my knight armor. The other three also removed their maid outfits.

In less than five minutes, we arrive at the lake where the mermaid resides.

The lake is about 500 meters in diameter, with clear water. Forest animals like boars come to drink here. Animals that survive in monster territory tend to be quite powerful.

“Luu ruu ruu~”

While observing the lake, a song suddenly rises from within.

It’s probably the mermaid’s song.

—Splash!—

A different sound draws my eye. A boar that had been drinking water fell into the lake.

Without struggling, it sinks.

A: The boar was charmed by Enthralling Voice and made to drown itself. It is food.

…I’m not saying it’s wrong, but that’s a pretty brutal hunting method.

For the record, due to Multiple Existence, mind-control skills don’t affect us.

“By the way, Master, there’s something I want to ask.”

“What is it, Mio?”

“How do you plan to reach the mermaid princess? Swim? A swimsuit episode?”

“If it were a swimsuit episode, I wouldn’t leave Sera behind.”

Among Maria, Mio, and Dora (by age), the service is clearly lacking.

Maria is developing somewhat, but she can’t compare to Sera’s impact.

Sakura… well, she has something.

“And there’s no need to go to her.”

“What do you mea… Ah, she’s coming this way.”

As Mio notices, the mermaid is swimming toward us.

She swims near the surface and leaps out, spinning once midair before splashing back down.

“Master… That girl is three years old?”

“Seems so. They probably grow differently than us…”

《Dora is the big sister though…》

The mermaid didn’t match our image of a three-year-old.

Beautiful features, emerald-green long hair, a fish lower body covered in pale pink scales… all fine.

But her upper body had a voluptuous chest impossible for a human three-year-old. Proportionally, she looked like a mid-teen.

Thinking calmly, mermaids are monsters, so there’s no guarantee they grow like humans.

Mermaids reproduce biologically like dragonkin, and since dragonkin grow like humans, we assumed the same for mermaids.

A: Mermaids generally grow like humans. However, mermaid royalty mature physically at an accelerated rate.

So she’s special in many ways.

“Come to think of it, she wasn’t wearing a bra.”

“That’s true.”

If there’s no such culture, that explains it, but she wasn’t wearing even a shell bra common in stories.

Things that shouldn’t be visible were fully visible.

Monsters generally lack shame. There are exceptions, but…

“Once she’s tamed, we should make her wear a bra… If we contact the Advance Trading Company, could they prepare a shell bra?… They say they can.”

“I can’t comment. I’ll leave it to you, Mio.”

Mio apparently contacted them via telepathy immediately.

This is beyond me.

“Alright, let’s tame her.”

The mermaid has been staring at us intently.

She sticks her upper body out of the water, watching us with curiosity.

I toss a taming magic circle.

When it smacks against her upper body, she smiles happily.

“Luu raa ruu…”

As she sings, I feel something deflect.

Ah, so it blocked Enthralling Voice.

A: She is commanding Master to enter the water.

…Same treatment as the boar.

I get a little irritated.

《I’ll pretend to be charmed.》

I stagger toward the lake, sending a telepathic message to the others.

《Have fun!》

《Please be careful, Jin-sama.》

《Master, your hobbies are as bad as ever…》

Bad hobbies aside, if she treats me like a boar, I’ll teach her the difference in status.

…Why am I competing with a boar?

—Splash!—

I fall into the lake like the boar and sink.

“Luu~♪”

Seeing this, the mermaid nods in satisfaction and swims toward me, completely unguarded.

For reference, the boar from earlier is stored in the mermaid’s underwater dwelling.

Other fish don’t touch it because they’re under Mermaid Princess’s control.

She’s probably planning to treat me as food too.

She grabs my hand and heads toward her dwelling.

“Bibbabubabu!”

“L-Luu!?”

I shout that and hug her with all my might (not attack power-wise).

From behind, a full nelson.

I shouted “Deadly Hug!” by the way.

“Luu!?”

The mermaid panics and struggles, not expecting me to move.

Considering our stat difference, it’s obvious she can’t escape.

“Luu…”

When she tries to activate a skill, I cover her mouth.

Given her skill set, blocking her mouth renders her helpless.

“Mmph!?”

Struggling, she sinks with me.

I gradually increase the pressure.

Like a countdown to death.

“Mmm…!? Gah…!?”

Her movements weaken. Naturally.

Soon, she goes limp, completely losing the will to resist.

Mermaid has been tamed.

Please name the mermaid.

Whew, tamed successfully.

I release her and pull her toward the surface.

“Gasp!”

Reaching shore, I pull her onto land.

Alta confirmed she can breathe on land and underwater, so it’s fine. She just can’t move well without legs.

“Good work, Jin-sama.”

《Good job!》

“Nice work… She looks completely exhausted though.”

“Yeah. It was a fierce battle.”

As Mio says, the mermaid lies limp.

Her expression is pure resignation.

“Sorry, that doesn’t explain anything.”

So I explain the whole battle to the three.

“…And after an intense battle, she accepted taming.”

“Only the mermaid princess was moving intensely! Against someone like you, Master, using such a slow, suffocating method would break anyone mentally.”

Her spirit is still broken.

A wet, half-naked beautiful girl lying there in despair is quite provocative.

“Oh, right. I got the shell bra. I’ll put it on her.”

“Please do.”

Noticing my gaze, Mio equips the shell bra.

That halves the erotic factor… though the base level was absurdly high.

“Alright, taming’s done. Let’s head back.”

“What about the mermaid princess?”

“Let’s ask her what she wants.”

I lift the limp mermaid.

She trembles and looks up at me fearfully.

I might’ve gone too far.

“L-Luu…”

According to Translation, she’s muttering “Don’t bully me…”

She probably doesn’t understand our language.

“Hey, can you understand me?”

“Luu…? (What are you saying? Are you bullying me?)”

She definitely doesn’t understand.

And the translation sounds childishly lisped.

…Well, she’s three (physically adult).

Since mermaids reproduce biologically, if no one teaches them, they can’t learn language.

Naturally spawned monsters are born with some knowledge.

《How about now?》

“L-Luu? (Eh? A voice in my head? Where?)”

Switching to telepathy makes her look around.

A textbook reaction.

From there, I explain who we are, focusing only on what’s relevant to her.

It’s been a while since I explained things myself. Usually Maria handles this.

---

Behind-the-Scenes

· Mermaid

In this world, mermaids are classified as monsters.

As explained, they reproduce biologically and do not naturally spawn from miasma, similar to dragonkin.

Mermaids have both males and females; they are not a female-only species. They generally reproduce within the species, though mermaid-style reproduction exists.

Their ability to breathe underwater comes from the Aquatic skill, not gills. If Jin were to steal Aquatic, the mermaid would drown in water.

Monsters that reproduce biologically are long-lived; mermaids are said to live at least 1,000 years. Encountering a juvenile is extremely rare.

As fate would have it, mermaids are often targeted by humans. Some desire their beauty, others believe eating their flesh grants immortality.

However, they often escape danger using their racial skill, Enthralling Voice.

## **129.5: How to Raise a Mermaid Princess**

**AN:** This is a continuation of the mermaid princess story.

---

“So, with that settled, your name is Leila. Nice to meet you from now on.”

《O-okay…》

“Is it based on Lorelei?”

With all the explanations out of the way, we decided to give the mermaid princess a name.

…She still looks a bit frightened.

By the way, Mio’s guess was correct.

The mermaid princess picked things up faster than I had expected. She was already making good use of telepathy, so it only took one explanation to get our situation across.

As an aside, Alta told me that merfolk royalty develop a mental age roughly equivalent to humans. In other words, an adult body with a child’s mind.

Maybe it’s simply because of her low mental age that she doesn’t fully understand how abnormal our actions are.

《W-what’s going to happen to me now?》

“Since I’ve tamed you, you’ll be working for me. That said, if there’s something you want to do, and it benefits me even a little, I don’t mind prioritizing that.”

As long as it’s not something too strange, I have no intention of saying no.

That applies whether they’re human slaves or monster familiars.

《It’s okay-. Master is kind to kids he tames-》

Dora stepped in to back me up.

《Really? You’re Dora, right?》

《You can call me Big Sister Dora-》

Since this was the first familiar younger than her (in actual age only) aside from spontaneously generated monsters (who are effectively zero years old but mentally mature), Dora was going all out acting like an older sister.

Even in the Dragonkin Sanctuary, there hadn’t been anyone younger than Dora.

《Okay, I got it. …Big Sister Dora, are you happy being tamed by Jin?》

By the way, Leila calls me Jin.

She’s the second familiar to do that after Midori. Conversely, there’s no one besides familiars who calls me by my name without honorifics.

《Of course! I get to eat tasty things-. I get to go to lots of places-. He pats me gently-. He hugs me tight-》

《That sounds nice-…》

Hearing Dora’s barrage of praise, Leila looked envious.

I also heard about Leila’s past, and it seems that as far back as she can remember, she’s been in this lake.

She’s not a naturally occurring monster, so there’s no doubt there were circumstances behind it. Somehow, it reminded me of how Dora ended up being tamed by me.

According to Leila, she doesn’t have much attachment to this lake.

Leila is surprisingly adventurous, and she had long wanted to leave the lake, but that wish never came true.

Princess of the Merfolk shows overwhelming effectiveness underwater, but once on land, it loses its effect. On top of that, she doesn’t even have legs, so moving around is difficult to begin with.

With Enchanting Voice, she could protect herself, but she can’t sing nonstop, and the commands she can give aren’t that complex, so it didn’t work out well.

Since she doesn’t even have the concept of cooking, she spent her days eating raw meat and raw fish that didn’t taste very good.

She also lacked physical strength, so she couldn’t even separate out the inedible parts.

Fortunately, or perhaps unfortunately, we were the first humans she’d ever encountered.

Apparently, since we looked soft at a glance, she thought we’d be easy to eat and wanted to try. …If she’d eaten humans before, there’s a chance our response would’ve been different.

Among Dora’s reassurances, the parts about “eating tasty food” and “going to various places” seemed to strike a chord with Leila.

Neither of those has anything to do with my personality.

So, as an experiment, we gave Leila some food prepared by the maids.

One of the maids specialty dishes they’re confident in: cricket.

A: Master. I believe you mean croquette. Also, since it’s been arranged and is basically Japanese cuisine, it’s apparently called korokke even overseas. Mio said so.

I tried to sound classy by using a foreign word and failed? I failed badly, you know?

《This… what is it?》

“It’s human food. Try eating it.”

Since no one noticed my big failure, I decided to bury it in the darkness.

A: …

I handed the croquette to Leila with what I hoped was a gentle expression.

Leila cautiously sniffed the croquette, and the next moment, she took a big bite.

《I’ll do my best for Jin! So please take me away from this lake!》

Fiiish!

There was no rod or lure, but I sure caught a pretty big fish.

“So the winning move was feeding her…”

“As expected of Lord Jin.”

Mio let out an exasperated voice, but Maria praised me.

Since Maria only ever praises me, she doesn’t count.

《Master-. Can I have one too-?》

“Yeah, sure.”

Saying that, I handed Dora a croquette as well.

I also gave one each to Maria and Mio, and ate one myself.

There we were, munching on croquettes beside a spring in a forest crawling with monsters.

Naturally, if you relax like that, it stands to reason that monsters drawn in would attack.

What appeared were the familiar Fang Wolves.

They were probably drawn by the nice smell of the croquettes. I’m not even fishing, yet it’s been nonstop bites since earlier…

More than ten Fang Wolves were slowly closing in around us.

Looking closely, there was what appeared to be a leader, an upper variant. It seemed to be a pack led by a Big Black Wolf.

…At this point, what threat am I supposed to feel from such low-level wolf-type monsters?

I’ve already killed a divine wolf in another world, you know?

“Maria, I’ll handle this.”

“Is that acceptable?”

I stopped Maria, who had her hand on her sword, and stood up while tossing the remaining croquette into my mouth.

“Yeah. I want to show the newcomer something cool.”

Since I’d basically tricked Leila into it, this was a good chance to show her my raw strength.

《What are you going to do?》

“An uncompromising slaughter against small fry. As expected of Master!”

“Watch your wording…”

Mio said something completely unvarnished, killing my mood.

Even if my mood drops, I still have to do what needs doing…

“Alright, I’ll be right back…”

Using \<Shukuchi>, I closed in on the nearest wolf and kicked it to death.

Belatedly realizing what was happening, the leader howled, and the wolves all lunged at once, so I carefully beat each one to death. I landed a spinning back kick on a wolf that came at me from behind.

I kicked up a wolf that leapt from a tree, sending it flying about ten meters into the air.

It seemed the leader ordered a retreat, so I killed the wolves starting from the ones farther away.

When only the leader remained and it made a desperate leap at me, I jumped aside and struck down from above. The leader’s head was crushed, leaving behind a small crater.

“It’s over.”

《Hii!》

Leila screamed and put distance between us.

I thought we’d started to get closer after giving her croquettes, but it feels like the distance just widened again.

“What’s wrong?”

《Jin is too strong… Jin is scary…》

It seems instead of showing her something cool, I just scared her normally.

《I won’t oppose you, Jin, so please don’t kill me…》

Trembling, she hid behind Dora.

Given the size difference, she wasn’t hiding at all, though.

“It seems Master’s massacre scene was too stimulating for a three-year-old. She looks pretty shaken, so maybe we should leave the rest to the maids?”

“Yeah. For now, let’s move her to the labyrinth’s water area. It’s spacious enough there.”

On the 52nd floor of the labyrinth, there’s a huge lake.

It’s a lake set up by the former labyrinth ruler, Azuma, and it’s home to quite a variety of fish. There are no monsters living there.

Apparently, it was a lake created as a hobby by Azuma, with lots of fish you’d recognize from Japan. They sometimes end up on the dinner table.

That lake should make a good new home for Leila.

It’s relatively safe, and it’ll be convenient for teaching her various things.

“Teaching her Portal would be a hassle, so I’ll just call her with Summon.”

No sooner said than done, I used Portal to move to the 52nd floor of the labyrinth, then used Summon to call the others.

I also contacted Lucea, the head maid, and had her dispatch several maids.

《So big-. So wide-》

《Heh-heh!》

Probably because she’s three, Leila’s vocabulary is pretty poor.

And for some reason, Dora is brimming with confidence.

“Leila, you’ll be living here. Follow their instructions.”

《O-okay…》

When I pointed out the maids who would be in charge of her education, Leila nodded timidly.

She still seems scared of me after all.

“Leila isn’t good at moving outside of water, so it might be inconvenient, but I appreciate it.”

“Please don’t worry about it.”

“Thanks. I’m counting on you.”

Since educating Leila, who can’t move properly on land, will be tough, I encouraged the maids.

“Come to think of it, Leila-chan has the Transformation skill, right? If so, shouldn’t she be able to take on a human form?”

“Ah…”

Right. She did have it. Transformation!

The other skills were so rare I completely overlooked it.

“Mio, good job. Leila, can you try using Transformation to become human?”

《What’s hen-ge?》

“…”

And that’s where we started.

After giving a simple lecture on skills, we had Maple, the great sea serpent with Transformation, demonstrate it in practice.

“Picture how you want to be, focus strongly on the Transformation skill, and imagine energy circulating through your whole body from deep inside. That should let you transform, ssu.”

It’s extremely abstract, but skill activation is usually like that.

By the way, the reason Maple was chosen as the instructor is because she has two Transformation targets: mermaid form and human form. It was my first time seeing Maple’s mermaid form.

Since it was her first time seeing another mermaid, she seemed to feel a sense of kinship toward Maple.

《I’ll try》

Leila groaned as she focused her strength.

After a while, Leila’s lower body (the fish part) began to glow.

《I did it!》

When the light faded, there were two perfectly formed legs.

“She’s naked on the bottom! Seashell panties, seashell panties…”

“Wouldn’t normal panties be fine?”

Mio started saying strange things in a frenzy, so I calmly corrected her.

“That’s true… It wouldn’t really work to match seashell panties with a bra, would it?”

Seashell bras are only acceptable because she’s a mermaid.

If a normal human wore a seashell bra and seashell panties, they’d just be a pervert.

Still, I think there’d be demand.

By the time our conversation ended, the maids had already put panties and a skirt on Leila.

《I-I can’t stand…》

“You just have to get used to it, ssu. Do your best, ssu!”

《O-okay!》

Unable to immediately adapt to the drastic change brought on by Transformation, Leila couldn’t even stand properly.

Maple may have gone through something similar, but “get used to it” isn’t exactly advice.

“Then we’ll teach her language, human common sense, our common sense, combat methods, and so on. With her skills, catching fish will be easier, so she should be useful to Lord Jin.”

“It’ll make cooking fish easier too, which is nice.”

Hearing the maid’s words, Mio’s motivation surged.

“Yeah, that’s true. Though, I don’t really like fish that much.”

“Because you’re young and like meat, right?”

What a terrible prejudice.

Also, physically speaking, Mio is younger than me.

“No, it’s not that. Fish have bones, right? I don’t like that.”

“Are you a child!?”

Technically, I’m still a minor.

“When I eat, I don’t want to focus on anything other than eating. Picking out fish bones doesn’t fill you up, and it doesn’t taste good either, right? If I’m going to eat it, I want all the bones removed first. And while I’m at it, I like fish you can eat whole, like shishamo or whitebait.”

With my current stats, I could eat fish bones without issue, but it still feels off somehow.

Actually, for the same reason, I don’t like watermelon that much either. I like the taste, but having to pay attention to the seeds keeps me from focusing on eating, which is really unfortunate. Maybe I just don’t like the feeling of foreign objects.

“I get what you’re saying, but that’s kind of a weird stance…”

“But if you say things like that, next time it feels like fish with every bone removed will start showing up…”

“Ah… Yeah. It definitely will. Absolutely.”

The maids overprotectiveness knows no bounds.

By the way, those maids are furiously taking notes right beside me.

From that day on, dishes that required effort from the eater almost completely disappeared from my meals.

It’s fine. I knew this would happen.

As for Leila, she seems to have taken a liking to her human form. After she learned to walk, she started spending most of her time in human form except when sleeping.

She does seem to enjoy swimming itself, though, and swims on the 52nd floor once a day.

And before we knew it, she started eating meals at the mansion as a matter of course.

She seems to like human cooking. Naturally.

She’s a fast learner, so she quickly picked up language and common sense, and her underwater combat also started taking shape under Maple’s guidance.

Unfortunately, she showed absolutely no aptitude for combat on land, so that was ignored. You really shouldn’t make a water-specialized type fight on land.

Well, I heard about all this through telepathy while we were away in the Elgant Theocracy.

---

**AN:** What should I do? It’s already late January, and I still can’t think of a joke for this year’s April Fool’s.

Side stories are fine, but I’m thinking of avoiding IF stories or overly meta jokes.

I want to tell a lie that feels natural, after all (raising the bar myself).
