## **132: Dangerous Individuals and Arrival at the Divine Capital**

**AN:** In this chapter, I am going to do something a little sneaky.

Specifically, this is a case of “the protagonists know, but the readers are not told”.

After all, is it really interesting if every character’s status is fully revealed in advance? (Well, there are stories like that, too.)

---

Now that we have finished talking about Zenon Grants, the king of the Kingdom of Grants, we will continue discussing other individuals who require caution.

More precisely, among those requiring caution, we will focus only on the truly dangerous ones who are highly likely to become enemies…

“I think the Pope of the Elgant Theocracy is likely to be hostile, at least from Mio-chan’s perspective. In games, the head of a theocracy is almost always an enemy. And besides, this title…”

“I believe the S-rank adventurer swordsman is dangerous. This weapon of theirs…”

“There was a teacher among the Heroes who had dangerous titles and skills… Jin-kun, this is…”

《I do not like dragons!》

“Onii-chan, this country is hostile toward humans. If we become enemies, it could get pretty dangerous…”

Everyone started listing dangerous individuals as they pleased.

Every single one of them seemed to have more than one quirk to worry about.

Isn’t this a bit much for dangerous individuals to be concentrated in a single country?

In the end, the number of dangerous individuals came to nearly twenty.

In addition, there were about forty more people who probably would not become enemies, but still possessed concerning skills or titles.

“As expected of the capital of the world’s largest religious nation.”

“No, you absolutely cannot brush it off like that!? Having two ‘Final Trials’ hiding in an ordinary city is nothing short of an abnormal situation!?”

When I muttered that with a sense of awe, Sakuya rejected it with full force.

In fact, there are currently two ‘Final Trials’ staying in the capital of the Elgant Theocracy.

We count them as two because they are taking human forms.

“Isn’t that perfect? There are two Final Trials, and there are also two people without Transcendence, Sakura and Dora. It lines up exactly.”

Sakura would probably dislike defeating opponents who are in human form, so it should be fine if we return them to their original forms before finishing them off. If they are in their original forms, I doubt she would resist…

Incidentally, there is a reason we are speaking under the assumption that they will be completely defeated.

To put it simply, the monsters known as ‘Final Trials’ have been tamed. And their master is genuinely, seriously dangerous.

“Sakuya-chan, to Master, ‘Final Trials’ are only worth that much.”

“After all, he uses them as test subjects for new weapons.”

“I understand that Onii-chan is unreasonable, but still…”

After being persuaded, or something like it, by Mio and Sera, Sakuya groaned unhappily.

“Relax. Whether they are Final Trials or royalty from any country, I will properly protect your safety, Sakuya.”

“I am happy to hear you say that, Onii-chan, but…!”

Sakuya looked troubled and happy at the same time. She is surprisingly expressive.

“I will protect Master as he protects Sakuya-san.”

“Sera-chan, I am counting on you.”

Maria cannot attend the summit conference, so Sera has been entrusted with the role of guard.

During the summit, the group will be split up, which inevitably increases the level of danger.

“There is something I just remembered. May I bring it up…?”

“Sakura, what is it?”

“Yes… When the summit conference was first mentioned, didn’t Sakuya-chan say she would act as a breakwater to protect Jin-kun…?”

That did happen.

Because whenever I take action, things escalate, I was asked to behave as calmly as possible.

To that end, Sakuya said she would act as a buffer between me and the nobles.

“Ah, yes, she did say that.”

“In this situation, do you really think Sakuya-chan alone can act as a breakwater…?”

Our gazes all gathered on Sakuya.

Sakuya smiled brightly…

“Yeah, absolutely impossible!”

She declared it without hesitation.

Negotiating among heads of state might be one thing, but dealing with monsters that rely entirely on brute force is obviously impossible.

If anything, we need to act as Sakuya’s breakwater in terms of combat power.

For now, I need to strengthen Sakuya’s status to the point where she will not die easily.

As things stand, if she gets caught up in a fight, she would die instantly…

That more or less concluded our discussion of dangerous individuals.

First, we set the basic policy of “not making the first move” against dangerous individuals.

It might feel somewhat passive, but we promised Sakuya, and attacking preemptively without a just cause would only cause endless trouble.

…The drawback of information obtained through Special Powers is that we cannot clearly present it as evidence or justification.

However, we also decided that “if we are attacked, we will not hold back in retaliating”.

Once the other side resorts to force, the chances of Sakuya’s negotiations succeeding drop to nearly zero.

Even Sakuya seemed unable to say “do not fight back” in that situation, and reluctantly approved retaliation. Though she did add, “If possible, please do not go overboard”.

I said, “I will think about it.” Sakuya said, “Say it definitively!”

Among the dangerous individuals, there are five who require particular caution.

The first is the previously mentioned King of the Kingdom of Grants, Zenon Grants.

His race is listed as “Possessed”, and as a man bearing a curse mark, there is a strong possibility he is connected to the demon race.

Considering that we were nearly attacked by soldiers of the Kingdom of Grants, the likelihood of hostility is extremely high. We need to be especially vigilant during the summit.

The second is Sharon, the queen of Regalia, the beastman nation.

The Regalia Beastman Nation is composed of over ninety percent beastmen, and is located north of the Elgant Theocracy.

It has historically had poor relations with human nations, and is a dangerous country that frequently engages in skirmishes.

Since it is unclear why they chose to participate in this summit, caution is required.

Incidentally, the queen herself is quite strong.

The third is one of the Heroes, a girl named Kino Aichi.

Astonishingly, her Blessing value was +14. In other words, she has witnessed the deaths of fourteen Heroes. If she killed them herself, that would be quite something.

Her level is also among the highest, and she likely occupies a representative position among the Heroes.

There is also one more concerning point: the color of her marker. It is red, indicating an enemy, but it also has a faint yellow tint. …A believer?

A: It is believed she is a believer. This cannot be stated definitively.

For some reason, there are quite a few red markers with a yellowish tint. WHY?

An enemy, a believer, a Hero, and a killer. It is impossible not to be cautious.

The fourth and fifth are the two ‘Final Trials.’

Their names are ‘Wind God Tornado’ and ‘Thunder God Lightning.’

They are tamed Final Trials, hiding in the divine capital while taking human form.

There are no decent individuals among the Final Trials, so we cannot ignore their movements.

Also, on a personal note, I would like Sakura and Dora to defeat them. Leaving them out would not be good.

“That should cover everything we needed to discuss regarding dangerous individuals, right?”

I said, summarizing the discussion.

“If we start listing people of concern, there is no end to it.”

“Indeed… Just this alone has been quite exhausting…”

Mio and Sakura both looked tired.

《Fwaa… is it over?》

After mentioning the dragons hidden within the city, Dora had fallen asleep shortly afterward.

Yeah, complicated discussions are impossible for Dora.

“I believe Sera-chan will be fine, but I really wish we had a precognition skill. The situation is too complex, and unforeseen circumstances seem likely.”

“Indeed. Let us hope that Rico-san’s training concludes soon.”

Maria and Sera were discussing the matter of guards.

According to Lucea, Rico’s training is progressing smoothly.

She has an excellent memory and is absorbing techniques one after another. She has grown accustomed to activating her precognition skill, and has shown high aptitude for close combat. That is Lucea’s assessment.

Once she has fully mastered it, I plan to make her one of Sakuya’s guards.

Three days have passed since we checked the map of the divine capital of the Elgant Theocracy.

At this pace, we should arrive at the divine capital today.

“Thank you very much for having me!”

Inside the swaying carriage, the one who bowed energetically in greeting was the dwarf Hero who had just completed her maid training.

Her messy orange hair had regained its luster and was neatly styled into a short bob. Her skin had been well cared for, and if she were not wearing a maid outfit, she would look exactly like a young lady from a noble family.

Her eyes, the same orange as her hair, were wide open and lively, giving her a bright, energetic impression.

Being a dwarf, she looks like nothing more than a little girl, but…

“Ah, likewise.”

“Yes!”

Rico went around greeting each member one by one.

When greeting Maria, her eyes sparkled fifty percent brighter as she said, “Senior! I look forward to working with you!” In reality, Rico is older, though…

“Then I am thinking of assigning Rico as Sakuya’s guard. During the summit, she will participate in the maid role.”

“Yes! Leave it to me!”

Rico is incredibly energetic.

She looks nothing like the girl who once wore a face of complete resignation at the slave trader.

“Still, you really made it just in time. I have heard that Lucea-san’s maid training is quite severe.”

“Yes, it was very difficult! But today, I somehow managed to receive Lucea-sama’s approval! If I had more talent, I could have joined everyone sooner, but…”

Rico answered Sera’s question with a wry smile, but the fact that she overcame Lucea’s serious training is something she can be proud of.

“Also, aside from combat training, my maid skills are barely at a passing level, so it has already been decided that I will retrain after this is over! I am still inexperienced!”

She is far more stoic than I expected.

“Then is your combat training sufficient?”

“Yes! I have also received full certification from Lucea-sama!”

“Oh? Achieving that in just one week is impressive.”

Lucea would never give sloppy training to someone she allows to accompany me.

If she granted full certification, then Rico must be quite capable.

“I am honored!”

Out of curiosity, I examined Rico’s equipment as she bowed.

What caught my attention was her main weapon.

Maria is a dual-wielding swordswoman.

Cynthia uses staff techniques… no, she is basically a martial artist now.

Since the two Heroes have fairly specialized combat styles, I was curious about how the third, Rico, fought.

“…Don’t tell me, a hidden-weapon user?”

“Yes! Maid outfits are very convenient for hiding many things! Since I am a guard, I will use any weapon or method necessary to protect my charge!”

As she declared, Rico had numerous concealed weapons hidden within her maid outfit.

Because she is small, she cannot carry many, but she makes up for that with Storage magic and item bags.

She does not use Infinite Storage so that she can explain the origin of her weapons if questioned.

If she replenished her hidden weapons frequently, someone might ask where they came from. She does not want to lie, so she avoids relying on Infinite Storage from the start.

“Speaking of combat ability, how is your precognition skill? Is it usable in battle?”

“Yes! I am still training, but it has taken shape to some extent!”

“Specifically?”

“I can now almost perfectly avoid surprise attacks!”

According to Rico, precognition activates just before a fatal attack, allowing her to take evasive action.

This makes it possible to prevent surprise attacks while in an unguarded state.

However, several weaknesses have also become apparent.

First, Unavoidable Tragedy cannot be used consecutively.

After one use, there is a thirty-second cooldown, so facing repeated lethal attacks would be difficult.

So far, there has never been a situation where another crisis occurred before the thirty seconds elapsed.

Additionally, if the opponent is powerful enough to twist fate itself, they may respond to her evasive or defensive actions with further attacks.

In such cases, Unavoidable Tragedy becomes completely useless, and it turns into a pure contest of strength.

In the end, it became clear that rather than using it continuously as support during battle, it is better to focus on using it to prevent the initial dangerous strike.

“Therefore, I cannot constantly evade using Unavoidable Tragedy! It is strictly a skill for guarding!”

“I see… As expected, it did not work that conveniently.”

If one could continuously foresee their own danger during combat, that would be practically invincibility.

“Lucea-sama told me, ‘You can rely on it, but you must not depend on it entirely.’”

“Lucea says good things.”

“Yes!”

Since she understands its characteristics that well, there is nothing more I need to say.

“Rico-chan, Rico-chan, may I have a moment?”

“What is it, Mio-san?”

Before I knew it, Mio was holding a plate.

On it were several cream puffs…

“I want to see the power of Rico-chan’s precognition skill. So, I have prepared Mio-chan’s special cream puffs. Out of eight puffs, only one contains extremely spicy cream! Can you successfully avoid the spicy one until the end!? That is the skit!”

She called it a skit herself.

Well, the probability of the spicy puff being last is one out of eight. Anyone could do that without precognition.

“That is fine, but is it really okay for me to receive the sweets?”

“Of course. I have always wanted to do this kind of thing with a precognitive ability user.”

Ah, I understand that feeling…

“Playing with food is not good, but we are not wasting ingredients, so it is fine! If the spicy one remains at the end, I plan to give it to a maid who likes spicy food.”

“What happens if I draw the spicy one along the way?”

It is possible that Unavoidable Tragedy would not activate for something like a spicy cream puff.

“The remaining sweet ones can be eaten by anyone who wants them.”

《Dora wants to eat!》

Dora raised her hand without hesitation.

“Understood! Then here I go!”

“You are decisive!”

No sooner had she spoken than Rico swiftly took a cream puff and stuffed it into her mouth in a single bite.

“!!!”

Rico’s face turned bright red as she covered her mouth.

“Eh? A one-shot hit!?”

Even Mio was left dumbfounded.

She probably never imagined that someone with precognition would draw the spicy puff on the first try.

“Haa, haa… P-please share the rest among yourselves…”

“Ah, I see…”

At that moment, we realized Rico’s intention.

In other words, she deliberately ate the spicy puff so that everyone else could enjoy the remaining sweet ones.

“Isn’t your self-sacrificial spirit way too strong!?”

“I-I am a guard!”

“That has nothing to do with it… Here, drink some water.”

“Th-thank you.”

After gulping down the water Mio gave her, Rico finally caught her breath.

Mio then spoke to Rico with a troubled expression.

“I am sorry, Rico-chan, but there are still plenty of cream puffs, you know? Since you joined us as a travel companion, I also intended to give you extra cream puffs as a service. You did not need to push yourself like that.”

“S-so that was the case!?”

Realizing her consideration had completely backfired, Rico slumped her shoulders dejectedly.

It was probably Dora saying she wanted to eat cream puffs that triggered it.

After that, while letting Rico cleanse her palate, we gave her extra cream puffs and enjoyed Mio’s special cream puffs ourselves as well.

“Master, it is almost time. What shall we do?”

With less than two hours remaining until arrival at the divine capital, Vega reported in.

“Already? …Well then, what should we do?”

“Honestly… what a pain. What on earth are they thinking?”

“It is surely nothing reasonable.”

It is no wonder Mio and Sera look exasperated.

The others all wear similar expressions.

What awaits us ahead?

Simply put, bandits from the Elgant Theocracy are lying in wait for us.

To reach the divine capital, one must pass through several fixed routes, and bandits have been placed along them.

This method is similar to that of the Kingdom of Grants, but instead of using regular soldiers disguised as bandits, they are using real bandits.

They captured bandits, promised them amnesty if they killed us, and released them back into the wild.

There are two points I dislike about this.

First, the bandits are clearly disposable pawns.

Their levels and equipment are poor. They are nowhere near worthy of being sent against the knights who destroyed Eldia.

The purpose is likely to measure our strength. From a distant location, regular soldiers of the Elgant Theocracy are observing with something akin to telescopes.

Second, there is nothing to gain from defeating the bandits.

Their weapons are cheap, they have almost no money, and rare magical tools are out of the question. There is almost no benefit to dealing with them.

Frankly, it is a waste of time to deal with such people.

I also do not want to reveal our combat strength under surveillance.

However, since they are bandits, ignoring them entirely is also not an option.

“Jin-sama! If you do not mind, may I take care of the bandits?”

As I was thinking about how to handle the bandits, Rico raised her hand energetically and made that proposal.

“Normally, it is not ideal for a guard to step forward, but I want you to see my abilities first!”

“Hmm, there are about twenty of them. Are you sure you will be alright?”

Even if their equipment is poor, they are still an armed group of around twenty.

For a girl with only training experience, that might be too much… though I am sure Lucea prepared her for this.

“I will be fine! I have wiped out larger bandit groups by myself before! I am already accustomed to killing people!”

Lucea’s training. Just as I thought… no, even more ruthless than I imagined.

In just about ten days, how far did she push her?

“That is brutal. Lucea-san’s training…”

“Yes… I would never receive a passing mark…”

“As expected of Lucea-san. Splendid education.”

“Indeed. To finish both body and mind in such a short time…”

Opinions split between Mio and Sakura, and Maria and Sera.

Native inhabitants of this world really do react differently.

“If you say that much, then let us leave the bandits to Rico. …Ah, but we should take care of the observers first.”

《What are you doing?》

“I just said it. Blinding their eyes.”

As I answered Dora, I activated Flash from Light Magic Level 2.

Flash is a simple blinding spell, but if you increase its light output through Expanded Interpretation and look at it through lenses, what do you think happens?

Naturally, it blinds them, right? …Good. The observing soldiers are clutching their eyes and writhing in pain.

“Master is just as brutal…”

“Alright, Rico. Do it.”

“Yes! Leave it to me!”

With that, Rico leapt out of the carriage.

Incidentally, the carriage was still moving at full speed.

The bandits had locked onto our carriage and were moving to block the road.

Rico moved faster than the carriage and closed in on them in an instant.

She was not using \<Shukuchi> or anything like that. That was her raw speed. Fast.

She slipped through the bandits as she advanced.

As she passed, the bandits collapsed one after another.

It seemed she was throwing needle-like objects at their necks as she passed by.

That alone was enough to kill them.

Rico collected the dead bandits into Storage and ran back to the carriage.

During all this, the carriage never stopped even once.

“It is done!”

Rico declared with a refreshing smile.

There was no blood on her, and she was not even out of breath. It was hard to believe she had just wiped out a bandit group.

Heroes born in this world are truly something else.

“I would like to praise you for a job well done, but with that fighting style, I cannot judge whether you can handle close combat as a guard…”

“Ah!? That is true…”

Rico collapsed dejectedly, her expression fitting a dramatic sound effect.

We learned that she has combat power and the resolve to kill without hesitation, but she did not seem to use her precognition skill, so her aptitude as a guard remains undetermined.

Extermination ability and guarding aptitude have no correlation at all.

“It might have been better to bring Sakuya in front of the bandits and see if you could protect her while exterminating them.”

“Why would I be brought in front of bandits!?”

Sakuya cried out in shock at my suggestion.

…Yeah, there was no need to use the real guard target.

“…Well, setting aside guard aptitude, I have confirmed that Rico has combat sense. I hope I never need to, but I will have you show your abilities after we arrive at the divine capital.”

“Yes! I will meet your expectations next time, Jin-sama! I will not let my guard down for even a moment!”

Revitalized, Rico clenched her fists.

“Alright, do your best. But for now, I think you do not need to be that tense. According to the map, there should be no more obstacles. All that is left is to relax and wait until we arrive at the divine capital.”

“Once we arrive at the divine capital, relaxing will be impossible, right…”

“That is likely. Jin-sama’s desired sightseeing may also be difficult.”

We had originally decided, “While sightseeing in the divine nation, do not involve yourself in trouble”, but given this situation, I am not optimistic enough to believe we can tour the divine capital without incident.

“Yeah. This is far different from what I imagined. Sightseeing will probably be impossible.”

Frankly, I do not even want to sightsee in such a chaotic city. Sightseeing is best done in times of peace, or during events unique to the land.

Sudden, non-reproducible events do not convey the character of a place, making them unsatisfying as sightseeing.

“Even if it is just an act, becoming important really does restrict your freedom…”

I muttered with feeling.

Even when there are enemies you are certain will be hostile, you cannot strike first.

Even when there are places to see, you cannot go out due to trouble prevention.

If I were not pretending to be a knight of the queen, perhaps I could act freely…

“No, Onii-chan is still more than free enough?”

At Sakuya’s retort, the others nodded. …I do not accept that.

After defeating the bandits, we traveled for about two more hours by carriage, and finally, the divine capital of the Elgant Theocracy, Elgare, came into view.

Elgare has a population exceeding two hundred thousand, making it a super-megacity, the largest in this world.

The city is a perfect circle, with an exact diameter of ten kilometers.

There is not even a one-centimeter deviation. …Given the level of civilization, that is impossible without external help, right? Probably a Hero was involved somehow?

A: Yes. As mentioned before, the Hero of the generation that defeated the Demon King who destroyed the old divine capital was involved in the construction.

Ah, the place that once housed the Boundary Gate connecting this world and the Gray World was originally the divine capital, right?

So a Hero was involved during the relocation. Well, originally, stopping the destruction of the city would have been the Hero’s job… A Hero specialized in reconstruction feels oddly ominous.

Setting aside omens, the cityscape is impressive, as expected of something a Hero was involved in.

The entire city being white is typical of the Elgant Theocracy, but above all else, the most magnificent structure is the grand cathedral towering at the city center.

Normally, a royal castle would occupy that position, but fitting for a religious nation, a grand cathedral stands there instead.

Although it is called a cathedral, in practice it is no different from a royal castle. It does not merely serve as a place of prayer, but also handles the practical affairs of state.

The summit conference will also be held in this cathedral. Precisely enemy territory!

“We are entering enemy territory, so we need to be properly armed.”

“Oni… Jin, you are already strong enough without arming yourself.”

Seeing me fully equipped in armor, Sakuya muttered.

We are close to reaching the city gates, so I need to enter Gene mode.

It makes me very uneasy that Sakuya almost said “Onii-chan.”

“If anything, it might even reduce your combat effectiveness by restricting movement.”

“Even so, compared to ordinary armor, it places virtually no burden on the wearer.”

The armor made by Mimi, who possesses \<Sacred Demonic Blacksmithing>, is certainly designed to minimize burden on the wearer, but as long as one wears armor, it will inevitably impede movement to some degree.

There is no point in increasing defense if it results in taking more hits. If you are not hit, it does not matter. Paper defense and godly evasion are justice. …That might be an exaggeration.

“I guess I am just not used to it, since I rarely wear armor.”

“For an adventurer, Master’s lack of interest in armor is still strange, you know?”

“Mio-chan, Jin-kun has high base defense, after all…”

It seems I am an outlier among adventurers for barely wearing armor at all.

The problem is that the stat increase from armor is like a rounding error.

Only Mimi’s fantasy-grade equipment is even worth using.

“In this world, the only one who managed to seriously injure Master was that old butler you fought when leaving Eldia, right?”

“Yes. Since then, I have never seen Jin-sama injured.”

As Mio and Maria said, aside from the scratch I received while fighting the old butler, I have not taken any meaningful damage in this world.

The battle with Orihara does not count, since that was not in this world.

“Maria-senpai, may I ask you something?”

“What is it?”

Rico asked Maria a question.

“Is a guard truly necessary for Jin-sama?”

“…He has been ambushed before, so I believe a guard with a precognition skill may have some value.”

Maria said this while suppressing her own sense of powerlessness.

Maria calls herself my guard, but she has never truly protected me.

“Then can I truly be of use as Jin-sama’s guard!?”

“Yes, there is a possibility. However, if the opponent is someone capable of placing Jin-sama in a truly dangerous situation, there is a high chance that Rico-san’s precognition could be twisted, so it cannot be said with certainty.”

“That… cannot be helped.”

Rico’s \<Unavoidable Tragedy> is powerless against someone capable of twisting fate itself.

The clearest example would be that it would be difficult for Rico’s precognition to stop Orihara.

That is precisely why Maria desperately wants a more reliable precognitive skill.

With such a skill, there would at least be a non-zero chance of stopping Orihara… not that the chance would be high.

---

**AN:** Kino-chan appears casually by name. For details, see Side Story 8 in Volume 6.

Also, sorry about this. Since my writing has not been progressing smoothly, it looks like updates will continue at a ten-day interval for a while.

**Editor’s Note:** Don’t worry about the author’s update notice(s), Chapter 132 was written way back in 2018/02/20. Sometimes there’s good information, so I’ll keep including the pre-word and afterwords, but sometimes they are meaningless and I’m tempted to omit them.

## **133: Assassins and Speed Freaks**

**AN:** Since February does not have 30 days, I am posting this as a substitute.

I think January and March should each donate one day to February.

---

This time, we truly arrived at the divine capital Elgare of the Elgant Theocracy.

It is surrounded by tall outer walls, with one gate each to the east, west, south, and north. This part is the same as Eldia.

Of those, we arrived at the west gate. Incidentally, if we had headed straight to the divine capital from the Kingdom of Sanokia, we should have arrived at the south gate.

The guards at the west gate seemed surprised that Castal’s carriage had come through the west gate, but I could not tell whether they were surprised that we entered from the west rather than the south, or that we arrived at the divine capital alive at all.

Guided by the gate guards, we advanced our carriage toward the inn.

I want to believe there would be no fools who would attack us after we arrived at the divine capital, but given precedent, I cannot relax.

As proof, most of the map display is red (enemies).

Most of the representatives from each country have already gathered, and aside from Castal, it seems only one country has yet to arrive.

According to a fast courier, that country should arrive tomorrow, so including preparations, the summit meeting is expected to be held the day after tomorrow. Assuming the courier does not do anything unnecessary.

I checked on the map just in case, and it looked like they would arrive without incident.

After proceeding for a while, we arrived at the inn where we would be staying.

It was a luxurious inn befitting royalty.

Unlike in the city of Elrim, there was no attempt to split us up.

Apparently, royalty and nobles participating in the summit are each assigned to separate inns. Well, that is essential to avoid trouble.

As we were about to enter the inn, a man who looked like the manager stopped us at the entrance.

“At our hotel, for safety and identity verification, we require guests to temporarily disarm upon entry. We appreciate your cooperation.”

I see, so that is how they intend to handle it.

In terms of probing my identity, it might be a reasonably effective method.

…Ah, what a truly ridiculous country.

“I have not heard of any such arrangement up to this point. If there is such a rule, is it not proper to inform us in advance?”

Before I could say anything, Sakuya questioned the manager.

Even Sakuya seemed irritated, her tone unusually sharp.

“It appears there was a lapse in communication. We sincerely apologize. We will impose strict punishment on those who failed to inform you, so could you please comply with the hotel’s rules?”

The manager apologized and humbled himself, yet did not bend the rules.

“Hm, so you are saying that, even temporarily, you wish to reduce my escort?”

“N-no! Of course not! While your guards are disarming, our hotel’s own security staff will ensure everyone’s safety.”

“Haa… You truly do not understand.”

Sakuya let out a deep sigh.

“And what do you mean by that?”

“I am saying that this entire hotel, including that security staff, is not worthy of trust!”

“W-what!?”

Apparently not expecting to be openly insulted at the entrance, the manager and all the staff froze in shock.

“To begin with, this so-called disarmament rule was established after the summit was decided, was it not? And at the request of the state, no less… It is far too blatant!”

“H-how do you know that…”

“There is no obligation for me to explain such things to the likes of you!”

Needless to say, this information came from Alta.

“I have no intention of staying at such a worthless hotel! Camping would be preferable to this!”

Sakuya turned on her heel and walked back toward the carriage, ignoring the stunned manager and staff.

Even for a manager, being told their hotel was ‘worse than camping’ must have been a first.

Because of these circumstances, we have now set up a temporary base outside the walls of Elgare, the divine capital of the Elgant Theocracy.

According to Sakuya, she did consider staying at another inn, but judged that any other would be no different from that one.

South of the Elgant Theocracy, slightly off the main road on a grassland, we lined up our carriages, and using lumber taken from item boxes by the maids, temporary housing was completed in no time.

We did not obtain permission from the Elgant Theocracy, but apparently there is no law forbidding the construction of temporary housing on grasslands. It is dangerous since it is outside the range of barrier stones that repel monsters, so monsters normally inhabit the area.

As it was already dusk, we hurriedly set up the temporary housing and then had dinner.

The housing is divided into several buildings, with Sakuya and me in the same one. Since we have private matters to discuss, the ministers are in a separate building.

“That was quite a declaration, Sakuya.”

“Even I could not keep enduring such atrocious treatment.”

“But is it really alright to leave like that? Won’t it become a problem?”

In response to Sera’s question, Sakuya shook her head.

“I do not think it will be a problem, but it will be a nuisance. …See?”

“That was within expectations. Jin-sama, what will you do?”

Maria asked me after looking in the direction Sakuya indicated.

“There is no option but annihilation. Kill them all.”

As expected from the inn’s attitude, assassins were already heading toward our temporary housing from Elgare. Naturally, the response is annihilation.

“Haha… You seem quite irritated too, Master.”

“Of course. Do you think I would like a country where I cannot even sightsee and hostility is laid bare?”

“No way.”

Mio gave a wry smile upon hearing my serious declaration.

“Now then, the remaining question is who will do the annihilating…”

“Yes! Please give me another chance!”

The one who raised her hand was Rico.

She must have been frustrated at not being able to demonstrate her skills as an escort during the bandit incident earlier, and seemed eager this time.

Since someone is motivated, there is no need to dampen that enthusiasm.

“Alright, understood. We will leave this to Rico.”

“Yes! Leave it to me!”

“…Since I want to verify your escort ability, Rico, annihilate the enemies while guarding me.”

(twitch)

“I will do my best!”

Rico’s escort target is Sakuya, but we cannot exactly use Sakuya as a practice dummy.

It is better to have her escort me and verify her ability.

This is trivial, but the moment I said I would be the escort target, Maria reacted ever so slightly.

However, after confirming Rico’s skills and the assassins abilities, judging there was no danger to me, she said nothing. If Maria accompanied us, the point of using Rico as the escort would be diminished.

The assassins appear to be the assassin type, approaching our temporary housing while hiding themselves.

Naturally, they are powerless before the map.

They did not even glance at the building where the other ministers were, heading straight for the building where Sakuya and I are. They must be monitoring from the outer walls.

A: Yes.

After a while, the assassins who had been observing the surroundings gathered near the entrance and window.

This temporary housing has only one window and one door. There are also no partitions that could really be called rooms.

The assassins nodded to each other, smashed the window, kicked in the door, and rushed in all at once.

Men clad in black filled the room. There were ten of them! It is cramped!

“What!?”

One of the assassins cried out involuntarily.

Given that there were only two people in the room, Rico and me, that reaction was understandable.

The others are staying in rooms created by the Room spell so as not to get in the way.

If other members were present, it would be impossible to accurately gauge Rico’s abilities.

For indoor combat, we deliberately left things like the table in place.

“Leader!”

“It does not matter. Kill whoever is here!”

At the leader’s command, one assassin lunged at Rico.

“You uninvited guests are quite rude!”

“Ugh!? Gah!”

Rico ducked under the assassin’s knife, swiftly swept his legs out from under him, and knocked him down.

The moment he fell, she stabbed a needle into his neck, finishing him without fail.

“Impossible! Was the only guard in this room not that man!?”

“That is a lovely misunderstanding. All of our maids receive combat training.”

Rico replied politely to the assassin’s shout.

“In here, they cannot swing long weapons! In a melee, we have the advantage in numbers! Everyone, target the knight first!”

At the leader’s words, the remaining eight charged at me simultaneously.

“I will not allow it!”

Rico stepped between me and the assassins and dealt with them one by one.

Against assassins who approached in irregular movements to create chaos, Rico closed in with minimal motion and delivered decisive strikes with concealed weapons.

After stabbing three in rapid succession, she dashed toward the fourth.

Rico’s greatest weapons are her agility due to her small frame and her speed.

Her lack of strength and her weapons low attack power are compensated by striking vital points.

Including her precognition, her abilities are fundamentally specialized for fighting people.

After killing the fourth assassin, Rico picked up the knife he carried and threw it at the fifth.

“Why can we not even kill a single little girl!? Guh!”

The fifth died with a knife embedded in his throat, his face frozen in shock.

Even though her Throwing skill is only level 1, she could accurately throw an unfamiliar weapon. She is dexterous in a different way than Maria.

“Retreat! At least bring back information!”

When the sixth (seventh if you included the very first) died, the leader ordered a retreat.

The remaining two besides the leader turned and tried to flee.

“I will not let you escape!”

Rico threw knives at the fleeing assassins.

“Gah!?”

“Ghk!?”

“Tch!”

The two underlings were struck and killed, but the leader deflected the knife aimed at his neck with his own and tried to escape through the door.

Rico did pursue, but did not chase the fleeing assassin further.

As an escort, she prioritized protecting her charge over killing the assassin. Excellent.

“You pass.”

“W-why… how…”

Having confirmed Rico’s abilities, I approached the assassin who had finished his role using Shukuchi and cut him down.

Sorry. I could not let him escape.

It is not because information leaking would be a problem or anything like that.

I had already said ‘annihilation’ at the start, and I did not want to take it back.

We quickly disposed of the assassins bodies and called back the other members who had been waiting in the Room.

Dora was already asleep, and it would be cruel to wake her, so we left her be.

“Jin-sama, how was it?”

Rico asked, looking slightly anxious.

“As I said earlier, you pass. One hundred points.”

“Huh? You let the last assassin escape, but is it really okay to give a hundred points?”

Mio asked curiously after hearing my evaluation.

“That does not count toward the evaluation of escort ability. For escort duties, stopping at throwing knives without pursuing deeply is sufficient.”

“I see, you are evaluating purely escort ability.”

Mio nodded in understanding.

“If I had to point out an improvement, in that final throw, aiming for the legs rather than a killing blow would have been better, assuming allies would pursue. It is harder to block that way.”

“I will keep that in mind!”

Granted, there were no allies nearby at that moment, but still.

“Still, Rico-san, you are incredibly fast. Just watching the map display, it was hard to grasp what you were doing.”

“I… I gave up halfway… I could not follow it with the simplified display…”

For Sera and the others observing via the map from inside the Room, Rico’s speed was difficult to track.

In simplified display mode, the map is not suitable for grasping specific movements.

Someone like Kate from the explorer group, using the full 3D display, might be able to tell, but the processing load would fry the brain.

“Yes, thank you! I trained with an emphasis on speed, so I am happy about that evaluation! But it is still not fast enough! Jin-sama was moving even faster! I could not follow you at all!”

I had suspected it, but Rico’s speed-focused tactics were indeed deliberate.

“Um… I believe that is probably a skill called Shukuchi?”

“Is that so!? Jin-sama, I want to use that skill! What should I do!?”

She seems obsessed with speed, immediately wanting Shukuchi.

“Rico-san, I learned that skill on my own, so I can teach you when we have time.”

“Really!? Maria-senpai, please teach me!”

As an aside, surprisingly many of my subordinates have learned \<Shukuchi> on their own.

It is not easy, but with proper instruction, it is an attainable technique.

Me? I cannot self-learn any skills at all. I tried, but it did not work.

“By the way, Rico, may I ask why you chose speed-focused tactics? You must have had a clear reason.”

“Yes! To achieve my goal, speed was more important than anything!”

“And your goal is…?”

“To overturn my precognition!”

That was equal to her reason for seeking strength.

“My precognition lets me know of misfortune befalling those close to me! With power, I can twist that future! But there is no guarantee that the twisted future will be better than the original!”

Even if she can overturn the future, it could end up worse than what she foresaw.

“To improve the twisted future even a little, to get ahead of incoming misfortune even slightly, I decided to prioritize speed above all else!”

If she can move faster and respond quicker, the chances of twisting misfortune in a better direction increase.

She sought the most useful ability in line with her purpose.

“That makes sense. Rather than increasing attack or defense, increasing speed does offer more versatility.”

“Yes! Given my race’s agility, I think the direction is not wrong!”

Because she is a dwarf, her appearance makes her look young, but she is the same age as Sera, right?

Of course she has thought things through.

“I agree. I think you are right.”

“Yes! Thank you very much!”

Watching Rico pursue speed, something suddenly came to mind.

“By the way, I have a blessing-derived skill stolen from a Hero called Acceleration.”

“What kind of skill is that?”

Rico tilted her head, apparently not having been told about it yet.

“When activated, time slows down, and only I can move at normal speed within it. Simply put, I can move faster than my surroundings.”

“!?”

Rico’s eyes widened.

As she was about to speak, I continued.

“Unfortunately, blessing-derived skills cannot be increased or learned later, so there are only the ones I have.”

“… (slump)”

It must be a skill she desperately wants, but she cannot ask for a skill I am using, and being told it is impossible leaves her helpless.

Her shoulders slumped in disappointment.

Raise… and drop!

“Master, you really are mean…”

“Mio, would you like to take a solo tour of the graveyard?”

“Hii!? N-no, nothing at all!”

I silenced Mio for her unnecessary remark.

Rico might actually be fun to tease. I am looking forward to it.

The next day, we spent our time relaxing at the temporary housing instead of going into Elgare.

There was nothing good to be gained by going into the city, so it was obvious.

Assassins came from time to time, but the maid knights dealt with them, so there was no problem.

The maids who are not knights do not fight. It would not be good for it to become known that ordinary maids have combat ability.

Incidentally, there were also those who tried to take Sakuya and the others away under the guise of an apology from the Elgant Theocracy, but they were firmly repelled as well.

For the record, we did not kill them. They came as official envoys, so we politely but coldly sent them back.

Apparently, these assassins are acting on the orders of one of the Elgant Theocracy’s leaders, a certain priest. A devout follower of the goddess and Heroes, he cannot forgive Castal and me for killing a Hero and harming Eldia.

Furthermore, the Pope, the top of the Elgant Theocracy, is tacitly approving this.

Tacit approval from a superior basically makes them an accomplice, does it not?

At this point… or rather, from even earlier, my interest in the Elgant Theocracy had completely dropped to zero.

I want to hurry up and finish this annoying meeting and go sightseeing somewhere else…

Around noon, a report from Alta revealed that a group of monsters was approaching us.

What was happening was that several carriages carrying a participating country that would arrive in the Elgant Theocracy today were being chased by a horde of monsters.

I immediately had the maid knights prepare and ordered them to rescue the fleeing carriages.

I would prefer to go myself, but with eyes watching, I cannot move too openly.

“…I cannot exactly let Cattleya’s younger brother die.”

In fact, the carriages being chased belong to the Kingdom of Estea, which is participating in the summit.

Since the king could not leave his country, Estea’s prince, Cattleya’s younger brother, is attending in his stead. Cattleya mentioned it at dinner (probably classified information).

Apparently, although Estea was invited to the summit due to its relation to the Castal-Eldia war, they were not sent the long-distance communication magic tool, the Far-Sight Paired Mirror, and were told to attend in person.

Normally, for a country as distant as Estea, a Far-Sight Paired Mirror should be sent, but the Elgant Theocracy refused, citing a shortage.

Unable to skip the summit, Estea finally arrived after a journey even longer than ours.

Incidentally, countries closer than Estea did receive Far-Sight Paired Mirrors. Estea is pro-Castal, so this was harassment. Damn them.

Furthermore, this monster attack does not seem to be a coincidence.

It appears to be the result of the same priest who hates Castal giving orders to his subordinate monster tamers.

If Estea’s carriages are wiped out, fine. If Castal, which lies along their route, suffers damage, also fine. If they reach Elgare and the Elgant Theocracy suppresses it, creating a debt for Estea, also fine. A flawless plan. Damn them.

This plan was originally prepared to annihilate Castal.

Since we took a different route, it became completely pointless… or rather, since they reused it on Estea, perhaps it was not pointless? Damn them.

“We are heading out.”

“Ah, I am counting on you.”

The maid knights mounted their horses and departed one after another.

Objective one: rescue the Kingdom of Estea’s carriages. Objective two: subjugate the monsters being stirred up. Objective three: secure the Elgant Theocracy’s monster tamer.

Monster tamers have Monster Training, and the monsters they use are rare monsters with rare skills. When someone you can kill has rare skills, you cannot help but feel happy, right?

Stampede Devil (Rare)

LV30

\<Night Vision LV2> \<Flight LV2> \<Mad Screech LV5>

Notes: A vicious monster that drives other monsters into a berserk state and intentionally causes stampedes.

\<Mad Screech>

Drives monsters that hear the scream into a berserk state. Can be given some directional guidance. Does not work on stronger monsters.

It looks like a squat-bodied bat, and honestly, it is neither cool nor cute.

Even if told it is rare, I do not want it at all. The skill is not to my taste either.

Well, it is not my taste, but rare is rare, so I will take it anyway.

I check the maid knights’ movements on the map.

They seem to have split into two groups based on objectives. There are three objectives but two groups because the monster tamer and the monster are acting together.

The first group headed to rescue Estea’s carriages.

There are about one hundred rampaging monsters. With ten maid knights, they can easily annihilate them. Many are beast-type monsters, with none posing a real threat.

As expected, the monsters were eliminated one after another. The Estea party stopped their carriages and joined the fight, so it should be over faster than expected.

The second group went to subjugate the Stampede Devil and restrain the monster tamer.

These disgusting individuals gave the rampaging monsters direction to attack Estea’s carriages and watched from behind, so there is no need for mercy.

The maid knights ambushed the monster tamers who were grinning as they watched, quickly killed the Stampede Devil, and restrained the monster tamers.

Fortunately, the monster tamer was in a position not visible from those monitoring us, so I had a Portal set up and went to interrogate him myself.

I left Maria behind.

“W-what the hell are you! Do you know who I am!? I am a subordinate of a priest of the Elgant Theocracy! You think you can get away with this!?”

So, this small fry overflowing with loser energy is the captured monster tamer.

He is bound by the maid knights and now lies at my feet.

In that state, his bluster is merely comical.

Oh, I will skip introducing his name and status. Aside from Monster Training, he is a worthless nobody. How did he even manage to tame a Stampede Devil?

“You are the one who set the monsters upon the carriage carrying Estea royalty, are you not?”

I interrogate the small fry in my knightly tone.

“Hah! I have no idea what you are talking about. Are you people from the Kingdom of Estea? I told you, I am a subordinate of a high-ranking priest of the Elgant Theocracy! Do you understand this will become an international incident!?”

To be blunt, this has gone too far.

I promised Sakuya to keep things as discreet as possible, but this has easily exceeded the limits of ‘as possible’.

They have clearly directed killing intent at us and even targeted Estea royalty.

There is no way that priest can be forgiven. And since he cannot be forgiven, his fate is decided.

“There is only one thing I want to ask. …Where did you tame the Stampede Devil?”

That is the reason I personally approached this small fry.

This Stampede Devil is clearly different in nature from monsters I have encountered so far.

I am curious where it was tamed. I am not interested in the Stampede Devil itself, but there might be other monsters to my taste.

“Hah? I told you, I do not know anything about such a monster!”

“Is the Stampede Devil to the north? South? East? West? …I see. West.”

“W-why…”

Because when I said west, there was a tiny reaction.

Given that, it is probably correct. I might look into it.

A: Leave it to me.

Ah, Alta will handle it.

“Now then, I have nothing more to ask. You will receive punishment. Having attacked foreign royalty, you will atone with your life.”

My business is done, so the monster tamer will die.

There is an option to take him alive, but frankly, it is a hassle.

If we protested to the Elgant Theocracy, they would surely feign ignorance, and handing him over would risk leaking our information. There is no benefit.

If I really wanted, I could gather evidence and condemn the Elgant Theocracy, but what would we gain from that?

I thought it through, and I no longer believe we can have proper negotiations with the Elgant Theocracy.

“What!? Don’t mess with me! Weren’t you listening!? You plan to kill a church affiliate of the Elgant Theocracy without evidence!?”

As an aside, the assassins so far carried no items that could serve as evidence of ties to the Elgant Theocracy, nor did they make statements implying involvement. This small fry, however, openly acknowledges being affiliated.

Unlike the others, he did not act with resolve. Perhaps he never imagined this plan carried the risk of capture.

“You do not need evidence. There are witnesses. And since the order came from an Elgant Theocracy priest, the judiciary cannot be trusted. Summary execution on site is the only option.”

“W-witnesses…!”

Yes, of course, Alta.

“There is no point telling you this, since you are about to die.”

“Hii!”

I draw Mimi’s holy sword, Ultimesia, from its scabbard, then decide it is wasted on such a small fry and put it away, taking out a normal sword instead.

Sword in hand, I slowly approach the monster tamer.

“S-stop… Please don’t kill me… No…”

Since I do not enjoy prolonging suffering, I beheaded the monster tamer in a single strike.

“It looks like the Estea carriages are taken care of. …Can I leave the cleanup here to you?”

“Yes, leave it to us.”

Leaving the rest to the maid knights, I returned to the temporary housing.

The Estea party is being escorted to Castal’s temporary housing, and it would be bad to be absent.

Oh, and while the maid knights were away rescuing Estea, assassins apparently attacked the temporary housing again. Did they think it was a chance because there were fewer people?

Naturally, they were immediately annihilated. Truly persistent.
