**AN:** Next time, updates will resume on the 10-day schedule.

The conference arc, which took an unreasonable amount time to write, begins.

+++

## **134: The Summit Conference and the First Agenda Item**

**AN:** The summit conference begins. There are surprisingly few new characters.

---

One hour had passed since the maid knights rescued the carriage carrying the princes of the Kingdom of Estea.

At present, the envoys, including the prince from the Kingdom of Estea, were resting inside a newly set-up temporary housing unit near our own temporary residences.

Fortunately, there had been no fatalities among the escort soldiers of the Kingdom of Estea, but there were quite a number of injured, including several with serious wounds.

It seemed they had risked their lives to buy time for the carriage to depart just before being pursued by a monster horde.

There was no reason to hide anything, so we had given the members of the Kingdom of Estea a full explanation regarding the monster attack.

The explanation itself had been given by the maid knights, so I did not hear it directly, but apparently the prince had muttered, “So it really was as we thought…”

They had apparently encountered danger many times along the journey here.

Naturally, there was no proof showing the involvement of the Elgant Theocracy, but there was no other party to suspect.

It was pointless to say it now, but perhaps we should have assigned subordinates to the Estean envoys as well.

After all, we already had subordinates embedded within the Estean royal palace via the princess.

As an aside, in countries where royal subordinates are present, those subordinates are also embedded within the national leadership beyond just the royalty.

Their official positions are generally maids or close attendants, but I have heard they are valued quite highly due to their competence. Given their inherent abilities plus the benefits of special powers, that is only natural.

Back to the topic at hand.

After resting briefly in the temporary housing, the Estean envoys reported their arrival to the Elgant Theocracy, but they refused to stay at Elgant-provided lodging.

The reason was obvious: “Because the Elgant Theocracy cannot be trusted.”

Before making their arrival report, they had already heard our story, which had pushed their distrust of Elgant to its peak, and we had also told them we were prepared to build temporary housing for Estea as well. That likely played a role. Incidentally, the temporary housing was not free.

Even if they were not friendly nations, being deemed untrustworthy by two countries and having lodging refused would severely damage the reputation of a major power. That, however, was not our concern. The fact was that they were untrustworthy.

“This is delicious. This flavor… it resembles the seasoning used in the restaurants of the Advance Trading Company.”

The one saying this as he brought food to his mouth was the prince of the Kingdom of Estea.

The Estean prince, Ruan, said he wished to formally express his thanks, so we decided it would be a good opportunity for him to have lunch together with Sakuya.

Ruan expressed his gratitude for the rescue, Sakuya accepted it, and afterward it became a casual lunch and conversation.

It seemed they had done a poison check, but judging by Ruan’s demeanor, he did not appear to have doubted us from the start.

I was present as a guard, with Rico by my side. Sakura and the others were not here since their faces were already known.

Well, the upper echelons of the Kingdom of Estea already knew that Sakuya and I were acquainted, so even if it came out, it would not be a problem…

If anything, the bigger issue was the possibility of Gene’s identity being exposed.

Think about it. If I was not with Sakura and the others, and instead there was some unknown person named Gene with them, what would you think? I would suspect they were the same person.

Honestly, using the easily exposed alias “Gene” might have been my biggest mistake. But it is such a standard name to use in games… It cannot be helped!

“Oh, you have a refined palate. That is correct. We employ people affiliated with the Advance Trading Company as maids. Meals during travel are extremely important.”

“Yes, I agree. That said, hiring cooks from the Advance Trading Company… I never would have thought of it. We should have done the same.”

Ruan likely struggled with meals during travel as well, muttering in admiration.

“No, that would have been difficult. That company does not bow to authority at all.”

“I have heard those rumors. If someone tries to force them into submission with power, they abandon the land immediately, and by the next morning, the site where their branch stood is reduced to empty ground…”

Given the maid’s mobility, that would be easy for them. Especially since they act at night.

“Indeed. I was able to ask only because I happened to have a connection, but even so, it was quite difficult.”

“Considering that, it would have been impossible for the Estean royal family without such connections. We have also tried to offer conveniences, but the Advance Trading Company refuses those as well.”

“It seems they do not approve of being absorbed by authority. They likely have some other clear objective. One so unappealing that even royalty would not look twice at it.”

I felt Sakuya’s awareness shift slightly toward me.

“Hearing that is rather frightening. To think that forces even royalty cannot control exist throughout various countries and regions.”

“Indeed. It is best not to make enemies of such opponents.”

“Absolutely.”

Why was the Advance Trading Company coming up in a discussion between royalty?

“It seems that the Advance Trading Company has not opened a single branch in the Elgant Theocracy.”

“That is so. Until the Castal-Eldia War ended, they apparently did not open any branches in the Eldia direction as seen from Castal.”

“I have also heard that there are surprisingly few branches in Hero-supporting nations. Like my own country, perhaps they are not very fond of Heroes.”

Quite sharp.

As expected, Cattleya’s younger brother has a promising future.

“As a country that killed a Hero, we came here intending to fulfill our responsibility, but to be honest, I almost regret it. This country’s response has been far too atrocious.”

Ruan said this with a sigh.

“At the point they tried to take your lives, I think the notion of responsibility becomes irrelevant…”

“…When you put it that way, you are right. They already acted to take our lives.”

Their actions had already gone beyond harassment and into physical violence.

“…I know it is an audacious request after being saved from a monster horde, but would you be willing to conclude an agreement ahead of this conference?”

According to Ruan, since the conference was hosted by the Elgant Theocracy, Castal and Estea were entirely in enemy territory. There was a high possibility that unreasonable demands would be forced upon them by sheer numbers. To counter that, even slightly, he wanted to establish an agreement between Castal and Estea beforehand so they could support each other.

“That would be most welcome. I have little experience dealing with other nations, so just having allies in a similar position is reassuring.”

“I lack experience as well. Come to think of it, among the royalty gathered, we are probably the youngest group.”

Too bad! The youngest royal is King Zenon Grants of the Kingdom of Grants, age nine!

Well, that is probably just his physical age. I have no idea about his soul’s age.

Thus, Sakuya and Ruan, or rather, the Kingdom of Castal and the Kingdom of Estea, concluded a private agreement.

With nothing to do, I stood idly as Sakuya’s guard.

“…That is correct, right?”

“Yes, indeed. As you know, his name is Gene, my personal guard and the strongest knight in Castal. As he is a guard, please forgive his lack of formal greeting.”

Huh! They are talking about me.

I was not listening at all. Alta, what are they talking about?

A: They are discussing what would happen if the Elgant Theocracy resorted to military force. Estea has brought elite troops, but they likely do not match the strength of Castal’s knights. They were also confirming whether you are indeed Gene, the one who almost single-handedly brought down Eldia.

Ah, that helps.

“Yes, that is fine. Since he is deliberately hiding his identity, we have no intention of rudely exposing it.”

“…Just as a precaution. Fame only brings more trouble.”

“I understand. That said, that is impressive equipment. I am not deeply versed in arms and armor, but even to an amateur eye, it radiates an overwhelming presence.”

“Hmm, that is so. However, Gene’s strength is not strength that relies on weapons.”

Stop it, you are making me blush.

“I can sense that as well. Probably, Gene himself is more formidable than those incredible weapons, right? I may not have an eye for weapons, but I am confident in my ability to judge people.”

He added a punchline at the end: “Even through armor.”

While chatting, documents were compiled and future policy decided, bringing the meeting to a close.

As part of mutual support, several maid knights were assigned to Estea’s temporary housing. In terms of combat strength, I feel sorry for Estea, but ours are superior.

After a night passed, the long-awaited day of the summit conference arrived.

The reason it was long-awaited was because I wanted to go home as soon as possible.

Assassins had come again yesterday as well, after all. Naturally, they were all killed. There is no way to like a country where assassins come every day.

We dismantled the temporary housing that would no longer be used, boarded our carriage, and passed through the gates of Elgare.

Led by gate guards, we headed toward the grand cathedral. Even within the city, the cathedral at the center was far enough away that carriage travel was only natural.

Like other cities, the buildings were predominantly white… no, almost all buildings were white. As expected of a holy capital, the thoroughness surpassed other cities.

It was a beautiful, peaceful-looking cityscape, but it did not stir my heart at all. To me, the Elgant Theocracy was already not a tourist destination.

Looking at the map, it seemed most representatives had already gathered.

We were probably the last to arrive. I did not feel particularly bad about it.

As decided beforehand, Sera and I would attend the conference as Sakuya’s guards, with Rico attending as a maid.

The other members would wait in the cathedral’s waiting rooms. These were assigned by country and equipped with a television-like magical device that allowed viewing of the conference chamber. That device was absolutely related to Heroes.

Not all accompanying ministers would participate directly. As a representative, Finance Minister Rudolf would attend. The other ministers would remain in the waiting room.

Despite his title, Finance Minister Rudolf handled several other important governmental affairs. With Sakuya and Rudolf present, most matters concerning Castal could be decided.

In fact, Castal was in more trouble when those two were absent.

A: There is no problem because the maids are there.

…Normally, one would ask what maids have to do with it, but our case is different.

In any event, the group was inevitably split, so caution, no, vigilance was required.

Surely assassins would not come during a meeting inside the cathedral, right? …There is no guarantee.

After proceeding for a while, we finally arrived at the cathedral.

As decided in advance, bringing weapons into the cathedral was not prohibited.

As royal guards, carrying weapons was only natural.

That said, if one stopped playing knight (a blunt expression ignoring pretense), even being forbidden from arming oneself would pose no problem.

In that case, a wild-type knight would simply emerge, wearing cool armor and beating people with fists and kicks.

Someone whose greatest strength is unarmed combat is among the most formidable opponents, right?

As we moved through the cathedral and reached the point where we would part from the waiting-room group, we exchanged greetings via telepathy.

《I am heading in.》

《We will be off.》

《Lord Jin, please be careful. Sera-chan, please take care of Lord Jin.》

《Of course.》

《Master, do your best!》

Maria is as worried as ever. Given how many enemies we have, it is understandable.

《I would be happy if you did not forget about me as well. I am a queen, after all…》

《Sakuya-chan, please do your best…》

《Yeah, I will. Sakura-chan, thank you for your concern.》

Naturally, Sakuya has to work harder than I do at the summit.

《Things are not safe on our end either. It seems that priest is preparing assassins for the waiting rooms…》

《So it comes to that…》

As Mio said, the priest seemed to be planning to unleash assassins on the waiting rooms during the summit.

For now, I would send Tamo-san. With Split, his numbers had increased quite a bit, so I had brought a decent number.

Go on, off you go.

《Master, what did you do?》

《I instructed Tamo-san to wipe out the assassination organization that serves as the assassins source. Killing the priest here would be troublesome, so cutting off his limbs first is best, right?》

Even if the priest gives orders, an organization capable of sending dozens of assassins can be considered an enemy itself.

And if they are enemies, there is no reason for mercy. Unfortunately, I cannot go myself, so I have to ask Tamo-san…

《Assassin Tamo-san… just imagining it is terrifying.》

《For that reason, I think the frequency of dealing with assassins will decrease from here on. It might not drop to zero if there are other organizations, though.》

《Roger.》

After sending Tamo-san out to secure safety, we headed toward the conference room while the others went to the waiting rooms.

The conference room was on the fourth floor, accessible via an elevator-like magical device. I want one!

After proceeding again, the conference room came into view.

As expected of a room gathering royalty from various nations, it was exceptionally spacious and lavish even among the cathedral’s rooms.

“Please enter. Representatives from the other countries are already present.”

At the guide’s prompting, the soldiers guarding the doors opened them.

As stated, many participants were already gathered inside.

A massive round table occupied the center, with leaders seated by country. Behind them stood guards, soldiers, and knights.

Also arranged around the table were long-distance communication magical devices called “Far-Seer Paired Mirrors.”

Tall and wide full-length mirrors, taller than a person, lined the table like participants, creating a subtly comical scene.

“Thank you for waiting. Please, take your seats.”

The one saying this was the female pope, the supreme authority of the Elgant Theocracy and the host of this conference.

At first glance, she appeared to be a gentle woman in her late twenties, but the map display was red (enemy), so I could not let my guard down at all.

From Castal, Sakuya and Finance Minister Rudolf took their seats. From Estea, Ruan and another senior figure did the same.

We guards stood directly behind Sakuya and the others, with the maids behind us.

If only our seats were a bit farther back, we could have seen the outside scenery through the windows…

Once Sakuya and the others were seated, the female pope began speaking again.

“Now that it appears everyone is present, let us begin the summit conference. First, allow me to express my heartfelt thanks to you all for gathering here today. I am the host of this conference and the Pope of the Elgant Theocracy. My name is Linforce Mei Elgant.”

Huh? The map display and name do not match.

A: It appears to be a public alias.

Then it cannot be helped. I am not in a position to complain.

“This summit conference was prompted by the Castal-Eldia War, and I would like to discuss three major agenda items. First, an explanation of the Castal-Eldia War. Second, the future treatment of the Heroes. Third, future countermeasures against the Demon Race.”

The issues we need to care about are the first and third.

I do not care about the Heroes, but being held responsible for the war or being forced to fight the Demon Race would be unacceptable.

“Let us proceed with the first agenda item. The explanation of the Castal-Eldia War. This was an extremely sudden event for all countries, and it ended in an instant, so very little information has reached us. We would like to hear directly from the Castal side about the course of events.”

At Linforce’s prompting, Finance Minister Rudolf stood.

“I am Rudolf, Finance Minister of the Kingdom of Castal. I will explain the course of events regarding the Castal-Eldia War.”

Rudolf explained how relations had gradually deteriorated after Castal refused to become a Hero-supporting nation. How Castal sheltered Eldia after the Hero killing incident in Estea, and how Eldia had targeted them since. He described how the city of Riralca was occupied without a declaration of war, marking the beginning of the war.

“Thank you. Are there any questions so far?”

When Linforce invited questions, a young girl raised her hand.

“I am Ekaterina, Queen of the Kingdom of Sanokia. May I ask one question?”

The Queen of Sanokia…

She is a figure of interest in many ways, but at least she is not an enemy, so I can leave that aside for now.

“Yes, please.”

“Why did Castal not become a Hero-supporting nation in the first place? Since Castal borders Eldia, would it not suffer great damage if the Demon Race invaded?”

“There are two main reasons. The first is…”

Many countries likely did not know of Eldia’s actions or Castal’s internal situation.

Anticipating such questions, Finance Minister Rudolf answered smoothly.

He spoke of Eldia’s history of invading and destroying neighboring countries without declarations of war and evading responsibility through Hero summoning, as well as Castal’s S-rank adventurer knights, their numbers and quality, as a basis for choosing a military that does not rely on Heroes.

If one must choose between aiding and relying on an untrustworthy country or protecting oneself, the latter is the natural choice, he concluded.

“Is there proof that Eldia did such things?”

“There is. After the war, numerous documents regarding invasion wars were found within Eldia Castle.”

Rudolf answered immediately.

How did they even find such things?

A: They seemed like important evidence, so I had the subordinate maids find them.

Alta guided it.

With that, nothing important could be hidden.

“I understand. That is all.”

As there were no further questions, Rudolf continued.

When the war began, it was finally my turn to appear.

He explained how Queen’s Knight Gene liberated Riralca with adventurers, annihilated the invading army, then attacked Eldia with a rapid assault force of inferior wind dragons, and finally secured the capital, which had already suffered catastrophic damage from the Demon Race.

That was basically the end of it.

Gene-san sure was active.

Hearing it objectively from someone outside our group, it sounds monstrous.

“Thank you. Are there any further questions?”

This time, more people, four or five, raised their hands.

Linforce selected one, who introduced themselves and asked a question.

I had never heard of their country, but their marker was red (enemy), meaning they were aligned with the Elgant Theocracy.

“Why did Castal kill the Hero during the war? Heroes are indispensable in the fight against the Demon Race. Was killing one by Castal’s own decision not an act of hostility toward humanity?”

They came at us faster than expected.

And Elgant is not condemning us directly?

…No, perhaps they are having other countries condemn us to collectively pressure Castal.

“Are you saying that Castal should have remained passive and perished in response to Eldia’s invasion?”

“No, that is not what I am saying. I simply thought there might have been another way. If one truly cares for humanity, that is. That is all.”

They cut it off forcefully without pressing further.

Perhaps they want to color the atmosphere as Castal being in the wrong?

Then the next question…

“Please tell us who this knight called Gene is. Considering he had the power to face a Hero yet remained unknown until now, does he not have some questionable past?”

Now it was a question about me.

In a way, this was expected.

“There is little I can say about him. He is Queen Sakuya’s royal guard and likely her most trusted knight. For us, that is sufficient.”

“That explains nothing! Then Queen Sakuya, please explain it yourself!”

The woman raised her voice at Rudolf’s response.

Hearing this, Sakuya stood.

“I am Sakuya, Queen of the Kingdom of Castal. I wish to ask one thing. Why must we speak of our nation’s military strength?”

“This is a forum for Castal to explain itself regarding the war…”

“It is not an explanation. It is a description. We have nothing to feel guilty about in that war. We will only provide an explanation of the war. We have no intention of discussing the forces used or the disadvantages suffered by others as a result.”

Sakuya interrupted and declared.

It is not bad for her to assert our stance early, since there will be more remarks later.

However, overly strong statements can easily provoke resentment from other nations. …Is that even a concern now?

“What a selfish thing to say! To begin with, Castal…”

As expected, the woman raised her voice again.

Sakuya ignored her and turned to Linforce.

“Have we been called to a conference of a completely different nature than what we were told? This is a place to explain the war, correct? Is it not? Linforce-dono?”

“Queen Sakuya is correct. The first agenda item is purely for information sharing to proceed with the second and third. Castal also has the option of not answering questions that would be disadvantageous.”

Linforce said this, looking slightly disappointed.

Perhaps she did not expect Castal to reject things so early.

She likely intended to overwhelm us with numbers. But having declared I would protect her, Sakuya is now brimming with confidence.

“Are there any other questions?”

Perhaps due to the shift in tone, those who had raised their hands earlier no longer did.

They may have judged that pushing Castal further here would only worsen their own position.

In that moment, a young boy raised his hand.

As you know, it was King Zenon Grants of the Kingdom of Grants.

At the Grants table, only Zenon and two attendants were present. It did not seem that others were left in waiting rooms.

“May I ask one thing?”

“Yes, please.”

“I am Zenon, King of the Kingdom of Grants. One thing concerns me. Why did the Demon Race attack the Eldian capital? The Heroes and soldiers were away at war, so there should have been no forces in the capital. Why did they attack precisely when it was undefended?”

Because Orihara brought in the Demon Race to create a one-on-one situation with me.

I cannot say it… but I want to…

“It must be because Castal colluded with the Demon Race! That is why Eldia was destroyed!”

The woman who questioned Gene raised her voice again.

“…Be silent. Think for a moment and you will see. If Castal had colluded with the Demon Race, it would be unnatural for Castal to annihilate them. The Demon Race would not cooperate under the assumption that their allies would die.”

It was Zenon who cut down her nonsense with a reasonable argument.

“I can imagine several possibilities, but what does Castal think?”

Oh, Zenon’s first-person pronoun is “yo”…

“Two main possibilities. Either the Demon Race had infiltrated Eldia, or Eldia had an internal collaborator. At present, we have found no evidence to conclusively determine which.”

Finance Minister Rudolf answered Zenon’s question.

Sakuya had already taken her seat again.

“Hmm. If there was a collaborator, then the Heroes in this country are suspicious.”

“Are you suggesting that the Heroes in our country are suspects?”

Linforce reacted to Zenon’s words.

Her expression did not change, but the atmosphere around her sharpened.

Even she could not tolerate statements that disparaged the Heroes in her country.

“What are you getting angry about? I am merely stating a possibility derived from the facts. Someone who could know when the war would start and escape to safety. I think the probability is not low.”

“There is no way any Hero would consort with the Demon Race. Say any more, and we will consider it a provocation against our country. Are you prepared for that?”

There are Heroes who consort with the Demon Race, you know?

“Oh? How interesting. If the Elgant Theocracy were to fall, which country would host the Heroes next, I wonder? Ah, that is assuming the Heroes survive…”

“What!?”

It was the surrounding countries that were shocked by Zenon’s provocative words.

His phrasing was tantamount to declaring that if Elgant and Grants went to war, Elgant would be the one destroyed.

“You say such things boldly against our country and the Heroes.”

“Do not underestimate us as a small country. We sharpen our claws as well.”

Linforce’s eyes sharpened, but Zenon was unfazed.

“Very well. I would like to have a thorough discussion with the Kingdom of Grants later. For now, as this is a conference, let us end this topic.”

“Fine.”

Neither side intended to escalate further here, and both withdrew.

“Investigating collaborators will likely yield little. However, please keep in mind the possibility that such individuals may exist.”

Linforce summarized the discussion.

If an investigation were pursued, Elgant would need to probe the Heroes.

To avoid that, she seems to be steering toward not pursuing the investigation.

Well, since I know the truth, I do not care.

Linforce asked if there were further questions, but none arose, so the first agenda item concluded.

As it was midday, we returned to the waiting rooms for lunch and time to organize information. Given the complexity, a generous three-hour break was provided.

Also, the second and third agenda items were expected to be far longer than the first, so there was no need to rush.

The first agenda was merely a presentation of premises.

The Castal leaders returned to the waiting room, enjoyed Mio’s cooking, and then began discussions.

I did not participate, of course. I have no intention of meddling in politics.

We moved away from where the leaders were talking and chatted among ourselves.

“No assassins have come since we arrived. The destruction of the assassination group must have had a big impact.”

“Tamo-san really is scary.”

Mio nodded along with Maria’s explanation.

“But it seems they are gathering people through other connections, so we cannot let our guard down.”

“I wish they would just give up…”

《So persistent!》

The priest had not given up either.

Like Dora said, truly persistent.

“Well, depending on how you look at it, it is not a bad thing.”

“Why?”

I answered Mio’s question with a smile.

“Because we can obtain Assassin Arts skills that ordinary monsters rarely have, and it is a great opportunity to increase other human-exclusive skills.”

“You finally stopped treating humans as humans and started treating them as skill points… Master, that is bad.”

Ignoring Mio’s shudder, I pondered the skill compositions of the next assassins.

It would be nice if they had rare skills.

About an hour into the lunch break, I detected someone approaching.

Not an enemy, but not someone we could ignore.

-Knock knock-

There was a knock, and a maid knight responded.

“This is the waiting room for the Kingdom of Castal, correct? I am Ekaterina of the Kingdom of Sanokia. I have come to speak with Gene-sama, no, with Shindo Jin-sama.”

---

**AN:** Ekaterina is not strictly a new character.

Who in the Kingdom of Sanokia knows the name Shindo Jin…?

+++

## **135: The Errand Queen and the Second Agenda Item**

**AN:** In this chapter, Jin-kun fades into the background quite a lot.

Of course, his influence alone is pointlessly strong, but still…

---

The ones who came barging into the Castal Kingdom’s antechamber and dropped a bombshell were Ekaterina, the queen of the Kingdom of Sanokia, along with four guards.

All of them were beautiful young women, but they seemed to possess a reasonable degree of combat ability as well.

Judging by their skill compositions, with Ekaterina as the healer, they would be a knight, a hunter, a sorcerer, and a thief. That is an absurdly well-balanced party.

Ekaterina looked slightly younger than us and was wearing something like a white ceremonial robe.

Her shoulder-length blonde hair looked well cared for, gleaming dazzlingly, making her resemble an angel (I have no good memories of angels).

“Excuse me, but what business do you have with Gene-sama?”

The maid knight asked Ekaterina in as calm a manner as she could.

Due to Ekaterina’s bombshell statement, the key figures of Castal had all been left speechless.

“Yes. From the one I love most dearly, to Shindo Jin-sama… no, it would be better to call you Gene-sama, wouldn’t it? I have been entrusted with a message for Gene-sama.”

“The queen herself is delivering a message…?”

It was only natural for the maid knight to find that strange.

It made it sound as if the queen herself was being used as an errand runner.

“Yes. That is the primary reason we are participating in this conference.”

There was not the slightest hesitation in Ekaterina’s eyes.

Whatever this objective was, it must take precedence over heroes, demons, and the like.

“Ekaterina-sama, should you not first show your sincerity?”

“That is true. Everyone, please.”

“Yes.” x4

Nodding at the words of one of her guards, a female knight, Ekaterina urged the others to do something.

Then, the guards removed the weapons and armor they were carrying and lined them up on the floor.

“May we enter Castal’s antechamber? As you can see, we will disarm completely. If that is still insufficient, we will even remove all our clothing.”

A sudden declaration of stripping!

And the guards were nodding along with Ekaterina’s words.

Was there really a message so important that it required going that far?

The maid knight looked at us with a troubled expression.

The key figures of Castal seemed busy tidying up their documents.

According to the map, it didn’t look like they were carrying any hidden weapons, but…

Well, since they are offering, we might as well strip them. That will show how resolved they are.

《Have them remove everything except their underwear before letting them in.》

I conveyed that to the maid knight via telepathy.

“Understood. Then please remove everything except your underwear before entering.”

“Very well. Excuse us.”

When the maid knight said that, Ekaterina and the others actually began undressing right there on the spot.

Ekaterina’s was pure white.

It had some decoration, but it did not give an overly extravagant impression.

Her figure was not particularly voluptuous, but it matched her neat and modest body, giving a refined impression.

The female knight guarding Ekaterina was wearing black.

Putting aside the color, it was clearly something designed with practicality in mind, without unnecessary ornamentation, and it wrapped around a fairly ample amount.

As expected of a knight, prioritizing practicality over decoration was something I could appreciate.

The girl in the dress was wearing crimson.

Her dress itself had been a flashy red, and the contents were equally flashy crimson. Both her appearance and what was underneath were more flamboyant than Ekaterina’s.

Incidentally, she boasted the largest size among the girls, looking as though it might spill out.

The girl who had been carrying a bow was wearing a sarashi and a fundoshi.

As if artificial items did not suit her wild, overflowing physique, she was clad only in unprocessed cloth.

The way the things compressed by the sarashi were making such a bold assertion was also a high point. She was probably second-largest among the girls.

The small girl was wearing strings.

Not cloth. Strings. They were gray.

Her immature body could be concealed entirely by just that.

…Why am I describing this in such detail?

Incidentally, Ekaterina and the female knight looked embarrassed, but the other three were completely unfazed.

“Is this sufficient?”

“Yes. Then please, this way.”

The maid knight guided the now half-naked Ekaterina and her group over to us.

I saw Maria quietly shift to a position where it would be easier to protect me.

When they reached us, Ekaterina and the others knelt on the spot in their underwear and bowed.

It was clearly a gesture of respect toward someone of much higher standing.

“My apologies for not being able to properly greet you at the conference venue. Allow me to introduce myself anew. I am Ekaterina, queen of the Kingdom of Sanokia.”

“Queen’s Knight of the Castal Kingdom, Gene.”

It probably didn’t look like a proper greeting toward royalty, but Queen’s Knight Gene has a taciturn setting, after all (news to me).

“Without further delay, I will deliver the message. ‘You may use them freely.’”

“WHY?”

My true self slipped out.

“Shindo… Gene-sama would understand from just that alone, she said, but if that is insufficient, I can explain…”

“I can more or less guess, but…”

The reason I could guess what she meant was because Ekaterina’s title spoke volumes.

Name: Ekaterina

LV 23

Gender: Female

Age: 15

Race: Human

Skills: \<Staff Technique LV1> \<Light Magic LV2> \<Recovery Magic LV4>

Titles: Queen of the Kingdom of Sanokia, Messenger of Saki

Yes, this is Ekaterina’s status.

Please look at the title column. This is the problematic one.

“Messenger of Saki”

There is no doubt that “Saki” refers to my childhood friend (female), Mizuhara Saki.

Saki was also summoned to this world as a hero, and in Eldia, just like the other heroes, she had glared at me with eyes full of hostility.

She was my childhood friend, so I had been somewhat concerned, but Saki is the type who can survive anywhere, so I had not worried about her at all.

Considering the personality of the Saki I know, she is probably agonizing over the fact that she directed hostility at me. She probably cannot forgive herself.

It might not be definitive proof, but the fact that I still have not reunited with Saki might be because she is avoiding me.

Oh right, I should also explain the “Messenger” title. The other four also have this title, and when I first saw it, I asked Alta about it…

A: Like the “Slave” title, it is a title granted by a special skill. It does not have particularly significant effects, and it can overlap with the “Slave” title.

That is what she said.

Unlike \<Slave Art>, it apparently does not generate anything like command authority, so it is hard to tell why it exists at all. If I had to guess, it is proof of being a messenger.

“You are Saki’s messengers, correct?”

“Yes. We have come to Gene-sama as messengers of Sister Saki. Sister Saki said that she…”

Ekaterina trailed off.

“She said she has no face to show me, didn’t she?”

“Yes. Exactly. You understand so well…”

I am not a childhood friend for nothing.

“So, what exactly does ‘you may use them freely’ mean?”

“Please use us freely in every respect. We are resolved to accept all of Gene-sama’s demands. You may do as you wish with the Kingdom of Sanokia, and with our bodies as well.”

A sudden slave declaration! And an unconditional surrender declaration!

Well, I feel like I am somewhat used to slave declarations by now. Slaves seem to increase before I even realize it…

And with the unconditional surrender declaration, I became convinced.

The political upheaval, the coup that supposedly occurred in the Kingdom of Sanokia some time ago, must have involved Saki.

As a result, this girl named Ekaterina likely ascended the throne.

“Use them freely” is probably Saki’s way of atonement. Handing over an entire country as atonement is quite a scale, though…

But then again, if it is Saki, it would not be strange for her to act on that scale.

“Are you truly fine with that?”

“It is not that we have no reservations at all. However, we do not want to do anything that would cause Sister Saki to dislike us. Compared to being hated by Sister Saki, death would be far preferable.”

Not only Ekaterina, but the guards also nodded.

For a brief moment, I felt something similar to the look Maria gives me…

Still, there were parts that now made sense.

That must be why their map markers were blue (allies) from the very beginning.

It was not out of reluctance. Because it was Saki’s instruction, they had intended from the start to be fully on my side.

But really, if complete strangers start off with blue (ally) markers, that is terrifying.

It is like they have the level of trust you would reserve for a best friend or a lover from the outset…

Even if you know they are not enemies, you would hesitate to approach them yourself.

“If you cannot trust us, you may make us your slaves. When we return to the antechamber, we have both a slave art user and the necessary number of ‘Collars of Subjugation’ prepared.”

The way they were cutting themselves down was extreme.

I see… The “Messenger” title and the “Slave” title can overlap…

And they are conveniently half-naked right now, making it easy to use \<Slave Art> on them.

So this is “Saki’s sincerity”…

What should I do. I would not really be troubled if I refused to accept it.

But if I choose not to accept Saki’s sincerity here, Saki will probably misunderstand and think that I am still angry.

If that happens, who knows what she will do next. As part of her atonement, she is offering up an entire country and girls including royalty.

If she were to seriously seek my forgiveness, just how far would she go…?

In that case, it would be best to signal that I am not angry.

However, as long as they have the “Messenger of Saki” title, I do not intend to explain my abilities, including my special powers.

“Fine. I will make you my slaves. In that case, even if there were instructions from Saki, there is no guarantee that I would release you from the slave contract. Are you prepared for that?”

“That is, of course, understood. Sister Saki said she would keep her distance from Gene-sama for a while. During that time, and after, we have been instructed to be of service to Gene-sama.”

They really think of nothing but Saki.

“Then how shall we proceed with the slave contract?”

“I can use \<Slave Art>. You only need to turn your backs.”

“Understood.”

With that, Ekaterina and the others lined up side by side and turned their backs to me.

I took out a small vial of blood and applied \<Slave Art> to each of them in turn.

Since they were already in their underwear, \<Slave Art> was very easy to apply.

“Now then, Gene-sama, please issue any command you wish.”

This was my first order to Ekaterina, now officially my slave.

“First, cooperate with Castal at this summit. You will need to coordinate with the other key figures of Sanokia, but I do not want to tilt your country too far…”

“There is no problem. Sanokia was corrupt for a long time, and now that the rot has been purged, there is a lack of capable personnel in the upper ranks. Likewise, there is no one capable of raising grounded objections to our decisions.”

It is not something to celebrate as a nation, but right now it is convenient for Castal.

“To begin with, we are not aligned with the Elgant Theocracy. We assisted the heroes’ defection to the Elgant Theocracy only because it was Saki’s instruction. Otherwise, we have no particular interest.”

As I said earlier, they really think only of Saki.

“Master, may I ask something?”

“What’s wrong?”

Mio tugged lightly at my clothes (the part sticking out from my armor).

“Shouldn’t you ask about hiding your identity, and about how they knew who you really are?”

“Ah, right. That is necessary too. My name is Gene. You are forbidden from calling me Shindo Jin. At least while I am in this form. And how did you know who Gene really is?”

As for the latter question, I could already guess the answer.

“Understood regarding your name. As for Gene-sama’s identity, we heard it from Sister Saki. She said that based on that name and your actions, there could be no mistake.”

Well, if it is someone you’ve known for that long, it is only natural to be found out.

It cannot be helped. This really cannot be helped.

“So be it… Is there anything else you were told to convey?”

“Yes. We have also been entrusted with an apology gift from Sister Saki. If Gene-sama were to accept us, even provisionally, we were instructed to give it to you.”

Saying that, Ekaterina asked the maid knight to bring over an item box from among the things they had disarmed earlier.

I took the item box and checked its contents.

…This is bad.

It is filled with an absurd amount of rare materials and magical tools.

It is a fortune. And since they are rare materials from places I have never been to, they are all things I have never obtained before.

As expected of my childhood friend. …But Orihara, I will not forgive.

“I will accept it gratefully.”

“Is that so? Sister Saki will be pleased to hear that.”

Showing that I am not angry is important.

That said, I cannot deny that I simply want these things as well.

Now then, are there any other instructions I should give Ekaterina and the others…?

“…Since Sanokia is siding with Castal anyway, it would be quicker to have you participate in the conference here.”

“Understood. We will fully align ourselves with Castal’s interests.”

Bringing along Ekaterina, who had just declared that she would completely ignore Sanokia’s national interests, we headed toward the key figures…

Before that, I had them get dressed again. Since they are slaves now, there is no need to keep them stripped.

We then headed back to Sakuya and Finance Minister Rudolf.

“We have secured the cooperation of the Kingdom of Sanokia. Please convey Castal’s policies and requests.”

“I was listening from the side, but… this is truly an unbelievable development…”

Finance Minister Rudolf said, pressing his temple.

“Rudolf. There is no point in thinking too deeply about it. Accept it as one of those things. At the very least, it is not a loss for Castal.”

“Indeed… For now, that is the only way to look at it.”

Finance Minister Rudolf gave up on thinking too deeply.

Ekaterina took a seat on a chair brought by the maids and joined Castal’s discussion.

Partway through, Prince Luan of Estair also came by, and he was surprised to see Sanokian royalty present, but in the end, the three countries formed a cooperative framework.

When the scheduled time arrived, we headed to the conference room to discuss the second agenda item.

The second agenda item was “The future of the heroes”, so it was only natural that three heroes were already present in the conference room.

One of them was the person requiring special caution, Kino Aichi.

They had probably gathered the most influential heroes. Their Blessings were all quite powerful.

In addition, many of them also had decent skill compositions aside from their Blessings.

Due to the distance between antechambers, it seems some countries are arriving later than us this time.

We entered the conference room, which still had many empty seats.

The heroes were seated at tables set up slightly away from the round table.

So that is Kino Aichi…

She has a perfectly arranged appearance, like a Japanese doll.

Hmm, I feel like I have met her somewhere before. …Where was it? Huh? The girl next to Kino (a beautiful girl) also looks familiar… Judging by her age, she seems like a classmate. Did I meet her at school?

If we talk for a while, I might remember, but right now it is difficult.

From their perspective, Gene is the enemy who killed people from their homeland, so it would be hard to build a friendly relationship.

Indeed, most of the heroes have red markers on the map.

The exception was Kino, who had some yellow mixed in… but it seems the girl next to Kino also had some yellow mixed in. Her name was… Shippouin, was it? I think that was the name of a famous wealthy family in our original world.

While I was thinking about that, the empty seats gradually filled, and the conference was about to begin.

“Now that everyone appears to be present, we would like to proceed with the discussion of the second agenda item.”

Seeing that everyone was seated, Linforce declared the resumption of the conference.

“The second agenda item concerns the future of the heroes. In the Castal-Eldia War, those heroes who abhorred war transferred their affiliation to the Elgant Theocracy. When the Kingdom of Eldia fell, almost all heroes affiliated with Eldia perished, so nearly all heroes are now affiliated with the Elgant Theocracy.”

There are probably exceptions, though.

For example, Orihara and those associated with him, and Saki, who is avoiding me. My childhood friends have a lot of exceptions…

“Since Eldia has fallen, the previous discussions regarding hero support have fallen apart, so we would like to revisit that topic. This time, in order to secure your willing cooperation, we have invited several heroes, so I would like to introduce them first.”

With that, Linforce began introducing the heroes participating in the conference.

There were twelve heroes in total. Frankly, they should be the ones using the round table.

Since it would not be feasible to have each of them comment, when their names were called, they simply stood up and gave a small bow.

After that, Linforce explained the currently planned policies regarding heroes, as well as the support required, including the necessary funding, clearly laying out the rationale.

From the content of that support, it was clear that the focus was on strengthening the heroes overall combat power.

It seems they view the heroes crushing defeat in the Castal-Eldia War as being due to Eldia’s insufficient support for its heroes.

The basic stance of the Elgant Theocracy appears to be that “properly trained heroes cannot lose”.

Apparently, this is based on the fact that throughout long history, the Demon King has always been defeated by heroes.

“…For these reasons, we would like each country to become a hero-supporting nation and cooperate in the subjugation of the demons. Now then, does anyone have any questions?”

At Linforce’s prompting, the woman who had pressed Sakuya during the first agenda item raised her hand again.

“I understand that cooperation is necessary to strengthen the heroes. However, what happened to the funds we previously paid to the Kingdom of Eldia for hero support? At that time, we paid no small price and were promised protection from the heroes, were we not?”

The money paid to the Kingdom of Eldia?

Apparently, it was spent on military equipment for attacking Castal and on compensation for the damage caused by the heroes.

“I am terribly sorry, but the Elgant Theocracy cannot guarantee contracts made with the Kingdom of Eldia. This is the first time that a country which summoned heroes has fallen due to conflict among humans before the Demon King was defeated, so there is no precedent to follow.”

“Then what of Castal, which destroyed the Kingdom of Eldia? The fall of Eldia has had no small impact on the surrounding nations.”

Hearing Linforce’s response, the woman turned her spear toward Castal.

Interpreted loosely, it was something like, “How dare you destroy the country we paid to support.”

“The fall of the Kingdom of Eldia was caused by a war that Eldia itself initiated. Nothing more, nothing less. There is no reason for our country, which was unjustly attacked, to clean up after the defeated Eldia.”

Finance Minister Rudolf cut it off bluntly.

Eldia misused the support funds from other nations.

When its treasury was about to run dry, Eldia initiated a war, pouring in its remaining funds in hopes of compensation.

But it was repelled, and Eldia’s treasury was emptied in the truest sense.

Should Castal, the victorious nation, bear the burden of contracts that such a trash country made with its neighbors? Give me a break.

“But I do not think the surrounding nations will accept that. Killing heroes essential to the fight against demons affects the national defense of neighboring states as well, does it not?”

At the woman’s words, the key figures of the surrounding nations (pro-Elgant Theocracy) nodded.

These are anti-Castal countries, so they are outside the scope of those Castal needs to consider.

“Please do not make me repeat myself. Castal has no intention of bearing any responsibility that the Kingdom of Eldia once held. No matter what or how much the surrounding nations say, that will not change.”

“But…”

“Then allow me to ask you in return.”

Sakuya stood up, cutting off the woman who was about to continue.

Sakuya’s words have the power to change the atmosphere of a room. Her voice carries well, too.

“Eldia’s treasury was nearly empty at the end of the war. In other words, the funds for hero support were used in the Castal-Eldia War.”

“So what?”

The woman asked suspiciously, not understanding Sakuya’s point.

“How do you view the fact that our people were harmed using money you paid? One could say that, indirectly, you attacked our country. Why should we guarantee the obligations of those who attacked us?”

“How cruel! Our country had no intention of attacking Castal! That was something Eldia did on its own!”

“Allowing them to do so is also a problem. You paid the money and paid no attention to how it was used. Do you not bear responsibility for that? Had you paid closer attention to Eldia’s actions, the Castal-Eldia War might have been prevented. Why are you acting as if you are the victim?”

“Gh…”

The woman shrank back under Sakuya’s merciless logic.

With a snort, Sakuya sat back down.

“My guess is that the Elgant Theocracy took Eldia’s mistakes to heart and drew up extremely detailed budget plans in advance. The budget explanation was unusually specific, after all.”

“Yes, that is correct. Using hero support funds for war was an unprecedented situation. To prevent such a thing from happening again, budget management has been strictly defined.”

Linforce affirmed Finance Minister Rudolf’s question.

“In other words, you are saying that there were many points to reflect upon in Eldia’s methods and in the approaches of the surrounding nations at the time. Yet you make no mention of that responsibility and instead demand that our country, the victim, bear Eldia’s burden. …Should you not be a little ashamed?”

Finance Minister Rudolf is surprisingly sharp-tongued.

At the words of Sakuya and Finance Minister Rudolf, the representatives of the surrounding nations grew tense.

It feels like the word “amicable” has disappeared from Sakuya’s side as well.

It is probably nearing the limit of their patience.

“Are the representatives of Castal not going too far? Do you wish to make enemies of the surrounding nations?”

Linforce asked, without changing his expression, though the atmosphere grew tense.

“Kuahahaha!”

However, a loud laugh shattered the tense atmosphere.

“Kukuku, and then the surrounding nations that oppose Castal start a war, only to be repelled like Eldia? If Elgant attacks, perhaps this time the heroes will be wiped out entirely. How delightful, how delightful!”

Once again, the one who shattered the atmosphere was Zenon Grants.

“Zenon-sama. Do you understand what you are saying?”

Ignoring Linforce’s rebuke, he continued.

“If this is Castal’s strategy, it is a terrifying one! Without lifting a finger themselves, they provoke powerful nations, annihilate and absorb them once they strike first. They remain the victims who were attacked. Such a perfect justification is rare indeed! What a scheme. It deserves praise. And the truly terrifying part of Castal is that they possess enough military strength to annihilate even heroes!”

Zenon took exaggerated reactions, exposing Castal’s supposed scheme.

No, that is not our intention at all…

“Could it be that Castal attended this conference for that very purpose…”

Linforce, who had been expressionless until now, please do not suddenly look so shocked.

“This is a cruel conspiracy theory. Our country has no desire for war with other nations. With a common enemy in the demons, do you not think it foolish for humans to fight among themselves?”

“On the contrary, in times of confusion with a powerful enemy like the demons, expanding one’s territory by taking advantage of the situation is not a bad move, you know? I would like to learn from that myself.”

Finance Minister Rudolf’s words were twisted by Zenon into the exact opposite meaning.

Zenon, how badly do you want Castal to be the mastermind?

Look. The surrounding nations, who had been directing clear hostility at Castal, are now showing fear and dread, deliberately averting their eyes.

“No matter what we say, if it is taken in the worst possible way, discussion is impossible. Linforce-dono, we are straying far from the point. Do you intend to continue this discussion? As I said earlier, our country has no intention of bearing Eldia’s responsibility. Or do you desire a fruitless exchange of accusations?”

“No. That would deviate greatly from the original purpose of this conference. Therefore, we will end this topic here.”

Linforce cut off the derailed discussion.

After that, relatively normal questions continued. None concerned Castal.

Occasionally, questions were directed at the heroes as well, but only the teacher and Shippouin answered.

While the teacher was accustomed to speaking in public, Shippouin was supposed to be an ordinary high school girl, yet she carried herself with considerable presence.

Aside from Kino and Shippouin occasionally glancing my way, nothing particularly unusual happened…

A: Master. I have something to report.

When Alta says that, something unusual must have occurred.

Her timing is always impeccable…

I listened to Altas report and checked the map.

…Oh? This might get interesting.

“I have one question as well.”

When Zenon raised his hand to ask a question, a collective intake of breath echoed through the conference room.

Zenon’s remarks are usually outrageous, after all.

“Can the heroes of this generation truly defeat the Demon King? To my knowledge, there has never been a case where a country possessing heroes initiated a war against another human nation, much less suffered defeat. Could it be that the heroes of this generation are weaker than their predecessors?”

–Rustle!–

Zenon Grants’ statement called into question the very foundation of this conference.

The room erupted into murmurs. And of course, there were those who could not tolerate this statement.

“Is that all you wished to say…?”

As you know, that was Linforce.

Maintaining her basic expressionless face, she was emitting an overwhelming killing intent.

Bathed in the killing intent of Linforce, a powerful individual, some of those seated nearby foamed at the mouth and fainted.

Ah, this is getting interesting too!

---

**AN:** The main stars of the conference arc are Sakuya and Zenon.
