## **136: Suspension of the Conference and the Sword Emperor Style**

**AN:** It looks like I will not be able to do anything interesting on April 1 this year.

I messed up the scheduling if I wanted to make it a joke tied into the main story…

For now, I will put out a short piece.

---

“Very well. That is all I wished to ask. If someone could answer, I would appreciate it.”

Zenon wrapped up his question, ignoring the killing intent in the room.

“You are saying… that you cannot trust the Heroes chosen by the Goddess?”

“Naturally. A Hero who loses to humans has no reason to be able to defeat demonkind, who surpass humans.”

The killing intent radiating from Linforce continued to intensify.

In proportion to that, the number of people fainting increased as well. Ah, Prince Luan of Estea fainted too.

“You say they lost to humans, but most of the Heroes remaining in the Kingdom of Eldia possessed Blessings unsuited for combat, and the ones who killed those Heroes were the demon army.”

“That does not matter. The problem is the Hero unit that invaded Castal. I hear there were over one hundred of them?”

“It is true that over a hundred Heroes were defeated in Castal. However, I believe it was the result of several factors overlapping.”

Were there really that many factors?

I only remember killing them quickly…

“First, the Heroes lacked experience in marching. While they had party-level combat experience, they had no army-level combat experience, and thus could not make full use of their individual combat abilities.”

“Hmm, indeed. The Kingdom of Eldia likely did not provide support down to that level.”

Zenon nodded at Linforce’s explanation.

That’s right. The Heroes made the worst possible move by feeding their forces in piecemeal against a superior opponent.

“In addition, the battlefield was Castal. It is recorded that the invasion force was annihilated by the unit led by Lord Gene, the Queen’s Knight of Castal, but Castal did not provide details regarding their concrete military strength. …Castal is home to many famous adventurers. I surmise that they borrowed the Adventurers strength, made use of the terrain, and defeated the Heroes at the cost of great sacrifices.”

Help from adventurers? Zero people.

Great sacrifices? Zero people.

“I see. If Castal intentionally provoked Eldia, then it would be only natural for them to have prepared countermeasures in case they were attacked.”

Hey, you bastard Zenon!

Don’t casually mix that Castal conspiracy theory back into the conversation when it was supposed to be over!

“No way…”

Linforce arrived at that possibility as well, showed a startled expression, and then immediately turned her killing intent toward me. Yes, this is comfortable killing intent.

Ah, Minister of Finance Rudolf is desperately gritting his teeth and enduring it.

…This is strange. The flow of this meeting is quite different from what I expected.

The culprit is Zenon-kun. No doubt about it.

“I understand. In other words, Lady Linforce, you wish to say that this incident was not something that devalues the Heroes’ abilities, but was merely an exceptional case?”

“Exactly. It is unfortunate that Heroes lost their lives, but that was due solely to flaws in Eldia’s approach. I do not believe it should be taken as something that diminishes the authority of the Heroes.”

They say the winners write history and the losers are branded criminals.

If we just say Eldia was at fault since they ultimately lost, most problems go away.

“Furthermore, I would like to deny the claim that they were weaker than past Heroes.”

“Oh? Do you have any basis for that?”

“Our country possesses records regarding the Blessings of past Heroes. According to those, among the current generation of Heroes’ Blessings, there are ones identical to those held by past Heroes. Research indicates that the scale of the abilities is also comparable. Since these abilities once defeated a Demon King, they should not be insufficient. The rest depends on how the nation supports them.”

Oh? They researched that too?

A: The documents have already been copied. Other information believed to be state secrets has also been copied.

…The secrets of any land I step into basically get neutralized, don’t they?

“Hmm. If you have such evidence, you should have said so sooner. It is only natural that elevating Heroes once stained by disgrace requires sufficient justification, is it not?”

“…My apologies.”

Having been convinced, Zenon proceeded to lecture Linforce from a superior position.

Linforce apologized, acknowledging that her explanation had been insufficient, but she could not maintain a completely expressionless face. A faint trace of frustration and anger could be seen.

“However, with this, it will be impossible to resume today’s meeting.”

Linforce muttered as she looked at the devastation she herself had caused.

The conference room was in a terrible state. Senior figures from various countries were foaming at the mouth and unconscious, some unconscious and having lost bladder control, a sight that could truly be described as bodies piled everywhere.

Those who were unharmed were limited to the Heroes, the Kingdom of Grants, the Kingdom of Sanokia, the Regalia Beastman Nation, and the Kingdom of Castal (Rudolf did his best). In the other countries, at least one or two people had fainted. In the worst cases, even the escort knights were all wiped out.

“It cannot be helped. We will adjourn today’s meeting here, and tomorrow we will resume from the continuation of the second agenda item.”

And thus, the first day of the world leaders’ summit came to a peaceful conclusion.

What do you mean by peaceful? If no one died, it’s peaceful.

After this, there was apparently to be a social gathering with representatives from each country and the Heroes, but Castal and Estea declined as a matter of course.

Thinking normally, you cannot relax and eat in enemy territory.

We returned to the waiting room once, regrouped with the other members, and then headed back outside the city.

The side of the Elgant Theocracy tried to insist that we stay at an inn in the city, but I did not care.

This time, reflecting on the previous experience, we decided to assemble temporary housing in a forest some distance away from Elgare. The reason was so that we could intercept assassins outside the temporary housing.

At the previous location, there had been surveillance from Elgare’s outer walls, so we had to lure assassins into the temporary housing before killing them. Having to clean up every time was a hassle.

Here, unless they got very close, surveillance would be impossible. And if they did get close, we could just eliminate them.

“Nooo, I hate this!”

“Sakuya-chan, your clothes will get wrinkled…”

As soon as the temporary housing was assembled, Sakura admonished Sakuya, who had collapsed face-down on the table.

“Why do I have to attend a meeting with those monsters? I was on edge the whole time, wondering when fighting would break out, geez…”

“If fighting starts, Rico will protect you, so it’s fine!”

“That does not make it fine!”

Rico was encouraging Sakuya, who was sulking.

Indeed, if fighting had broken out in that conference hall, it would have been a considerable disaster.

Needless to say, Zenon Grants’ combat power was immense, and Linforce, as the Pope, was also an existence beyond what ordinary humans could defeat.

Sharon of the Regalia Beastman Nation hardly spoke this time, but if it came to battle, she would surely demonstrate her full strength.

“To be honest, I do not expect the conference to end peacefully without incident.”

“Right? Haa…”

Due to several factors, the collapse of this conference is already visible.

The problem is which factor will cause the collapse.

Rather than multiple factors combining to collapse the conference, there are several individual factors that would each be sufficient on their own to bring it down. Whichever one occurs, the conference will certainly collapse.

“If the damage grows large, not just the conference hall being destroyed, it will be a great deal of trouble to evacuate those involved outside our subordinates. For now, I intend to absolutely protect the people of Castal and Estea.”

My subordinates can manage themselves, but the key figures of Castal and the Estea conference participants cannot.

When the conference collapses, the surrounding area will likely become a situation where ordinary humans cannot survive.

Without the benefits of Special Powers, they would almost certainly die unless we help them.

“That’s where I trust you, big brother. I’m not worried. But you don’t plan to protect the other royalty, do you?”

“Of course not.”

The people of the Kingdom of Sanokia are technically under my command, so I plan to protect them, but I do not care about the safety of the other royalty.

Therefore, I have no intention of protecting them of my own volition.

“If the other royalty die, all the countries will be thrown into chaos again. That’s the problem.”

“Yeah, there is no reason it wouldn’t cause chaos.”

Picking up on Sakuya’s mutter, Mio nodded as if it were obvious.

It seems Sakuya is concerned not about her own safety, but about the world descending into chaos.

As a queen, she cannot say, “Other countries don’t matter.”

And on top of that, her own safety might be outside her concerns because I guarantee it. She trusts me.

“The easiest thing would be to nip the seeds of trouble in the bud before anything happens, but…”

“That clearly goes against my principles, so I will refuse.”

“I knew you’d say that… Haa, what should I do…”

Sakuya slumped her shoulders.

The seeds of trouble Sakuya refers to can be broadly divided into three.

The first has nothing to do with me at all. Simply put, plans to kill people outside my inner circle.

The second is self-inflicted. Simply put, backlash from assassination plots.

The third is not yet clearly my enemy. Simply put, a future enemy.

All of them are types of opponents I do not actively involve myself with.

I have no intention of protecting those who are neither allies nor friendly nor decent, and I absolutely refuse to clean up after others. I defeat enemies once they become clear enemies; I will not launch preemptive strikes against potential enemies without allowing objections.

“More than anything, the biggest issue is that while I think it would be troublesome if all the countries fall into chaos, I don’t feel like forcing you to bend your principles just to save them…”

In short, it seems Sakuya herself does not truly want to protect the conference participants from the bottom of her heart.

Her stock of ‘consideration’ for other countries is probably sold out.

“Well, if you really end up wanting to save the others, let me know. If you can prepare a price that makes me bend my principles, I’ll protect them as much as you like.”

“There’s no way something like that would come up so easily!”

For some reason, Sakuya shouted loudly.

This temporary housing is also soundproof.

Apparently it was built so that spies not could listen in (according to the maids). Temporary housing…?

“M-Making Master bend his principles… isn’t that impossible?”

“W-Would a legendary-class weapon work…?”

“Sakura-sama, Master’s weapons are already mythical-class, so unless it has an extremely interesting effect, even legendary-class would be difficult.”

Sera, Sakura, and Mio, who had been relatively quiet until now, began discussing what kind of price could bend my principles.

“What about Maria-chan and Dora-chan…”

“I will always respect Jin-sama’s principles.”

《Dora is on master’s side too》

“Ah, okay.”

Mio’s question was not even allowed to be finished.

After changing clothes, Sakuya headed out to meetings with the senior figures.

Just because the summit was suspended does not mean she has enough free time to relax.

Even if Zenon stirred things up, the situation facing the Kingdom of Castal is still far from good.

As usual, I do not participate in Sakuya’s meetings with the senior figures.

Sakuya’s guard duties are also left to the maids while I rest.

There are many maid knights, so there is absolutely no need for me to guard her personally.

In other words, what I want to say is…

“I’m bored.”

I have become bored enough to laze around.

The sun is still out, so I could go out a bit.

However, there are no sightseeing spots I can go to right now. Going sightseeing in Elgare in this getup would cause trouble, and even if I removed my armor, I might run into Heroes.

If I disguised myself, those worries would disappear, but if you ask whether I want to go that far just to sightsee in the Elgant Theocracy, the answer is no.

In the end, unable to find anything to do, I ended up lazing around in the temporary housing. Dora is healing.

《Master~♡》

However, even if I do not go to interesting places, interesting things often come to me.

I stopped teasing Dora and once more checked the status of the person who was about to arrive.

Name: Kiene

LV75

Gender: Female

Age: 201

Race: Elf

Title: Sword Emperor, S-Rank Adventurer

Skills: \<Swordsmanship LV10> \<Physical Enhancement LV10> \<Sword Emperor LV >

A fairly common swordsmanship-specialist, a one-trick type.

It seems she used the long lifespan of elves to raise her skill levels.

People tend to think that longer-lived races have an advantage in raising skill levels, but in reality, the longer-lived the race, the harder it is for skill levels to increase.

Of course, harder does not mean impossible, and if one masters them, the results are as you see.

In exchange, it is a disappointing build lacking other elf-like skills, but…

Now then, even for this disappointing build, there are two interesting points.

The first is, as you can see, the unique skill \<Sword Emperor>.

\<Sword Emperor>

Granted to those who hold the title “Sword Emperor”. Greatly increases the effects of the \<Swordsmanship> skill.

This is a type of skill that only functions when paired with its title.

It is the same relationship as my \<Labyrinth Dominion> skill and the “Dungeon Master” title.

However, unlike “Dungeon Master”, which can be transferred relatively easily, the method of obtaining “Sword Emperor” is, to say the least, rather violent.

The method is extremely simple: “Kill the previous Sword Emperor.”

The moment you kill the previous Sword Emperor, you obtain the title “Sword Emperor” and the skill \<Sword Emperor>.

At the very least, to become the next Sword Emperor, you must have the ability to defeat someone who possesses \<Sword Emperor>.

A trick that comes to mind is “wait for the opponent to grow old”.

Considering that, Kiene the elf has various advantages.

That is enough about \<Sword Emperor>. Let me introduce the second interesting point.

Infernal Grudge Cursed Sword

Category: One-handed sword, curse

Rarity: Legendary-class

Notes: Strengthens according to the number of humanoid kills, auto-repair

It has an effect that looks familiar, similar to the “Grudge Great Axe” wielded by the bandit Dolg, whom I fought when escaping the Kingdom of Eldia.

According to Alta, it is a later work by the same creator. As such, it has stronger effects and a higher rarity. An extremely annoying creator.

And at the point where someone can wield this sword effectively, it can be concluded that the owner is a people-slayer.

Because the kill count of this sword resets when the owner changes…

So then, why is Kiene heading toward Castal’s temporary housing?

Simply put, she is an ‘assassin’.

Yes, that priest, not satisfied with just an assassination organization, also sent an external force, an S-rank adventurer active in the Elgant Theocracy, Kiene, as an assassin.

Apparently, Kiene and the priest are old acquaintances (the priest is actually an elf as well), and he requested that she kill us. And Kiene accepted.

Normally, S-rank adventurers are not assassins, so there is no reason they would accept such a request, but Kiene was a bit different.

Her hobby is “cutting down strong swordsmen”.

Strictly speaking, it is “fighting strong swordsmen”, but due to her dangerous principle that it makes no sense for the loser of a duel to remain alive, she kills everyone she defeats, so it amounts to the same thing.

It is unclear how someone like this became S-rank, but she has apparently made an agreement with the Adventurers Guild not to fight adventurers of B-rank or higher.

As for others, if both parties consent to a “duel to the death”, it is tacitly approved.

The priest told Kiene that Gene is not an adventurer, that he drove off the demon race that attacked the Kingdom of Eldia, and that he is a swordsman.

At that point, regardless of the request, there is no way Kiene would not act.

And thus, an S-rank adventurer assassin is born.

Kiene is the master of a style called the Sword Emperor Style and has about ten disciples.

This time, she has brought those disciples with her to the forest where the temporary housing is located.

The disciples have two roles.

The first is to act as witnesses to the duel, reporting the existence of mutual consent and the outcome to the Guild and others.

The second is to provoke the opponent and drag them into a duel. By provoking with large numbers, they make the duel happen.

Bring disciples, propose a duel. If the duel is refused, ridicule them as cowards. If the duel is accepted, defeat and kill them. …I see. An extremely troublesome assassin.

“Jin-sama, what will you do?”

What Maria is asking is, of course, what to do about Kiene.

As an aside, besides Maria, who is by my side as a guard, and Dora, whom I am petting, the other members are acting separately.

“Well, what should I do…”

Asked by Maria about how to handle Kiene, I decided to think for a bit.

First, Kiene’s life or death.

Unfortunately, there is no route other than “death”.

She is coming as an assassin to kill me. While it is not assassination in the strict sense, she is challenging me to a duel to the death with the premise of killing me, so I have no intention of letting her make excuses.

And the other criterion: whether she is decent or not, is also a fail. I have no intention of adding a people-slayer to my subordinates.

Therefore, Kiene will certainly be killed.

Next, I consider skills.

Killing Kiene means inheriting her title “Sword Emperor” and the \<Sword Emperor> skill.

However, despite this rare opportunity to obtain a unique skill, I feel not even the slightest desire to try using \<Sword Emperor>. Strange things happen.

“Jin-sama does not seem to particularly want the \<Sword Emperor> skill.”

“You can tell?”

“Your eyes shine differently compared to when you face skills you want to try.”

“You observe well.”

It seems my reaction was quite easy to read.

“I am always watching Jin-sama. …So, if you would allow it, may I be the one to face her?”

“I do not mind, but is there a reason?”

“Yes. Normally, I would want Jin-sama to acquire as many powerful skills as possible to better ensure your safety. However, Jin-sama tends not to use even useful skills if you are not interested in them.”

I have plenty of reasons to agree with that.

I am aware that I decide what to use based more on interest than on effectiveness or utility.

“This skill cannot be used without the title. Rather than Jin-sama obtaining the title and letting it gather dust, I thought it would be better for me to acquire it and use it to protect you.”

I see. With title-bound skills, unlike others, you need to think ahead from the moment of acquisition.

Come to think of it, it is similar to how the \<Transcendence> skill is handled.

“Understood. Then I will leave Kiene to you.”

“Thank you very much.”

And thus, the duel with “Sword Emperor” Kiene would be handled by Maria.

“Sword Emperor VS Beastman Hero”. That is a hot matchup.

Wearing my Gene equipment and with Maria in her maid outfit, we left the temporary housing and advanced into the forest.

Ahead of us, the maid knights and Kiene’s group were exchanging words.

Kiene’s group kept insisting, “We are here for a duel, bring out Gene.”

The maid knights kept insisting, “We cannot dispatch knights for something like that.”

Which side do you think is being reasonable?

Kiene’s group seemed to notice my approach.

Kiene, as expected of an elf, was tall and slender (a prejudice), with short green hair, and was a beauty.

That said, perhaps due to her personality showing on her face, she was the type of beauty prefixed with “sharp”.

“Silver armor… You must be Gene! My name is Kiene, master of the Sword Emperor Style! Duel me! If you refuse, we will mock you forever within the Sword Emperor Style!”

“That’s right! If you’re not a coward, accept the duel!”

“Don’t get cocky just because you got a little famous!”

Kiene declared the duel, and her disciples followed up with provocations.

Kiene is female, but her disciples seem to be about half male and half female. Not that it matters.

If they provoke us, we have to provoke back, right?

“You want to fight me? I am not so idle as to deal with small fry. If you truly wish to fight me, then defeat my personal maid first. Well, that is impossible for the likes of you.”

I answered in a mocking tone and pointed to my personal maid… Maria.

As an aside, I was idle enough to play around.

“A maid? That little girl will fight me? Don’t be ridiculous! Even my disciples could defeat someone like that easily! Are you so frightened that you would sacrifice your maid!”

“If you think so, then try it. You can handle it, right?”

Ignoring the indignant Kiene, I checked with Maria.

“Yes. Leave it to me.”

“Can you handle it?” or not, this is Maria’s own wish, so there is no issue.

“Master! Let me do it! I will cut that little girl in half with one blow!”

“Salt, is it? Very well. Gene, we will have your maid fight my disciple. If my disciple wins, next it will be my turn against you. If your maid wins, I will face that maid. If the maid loses, then next is your turn. …How about that?”

A disciple named Salt appealed to Kiene, and after she nodded, she made that proposal to me.

In other words, if Maria loses, it becomes a fight between me and Kiene. Well, that would not be a problem.

“Fine. What are the match rules?”

“Naturally, one-on-one, no time limit. It continues until one party dies.”

“Surrender?”

“None. In a battle where lives are at stake, surrender is not permitted.”

Kiene answered my questions without hesitation. Her disciples nodded as well.

Really, what a dangerous bunch. They should learn from that honest battle maniac, the fighting vampire.

“Understood. There is an open area a short walk away, so let’s hold the match there.”

“All right.”

We walked a short distance at my suggestion and emerged into an open clearing in the forest.

It was a suitable size for a one-on-one fight.

“Then first, Sword Emperor Style disciple Salt and Gene’s personal maid…”

“Marie.”

“…Marie will begin their duel. Both parties, step forward.”

Maria and Salt faced each other in the center of the clearing.

It should go without saying at this point that Marie is Maria’s alias.

“You will regret mocking the Sword Emperor Style.”

Salt glared sharply at Maria and me as he said that. He is apparently 15 years old, but since he is close to 180 cm tall, compared to Maria he feels older than his age.

Well, in this world, appearance is mostly useless as reference information.

Salt held a two-handed sword (rare-class) in front of him.

Combined with his large build, he has a certain presence.

I debated what equipment to give Maria, but in the end chose the “Treasure Sword: Everdark”.

It is the weapon Maria used back when we were in Castal.

This opponent does not warrant giving her a mythical-class weapon, and I would prefer not to show one.

And since she is facing Kiene’s legendary-class sword, if the weapon is too low-grade it would look bad. Everdark is secret-treasure class, one rank below legendary, so it should be fine.

Maria stood naturally without taking a stance.

“Marie. You will not take a stance?”

“There is no problem. Please begin.”

“Brat! Don’t mock me!”

When Maria answered Kiene’s question, Salt flared up, thinking he was being mocked.

“Salt, if you have complaints, show them with your sword.”

“…Yes.”

“It seems both are ready, so let us begin. …Duel start!”

“Uooooooo!”

At Kiene’s signal, Salt charged straight at Maria.

He swung down from overhead.

The crude, force-driven attack had no chance of reaching Maria. She evaded it by moving just half a step.

With a loud crash, the sword gouged into the ground.

“Don’t just dodge!”

From his lowered position, Salt swung his sword horizontally, trying to cut Maria.

However, the hasty slash lacked power, and again had no chance of reaching her. Maria lightly leapt, used Salt’s sword as a foothold, and jumped once more.

“Geh!”

She stepped on Salt’s head and landed behind him.

“It seems there is not much I can learn from you.”

Maria muttered in disappointment.

As a swordsman of the Sword Emperor Style, she must have expected to learn something.

But when all was said and done, he was an opponent whose attacks could not possibly reach her.

It would be cruel to tell her not to be disappointed.

“Stop making fun of meeeee!”

Salt swung his sword as he turned, but again, there was little technique and no power.

“That is enough.”

-Slash-

“Eh…?”

“W-What!?”

Maria cut down Salt before his sword could reach her.

It happened so fast that none of the swordsmen except Kiene could even react.

A moment later, blood sprayed from Salt, who had been cut diagonally.

Maria had already taken distance, without even getting splashed by the blood.

**AN:** Cold treatment for Salt-kun. That was all I wanted to say.

The story about the Sword Emperor Style will conclude in the first half of the next chapter. To be honest, it has zero impact on the main plot.

## **136 Short Story: A Little Questionnaire for Subordinates**

**AN:** This is a hypothetical “what if” scenario about asking subordinates the following question.

It is another version of the “How is that person these days” short piece I have not done recently. The content of the question has been blacked out. It has no particular meaning.

Ah, it is not finished yet, but I am thinking (wishfully) of releasing one more short story around noon.

---

Q: If Jindou Jin were to ask you for XXX.

① I like him as the opposite sex, so OK

② I want his seed

③ I would not refuse if asked

④ I do not want to right now

⑤ Absolutely not

Main Party

Sakura: ①

“I think that is probably the case…”

Dora: ③

## **136 Side Story 10: The Saintess Departure**

**AN:** It is short, but this is the second short piece for today.

I will say this in advance. This was not a retroactive addition, but part of the initial plan.

---

As the leaders summit to be held in the Elgant Theocracy drew near, a group of girls had gathered in the private chambers of the king inside the royal castle of the Kingdom of Sanokia.

“I understand. All we need to do is convey Sister Saki’s words and offer everything we have to Shindo-sama, correct?”

“I’m sorry. I’m asking you to do something so unreasonable…”

Mizuhara Saki apologized to the girl who had once worn the clothes of a “priestess”, now dressed in a gown befitting the ruler of a nation.

“Please do not worry about it. If it is for Sister Saki, we can do anything. Everyone feels the same way, right?”

“Of course. If it is for Saki-sama, we can overcome any hardship.”

When the girl who had become a “queen” asked, the girl dressed as a “knight” nodded firmly.

“Mm… I’ll do my best. For Saki.”

“If it’s for Saki-chi, even whipping these old bones into shape ain’t no trouble.”

The girl dressed as a “scout”, and the girl dressed as a “hunter?” also nodded.

“Ohohohoho, of course! If Saki-san desires it, becoming the sexual slave of a man we have never met is hardly a big deal at all!”

Though her opinion aligned with the others, the way the girl dressed as a “mage” phrased it touched Saki’s raw nerve.

“After I explained Jin-kun to you in such detail, you still call him ‘a man we’ve never met’?”

“Hii!”

Glared at by Saki, the “mage” collapsed on the spot, soaking both her clothes and the expensive carpet beneath her.

Though they did not collapse, the other four were also caught in the aftershock and dampened their clothes.

To Mizuhara Saki, Shindo Jin was the most beloved existence in the world. If anyone spoke ill of him, even slightly, Mizuhara Saki would quietly snap. The “mage” occasionally let something slip and had received Saki’s cold gaze several times before.

As for the comment about being a sexual slave, Saki was not angry. Rather, she would be happy if she were used as a sexual slave. It would mean the things she had given were being happily used.

“Saki-chi! That was just an example! I wasn’t calling Shindo-sama a man we don’t know!”

“Y-yes! I’ve listened to Saki-san’s stories, so I do know Shindo-sama! He’s Saki-san’s childhood friend, and the man Saki-san loves most, right!?”

The “hunter”, still soaked from the waist down, hurried to cover for her, and the “mage” also tried to explain herself.

“Th-that’s… being told I love him like that… You’re right, though.”

Having Shindo Jin referred to as “the man she loves”, Mizuhara Saki’s anger dissipated like mist.

The five others, aside from Saki, let out sighs of relief. They would throw everything away for Saki, but being disliked by her was the one thing they could not accept.

And above all, they desperately wished for Mizuhara Saki to always live in peace of mind.

After changing their underwear and clothes, the five girls gathered once more in the same room.

“But Sister Saki, offering everything we have to Shindo-sama is fine, but may we offer our hearts to you alone? The reason we offer everything to Shindo-sama is because our hearts already belong to you.”

“Yes, that’s fine. But if my instructions ever contradict Jin-kun’s orders, follow Jin-kun’s orders, okay? I don’t think it will ever happen, but just in case.”

“Yes, if that is what Sister Saki wishes.”

Because Shindo Jin is whimsical, his patterns of behavior are difficult to predict.

Something Mizuhara Saki asked casually could potentially interfere with Shindo Jin’s actions.

That is why she asked them to prioritize Shindo Jin’s orders over her own.

“So, Saki-chi, you’re leaving this country, right?”

“It’ll be lonely without Saki.”

“I’m sorry. I still can’t go meet Jin-kun yet.”

Until she was forgiven by Shindo Jin, she could not approach him.

Whether Shindo Jin was actually angry or not was beside the point. This was something Mizuhara Saki had decided for herself.

“Even if you are careful, Saki-sama, isn’t there still a chance you might meet him by coincidence?”

When the “knight” asked, Mizuhara Saki shook her head.

“That won’t happen. There’s no way I’d mistake where Jin-kun is. Right now… he’s somewhere incredibly high up? What on earth is he doing?”

“Sister Saki, which direction are you looking? Castal isn’t that way, is it?”

“Yeah, but he’s over there…”

Mizuhara Saki’s gaze shifted away from Castal, where Shindo Jin was supposed to be, toward the Kingdom of Brown Wall.

“If Saki-chi says so, then he really is over there.”

“As always, Saki-san’s Blessing is incredible. And being the only Hero with two Blessings is amazing as well.”

Trying to make up for her earlier mistake, the “mage” went all out flattering Mizuhara Saki.

Forgetting the crucial fact that if you want to improve Mizuhara Saki’s mood, you should praise Shindo Jin.

“No, it’s not a Blessing anymore. It’s just a skill. Why would I keep a Blessing that makes me feel disgust toward Jin-kun just by having it?”

Though Blessings are proof of being a Hero, they hold no value for Mizuhara Saki.

On the contrary, since they were the cause of her feeling disgust toward Shindo Jin, they were nothing but harmful.

On the very day she received them, Mizuhara Saki removed the harmful elements from the Blessing \<Sword Saint> and the other Blessing, converting them into harmless skills.

Mizuhara Saki can do that.

“A skill… If Saki says so, I believe it exists. But I can’t really feel it.”

“But as Saki-sama said, there were times when I suddenly felt my swordsmanship improve. That must have been what they call leveling up… probably.”

The five girls, having received an explanation about skills from Mizuhara Saki, believed that “if Mizuhara Saki says it, it must be true”, but without any real sense of it, they could not speak definitively.

“You don’t have to force yourself to understand. I think it’s hard for people of this world to grasp. Besides, I hardly ever use skills myself.”

“Once she uses something even once, she can reproduce most phenomena just by seeing them. Sister Saki truly is beyond all standards.”

In truth, Mizuhara Saki possesses only a few things that can be called skills.

Furthermore, two of them were originally Blessings.

Mizuhara Saki can use \<Swordsmanship>, \<Archery>, \<Recovery Magic>, and \<Fire Magic>.

Because she has seen others use them.

And those are not skills. Or rather, they are not treated as skills. They are merely reproductions of phenomena.

Mizuhara Saki can do that. If it is something a person can do, she can do almost anything.

Naturally, she can do things beyond that as well.

“Back in the other world, I could do similar things too. I just didn’t bother, because Jin-kun didn’t want me to…”

Mizuhara Saki’s sole standard for action is Shindo Jin.

Even if she possessed the power to destroy the world, if Shindo Jin did not wish for it, Mizuhara Saki would never use it.

“Saki-sama truly loves Shindo-sama. However, from what you’ve told us, Shindo-sama does not seem like such a narrow-minded person who would never forgive a mistake. If you apologized, wouldn’t he forgive you?”

The “knight” had heard more than enough stories about Shindo Jin from Saki (though she never showed displeasure).

Even discounting Mizuhara Saki’s bias, Shindo Jin did not seem like someone so small-minded.

It is true that when Shindo Jin was driven out of the Kingdom of Eldia, he was met with hostility and was not helped. But no one directly insulted him, nor did they resort to violence.

If Shindo Jin is as omnipotent as rumored, it is hard to believe he would harbor resentment toward Mizuhara Saki over something like that.

“Yeah, I don’t think Jin-kun is that angry. But I can’t face him yet. At least, not now… If I went to see him like this, and on the off chance he really was still angry, I would never be able to forgive myself.”

“That is why we will go to Shindo-sama in your stead and gauge his will, correct?”

Mizuhara Saki nodded at the ruler’s question.

“I’m really sorry. Since it’s a leaders summit, I don’t think you’ll be killed, but I do think I’m asking you to walk a very dangerous path.”

“I told you at the start. For Saki-sama, we can overcome any hardship.”

“Yep.”

“Mm…”

“Indeed.”

“Of course.”

The girls pressed their hands to their chests.

There, a crest had been engraved by Mizuhara Saki’s skill.

The name of that skill is \<Bestowal>. Those granted a crest become apostles, and the one who bestows it can know whether they are safe. Conversely, if the crest disappears, it means the one who bestowed it has died. In this way, both sides can confirm each other’s safety.

One could say it is a skill with little influence, but because it allows them to feel their bond more strongly than anything else, the five girls would always touch this crest when swearing oaths to Mizuhara Saki.

“Thank you, everyone. Someday, I will properly apologize to Jin-kun.”

“Yes. We sincerely await the day that comes.”

The next day, Mizuhara Saki departed from the Kingdom of Sanokia.

Not even the five girls knew her destination. All they could do was check the crest on their chests several times a day to confirm her safety.

---

**AN:** If you read the stories where Saki appears carefully, there are quite a few unnatural scenes scattered about. No one ever pointed them out in the comments, though. If that was intentional, then thank you.

Example: In “Side Story 4: The Sword Saintess”, it is written that \<Sword Saint> was a Blessing given to Saki. But it is never stated that \<Sword Saint> is still a Blessing, nor is it ever written that she used \<Sword Saint> when fighting thieves.

The truth is, I had been quietly hiding this for over a year. This reveal is Koda’s April Fool’s joke.

Or rather, do you really think Jin’s childhood friend is just an ordinary person? Why do you think she never appeared in the main story? Why do you think Jin, who is kind to those close to him, never worried about his childhood friend?

Because both of them are cheat characters on par with Jin! There’s no need to worry about them, and it’s a pain to include them in the main story!

+++

## **137: The Sword Emperor and the Resumption of the Conference**

**AN:** The Sword Emperor style was originally the Sword Saint style, but it overlapped too much with Saki Mizuhara, so it was changed.

Now then, I really need to start thinking about next year’s April Fools joke soon…

---

“Soooolt!!!”

“No good! He’s dead!”

“How horrible! This isn’t something a human would do!”

The disciples of the Sword Emperor style surrounded Salt’s corpse, wailing in grief.

Huh? What is this farce…?

“He did this, he did something this cruel!”

“Salt was such a good boy! And yet!”

The disciples glared at Maria and me as if we were their parents’ murderers.

“I will avenge Salt myself, so you all stand back. I cannot remain silent when my disciple has been killed. Marie, you will fight me at once.”

Hearing Keane’s declaration, I understood a bit.

So this is a farce meant to assert that they are in the right and to make us feel guilty.

And then, without giving the opponent time to rest, they press on with shoddy reasoning…

“That’s fine. It’s a waste of time, so let’s begin quickly.”

Did they really think Maria or I would be shaken by such petty tricks?

Maria faced Keane, completely ignoring the heckling from the sidelines. The disciples dragged Salt’s corpse over to the edge of the plaza.

Once Maria and Keane faced each other, the disciples stopped paying any attention to Salt’s body.

As expected, it really was just a farce.

And then I realized my intuition had been right.

No wonder the \<Sword Emperor> skill hadn’t interested me at all.

In short, the title “Sword Emperor” is proof that you’re the boss of these trashy people, right? Even if it’s said to be a unique title required to use the \<Sword Emperor> skill, I wouldn’t want it at all.

《Maria, it’s the skill of people who do something this stupid, but do you want to use \<Sword Emperor>?》

Without thinking, I sent Maria a telepathic message.

If it were me, I wouldn’t want to become a “Sword Emperor” even if begged.

I don’t want to be thought of as the same kind as these people.

《If Lord Jin absolutely insists, I will refrain from obtaining the title “Sword Emperor”, but if you leave it to me, I would like to kill Keane as is and obtain the title.》

《Are you sure?》

《Yes. I intend to use anything that can be used. Of course, only by methods that Lord Jin does not dislike.》

That last line is actually very important.

Now then, I wouldn’t want to become a “Sword Emperor” even if begged, but do I dislike it enough to forbid Maria from doing so? When asked that way, the truth is, not quite that much.

The name of the title itself is kind of cool, after all.

《Alright. I’ll leave it to you, Maria.》

《Thank you very much.》

If Maria is fine with it, there’s nothing more I should say.

It’s only natural that what I want and what Maria wants are different.

“Then, Gene, give the signal to begin.”

As Keane said that, she took up that cursed legendary-class equipment, the “Cursed Sword of Purgatorial Resentment.”

Just like before, Maria stood naturally, relaxed and without unnecessary tension.

“Got it… Then, the match begins!”

“Hah!”

The moment I gave the signal, Keane leapt forward.

Is an opening charge the basic tactic of the Sword Emperor style?

However, her speed is on a completely different level from Salt’s.

In an instant she moved in front of Maria and swung her sword in a reverse diagonal slash.

Maria did not dodge, but instead received the strike with her sword.

– KIN! –

A sharp sound rang out, and Keane immediately moved on to her next action.

With footwork worthy of \<Physical Enhancement LV10>, she harassed Maria while repeatedly striking.

Maria did not initiate any attacks herself, continuing to block Keane’s blows.

Keane’s weapon performance is probably superior. Cursed though it may be, it’s a legendary-class sword. There’s no way it’s weak.

On top of that, it grows stronger with every person it kills, making it even more troublesome.

“Tch, it won’t break even after all this clashing! You’re using a sturdy weapon!”

However, the “Treasure Sword: Eternal Darkness” is also a secret-treasure-class weapon.

Though it is one rank lower in rarity, that difference is not fatal. It also has an auto-repair function, so it’s not flimsy enough to be broken one-sidedly in a fight like this.

Keane began to show irritation at the sword that would not break no matter how many times they exchanged blows.

Both have \<Swordsmanship> and \<Physical Enhancement> at level 10, equal in that regard.

In terms of pure sword skill, Keane might have the edge due to \<Sword Emperor>. However, Maria’s true strength is not \<Swordsmanship>, but the breadth of tactics made possible by her dexterity.

“Sword Emperor style secret art, ‘Seven Heavens Draw’!!!”

One of the secret arts usable only by holders of the \<Sword Emperor> skill, “Seven Falls Eight Rises”… or rather, “Seven Heavens Draw”, was unleashed by Keane. A pun, huh… I think it’s fine.

That secret art is a powerful technique that unleashes seven slashes in an instant.

“Hah!”

“What!?”

Maria avoided and blocked every one of those instant slashes by a hair’s breadth.

“Tch, again!”

The “Seven Heavens Draw” was unleashed once more, but…

Maria aimed for a counter in the gap between the first and second strikes, at a timing of less than a millisecond.

Because the counter was launched at such a perfect timing, Keane had no choice but to interrupt the “Seven Heavens Draw” and go on the defensive to block it.

“Guh!?”

“Using the same technique twice in a row without even a feint, are you looking down on me?”

“So arrogant for someone who’s been on the defensive the whole time!”

Indeed, as things stood, she could only snatch victory by aiming for counters.

Because Maria currently had only about eighty percent of Keane’s stats.

Simply put, it was a handicap match. You could even call it holding back.

This time, in order to polish her pure swordsmanship, Maria had deliberately lowered her stats as far as possible, reduced the quality of her weapon, and sealed off most of her skills as self-imposed restrictions.

I didn’t tell her to do it. Maria said she wanted to do it herself.

“It would seem so. Then, I will also raise things by one level.”

In addition, from the start of the match until now, she had not used any skills other than \<Swordsmanship> and \<Physical Enhancement>. Having gained confidence that she could manage on defense alone, she was now lifting the seal on other skills to go on the offensive.

“Lies!”

“Believe whatever you like.”

Maria ducked under Keane’s slash and smoothly unleashed a spinning back kick.

That’s some good \<Martial Arts>.

Assuming there would be no attacks from a crouched position, Keane hurriedly dodged, but the kick still grazed her side, clearly landing.

“Guh! Using kicks in a sword fight is underhanded!”

“In what you call a duel to the death, are only swords permitted? Calling it a duel while not using everything at your disposal and not fighting with all your might is hardly admirable.”

That said, Maria isn’t really fighting with all her might either, considering it’s a handicap match.

Well, with restrictions in place, she is using all of her ‘current’ power. In that sense, you could say she’s fighting with all her might.

“Tch! You’ve got a sharp tongue!”

Her bluster aside, the moment \<Martial Arts> was added to Maria’s skill set, Keane was driven entirely onto the defensive.

\<Sword Emperor> boosts the effects of \<Swordsmanship>, but that alone apparently cannot match the combination of two level 10 skills. It really highlights the lack of adaptability of a swordsmanship specialist.

“Khah!”

Perhaps Maria had begun to read Keane’s action patterns, because her attacks were gradually starting to land. Just now, her toes had grazed Keane’s solar plexus.

Of course, none of the slashes landed cleanly, but the \<Martial Arts> attacks were hitting enough to steadily accumulate damage.

Realizing the unfavorable situation, Keane made the worst possible move here.

“You lot, restrain Marie’s movements! While you do that, I’ll unleash my ultimate secret art!”

“””””Yes!”””””

The lowest of finishing moves, “Call your allies.”

Hearing Keane’s order, the disciples rushed toward Maria with weapons in hand.

Hey, what happened to the one-on-one rule?

As an aside, the maid knights had already returned to the temporary housing, so the only ones here were Maria and me. Somehow, I had a feeling it would be more entertaining to send them back.

You know, when people realize they have a numerical advantage, they tend to resort to the simplistic “violence of numbers”, right?

In other words, it was an obvious trap.

“Fighting many against one is troublesome. It can’t be helped. I’ll raise things by one more level.”

Maria drew a dagger from a belt hidden beneath her skirt.

Originally, Maria’s combat style is dual-wielding a longsword and a dagger.

Yes, in fact, up until now, Maria had continued fighting in a style different from her true one. And yet she was still managing. She’s really a versatile one.

And so the disciples attacked.

But how much use could disciples be against an opponent their master couldn’t defeat?

“Guh!?”

“Gah!?”

“Kyaa!?”

“Ugh!?”

…

Answer: They were completely useless.

In the blink of an eye, a pile of nine corpses was formed.

Even I can say this, but expecting mercy or hesitation from Maria is a mistake.

However, the original goal of buying time was achieved, and it seemed Keane’s ultimate secret art was ready.

The cursed sword in Keane’s hands glowed a bright red. Ominous.

“Sword Emperor style ultimate secret art, ‘Sword Soul One Foe’!!!”

What was unleashed along with the shout was an ultra-high-speed, ultra-powerful horizontal slash.

That slash was launched from nearly ten meters away, yet it traveled through the air and came rushing at Maria.

…Isn’t this just \<Flying Sword Art>!?

That said, the size of the flying slash was fairly large, making it difficult to dodge.

“It’s an imitation, but I’ll borrow the technique. ‘Flying Sword Barrage’!”

In response, Maria used my signature technique? “Flying Sword Barrage (repeatedly firing \<Flying Sword Art>).”

…Come to think of it, \<Flying Sword Art> wasn’t among the skills Maria had sealed.

She hadn’t used it because a one-sided match at long range wouldn’t be good experience, but she had kept it available just in case the opponent used a long-range attack.

The power itself was probably higher for “Sword Soul One Foe.”

A single \<Flying Sword Art> could not cancel it out. However, the second and third shots canceled out “Sword Soul One Foe.”

“Impossible!? My ultimate secret art is being broken!? Gyaaaaaah!!!!”

“Flying Sword Barrage” is not just three consecutive strikes.

The remaining slashes after canceling out “Sword Soul One Foe” naturally struck Keane, who was standing along their trajectory.

She should have run away, but Keane couldn’t move at all and took the full brunt of the “Flying Sword Barrage.” It seems “Sword Soul One Foe” is the type of technique that leaves the user unable to move for a while afterward.

A big move that requires charging before activation and leaves you rigid afterward… yeah, that’s not very practical.

In an instant, Keane’s HP dropped to zero, and the match was decided.

After the match with Keane ended, we called the maid knights and had them help with the cleanup.

Maria successfully obtained the title “Sword Emperor” and the \<Sword Emperor> skill.

That said, since all practitioners of the Sword Emperor style were wiped out in that fight, the style itself died out…

Whatever. A style like that.

After the cleanup was finished and we returned to the temporary housing, Sakuya was slumped over the table.

“Sakuya, what’s wrong?”

“Big Brother, you just killed an S-rank adventurer, didn’t you?”

“No, Sakuya. The one who killed her was me.”

Maria, who had actually killed Keane, corrected her.

“Yeah, that’s right. Well, S-rank adventurers are treated as nobles, so I was thinking this could become troublesome…”

“Even so, they were the ones who challenged us to a duel to the death.”

“Yeah, I understand that, but do you think that argument will honestly go through here?”

Considering how this country has handled things so far, it was obvious that it wouldn’t.

“Alright, then let’s say that the S-rank adventurer Keane never came here in the first place. The bodies are already stored, so there’s no way they’ll be found, and if everyone pretends they don’t know anything, it should be fine.”

“No, there’s no way that would… actually, maybe.”

Sakuya tried to reject my proposal, but changed her mind partway through.

In the first place, the problem is that an S-rank adventurer like Keane came here at all.

More precisely, the problem is that someone exists who has both pieces of information: “An S-rank adventurer went to the forest and didn’t return”, and “Important figures from Castal have built temporary housing in the forest”.

For example, suppose someone tries to condemn us over Keane’s case.

That person would be admitting that they knew Keane came to us. In other words, “They didn’t stop an S-rank adventurer whose hobby is killing from heading to a place where important figures of another country were present”.

That’s a problem, isn’t it?

Claiming she came to the forest by chance would also be difficult.

After all, there are maid knights stationed at the forest entrance.

We could even say that Keane came to the forest but was sent back after explaining her reason. If she forced her way in, that would be tantamount to declaring herself an assassin.

That’s a problem, isn’t it?

If they make baseless accusations, we can turn things around by pointing out their own faults.

It’s a sloppy assassination plan born of desperation. There’s plenty of room to rebut it.

“Thinking about it, it’s just an accusation that’s more annoying than harmful. I promised to be your shield, Big Brother, and it’s better than you going on a rampage, so I’ll just have to do my best!”

It’s good that Sakuya pulled herself together, but I’m not sure how I feel about her bringing up my rampage as a comparison. I don’t have any plans to go on a rampage right now, you know? There’s no need to.

The next day, we headed to Elgale once again to attend the leaders’ conference.

Just like yesterday, the temporary housing was being dismantled by the maids. Leaving it in a place like this would only cause disadvantages.

Naturally, the temporary housing we had lent to the Kingdom of Estea had also been removed. We did promise to assemble it again if it became necessary.

As yesterday, we passed through the outer wall gate, entered the grand cathedral, parted ways with the group not attending the conference, and headed for the conference room.

Up to this point, the topic of killing an S-rank adventurer had not come up. Even now, that priest seems to be behaving himself.

Did he realize that trying to condemn us would only get him killed?

We arrived at the conference room.

A lot happened yesterday, but it seems the conference would be held in the same room.

The traces of the previous mishap had been neatly cleaned up. …Wouldn’t it be mentally damaging to sit in the same spot where you had an accident yesterday?

It doesn’t concern our group, so there’s no need to worry about it.

Once all participants had gathered, Linforce declared the start of day two of the conference.

“Then, we will resume from the continuation of the questions regarding hero support that were interrupted yesterday. After that, we would like to open recruitment for hero-supporting nations.”

The interruption was caused by the killing intent Linforce released, but she made no mention of it.

Well, since quite a few people had accidents, dredging it up wouldn’t benefit anyone…

The questions progressed, and today seemed smoother than yesterday.

The biggest reason is probably that Zenon hasn’t been making disruptive remarks.

Zenon was leaning on the table with his cheek in his hand, yawning boredly.

“Are there any further questions? If not, I would like to begin recruitment for hero-supporting nations.”

Linforce swept her gaze around to confirm that no one raised their hand.

It’s probably not my imagination that her eyes paused briefly around Zenon.

“Then, we will proceed with the recruitment of hero-supporting nations. Representatives of nations who believe they can join as hero-supporting nations, please stand.”

At Linforce’s words, representatives of nations friendly with the Elgant Theocracy stood up.

Most of the nations receiving the “Paired Farseeing Mirrors” appear to be on Elgant’s side, and all the representatives visible through the mirrors stood.

Overall, more nations stood than remained seated, but of course, there were nations that did not stand.

Besides our own Castal Kingdom, the Kingdom of Estea, the Kingdom of Glantz, and the Regalia Beastman Nation fell into that category.

Though it has little presence, the Ato Confederation of Nations was actually invited to the conference as well.

However, since all twelve nations couldn’t come, three of the larger nations within the Ato Confederation (the scholarly nation “Neitune Academic Kingdom”, the martial nation “Argus Principality”, and the commercial nation “Mendel Principality”) came as representatives to consolidate whether the other nations would join as hero-supporting nations.

The Narnka Kingdom, which has subjugated many royal families, naturally will not become a hero-supporting nation.

Apparently, other nations strongly influenced by a certain trading company also will not become hero-supporting nations. How mysterious!

Incidentally, the Kingdom of Sanokia has applied to become a hero-supporting nation.

Of course, this choice was made after discussions with Sakuya and the others.

This takes into account Sanokia’s position adjacent to the Elgant Theocracy, and also serves as camouflage to avoid having our relationship discovered.

If Sanokia, which has had friendly relations with the heroes until now, were to suddenly take an anti-hero stance, it would likely cause various troubles. Honestly, I don’t want to take care of Sanokia’s problems too…

Looking over the standing participants, Linforce nodded with satisfaction.

Then she turned her gaze to those who remained seated.

“So there are some nations that will not become hero-supporting nations. Why will the Castal Kingdom not become a hero-supporting nation?”

Oh! You’re really asking that! You’re asking it!?

“It is the same reason as before. Even without heroes, demonkind does not pose a threat.”

“The Demon King can only be defeated by heroes. Not supporting heroes means enjoying the benefit of ‘the Demon King being eliminated’ without paying the price. Do you not think so?”

Hmm, Linforce’s argument does have a valid point.

Supporting heroes does connect to removing the threat known as the Demon King.

Conversely, not supporting heroes means placing the burden solely on other nations while doing nothing yourself and still reaping the benefits of the Demon King’s defeat.

“Indeed. Lady Linforce’s argument is reasonable. However, do you not think there is a major premise missing from that discussion?”

“…And what would that be?”

Linforce didn’t seem to realize it, and asked Sakuya.

“Results. Have the heroes achieved any significant results so far? Repelled a demon army. Defeated demon officers. …We have heard none of that. With all the time that has passed, they have accomplished nothing. We cannot gamble on such heroes.”

Yes, the heroes currently have almost no record of engagements with demonkind.

The few exceptions would be the Battle of the Eldia Royal Capital, where the heroes suffered a crushing defeat.

If anything, I feel like I’ve been clashing with demonkind more often. Even though it’s eight hundred against one.

“As we explained the other day, that was due to the poor management of the Kingdom of Eldia. Now that our country will be providing support, good news should come one after another.”

“Even if that were so, what reason would there be for our nation, which has suffered damage at the hands of the heroes, to support heroes who currently have no achievements?”

At that point, Prince Luan of the Kingdom of Estea also raised his hand.

“Our Kingdom of Estea has the same reason. We have no intention of aiding heroes who inflicted great damage upon our nation and never atoned for it. At the very least, they must perform well enough to inspire confidence in defeating the Demon King. Is there any basis for that?”

Prince Luan, nice follow-up!

With nations harmed by heroes saying this, is there any good way to respond?

“There are plenty of achievements. The achievements accumulated by past heroes.”

Calling that a basis is a stretch.

“That cannot be called a basis. The achievements of past heroes belong to them. They cannot possibly serve as grounds to trust the current heroes.”

“Past heroes and current heroes are the same. They are all heroes chosen by the goddess. They will surely slay the Demon King. Or are you saying you do not believe in the goddess?”

Linforce showed absolute trust in the goddess.

“I do not believe.”

“…What did you say?”

Linforce’s tone dropped.

The royalty of each nation flinched at the change. They probably want to avoid a repeat of yesterday.

“Earlier, you said ‘the management of the Kingdom of Eldia was bad’, did you not?”

“And what of it?”

Linforce didn’t seem to understand what Sakuya was getting at.

In fact, Linforce had already made a major slip of the tongue.

“Who was it that issued the divine revelation to summon heroes to the Kingdom of Eldia in the first place? You are acknowledging the goddess’s mistake yourself.”

“…Th-that is!?”

Linforce’s expression stiffened as if she had only just realized it.

“You yourself are doubting the goddess’s absolute infallibility, are you not?”

“N-no! I am not doubting the goddess!”

A flustered Linforce denied it.

“There is no need to be upset. Believing is a virtue, but not doubting is negligence. It is only natural for a diligent person like you to question the goddess.”

“I said that is not the case!!!”

Linforce raised her voice, and several participants wet themselves.

The burst of anger was brief, so no one fainted, but it was far from a safe situation.

Still, no one said anything. Among so many royals, it would be hard to admit you lost control of your bladder. With consciousness intact, the humiliation must be immense.

“Hah, hah, hah…”

“It seems Lady Linforce lacks the basis necessary to convince us.”

“It is unfortunate. If you are able to present a basis, please speak to us again then. We do not wish to abandon our duties as residents of this world.”

As Linforce panted, Sakuya murmured, and Prince Luan nodded.

“Indeed. Depending on the good news, we may raise our hand as a hero-supporting nation even midway.”

Yes. It wrapped up neatly.

If heroes do their job properly, neither Castal nor Estea are unwilling to pay money. They just don’t want to pay someone who doesn’t work.

However, there was something Sakuya likely omitted intentionally.

One of those points is that “the nations harboring heroes themselves are not trustworthy”. The Kingdom of Eldia, the Elgant Theocracy… so far, neither is trustworthy, right? Nations you don’t feel like paying money to, right?

It’s like wanting to donate as a volunteer, but not trusting the organization collecting the donations. Does it really all get delivered?

“…I understand the positions of the Castal Kingdom and the Kingdom of Estea. I believe we will be able to deliver good news soon, so please consider becoming hero-supporting nations at that time.”

Linforce concluded while glaring resentfully at the two, having regained her composure.

She restored her expression, then turned to the queen of the Regalia Beastman Nation, Sharon.

“May I ask why the Regalia Beastman Nation will not become a hero-supporting nation?”

“The reason Regalia will not become a hero-supporting nation is similar to Castor and Estea.”

Prompted by Linforce, Sharon spoke.

Sharon is the queen of the Regalia Beastman Nation, but she is a girl around the same age as us.

She is a white tiger beastman, with white hair flowing straight down to her waist. Her skin is similarly pale, making her appear sickly at first glance.

However, there is no way the king of a beastman nation could be sickly, and in reality, she possesses considerable combat power.

“Is it because there are no achievements?”

Linforce asked, slightly displeased, but Sharon shook her head.

“Achievements are irrelevant. What matters is whether there is strength. Choose one hero and have them fight me seriously. If the hero demonstrates strength, we will support them. If not, we will not.”

Sharon said these dangerous words calmly, without inflection or visible emotion.

As expected of the king of a beastman nation. Simple, muscle-brained logic. I don’t dislike it.

Beastman king versus hero. That could be an interesting matchup.

…The beastman hero versus the Sword Emperor ended rather poorly, after all.

“Will you use mock weapons or magic tools for the match?”

“No. Such toys cannot measure true strength. Besides, I fight unarmed, so mock magic tools cannot be used.”

When Linforce asked whether they would use mock weapons that do not deal damage, Sharon shook her head.

“In that case, we cannot permit the match. It is not worth risking injury or death. Either outcome would be a loss. It benefits neither side.”

It’s only natural, but Sharon’s proposal was rejected by Linforce.

“If you wish, there will be no need to worry about injury.”

“…You knew? We have instructed that it not be spread much outside our borders…”

At Sharon’s seemingly unconnected remark, Linforce realized the meaning and asked cautiously.

Ah, so this is what they’re talking about.

\<Divine Domain Protection>

The skill holder, and those designated by the holder, do not take damage from external factors within the Divine Capital. Conditions can be set individually.

It’s one of those unique skills that grant invincibility under specific conditions.

It’s widely known within the Divine Capital, but generally outsiders are instructed not to be told.

“I did a little research. An opportunity to fight heroes is rare. I cannot let it pass.”

“Could it be that this was your purpose in attending this conference?”

Filling in the outer moat and realizing a serious battle with heroes.

I thought she was just muscle-brained, but she’s thinking more than expected… though her objective is still muscle-brained.

“That is the second purpose.”

“May I ask what the first purpose is?”

“I cannot say. More importantly, will you grant permission for the match?”

It seems Sharon has yet another purpose.

Alta, do you have any idea?

A: None. Sharon truly speaks only the bare minimum, so even guessing is difficult.

Unfortunately, even Alta really doesn’t know what Sharon’s primary purpose is.

Linforce thought for a moment, then sighed and granted permission for the mock battle.

“Very well. We wish to increase the number of hero-supporting nations even slightly, and we will consider this a good opportunity to show everyone the heroes’ power. However, we cannot force heroes who do not wish to fight to do so. Please understand that.”

“Of course. I have no hobby of tormenting those who do not wish to fight.”

Oh, a proper battle-crazed line came out.

My favorability toward her increased by one.

“Then, are there any heroes who would be willing to spar with Lady Sharon? For reference, Lady Sharon is said to be the strongest in the Regalia Beastman Nation. It is also said she surpasses S-rank adventurers.”

Linforce cautioned them not to challenge her lightly.

Basically, don’t be fooled by her sickly appearance.

However, Linforce’s warning was a little too effective.

Hearing she surpasses S-rank adventurers, many of the heroes shrank back.

Even Linforce looked a bit flustered (though at a glance she’s expressionless).

She said she would show the heroes’ strength, but instead they were hesitating to fight a girl. It’s understandable she’d be flustered.

At that moment, one girl stepped forward.

“If no one else volunteers, then, with all due humility, I, Shichihouin Kannagi, would like to face Lady Sharon.”

“Mm. Good.”

Seeing the girl who volunteered, Shichihouin Kannagi, Sharon nodded in satisfaction.

Even without seeing skills or stats, the strong can recognize the strong.

If we’re talking purely base parameters, she’s probably the strongest among the heroes. If you factor in the massive amount of blessings absorbed, Kino Aichi might surpass her, though.

“Lady Shichihouin, are you truly sure? There is no need to force yourself.”

“Lady Linforce, thank you for your concern. Lady Sharon is strong, correct?”

“Yes. Very much so.”

She probably ranks around the top fifteen in this room.

“Opportunities to cross hands with someone like that are rare. If my strength is acknowledged, it will also lend prestige to me as a hero. For the sake of the future, I would very much like to face her.”

“Good courage. I can feel a strong will. I would very much like her to fight.”

With clear mutual consent confirmed, Linforce guided the participants to the venue for the mock battle.

In this situation, there was no option not to watch the heroes fight, and all participants headed for the training grounds.

Ah, one correction. All participants who were physically present headed for the training grounds.

Naturally, those attending via the “Paired Farseeing Mirrors” were left behind in the conference room.

Through the mirrors, you could clearly see them lamenting not being able to witness this famous match.

**AN:** Too many conference interruptions problem.

Next time, the story finally moves a bit. From this flow!?
