## **138: The Noble Lady Hero and the Girl Beast King**

**AN:** This chapter is just watching a duel that does not involve the protagonist.

The protagonist is basically air this chapter.

---

At the center of the divine capital Elgare, in the Holy Cathedral of Elgant Theocracy, the world’s largest religious nation.

Inside it, in the training grounds where temple knights normally trained, key figures from neighboring countries had gathered on this day.

Naturally, it was to witness the battle between the “Hero” Kamuna Shippouin and the “Beast King” Sharon.

“Time is unlimited. There are no restrictions on weapons or magic. The match will end the moment even a single effective hit lands. Effective hits will be nullified, so please attack without holding back. Conversely, attacks that are not considered effective will go through as-is, so please keep that in mind.”

“No problem.”

“I feel the same.”

Sharon and Shippouin answered Linforce’s explanation.

As for the matter of damage nullification by \<Divine Domain’s Protection>, it seemed they could not explain it in detail, so they glossed it over as the effect of a magical tool.

When something is hard to explain, blaming a magical tool really is convenient.

《Sera-chan. Share your vision with me!》

《Of course. That’s fine.》

Sera, who like me had come to the training grounds, accepted Mio’s plea.

Currently, only those who had been in the conference room were permitted to enter the training grounds.

Those waiting in the antechambers were not allowed in. Naturally, they could not see any footage either. Magical tools like broadcast televisions were large and difficult to move.

Thus, members waiting outside who were curious about the mock battle asked members inside the training grounds, including Sera, to share their vision.

Linforce finished her explanation, and Shippouin and Sharon prepared for battle.

As Sharon had said in the conference hall, she carried no weapon and was completely bare-handed, but she did wear some light armor. Both her clothes and armor were white.

Just because she’s a white tiger, does she really need to be dressed entirely in white? White tigers have black parts too…

Opposing her, Shippouin wore a school uniform. Perhaps because for a normal high school student, a uniform is the most appropriate attire for an official occasion? Kino was also wearing a uniform, but the other Heroes wore whatever they liked.

No, looking closer, the details seem different from a normal uniform…

A: I compared it to Sakura’s uniform, and it does not appear to be from their original world. It seems to be clothing made in imitation of a uniform in this world. It uses natural fibers, not synthetic ones.

Why go out of the way to make clothes resembling a uniform?

I changed into this world’s clothes quickly because I did not want my uniform getting tattered, so I never thought of recreating one.

Well, I doubt I will ever have a chance to ask, so whatever.

Shippouin’s weapon was a naginata.

She gave it a light practice swing, and the movement was astonishingly refined.

That is not something you achieve in a month or two. She likely had prior training in her original world. Proof of that is her astonishing \<Swordsmanship> and \<Spear Techniques>, both at level 5.

Seeing the naginata Shippouin wielded, Sharon could not help but smile.

Prompted by Linforce, the two faced each other at the center of the training grounds.

We watched the battle from the edge of the field.

Temple knights stood in front of the key figures from each nation, guarding against stray attacks. They were fully armed with shields and rendered invincible by \<Divine Domain’s Protection>.

“Then, we will begin the match. Are both of you ready?”

“Yes.”

“Yeah.”

“Then, begin!”

At Linforce’s signal, the match began.

“I’ll take the first strike.”

Sharon moved first, instantly closing the distance with Shippouin.

If she entered her range before the naginata could swing, the match would be decided immediately.

A blitz is one of the simplest tactics, and when it works, it is extremely powerful.

“It won’t be that easy.”

However, Shippouin seemed to have anticipated the blitz and lightly backstepped to create distance.

“Oh! Just a light jump, and she moved that far!?”

One of the key figures from a Hero-supporting nation muttered in admiration.

Shippouin had moved a full ten meters with a simple backstep.

“Is that your Blessing?”

With the blitz failing and distance reopened, Sharon stopped and asked.

From Sharon’s perspective, Shippouin’s movement should have been invisible, so she likely assumed the unnatural motion was due to a Blessing.

“Yes. It is called \<Noble Gravity>. Calling it ‘noble’ myself is a bit embarrassing, though. It took quite some effort to master, but once you do, it is an extremely powerful Blessing.”

As Shippouin said, her Blessing is exceptionally powerful.

\<Noble Gravity>

Generates gravity spheres within a one-meter radius around the user’s body. Up to three gravity spheres can be generated.

Simply put, it is a skill that manipulates gravity.

Across all ages and settings, gravity users are always strong characters.

Come to think of it, gravity actually refers to the sum of Earth’s gravitational pull and centrifugal force, so calling someone a “gravity user” is technically inaccurate, or so my best friend Azuma once said. Who cares.

During the backstep, she generated a gravity sphere behind her back. In other words, she backstepped while being pulled backward.

Since gravity spheres can be freely moved within their one-meter radius, if used well, you can jump considerable distances.

“This time, I will go on the offensive.”

Shippouin said so and generated a gravity sphere in front of herself, lightly jumping forward.

Just like before, she moved at an impossible speed and distance by normal physical laws.

“Hah!”

She closed in at high speed and swung her naginata, but Sharon lightly pulled back, attempting to evade with minimal movement.

“…Hm?”

At that moment, Shippouin generated a gravity sphere at the extreme edge of her range.

As a result, Sharon’s body was pulled slightly toward it, and at the same time, Shippouin’s naginata was also drawn in. In other words, weapon and enemy were forcibly brought together.

Realizing this, Sharon kicked off the ground hard and escaped.

That was close. If the gravity had been just a bit stronger, or if the sphere had been placed just a bit more precisely, the match might have been decided.

“…I thought that would land.”

Shippouin said regretfully after missing.

“Your timing was off. Perhaps you haven’t fully mastered it yet?”

“Yes, embarrassingly so. I cannot say I have fully mastered it yet. It takes a great deal of concentration.”

Although the Blessing description says she can control up to three gravity spheres, so far she has only used one. She is not holding back or saving a trump card, but is likely just at her limit with one.

“If mastered, it is an extremely powerful ability. The fact that you can still grow stronger means there is no need to be discouraged.”

“Yes. I believe the same, and I will not spare the effort required.”

So there really are Heroes with proper drive.

I just never happened to meet them before…

“Indeed, you are good. Let’s end the warm-up. I’m not even using gauntlets, though.”

Sharon declared she was getting serious, slipping in a strange joke.

What? Is that the kind of character she is?

“Hah!”

“So fast!?”

Sharon kicked off the ground and closed in on Shippouin faster than before.

Shippouin attempted the same long-distance backstep, but Sharon closed the gap faster than the gravity-assisted movement allowed.

Shippouin conserves stamina by relying on gravity spheres, but without a physical ability boost, she is slower than a full sprint by a true powerhouse.

“Gah!”

Shippouin slashed at Sharon.

Since she was backstepping, the strike lacked power, but since even one effective hit would win, that was enough.

-Kiin!-

Sharon caught the slash with her arm. The sound that rang out was a sharp metallic clash.

“Why!?”

Shippouin cried out in shock, but this was not mysterious at all.

It was Sharon’s skill, \<Hard Fist Technique LV6>.

\<Hard Fist Technique>

Temporarily hardens the fists and forearms to be as hard as metal.

Shippouin’s naginata is fine quality, but a powerless slash during a backstep is far from an effective hit.

After stopping the attack with her left arm, Sharon thrust her right fist toward Shippouin.

“Gah!?”

Shippouin twisted her body to evade, but the blow grazed her shoulder, tearing her clothes slightly.

Apparently, it was not judged an effective hit, as Linforce said nothing.

Cornered, Shippouin took a surprising action.

“Hah!”

She jumped straight up before a follow-up could come.

Naturally, with a gravity sphere pulling her upward.

“You can fly?”

“Strictly speaking, I am not flying. I am simply hanging in the air. It feels shameful, like running away, but I could think of no other option in that moment.”

Shippouin was currently suspended about ten meters above the ground.

So gravity spheres can be used like that.

Incidentally, for whatever force is at work, Shippouin’s skirt revealed absolutely nothing. Damn gravity user.

“Withdrawing to win is not running away. You have not given up yet. Correct?”

“Of course. I cannot give up when the match is not yet decided. For the sake of my purpose, I cannot show such a disgraceful display.”

She is fighting as the representative of the Heroes. She cannot afford to look pathetic.

“But I still cannot envision a path to victory. Even if this position is safe, I cannot stay here thinking forever…”

“That concern is unnecessary. This is not a safe zone. …‘Flying Swallow.’”

Sharon said this and thrust toward the airborne Shippouin.

Immediately after, a fist-shaped shockwave flew forth.

“Huh?”

Shippouin let out a dumbfounded sound for a split second, but quickly realized what was happening and blocked the incoming shockwave with her naginata.

-Bashii!-

“Ugh!”

“This is my trump card. The flying fist strike, ‘Flying Swallow.’ Though I am a white tiger, you know.”

The impact was stronger than expected, and Shippouin was blown back significantly.

And once again, Sharon slipped in a strange joke. The Flying Swallow was another of Sharon’s skills.

\<Flying Fist Technique>

Allows shockwaves to be launched through punches. Range and power depend on the level of this skill and the \<Martial Arts> skill.

Basically the fist version of my \<Flying Sword Technique>.

That said, Sharon really has a well-rounded set of martial-arts-related support skills.

“I’m not done yet.”

Sharon fired another \<Flying Fist Technique>. Only one, though. She could have spammed it…

A: With \<Flying Fist Technique LV2>, continuous firing is not feasible.

Ah, I see. Then it cannot be helped.

“Again!? Gah!”

-Bashii!-

Shippouin blocked again with her naginata and was blown back.

Since she is using gravity spheres to pull herself upward while airborne, she cannot move quickly.

“At this rate, I will be worn down…”

Shippouin showed signs of impatience.

Descending would create an opening, so she could not choose it easily. She had no option but to keep blocking in midair.

At this rate, it was only a matter of time before she was chipped away.

“Shall you give up soon? No one would laugh at you.”

After several shots, Sharon suggested this.

“Even if I lose, I will never give up!”

“Good resolve. Then I will finish this. ‘Flying Swallow!’”

Of course, Sharon probably never thought she would truly surrender.

She nodded with satisfaction.

Then she unleashed another punch.

A larger \<Flying Fist Technique> than before flew forth.

Deflecting these with a naginata must be hard on the arms. Shippouin’s arms trembled visibly, lacking strength. At this rate, she would not be able to block it.

“Now!!!”

Shippouin shouted, glaring at the incoming shockwave.

-Whump-

“As I thought, our compatibility was poor.”

Sharon muttered regretfully.

Indeed, Sharon’s \<Flying Fist Technique> was absorbed by a gravity sphere that appeared beside Shippouin, never reaching her.

It seems Shippouin managed to control a second gravity sphere at this critical moment.

“Hah… hah…”

The second gravity sphere vanished almost immediately, but even that brief simultaneous control left Shippouin gasping heavily. As she said, it requires tremendous concentration.

Still, deflecting \<Flying Fist Technique> with gravity spheres is fascinating. My \<Flying Sword Technique> might work the same way. Truly interesting.

As Sharon said, in terms of pure compatibility, \<Noble Gravity> has the edge over \<Flying Fist Technique>.

“This is rough… but I feel like I grasped something.”

“This is troublesome. But if it weren’t, it would not be interesting.”

Despite knowing it would be deflected, Sharon fired another \<Flying Fist Technique>.

Shippouin deflected it again with a gravity sphere.

Sharon knows the attack will not land, but also knows it is a burden.

They repeated this several times.

Little by little, it felt like Shippouin was adapting. Her breathing was steadying, and the duration of the gravity spheres was increasing.

“So? Getting used to it? It’s about time you came at me.”

“So you saw right through me. Understood. I will go.”

Responding to Sharon, Shippouin manipulated the gravity sphere and flew toward her.

“‘Flying Swallow.’”

“Hah!”

-Bashu!-

Sharon fired \<Flying Fist Technique> at the approaching Shippouin, but Shippouin deflected it with her naginata. It seems she recovered while blocking with gravity spheres.

“Then I’ll punch you directly.”

“It will not go as before!”

Shippouin’s naginata clashed with Sharon’s hardened fist, ringing with a sharp metallic sound.

Shippouin only has one weapon, so only one method of attack, while Sharon has both hands and both feet, effectively triple the options.

She blocked the naginata with one arm and tried to strike Shippouin with the other.

However, Shippouin evaded with lateral movement using a gravity sphere.

Sharon followed with a kick, but this time a gravity sphere at her feet disrupted her balance, halting the kick.

“Guh…”

“Now!”

Seizing the opening, Shippouin swung her naginata horizontally.

Sharon abandoned offense and hardened both arms, crossing them to block.

By shifting her center of gravity backward, Sharon reduced the impact and leapt back.

“‘Flying Swallow.’”

Creating distance, she used \<Flying Fist Technique> as a feint to prevent pursuit.

Since she was not airborne, Shippouin avoided it with footwork alone, but the chance to follow up was lost.

Their close-quarters battle continued for a while after that.

In raw specs, Sharon far surpasses Shippouin, but Shippouin uses her Blessing skillfully to close the gap.

Simultaneously controlling two gravity spheres is difficult, so she uses one constantly and saves the other for critical moments.

Still, her tactical options clearly expanded, allowing her to keep up in close combat. Growing stronger mid-battle… are you the protagonist or what?

Sharon, for her part, skillfully uses \<Hard Fist Technique> and \<Flying Fist Technique> to counter Shippouin’s tactics.

…In truth, if Sharon were serious, defeating Shippouin would not be difficult.

She is not holding back, but rather limiting the skills she uses.

Sharon possesses multiple powerful unique-class skills. Using even one would allow her to defeat Shippouin instantly. However, she stubbornly refuses to use them.

Likely because those skills are ill-suited for gauging another’s ability. She does not seem the type to use instant-kill or overkill skills in a duel meant to test strength.

Thanks to that, we get to watch an exciting match, so I have no complaints.

Even an enjoyable, intense battle must eventually end.

Is it because this is an unlimited-time match that ends only when one side loses?

No. That is not the reason.

“Hey, what is that?”

One of the key figures from another country looked up at the sky and pointed.

There was a black dragon, with a man riding atop it.

“Enemy attack!?”

Hearing that, Shippouin and Sharon immediately stopped fighting.

“You guys are having fun. Let me join in.”

The man shouted loudly and leapt off the black dragon he was riding.

The dragon was flying over twenty meters high, but the man showed no hesitation.

“Jumping from that height!? Is he trying to die!?”

-Dooon!!!-

With a thunderous crash far beyond the sound of a single human falling, the man landed in the training grounds.

The grim future one dignitary imagined did not occur. The man stood there calmly.

He was a large man in his thirties, with blazing red hair and jet-black armor.

His eyes were sharp like a feral beast’s, exuding the presence of a king.

“Sorry, but I’m cutting in. Come on, girls. Entertain me.”

He beckoned provocatively to Shippouin and Sharon.

“Such overwhelming fighting spirit. I don’t know who he is, but representatives of all nations are present. We cannot leave an intruder unchecked.”

“Indeed. His aura is ominous. We have no choice but to restrain him. Fortunately, both Sharon and I are still capable of fighting.”

“Enough talk. Just come at me already. That long flight really built up my stress. Come on, show me a good time.”

Not because they rose to his provocation, but the two rushed to capture him.

“Hah!”

Sharon, superior in burst speed, closed in and punched toward his abdomen.

The height difference probably made aiming for his face difficult.

“Good punch, but still too slow.”

“What!?”

The man casually caught Sharon’s fist in his palm.

“For now, take this.”

He then thrust toward Sharon’s exposed abdomen.

Sharon tried to block with her hardened arm, but…

-Bash!-

“Ow!”

She was easily deflected and punched square in the gut.

A dull thud echoed as Sharon collapsed. \<Divine Domain’s Protection> was completely useless.

“Why!?”

Linforce screamed in shock.

Perhaps because she had absolute faith in \<Divine Domain’s Protection>.

“Lady Sharon!?”

Shippouin cried out in shock, but did not stop advancing.

“Then how about this!”

Shippouin unleashed a full-power slash, also using gravity spheres to disrupt his posture.

However, the gravity spheres had no effect on the man at all.

“Sorry. I can stop that too.”

Shippouin’s all-out slash was caught between two of the man’s fingers.

…That was cool. I should practice that later.

Shippouin tried desperately to pull back or push through, but it did not budge.

“Interesting, but not enough. Go to sleep for now.”

“Ugh…”

The man swiftly struck Shippouin’s chin, knocking her unconscious.

The representatives of each nation could say nothing as the man instantly defeated the two who had fought so brilliantly, nullifying even those whose effective hits should have been invalidated, all while exuding a malevolent aura.

“Lady Linforce! Should we not restrain him?”

Sakuya, one of the few remaining calm, asked Linforce.

“R-right. Temple knights! Capture that man!”

Linforce’s voice held none of her usual composure.

She stared at the intruder as if gazing upon something terrifying.

“Yes!” x10

The temple knights charged, but the man raised his hands in surrender.

The knights stopped, looking confused.

“Sorry, sorry. Guess I scared you too much. Relax, I’ve got no intention of harming you. I just saw an interesting real fight while stressed out and couldn’t resist jumping in.”

“Honestly, you never outgrow that childish side of yours.”

Saying that, a woman in her mid-twenties descended lightly beside him.

She wore a black dress, with black eyes and black hair. Her facial features were clearly not Japanese. In fact, she was not Japanese at all.

You can probably guess, but I will explain anyway.

This woman was the black dragon from earlier. Or more precisely, “the human form of the black dragon-type dragonkin from earlier.”

“Come on. A man who forgets his inner child is like a withered tree. I’ve got no intention of becoming that pathetic. You’d hate it if I became boring too, right?”

The man asked her defensively.

“I wouldn’t go that far, but at your age, I do think you could show a bit more restraint.”

“Haha, hearing ‘age-appropriate composure’ hurts… Well, I’ll try…”

“That sounds like the usual ‘won’t actually try’ pattern…”

The temple knights were left dumbfounded by the casual exchange.

The man then turned back to them.

“Oops, sorry again. I should explain before this goes nowhere…”

“Y-yes! Who are you, and what are you doing here!? This is a summit of the world’s key figures! The ones you defeated were a Hero and the Queen of the Regalia Beastman Nation! Are you a terrorist!?”

Linforce’s first impression of a “calm adult woman” was nowhere to be found.

Though hidden by her long robe, Linforce’s legs were trembling violently.

To add, also hidden by her skirt, she had wet herself quite a bit.

“Terrorist is a harsh word. Though… a Hero and a Queen, huh. Guess I’ll have to apologize and compensate later.”

“If you are not a terrorist, then who are you!? State your name at once!”

Linforce’s voice continued to tremble.

Is she really that afraid of him? She was completely unfazed when I defeated Eldia nearby. What could she be afraid of?

A: Perhaps because \<Divine Domain’s Protection> was nullified? In other words, this may be Linforce’s first experience of a ‘threat to her life’.

Ah, that makes sense.

If you act assuming invincibility, someone who threatens that would be terrifying. Well, given this man’s nature, that is only natural.

…Still, even if she did not know, it feels a bit late to realize that now.

The man, asked again to state his name, drew the greatsword at his waist and stabbed it into the ground as he answered.

“Clean out your ears and listen well! The emperor of the mighty Crimson Empire, whose name resounds across the land, that’s me. Scarlet Crimson!”

Yes. This man was the Emperor of the Crimson Empire, Scarlet Crimson.

Since I never went to the Crimson Empire, the Crimson Empire came to me!

**AN:** Scarlet finally makes his appearance.

His existence was hinted at back in Chapter 53, when Rouge appeared, meaning he stayed off-stage for 85 chapters.

Might have dragged it out a bit too long.

## **139: The Emperor of the Crimson Empire and the Tragedy**

**AN:** Previous Chapter Summary:

A playful emperor appears. The two people named in the previous chapter title are unconscious.

---

“W-wait, you say you are the Emperor of the Crimson Empire!? W-why are you appearing at this leaders conference!?”

“Yeah. We weren’t invited to this one, so I figured it was rude, but I came to participate anyway. Had a little business to take care of.”

Scarlet answered Linforce’s question casually, but what he said was more than enough to send chills through most of those present.

In the first place, the reason the Crimson Empire had not been invited to this leaders conference was simply because it was too far away to be considered a neighboring country of the Elgant Theocracy, and because it had not become a Hero Support Nation back when Eldia possessed a Hero.

What business could it possibly have with a leaders conference now?

“Can you prove that you are truly the Emperor of the Crimson Empire!? You were not invited, so you surely do not possess an invitation either!”

“Hard to say if this counts as proof, but I do have the sealed letter from when Eldia previously sought Hero Support Nations. Addressed, of course, to Scarlet Crimson.”

“…Bring it here.”

Linforce’s attendant received the letter from Scarlet and brought it back.

“While you’re at it, take those girls who collapsed too. Leaving them lying on bare ground is pitiful, don’t you think?”

Coming from the one who knocked them out, that’s some nerve. Quite bold of you.

“…Temple Knights, escort Lady Shippouin and Lady Sharon to the infirmary.”

“Yes!” x4

The Temple Knights ordered by Linforce carried Shippouin and Sharon out of the training grounds.

As for the letter, a woman who looked to be Linforce’s secretary checked its contents and seemed to determine that it was genuine.

“…It appears to be authentic.”

“I see… However, that alone does not constitute proof!”

“Yeah, I know. When I say I’m participating in the conference, I don’t mean sitting at a desk in the meeting room and debating. I’m just here to present the Crimson Empire’s position. You can send an official written response to the Crimson Empire later. There’s no way to do identity verification here anyway.”

Given that identity verification was impossible to begin with, Scarlet’s apparent goal was simply to be allowed to make a proposal during the conference.

Linforce questioned Scarlet cautiously.

“What does the Crimson Empire desire?”

“Ah, the Crimson Empire… wishes to become a Hero Supporting Nation.”

A shocking statement at this stage.

I knew Scarlet was heading toward the Divine Capital Elgale riding a dragonkin, but I didn’t know his objective.

For the record, I realized this just before yesterday’s conference was interrupted, thanks to a report from Alta.

“When the Kingdom of Eldia previously sought Hero Support Nations, the Crimson Empire refused. We would like to hear your reason for now applying to become one.”

“It’s nothing complicated. The situation just changed.”

“That is not an explanation.”

I agree with Linforce.

At the very least, I want to know what the situation changed from, and into what.

“We considered whether we could defeat the Demon King without relying on an otherworldly ‘Hero’, but it seems impossible, so we figured we’d support the Hero and have them finish it quickly.”

“Y-you were considering such an outrageous thing!?”

“Yeah. In the end, we realized it wasn’t just impossible. It was meaningless.”

That’s an interesting choice of words.

Not ‘impossible’, but ‘meaningless’…

“I believe that matters of this world should be settled by the people of this world. Summoning a Hero from another world strikes me as the height of relying on others.”

“Are you insulting the Goddess’ Divine Revelation!?”

Is losing composure whenever the Goddess is mocked a traditional performing art of the Goddess Faith?

Perhaps because she had no margin left, Linforce no longer even tried to maintain appearances like she did when dealing with Zenon.

“Isn’t that Goddess mocking us by saying the people of this world can’t defeat the Demon King? That’s what pissed me off, so I searched for my own way to defeat him.”

“If the Goddess judged it impossible, then it is beyond human capability!”

“…Yeah. Seems that way. According to ancient texts, the Demon King takes almost no damage from attacks that aren’t from a Hero. Without breaking that, there’s nothing you can do.”

Unfortunately, the Demon King seems to possess a skill similar to \<Calamity Star>.

Oh, \<Calamity Star> is the curse mark that the Tyrannosaurus had.

\<Calamity Star>

Reduces damage from attacks by those without the ‘Hero’ title by 99%.

Multiplies damage from attacks by those with the ‘Hero’ title by 10.

If defeated by a Hero, grants ten times the experience.

How do I know?

Remember when we went to those ruins in Eldia the other day?

Apparently, the Hero’s journal lined up in the final chamber described the Demon King.

It said that warriors of equal strength using comparable weapons attacked him, yet the effect differed drastically between the Hero and their companions. In the Hero’s case, the Demon King took far more damage than expected. That was one of the deciding factors.

No other skill fits that description besides \<Calamity Star>. I can’t say it’s exactly the same, but there’s no doubt it has a similar effect.

“As for the Hero, what’s done is done. The Hero seems motivated to defeat the Demon King. In that case, I figured it was best for everyone if we support them and have the Demon King dealt with quickly.”

But that’s probably not the only reason, right?

You seem to be doing quite a bit behind the scenes…

“…I understand what you’re saying. I’m surprised you attempted to defeat the Demon King on your own, but the latter half of your logic makes sense. In any case, if you are willing to become a Hero Supporting Nation, we have no objection.”

“Glad to hear it. Makes the long trip worthwhile.”

It was quite a long flight.

Black Dragon dragonkin aren’t exactly known for their top speed…

“However! We lodge a formal protest regarding your knocking Lady Shippouin and Lady Sharon unconscious, and there are many other matters we wish to ask. We cannot permit you to participate in the conference, so at best, you will be allowed to observe from a waiting room. Can you accept that?”

Linforce drove in a wedge just as things were settling.

“Yeah, I get it. Got a little carried away. I’ll answer what I can. Still, this isn’t something to discuss standing around here, is it?”

“Indeed. Since matters have reached a temporary conclusion, we will suspend the conference for now and continue later. Scarlet-sama, we would like to hear from you in a separate room.”

Come to think of it, despite how chaotic things are, Zenon, who usually stirs things up, seems oddly quiet.

When I check on him… he’s pale blue.

Perfectly pale blue, trembling, his gaze never leaving Scarlet. Clearly, Scarlet is the object of his fear.

…Scarlet Crimson, feared by Linforce who led the conference, and by Zenon who disrupted it.

Scarlet Crimson, who instantly defeated Shippouin and Sharon after their high-level battle.

If asked who the protagonist of this place is right now, there is no answer other than Scarlet Crimson.

After that, everyone except Scarlet returned to the waiting room.

Scarlet’s appearance threw the conference into chaos, so this was essentially a reset.

Scarlet himself is currently in a room of the Grand Cathedral, being questioned by Elgant Theocracy officials. They must have countless things they want to ask.

However, Linforce, the head of the Elgant Theocracy, seems utterly terrified of Scarlet and has not approached him at all since leaving the training grounds.

That Linforce is currently in the middle of changing out of wet underwear.

In the waiting room, Sakuya and the ministers are talking, so I’m chatting with the same group off to the side as before.

Incidentally, Maria and Rico are discussing security with the guard maids. For some reason, Sera is not participating in that discussion.

“Just like I thought, things took a very interesting turn.”

I expected Scarlet’s appearance to cause some trouble, but it was even more entertaining than I imagined.

“It’s a complete mess. How do you even clean this up?”

“That’s for the Elgant Theocracy to worry about. They’re the hosts.”

Mio says this with exasperation, and I answer.

“Is this even something thinking can fix?”

“No idea.”

Even if it can’t be fixed, the Elgant Theocracy is the only one that will suffer losses, so it doesn’t concern us.

“Even without the Crimson Empire Emperor issue, there are countless potential troubles… I can’t even imagine which will happen…”

“If nothing else, a monster stampede is guaranteed.”

《Lots of monsters-》

Just as Sera says, a stampede is a disaster that’s certain to occur.

Why does a stampede happen?

Actually, the assassin we defeated the other day, the monster tamer, had a Stampede Devil whose skill had a special effect.

The Stampede Devil’s skill, \<Howl of Madness>, not only causes artificial stampedes, but also triggers a stampede unconsciously upon death.

In other words, a death scream.

No one could possibly know about such an ability of such an ultra-rare monster.

That’s why people recklessly tame Stampede Devils and even use them for assassinations.

Using that power within one’s own country is far too risky.

Safely handling it would have required stealing the \<Howl of Madness> skill before killing it, but there was no way I felt like doing that.

Why should I go out of my way to make killing an assassin easier for the country that sent them? And since they were an assassin, not killing them was never an option.

Currently, monsters in a berserk state are gradually gathering in the forest near Elgale.

Eventually, they’ll erupt and attack a nearby city. (Almost certainly) Elgale.

“That’s what the Temple Knights are for, right? They should at least handle a stampede.”

“Master, generally speaking, stampedes are not something that can be dealt with so easily. If things go poorly, one or two cities can be wiped out.”

Sera is lecturing me on common sense.

Sometimes I feel like there’s a gap between my sense of normalcy and the world’s, but it’s probably just my imagination.

“Temple Knights can’t win?”

“I doubt the elite knights of the Divine Capital would lose, but there will be significant damage. Depending on the monsters gathered, the worst case is possible.”

“Huh.”

She explained it, but honestly, I’m not that interested.

“My, Master, you’ve completely lost interest in the Elgant Theocracy.”

“Given how we’ve been treated here, it’s understandable…”

Just as Mio and Sakura say, I’m fed up with how this country treats us and have already lost interest.

There are many seeds of trouble, but I don’t feel like preemptively plucking them, nor do I intend to suffer their consequences.

We dismantle even temporary housing every time we move because it might be damaged.

“Still, the leaders conference itself is entertaining. The various intentions of these colorful characters mix together, and it never gets boring.”

I’m not interested in the Elgant Theocracy itself, but the leaders conference as a gathering of dangerous individuals is another matter. If they’re dangerous, that means they’re at least interesting.

“That makes it sound like you’re welcoming trouble.”

“That’s exactly right. Is there a problem with that? A tourist spot that’s not fun and not interesting leaves you with nothing to do but enjoy the trouble.”

“Right… you always said trouble was part of sightseeing…”

Let me correct one thing about Mio’s exasperated tone.

“Except unpleasant noble-related trouble.” so…

“What I’m most excited about is Scarlet joining in. He’s on a completely different level from the other participants, and I can’t predict how things will turn.”

The others’ goals are mostly clear, but Scarlet is the exception.

I’m really looking forward to it.

“We ended up meeting the Crimson Empire Emperor before even going there…”

“Exactly! That’s the point! I’ve never really felt like going to the Crimson Empire before, but now I think this timing is perfect! Because there’s no map spoilers!”

It’s only natural to overreact to Sakura’s comment.

With a map, you can see what the other side is doing, which kills surprise.

Scarlet’s actions are unpredictable precisely because we haven’t visited the Crimson Empire or gathered information.

Maybe I couldn’t bring myself to go there until now for this very moment.

If there’s some massive secret scheme, enjoying it without prior knowledge is its own kind of fun.

As long as we aren’t harmed, I won’t interfere beforehand, so feel free to relax.

“Jin-kun, you’re unusually excited…”

“Probably the only one in the conference happy about Scarlet joining is Master.”

“Indeed…”

I told you that once you get used to maps, you lose your sense of surprise, right?

That’s exactly why the unexpected things that come along once in a while are something you have to cherish.

I probably won’t get much understanding for that, so I won’t say it out loud.

An hour later, the leaders conference, entangled with various agendas, resumed.

With the resumption, we gathered in the conference room again.

However, the lineup had changed slightly due to the Scarlet incident.

First, Sharon, Queen of the Regalia Beastman Nation, who was knocked unconscious earlier, was absent. She hadn’t recovered yet, so a proxy attended.

Similarly, Shippouin was also absent, still unconscious. Kino Aichi was present, but the other Hero was gone. Apparently, he fled in fear of Scarlet.

A Hero discussion with only one Hero left. What a mess.

Scarlet himself was observing the conference via television from the waiting room.

As he said, he doesn’t intend to interfere.

The one most relieved by this is Linforce.

Linforce maintains a stern expression from the Scarlet incident.

Few realize she’s simply trembling in fear.

Because of that fear, the number of Temple Knights guarding her had doubled.

Incidentally, Linforce changed her underwear. Yes, completely irrelevant.

Zenon seemed to have regained his composure and entered the conference room with a fearless smile.

The two attendants who had been guarding him were gone, and he sat alone in the Granz Kingdom’s seat.

“With all participants present, let us resume the conference.”

Linforce’s declaration resumes the meeting, but many representatives fidget uneasily. Scarlet left deep scars.

“First, we will address the matter of Scarlet Crimson of the Crimson Empire.”

“Was he truly the Emperor of the Crimson Empire?”

“Yes. Upon confirmation, we determined that he is almost certainly Scarlet Crimson, Emperor of the Crimson Empire.”

Linforce answers the questions.

“His purpose was to participate in the conference. He arrived by the fastest means available, which is why he had no attendants.”

“Was that dragon his means of travel? And that woman who appeared later…?”

“It’s difficult to believe, but the dragon and the woman are the same individual, capable of changing form.”

-Murmurs-

The conference room erupts.

Old news to us, but shocking to the general public.

“Does that mean the woman is a monster?”

“Yes. According to him, she is a tamed monster. However, she possesses intelligence comparable to a human. The staff reported no difference from conversing with a normal human. She transformed before our eyes, so there is no doubt they are the same individual.”

“Hard to believe…”

“I’ve never heard of such a thing.”

Linforce is telling the truth, but the participants remain skeptical.

“She is likely a dragonkin.”

With a single statement, Queen Sakuya draws all attention.

“Sakuya-sama, do you know her?”

“I do not know her personally, but based on Linforce-dono’s account, no other race fits.”

The reason dragonkin existence wasn’t public was to avoid trouble.

Scarlet forced it into the open, so hiding it now is pointless.

Better to provide accurate information.

Incidentally, after confirming with the chief of the Dragonkin Sanctuary, the woman who appeared with Scarlet seems to be a dragonkin who went missing four years ago during a battle with a dragon that attacked the sanctuary.

Her true name is Yoiyami. She appears to have amnesia.

“Treat her as you would a normal human. However, like a dragon, she can use specialized magic, so recklessness is ill-advised.”

“You’re quite knowledgeable. Could it be that the Dragon Knights of the Castal Kingdom…”

“Unrelated.”

Linforce was close.

I’m the only one with a dragon mount, so the Dragon Knights have nothing to do with dragonkin.

“This is a highly important matter. We would like further information…”

“I will not elaborate here. It is completely outside the scope of this conference.”

“Then after the conference, could you stay and…”

“I refuse that as well.”

“Do you understand the gravity of this!? An undiscovered race unknown even to the Goddess!”

Linforce raises her voice in frustration at Sakuya’s unyielding stance.

So the Goddess left no records of dragonkin.

And that’s a problem for Linforce…

“That is your concern, Linforce-dono. It is of little importance to me, and I have no intention of remaining in Elgale beyond this conference. If you have business, send a messenger while we are outside the city. Though messengers from the Theocracy would likely be turned away at the gate as usual.”

“Th-that is…”

Linforce is at a loss for words.

Sakuya is plainly saying she won’t accept envoys due to the prior assassination attempts. Not even implied. Explicit.

Linforce may not have ordered them directly, but the responsibility is undeniable.

“If you insist, send an official envoy after the conference, once I have returned home.”

“…Understood. We will send an envoy after the conference concludes.”

“Very well.”

Sakuya is quite firm.

Given the circumstances, she’s probably nervous inside.

Linforce clears her throat and resets.

“One more note regarding Scarlet-sama. He is currently observing the conference from another room. He does not possess speaking rights, so please proceed with that understanding.”

“One question.”

The one who raised her hand was a beastwoman representing Regalia, Sharon’s proxy.

She looked every bit the secretary type. A sheep beastwoman. Sheep, not a butler.

“What is it?”

“What will be done regarding our Queen Sharon being knocked unconscious? Our nation cannot simply let that pass.”

“We have received a response. Scarlet-sama will formally apologize and provide compensation. A formal reply will be issued separately. Would you be willing to wait?”

So Scarlet really is going to apologize.

Given how bold his personality is, I thought he’d just brush it off.

“Understood. If they are sincere, we will refrain from pursuing it here. As for our participation as a Hero Supporting Nation…”

“That will be decided once Sharon-sama awakens?”

Because Scarlet joined the fray before things were settled, the agreement that was supposed to be decided by Sharon and Shippouin’s fight over becoming a Hero Support Nation was left hanging.

Naturally, you would think it would be decided after the person in question woke up, but…

“No. Sharon would not refuse someone she fought so fiercely. You may proceed assuming our participation.”

“Is it acceptable to decide without her consent?”

“Yes. I have been granted authority for such decisions…”

Linforce nods at the sheep secretary.

“Very well. We will proceed accordingly.”

Linforce then turns to Zenon.

“It has been some time, but why does the Granz Kingdom refuse to become a Hero Supporting Nation? May we hear your reason?”

Come to think of it, we heard the reasons from the Castal Kingdom (Estea Kingdom) and the Regalia Beastman Nation, but we never heard Granz Kingdom’s.

“Very well. I shall answer.”

Zenon speaks.

“To me, demons and other nations are all enemies to be defeated. Why should I support one enemy to defeat another? It is nothing but waste.”

That single statement was enough to turn every other nation’s representative present into an enemy.

It was not something that could be brushed off as one of his usual bad jokes, but something that demanded serious consideration of war.

“Is that statement serious…? Even as a joke, it is excessive.”

Linforce is radiating killing intent.

“I do not joke about such things. I will now show you proof!”

《Jin-sama! An attack is coming! Red… spears!》

Zenon shouts, and at the same moment, Rico sends an emergency telepathic message.

At that moment, the maid knights stationed throughout Castal, Estea, and Sanokia draw their swords and step forward to protect the non-combatants.

“My blood, dance! \<Creeping Bloodstain>!”

Zenon slashes his own abdomen with the dagger he holds.

Ritualistic suicide. Harakiri.

“Guuh!”

Blood gushes forth.

But it does not fall. It floats in the air.

“Kill them all!”

Spitting blood, Zenon shouts again.

The blood stretches like spears and attacks the participants.

“W-what is this!? Aaaah!!?”

“Stop! Stay away!”

“Goddess! Save me!”

The conference room becomes a hellscape.

Those pierced by \<blood spears> wither instantly, drained of blood.

There are only five spears initially.

After impaling those nearby, they prioritize those fleeing.

Participants are slaughtered one after another.

《Brother!? What do we do!?》

《We discussed this. It’s not a major attack. Focus on defense. We owe the others nothing.》

I respond to Sakuya’s telepathy.

I have neither the obligation nor the energy to help anyone outside Castal, Estea, and Sanokia.

I had already made that clear to Sakuya beforehand, and she did not try to force the issue.

《I-I understand… but it’s pretty scary. This is kind of a traumatic sight…》

Sakuya, who has been impaled before, breaks into a cold sweat.

She looks like a composed queen trusting her subordinates.

Hm?… Before I knew it, the number of “blood spears” has increased to over ten?

Ah, right. Because of \<Creeping Bloodstain>, he can treat the blood he absorbs as his own.

A: Yes. It’s the effect of \<Creeping Bloodstain>.

\<Creeping Bloodstain>

The user can manipulate their own blood and use it like a weapon. If they injure others with blood weapons, they can absorb that blood. The user is strengthened depending on the quality of the blood absorbed.

So that means the longer this drags on, the more troublesome it gets.

But controlling more than ten “blood spears” sounds like a lot of work…

A: It has an auto-control function.

…Boring. That’s exactly the kind of thing that should be manual control.

“Why!? Why won’t my blessing activate!?”

The one screaming that is Linforce, surrounded by a flesh wall of Temple Knights.

It seems she’s trying to grant to those around her, but it’s having no effect at all.

With her trump card nullified, she’s panicking beyond reason.

The Temple Knights are pierced one after another by the “blood spears,” losing their lives.

Some Temple Knights even charge Zenon bravely, but they collapse to the ground before their blades can reach him.

While I was watching Linforce and the others, a “blood spear” stretched toward me.

Just as I drew my sword to wipe out the “blood spears,” the figure of a girl stepped in front of me…

“…Guh!?”

Right before my eyes, the girl, Kino Aichi, is pierced through by a “blood spear.”

…Did she try to protect me? But why…?

Even Kino’s desperate defense is in vain, and the “blood spear” keeps aiming at me, its momentum only slightly reduced.

“Hey!”

I slash the “blood spear” and blow it away.

As I do, I catch Kino’s body as it’s thrown aside. It looks like her heart was pierced, so it was almost an instant death. Even so, her expression almost looks satisfied.

I collect the huge \<Blessing Remnant> that appeared there, and I also store Kino’s body in \<Infinite Storage>.

Throwing her life away to protect me is not normal.

There has to be some reason. And that reason might be connected to that yellowish red marker.

Honestly, I’m really curious, so leaving it alone isn’t an option.

“Why!? Why!?”

As Temple Knights are killed one after another and Linforce is reduced to nothing but screaming, Zenon walks up to her.

“I will personally teach you why your immortality blessing will not reach you.”

“Hii!?”

Linforce collapses, and she wets herself.

She just changed her underwear, too…

“Linforce-dono’s immortality blessing can only be granted to those who are within Elgale.”

He takes one step closer to Linforce. A Temple Knight swings at him, but is struck down in return.

“Then what defines Elgale? Its territory? Its people? No! The region protected by Elgale’s ‘Barrier Stone’ is Elgale itself!”

He takes one step closer to Linforce. The Temple Knights guarding her are stabbed to death one after another.

“Even now, my subordinates are likely destroying this city’s ‘Barrier Stone.’ Therefore, this is Elgale and yet not Elgale! Therefore, you cannot grant blessings here!”

He takes one step closer to Linforce. At last, every Temple Knight protecting her has been wiped out.

“This is the end. Become my nourishment.”

“Hiiiiiiiii!!?? No! No! No! No! Goddess! Goddess! Goddess! Goddess! Goooooddesss aaahhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhh!!!!!!!!”

-Zashu!-

“Ah, ah…”

The “blood spear” pierces Linforce, takes her life, and sucks her blood dry.

“Kuahahahaha! So this is the taste of a High Elf! Delicious, delicious! With this, I have become the strongest! Now no one can stop me!”

Sorry to ruin your excitement, Zenon, but Linforce isn’t dead yet.

More precisely, she did die once, but she still has lives left, so she hasn’t died for good.

All right, here’s Linforce’s status.

Name: Ann (Alias: Linforce May Elgant)

LV300

Gender: Female

Age: 1803

Race: High Elf

Skills:

Magic

\<Light Magic LV10> \<Recovery Magic LV10>

Techniques

\<Command LV10>

Body

\<MP Auto-Recovery LV10>

Other

\<Ageless LV > \<Divine Domain’s Blessing LV > \<Lethal Regeneration LV1>

Title: Pope of the Elgant Theocracy

\<Lethal Regeneration LV1>

Upon death, revive at the cost of one skill level.

Side Story

_Behind-the-scenes notes._

– The Pope

In Side Story Chapter 7, “The Oracle Maiden”, the Pope of the Elgant Theocracy was depicted as a middle-aged man, but at present, Linforce reigns as Pope.

However, Linforce is not Christopher’s successor.

Originally, Linforce was the first Pope of the Elgant Theocracy.

She relinquished the papacy long ago and had been living a semi-retired life, but following Christopher’s death, she was dragged back onto the public stage. In other words, this is not a succession, but a restoration.

It should also be noted that only elves may hold the positions of Pope and Oracle Maiden.

“The Elgant Theocracy Arc” or “The Elgant Theocracy Collapse Arc”…

My writing stock is running low due to slow output.

I want to avoid reducing update frequency, but the worst may happen.

Politics and international affairs really slow me down.

## **140: Escape and the Destroyer of the Divine Capital**

**AN:** Writing went unusually smoothly over Golden Week.

I managed to make up for some of the delay, so it looks like I can keep the ten-day update schedule for a while.

Going out during Golden Week? Hah hah hah.

---

Linforce possesses a skill called \<Lethal Regeneration>, which allows her to revive even after dying.

However, there is a time lag before revival, so it still means being removed from the battlefield.

Linforce has been killed, and nearly all of the representatives of the various nations who were nearby have also perished.

The only ones still conscious are the inner circles of the Kingdom of Castal, the Kingdom of Estea, and the Kingdom of Sanokia, along with the members of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

The other nations appear to have had lower-quality guards and were unable to block Zenon’s “Blood Spears.”

The Regalia Beastman Kingdom, including their maids, all survived. They do not seem completely unharmed, but at least everyone is intact. Impressive.

“Hmph… I thought I had slaughtered them all, but there were survivors after all. You are a lucky lot.”

Zenon, who had stabbed Linforce to death, looks our way and furrows his brow in displeasure.

It’s not luck! It’s skill!

Because the “Blood Spears” were on automatic control, it seems he failed to fully grasp our true strength.

“Still, I am in a good mood right now. In consideration of your luck, I shall spare you for the moment.”

Zenon suddenly wears a fearless grin.

“I will now destroy this Grand Cathedral… the symbol of the Goddess Faith’s authority. You may despair and share the cathedral’s fate!”

Saying that, he extends the “Blood Spears” and begins indiscriminately destroying the surrounding walls and pillars.

If he were aiming at us it would be one thing, but when he targets the surroundings, blocking everything becomes difficult. The “Blood Spears”, which had increased to around a hundred after absorbing Linforce’s blood, tear through the cathedral one after another.

He is also destroying the ceiling, so chunks of rubble rain down relentlessly, which is rather annoying.

After wrecking the area to a certain extent, Zenon starts moving the “Blood Spears” like legs and walks like a spider. Frankly, it’s disgusting.

Spreading destruction as he goes, Zenon leaves the conference room… no, the remains of the conference room.

If this continues, it’s only a matter of time before the Grand Cathedral is completely destroyed.

The conference room itself won’t hold much longer either…

“I am worried about Queen Sharon. Everyone, if you are unharmed, let us head to Queen Sharon at once!”

“Yes!” x many

Timing it so that Zenon had moved away, the sheep secretary from the Regalia Beastman Kingdom spoke, and the guards and maids nodded.

They then took a different route from Zenon’s path and headed toward Sharon.

Seeing the Regalia Beastman Kingdom’s response, Finance Minister Rudolf, who had been standing there in a daze, came back to his senses.

“Queen Sakuya, we should begin evacuation as well! At this rate, we will be caught in the collapse of the cathedral!”

“Indeed. Now that the conference has ended in such a manner, there is no reason for us to remain here.”

As Sakuya and the others were talking, Prince Luan of Estea approached them.

“May we accompany you? I am ashamed to say that with only our own guards, it seems unlikely we can survive this situation.”

“That is fine. What will Sanokia do?”

“If you would allow it, we would also like to accompany you.”

Ekaterina answers Sakuya’s question while glancing in my direction.

It seems she cares more about my response than Sakuya’s. I have no choice, so I quietly nod.

“Then it is decided. Let us withdraw at once…”

“W-wait…”

The one who stopped Sakuya was one of the fallen temple knights.

It seems he was pierced by a “Blood Spear.” There is a hole in his abdomen and he is dried out, but he appears to still be alive.

He somehow props up his upper body, but he likely does not have long to live (I have no intention of healing him).

“What is it? We are in a hurry as it is.”

“I-I know that… but I have a request… P-please, would you move Lady Linforce’s body to a safe place…?”

Looking closely, this knight seems to be an elf.

Could it be that he knows Linforce’s secret?

That might be why he is begging us to move Linforce, who will revive, to a safe location. If Linforce revives under rubble, she would just die again…

“Are you a fool? In this situation, how could we possibly take on extra baggage?”

“I-I understand… I am not asking for free… ‘Storage.’”

The temple knight chants the magic \<Storage> and pulls out something like a large backpack.

“As compensation, I will give you this item box… This item box was made using a special method and can store corpses… Please put Lady Linforce’s body inside and transport it to a safe place… Once you have finished transporting it, the item box is yours to do with as you please…”

The item box the temple knight offered was indeed designed to hold a corpse.

It was likely prepared to secure Linforce’s body in the event of her death.

Considering that, this temple knight must have been close to being Linforce’s personal attendant.

《Sakuya, accept his offer.》

《Is that alright?》

《Yes. He has offered a suitably interesting compensation. Grant him that much.》

I have no interest in the fate of the Elgant Theocracy, but if they are offering an interesting magical item as compensation, that is another matter.

Besides, granting this request does not seem to harm us in any way.

“Hm. If you insist that much, I shall hear your request.”

“Th-thank you…”

Having said that, the temple knight breathed his last.

We promptly placed Linforce’s body (temporary) into the item box as per the knight’s request.

Although we lost a bit of time, we left the conference room and began our escape from the Grand Cathedral.

Choosing corridors with minimal damage, we advanced while protecting non-combatants from falling rubble.

During the evacuation, we joined up with the waiting-room groups from Castal, Estea, and Sanokia.

Of course, we had already confirmed routes via telepathy beforehand, so this was the fastest possible rendezvous. It goes without saying that the maids subtly guided them.

“Queen Sakuya, thank goodness you are safe!”

“Talk later. We must leave this place quickly!”

“Yes!”

The emotional reunion ended swiftly, and our now large group aimed to escape the Grand Cathedral.

However, just as we were nearing the exit, we encountered a place where rubble had completely blocked the path.

“Hmph, we are so close!”

Sakuya glares irritably at the rubble.

“Gene, can you do it?”

I nod and ready my fist.

-BAM!-

With a single straight punch, the pile of rubble before us is blown away…

“Gehyu!?”

A priest who was standing in the line of fire is hit squarely as intended and sent flying off somewhere along with it.

As you can probably guess, this priest is the one who repeatedly sent assassins after us.

He was trying to flee ahead of everyone else, so I took advantage of the chaos to eliminate him.

After all the harassment he put us through, of course I would kill him if given the chance, right?

“Good, let us go!”

“Just now, something…”

“Good, let us go!”

“Ah, yes…”

Prince Luan’s mutter was glossed over by Sakuya, who knew the circumstances.

And thus, we arrived at the Grand Cathedral’s entrance relatively safely.

Escaping the cathedral safely is good, but reality is such that we cannot relax just yet.

Because the outside of the cathedral is by no means safe either.

“W-what… is that…?”

“M-monsters…”

Those who are not my subordinates, such as Finance Minister Rudolf and Prince Luan, mutter in shock.

In their line of sight, a battle was unfolding between two monsters and a single hero.

“GRYAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA!!!!!”

“BRYUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUU!!!!!”

In a word, the two monsters look like oni. Specifically, the evil demons from Japanese folktales.

They are about five meters tall. Their skin colors are an unhealthy green and yellow, respectively. Each is wrapped in wind and lightning and freely flies through the sky.

Their names are “Wind God Tornado” and “Thunder God Lightning.”

Yes, that’s right. They are the two Final Trials!

The two Final Trials unleash gales and lightning toward the hero below.

“I don’t know what you’re saying!!! Take this!!!”

With a single swing of the greatsword in his hands, the hero dispels both the gale and the lightning.

“Now it’s my turn!”

Saying that, the hero takes a running start and leaps.

Using buildings already half-collapsed from the battle’s aftereffects as footholds, he executes a triangular jump and unleashes a slash at Thunder God Lightning.

Lightning tries to evade but cannot avoid it completely, and the attack grazes his shoulder.

“GYAAAAAAAAAA!!!???”

Letting out a scream far too loud for a mere graze, Thunder God Lightning flees straight up into the sky.

Scarlet kicks off another building and this time lands a slash on Wind God Tornado.

“BYAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA!!!???”

That slash severs Wind God Tornado’s left arm, and with a scream even louder than Lightning’s, he too flees into the sky.

“Tch, fighting like this is a pain in the ass!”

The hero curses irritably while glaring at the sky.

The hero fighting on equal or superior footing against the two Final Trials.

His name is Scarlet Crimson.

The damage from the battle between the two Final Trials and Scarlet is severe, and the cityscape of Elgare has fallen into a pitiful state.

Buildings collapse under the violent winds, and fires erupt everywhere due to lightning strikes.

Since the battle has started, I might as well check the statuses of the monsters and the hero again.

Name: Wind God Tornado

LV 200

Skills: \<Wind God LV10> \<Transformation LV10> \<Complete Resistance LV >

Title: Demon King’s Familiar

Notes: An oni god who manipulates wind. One of the Final Trials imposed upon humanity.

\<Wind God>

A skill exclusive to Wind God. Allows manipulation of wind.

Name: Thunder God Lightning

LV 200

Skills: \<Thunder God LV10> \<Transformation LV10> \<Complete Resistance LV >

Title: Demon King’s Familiar

Notes: An oni god who manipulates lightning. One of the Final Trials imposed upon humanity.

\<Thunder God>

A skill exclusive to Thunder God. Allows manipulation of lightning.

No matter how many times I look at it, that skill setup is pretty underwhelming. Their levels are also the lowest among the Final Trials.

For Final Trials, being merely the Demon King’s familiars feels off… Or rather, so Final Trials can be tamed, huh. I never even considered doing that.

By the way, these two are the subordinates Zenon mentioned who destroyed the “Barrier Stones.”

More precisely, Zenon has borrowed the two Final Trials, who are Demon King familiars. Yes, the Demon King and Zenon are working together!

Their goals are likely the annihilation of the Heroes, the destruction of the troublesome theocracy, and Zenon’s own strengthening as a bonus.

After all, Final Trials have resistance against Hero attacks, right? The compatibility is good.

One more thing. The two attendants who were with Zenon were actually Wind God and Thunder God transformed into humans using the \<Transformation> skill.

So it was obvious from the start that the conference would be a mess.

I had been careful about the guards in case they rampaged in the conference room, but in the end it turned out they were a separate unit, making that preparation pointless.

I know this because I saw it on the map, but after destroying Elgare’s “Barrier Stones”, the two Final Trials began wrecking the city.

That’s when the hero, Scarlet Crimson, appeared.

Scarlet blocks their attacks while repeatedly landing effective blows on them. Each time, the two flee into the sky.

Even Scarlet can’t engage in aerial combat with just his own body. He could just ride a dragonkin though…

Now then, here is Scarlet Crimson’s status.

Name: Scarlet Crimson

LV 231

Gender: Male

Age: 34

Race: Human (Reincarnator)

Skills:

Martial Arts

\<Swordsmanship LV10> \<Martial Arts LV9>

Magic

\<Fire Magic LV4> \<Healing Magic LV2>

Techniques

\<Manners LV2> \<Monster Taming LV5> \<Horsemanship LV5> \<Restraint LV5>

Physical

\<Physical Enhancement LV10> \<Leap LV5> \<Search LV7> \<Fighting Spirit LV7> \<HP Auto Recovery LV6> \<Toughness LV3> \<Immovable LV4> \<Presence Detection LV7> \<Poison Resistance LV5> \<Heavenly Eye LV >

Other

\<Hero’s Proof LV8> \<Hostile Magic Nullification LV > \<Transcendence LV10> \<Soul Ascension LV1>

Titles: Transcendent One, Emperor of the Crimson Empire

There are too many things to comment on, so I will list only three particularly important points.

First: his race is Human (Reincarnator).

Second: he possesses the combination of \<Hero’s Proof> and \<Hostile Magic Nullification>.

Third: he holds the title “Transcendent One.”

The first point needs no explanation. He is a reincarnator.

As for details, they are unknown unless we hear them directly from him, so I will skip that.

The second point is that, like Sera, he has \<Hero’s Proof> and \<Hostile Magic Nullification>.

That is why I keep calling him a hero.

The reason he could erase Wind God and Thunder God’s attacks, why Shichihouin’s gravity sphere had no effect, and why \<Divine Domain’s Blessing> was nullified is because of this skill.

…Come to think of it, Tsukiyo mentioned it before. When Scarlet killed the golden foxes who were the parents of Tokoyo, “apparently all attacks were repelled.” Golden fox attacks are basically magic, right? Of course they would be repelled…

The third point is that he is a “Transcendent One.”

In other words, Scarlet has defeated Final Trials before. If his opponents are lower-ranked Final Trials level-wise, it would not be impossible for him to fight them advantageously.

Additionally, the weapon he wields is also a factor.

That weapon is this.

Royal Sword: Divine Curse

Category: Greatsword

Rarity: Phantasmal Class

Notes: Final Trial slayer. Deals damage to the wielder on attack. Recovers a fixed amount when dealing damage to others. Self-repairing.

Astonishingly, Scarlet Crimson owns equipment specialized against Final Trials.

The reason Thunder God screamed so dramatically from a mere graze earlier is because of that special-effect weapon.

To be honest, it’s rare to find someone this interesting.

Before meeting him, my impression was quite bad due to his thoughts of war with Estea and the fact that he killed Tokoyo’s parents, but seeing him in person, I never expected him to be this interesting.

Originally, I planned to let the two Final Trials rampage for a bit and then have Sakura and Dora kill them to grant them the “Transcendent One” title.

However, I have no intention of stealing someone else’s prey, and if Scarlet ends up defeating them, then so be it.

Since Scarlet already has “Transcendent One”, it feels a bit wasteful, but…

At that moment, Scarlet noticed us and came over.

“Hm? You guys are the representatives from Castal, Estea, and Sanokia, right? What are you doing here? What happened to the conference?”

“That is our line. What are those monsters?”

Sakuya responds to Scarlet’s question with a question of her own.

The traces of the battle between Wind God, Thunder God, and Scarlet spread throughout the city. In other words, Scarlet being near the Grand Cathedral was just coincidence.

That makes things easier to explain.

“Oh, those? Simply put, enemies of humanity. Divine Curse reacted right after the conference started, so I felt bad about it, but I ditched the waiting room to prioritize dealing with them.”

So Royal Sword Divine Curse also has a Final Trial detection function. Wonderful. Search!

“So then, why did you come out of the Grand Cathedral… Was the cathedral always this run-down?”

Only now does Scarlet notice the cathedral’s state and make a dubious face.

Zenon is in the middle of destroying it, so it is currently collapsing as we speak.

“Shortly after the conference began, Zenon of the Kingdom of Grants went mad. He killed the representatives present in the conference room and is destroying the Grand Cathedral. Among those in the conference room, only us and the people of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom survived.”

“Seriously…? You guys had your own mess to deal with too. But hey, if you’re the famed Queen’s Knight Gene of Castal, couldn’t you have subdued that mad Zenon and prevented the damage?”

Scarlet fixes me with a sharp glare.

Well, if you ask whether I could have, I think I could. But just because you can doesn’t mean you have to.

“Are you telling my knight to abandon my protection to save others? People from other nations with whom we have not even built good relations?”

“Ah… got it. So you never intended to protect them from the start. On the flip side, that means the people here are ones you did have good relations with. Makes sense.”

Scarlet seems to have grasped the general situation from that alone.

“By the way, do you know what the Heroes are doing right now?”

“Hm? Oh, the Heroes… Those monsters destroyed the building where the Heroes lived first. Most of the Heroes inside were rendered combat-incapable. I managed to rush in before they were finished off, but yeah, there’s no way they can handle those things… in more ways than one.”

Sakuya already knows this, but she is having Scarlet disclose information that cannot be made public through him.

As mentioned earlier, one of the goals of the Final Trials and Zenon is the annihilation of the Heroes.

There is nothing strange about them targeting the Heroes immediately after destroying the “Barrier Stones.”

Incidentally, one reason the “Barrier Stones” were destroyed so easily is that Linforce increased the number of temple knights in the Grand Cathedral for her own protection, reducing the number guarding the “Barrier Stones.”

For the same reason, there are also not enough temple knights to quell the chaos in the city. It’s adding insult to injury.

Thus, civilians who are still safe must escape the city on their own.

Furthermore, outside the city, preparations for a stampede are complete, and with the “Barrier Stones” gone, ordinary monsters are approaching as well. Truly a case of wolves at both the front and back gates.

“If the Heroes are unreliable, then this city, this country, may truly be finished… It would be wise to escape sooner rather than later.”

“So, in other words, you have no intention of calming this chaos?”

Scarlet looks at Sakuya, then me, as if appraising us.

“At present, no. At the very least, leaving the city and securing safety takes priority. More importantly, what about you? The fact that you are fighting those monsters suggests you want to protect this country, this city?”

“My goal is to kill those two. I don’t care about the country itself. The enemy is bad enough, but the fact that the Heroes are even more useless than I expected is a problem. I need to revise my plans, or this will get ugly…”

Although he said he would become a Hero-supporting nation, it seems the Heroes are even worse than Scarlet anticipated.

“Then is it acceptable for us to leave those two to you?”

“Yeah, leave them to me… is what I’d like to say, but they’re a bit troublesome. Look.”

Scarlet points at the two Final Trials in the sky.

“They run away into the air the moment things turn even slightly against them. And their recovery seems high. That arm I chopped off earlier will probably regenerate soon.”

Indeed, Wind God’s left arm seems to be regenerating.

Thunder God is fully recovered but does not approach alone. He’s scared of Scarlet.

“I don’t think I’ll lose, but at this rate I’ll never finish them off. It’s a stalemate. If possible, I want you to lend me a hand so I can go all out.”

“If you want aerial combat, why not ride the black dragonkin?”

“Ah… That one apparently has trauma with aerial combat, so she’s useless in a fight… Wait, dragonkin? So as expected, you do know something about her?”

“That was also mentioned in the conference earlier… No, you did not see the state of the conference room then. But more importantly, what do you mean by ‘as expected’?”

Scarlet’s remarks often contain words that pique my curiosity.

“One of my reasons for attending the conference was to get clues about an amnesiac dragon girl. Since Castal formed a Dragon Knight Corps, I figured you might know something.”

“Hm. So your purpose from the start was to make contact with us.”

Scarlet nods to Sakuya’s question.

“Yeah. I’d like to hear the details if possible, but…”

“That will be impossible in this situation. And as I said in the conference, I have no intention of explaining at leisure in this country. If you wish to hear, go through official channels.”

“Can’t be helped. Just knowing there are leads is a big gain.”

Oh my, Scarlet, you’re surprisingly reasonable.

That just makes it harder to understand why he targets Estea or skirmishes with neighboring countries.

“Tch, looks like they’re about to fully recover. Those monsters will probably start moving again soon. If you’re evacuating, do it quickly. And once you’re done, I’d appreciate the help.”

“I will think about it.”

“You won’t commit, huh… At least hurry, if you can.”

“I will think about it.”

And with that, we parted ways with Scarlet and boarded the carriages that had barely survived, escaping the Divine Capital Elgare. We passed through the gates without issue.

Incidentally, the carriages survived thanks to Tamo-san and the others protecting them.

Sanokia’s carriage was not under protection, so it didn’t make it.

“Queen Sakuya is more courageous than I expected…”

“What do you mean?”

Inside the carriage, which was a bit more crowded to accommodate Sanokia’s members, Finance Minister Rudolf mutters.

This carriage holds Finance Minister Rudolf, Prince Luan, and Ekaterina. Apparently, since I am here, it is the safest.

“Well, you faced Lord Scarlet without batting an eye.”

“Indeed. His oppressive presence was like needles on the skin even from a distance. I tried to join the conversation a few times, but my legs wouldn’t move.”

“I am ashamed to say I felt the same.”

It seems Finance Minister Rudolf and Prince Luan were overwhelmed by Scarlet’s oppressive aura.

If a non-combatant is exposed directly to a warrior’s fighting spirit on a battlefield, it would be unbearable.

Me? I keep that sort of thing suppressed, so I’m fine. I’m kind to the weak.

“That level was nothing.”

“As expected.”

“As one who will rule a nation someday, I would like to learn from you.”

For Sakuya, that level of pressure was apparently insignificant.

Seeing her calm demeanor, Finance Minister Rudolf and Prince Luan praise her.

《Compared to big brother’s pressure, it was like a gentle breeze! At least it wasn’t enough to make you wet yourself just from telepathic pressure!》

Hey, I don’t know what to do with you shouting that at full force over telepathy…

The carriage we rode left Elgare through the gate where monster rampages were not occurring and traveled for about thirty minutes.

At this distance, we are unlikely to encounter danger anytime soon.

The maids are currently rebuilding the temporary housing at super speed.

It looks like the fastest time record will be updated.

In ten minutes (new fastest time), rows of temporary housing were completed, and it was decided that non-combatants and key figures would wait there under the protection of maid knights. Key figures do not equal non-combatants, since Ekaterina can fight to some extent.

Combatants, or rather my main party plus Rico, are gathered in a separate temporary housing unit.

“Alright, Sakuya and the others are safe. After checking a few things, let’s head out to subjugate the Final Trials.”

“Master, what do you need to check?”

“Mio, didn’t you see it? When Zenon went on a rampage in the conference room, one of the Heroes died trying to protect me. And it was that Hero, Kino Aichi.”

When I ask, Mio shakes her head.

“Sorry, I didn’t see it. The cameras in the conference room were apparently destroyed soon after Zenon started rampaging, so we only have map-based information.”

“Yes. I really wanted to rush to Jin-sama’s side when the cameras broke, but there were many guards, so I held back.”

“Maria-chan’s tail was swaying restlessly, wasn’t it?”

Apparently, Maria was fidgeting in the waiting room when Zenon rampaged.

“I’m glad I didn’t see that scene, personally…”

《Dora wanted to see it!》

Sakura, who has low tolerance for gore, seems relieved that the cameras broke.

And Dora. It’s bad for your education, so you shouldn’t watch! …Though maybe it’s too late for that?

“I see. I hadn’t even considered the cameras, but they were destroyed, huh. Anyway, I’m curious why the Hero tried to protect me, so I’m thinking of reviving her and asking.”

Previously, Sakura created a magic called “Ankh” that can revive the dead.

If too much time passes after death, memories are lost, but Kino’s body was retrieved immediately into \<Infinite Storage>, so there should be no problem.

“If it works out, I might even give Kino the credit for subjugating the Final Trials. We need a public hero, after all.”

“Master, you say things so casually, but you’re talking about something pretty outrageous, you know?”

“Sera-chan, when it comes to Master, that’s par for the course.”

Hearing my plan, Sera gives a wry smile.

I think it’s a necessary plan. I have no intention of becoming the hero of the Elgant Theocracy…

“Oh, right. There’s one more thing I just remembered.”

“Is something wrong…?”

《What is it?》

I turn to Sakura and Dora and continue.

“I hate to say this, but depending on how things go, the finishing blow on the Final Trials might go to Scarlet. That means the \<Transcendence> skill might have to wait for another opportunity.”

Given the situation, it seems difficult to properly hand the killing blow to the two of them.

“Um… It’s not really something I want that badly anyway…”

《It’s fine, don’t worry!》

Yeah, neither of them seems to care at all.

Wanting to distribute the \<Transcendence> skill to everyone is really just my own selfishness. The two of them don’t seem to place that much importance on it.

“…Alright. Then I’ll go do the revivals.”

“We’ll wait here in case others arrive!”

“Thanks.”

“Yes!”

And so, we enter the “Room” set up in the temporary housing and attempt to revive the Hero.

Everyone except Rico accompanies me inside the Room.

Here, let me explain the resurrection magic “Ankh.”

“Ankh” has multiple levels, and depending on the level, the state of resurrection changes.

At the lowest level, it is like \<Necromancy>, a moving corpse. Next is a living doll with only the body revived. Then a talking doll with knowledge restored. Finally, it can restore the ego and consciousness.

This time, I want information, so I plan to stop at the “talking doll” stage. In this state, it is also easy to apply \<Slave Magic>, which is convenient in many ways.

I can overwrite it later, so full resurrection is possible if needed.

“This is my first time reviving a Hero.”

“So far, there hasn’t been a single Hero we wanted to revive…”

“Ankh” has been strengthened several times by Sakura. At first, it could not revive ability-users or Heroes, but now it can.

Additionally, upon revival, all skills except Blessings are fully reproduced.

Blessings have different acquisition conditions, so that’s only natural.

That said, as Sakura said, until now there hasn’t been a single Hero we wanted to revive…

Speaking of Heroes, what happened to the other Hero in the Grand Cathedral, Shichihouin?

Queen Sharon was apparently being protected by the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, but did someone take Shichihouin as well?

A: Shichihouin Kannagi was caught in the collapse of the Grand Cathedral and died. The Tamo deployed within the cathedral have already recovered her along with her Blessings. The members of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom evacuated safely.

Ah, so no one went to protect Shichihouin.

“…Reviving one or reviving two makes no difference.”

“Master, what’s wrong?”

Mio asks, picking up on my mutter.

“Well, it seems the Hero named Shichihouin who was in the conference room died in the cathedral collapse.”

“Oh my, that’s unfortunate. Well, she was unconscious, so it can’t be helped…”

“So I’m thinking of reviving Shichihouin as well while I’m reviving Kino. Her mock battle with Queen Sharon was quite good, so this can be her reward.”

She seems to be a central figure among the Heroes, so having her take on the role of hero might be good.

“You’re always kind to those who catch your interest, aren’t you?”

“Only when it’s positive interest and the person is decent. If it’s negative interest, like Zenon, I have no intention of being kind.”

Kind because I’m interested.

Crush them because I’m interested.

Rough handling because I’m not interested.

In most cases, my actions fall into one of these categories.
