Behind the Scenes

*Stories and tidbits behind the main story.

– Wind God and Thunder God

When Wind God and Thunder God are together, they can change the surrounding weather to violent storms and lightning.

Normally, their basic tactic is to change the weather to create advantageous conditions and then annihilate their opponent.

However, just having Scarlet within the effective range causes it to be canceled by \<Hostile Magic Nullification>, so they were forced to attack with minor gusts and lightning.

To begin with, almost all of Wind God’s and Thunder God’s attack methods are treated as magic, so they had no effective means of attack against Scarlet from the start. Defeat was inevitable.

Their abilities are inferior versions of the Yellow Dragon. Their opponent completely nullifies magic, so they have no chance to shine. Their level is the lowest among the Final Trials. At the time of their appearance, they are already tamed by the Demon King (meaning they have already lost once).

They are pitiful Final Trials. That is Wind God and Thunder God.

---

Scarlet’s settings were mostly finalized quite some time ago (such as the battle with the Golden Fox).

Also, originally, the plan was not to use “Ankh” in the main story, but it became absolutely necessary to have a death-and-revival process once, so “Ankh” was used reluctantly.

Shichihouin: “About the fact that I died because I was unconscious and got crushed by rubble.”

Scarlet: “Honestly, I’m sorry.”

## **141: The Hero’s Resurrection and the Believers**

**AN:** Kino Aichi appeared in Volume 6 and Side Story Episode 8.

One of the themes of this chapter is the entry of side-story characters into the main story.

Kudo-kun and Mizuhara-san do not appear directly, though. …I wonder what Kudo-kun is doing now? Is he alive?

---

“Ankh.”

I cast the spell “Ankh” on Kino, who was laid out on the bed.

By using the \<Chantless Casting> skill together with \<Expanded Interpretation>, I was now able to use even Sakura-created \<Unique Magic> without chanting.

Apparently, \<Unique Magic> is treated as LV10-or-higher magic, so when combined with \<Chantless Casting> (which increases MP consumption based on magic level), the amount of MP required became absolutely ridiculous.

This is bad.

“Once more, Ankh.”

This time, I cast “Ankh” on Shippouin, who was laid down next to Kino.

Since the first cast consumed far more mana than expected, I used an “Ankh” that had been stocked in \<Infinite Storage> this time.

The maids had actually prepared a stock of “Ankh” spells in advance.

Several other useful spells were also stored in \<Infinite Storage>.

…I should have used those from the beginning.

The two bodies began to glow brilliantly, and by the time the light subsided, their battered forms had returned to their original state.

Looking at her again like this, I could see that Kino had a face as perfectly arranged as a traditional Japanese doll.

Shippouin also had well-balanced features. She was more the Yamato nadeshiko type.

…Both of them feel familiar somehow. Have I met them somewhere before?

The two revived by “Ankh” opened their eyes, but there was nothing reflected in their gaze.

I had described Kino as doll-like, but lying there with vacant eyes, she really did look nothing like more than a doll.

To put it bluntly, the two of them were currently in a state like dolls that only answered what they were asked, so that comparison might not even be wrong.

“Alright then. First question. What are your names?”

“…Kino Aichi.”

“Shippouin Kanna.”

The two answered with vacant eyes.

Their voices were flat and emotionless. Well, that was to be expected, given they had almost no sense of self.

“Do you remember what happened just before your memories cut off?”

“I attacked the man who invaded the Grand Cathedral.”

“…Shindo-sama was in danger, so I instinctively jumped into the line of fire.”

Shippouin’s answer was fine. The problem was Kino.

She just casually said Shindo-sama, didn’t she?

Back then I was disguised as Gene, so it would be strange for her to know my identity, and why is she even using an honorific?

“Do you know that Gene is Jin-kun…?”

“…I know. It is a nickname Shindo-sama often used.”

Kino answered Sakura’s question.

It is true that I frequently used the name Gene in my original world, but why would Kino know that?

“Why do you know the nickname I used in my original world?”

“…Because I researched Shindo-sama.”

…And why did you do that!?

“What am I to you? Why do you use an honorific for me?”

“…To me, Shindo-sama is a god. It is only natural to use honorifics for a god.”

“Huh…?”

In response to my straight-down-the-middle question, Kino sent it right back with a perfect line drive.

When I reflexively checked the map, Kino was marked completely yellow (believer).

Not a yellow-tinged red (enemy), but a pure yellow.

For that matter, Shippouin was the same.

“I’m a god? What are you talking about?”

“…When I was in middle school, Shindo-sama saved my life. From that day on, Shindo-sama became the object of my worship.”

Middle school? I stared hard at Kino’s face once more.

…Oh!

“I remember now! You were the ‘No-Panties’ girl who jumped off!”

Back in middle school, I had once saved a girl who tried to commit suicide by jumping. That must have been Kino. I barely ever saw her after that, so I had forgotten.

I never even asked her name back then.

“…Master, why are you calling her ‘No-Panties’?”

“As I said earlier, Kino jumped off a building when she was in middle school.”

I answered Mio’s question.

“Jumped? Not tried to jump?”

“Yeah. She actually jumped, but I was on the floor below and grabbed her.”

“What kind of coincidence is that… Master, you were a master even in your original world.”

Please do not use ‘Master’ as some kind of weirdly loaded noun.

“When I grabbed her, her skirt flipped up, and she wasn’t wearing any underwear. That’s why she became ‘No-Panties’ in my head.”

“This girl has suffered too much!?”

I’ve always had a habit of giving people arbitrary nicknames. Especially in my head.

It only comes up occasionally now, though…

“Apparently the cause was bullying.”

“…”

Hearing the word bullying, Sakura made a very unpleasant, sad expression.

“It seems it was because her family was poor, so I gave her a winning lottery ticket, I think…”

“‘A winning lottery ticket’ is quite a novel expression. And that solution is rather forceful…”

“But thanks to Jin-kun, she was saved… I understand, since I have similar memories…”

“And so she came to worship Jin-sama. That makes sense.”

No, Maria. Please do not just accept that so easily…

Wait a second. It is one thing for Kino to worship me, but what about Shippouin, who is in almost the same state?

“Shippouin, what am I to you?”

“To me, Shindo-sama is a god.”

Same answer.

What is this situation…?

“Why do you worship me?”

“When I was in elementary school, I was kidnapped and locked in a shed, and you saved me. After witnessing a miracle firsthand, worship is the only thing one can do.”

…Oh!

Right, there was that too. When I fell off a cliff, I accidentally saved a girl. Yes, I can see Shippouin’s resemblance.

“I remember. You were the ‘Hostage’ back then.”

“Master… is ‘Hostage’ another nickname you used in your head?”

“Yeah, exactly.”

Mio asked in an exasperated tone, and I answered.

“This girl too!?”

“By the way, she wet herself in fear because of the kidnapper’s gun, so the nickname changed to ‘Bedwetter’ halfway through. That title belongs to Mio now.”

“That is unnecessary familiarity! And I do not want that title!”

Thus, Mio, our party’s designated bedwetter, crossed paths with her predecessor.

“It seems there is no hostility, so maybe it is time to fully resurrect them. Answering questions honestly is nice, but only answering what is asked is a bit troublesome.”

“Yeah. At least they do not seem hostile toward Master, so that should be fine. From the looks of it, they probably will not lie either.”

“Since they will be enslaved and their actions restricted, I do not think they can lie in the first place.”

As Maria said, resurrection and enslavement are a set, so there is little worry about being lied to afterward.

After that, I quickly enslaved the two and used “Ankh” again to perform a full resurrection.

Fully resurrected No… Kino and Bedw… Shippouin looked around, spotted each other, reacted in surprise, and then completely froze the moment they saw me.

The two stared at me and began to cry.

“To think Shindo-sama is so close… Could this be a dream…?”

“…It hurts. Not a dream.”

Without hesitation, Kino pinched her own cheek.

I do not dislike that aggressiveness.

“The fact that I feel no hostility toward Shindo-sama despite being this close means… the Blessing really is gone. In other words, we must have died once.”

“…And then Shindo-sama resurrected us.”

“That must be the case. …Was this good luck? Or bad luck? It is hard to judge.”

“…All’s well that ends well.”

The two calmly began analyzing their situation.

From the looks of it, they had noticed quite a few things about Blessings.

“You can think that clearly right after being resurrected? That saves me the trouble of explaining everything in detail.”

When I spoke, the two snapped to attention and turned to face me.

Their eyes were serious, as if they were trying not to miss a single word I said.

“As you might expect, I am the one who resurrected you. And I know part of the circumstances as well. For example, the fact that you somehow worship me.”

“Y-you knew that too!? Does that mean Shindo-sama remembers us?”

In response to Shippouin’s question, I shook my head.

“No. I vaguely felt you were familiar, but I only remembered just now. I interrogated you while resurrecting you, then traced those memories back.”

“I see. It is unfortunate to have been forgotten, but I am glad you remembered us in the end.”

“…A blessing in disguise?”

No, even if you put it as a question, I cannot answer that.

“Shindo-sama, may we confirm a few things?”

Shippouin asked after composing herself.

“Sure, what is it?”

“First, could you tell us how we died?”

“…Probably Zenon’s attack.”

Since their conscious periods differed, there was a slight information gap between the two.

I would explain it briefly.

“First, the one who defeated you and Sharon was the emperor of the Crimson Empire, Scarlet Crimson.”

Shippouin had fainted before Scarlet introduced himself, after all.

I had to start there.

“So he was the rumored… My apologies. Please continue.”

“Scarlet’s intrusion interrupted the meeting, which later resumed. During the meeting, Zenon of the Glantz Kingdom went berserk and slaughtered many people in the conference room, including Pope Linforce. The Grand Cathedral was badly damaged, and outside it, Scarlet is currently fighting two monsters that follow Zenon.”

Good. That was summarized quite concisely.

“Then where is this place? It seems far too quiet for a battlefield…”

“This is a temporary housing area set up about thirty minutes away from Elgare.”

“…So the rumors were true. The maids of Castal really can build temporary housing in a very short time. No, if they are related to Shindo-sama, that level of unnaturalness might be normal…”

It is unnatural!

“…If you know the current status of the other heroes, could you tell us?”

“The other heroes were attacked by those monsters I mentioned and are currently incapacitated. It seems there are no deaths.”

They are not dead, but without a proper healer, returning to the front lines will be difficult.

“That is good. If there are no deaths, that is what matters most.”

“…Even though we died?”

That was unexpectedly sharp of Kino.

“T-that hurts when you put it like that. But thanks to that, we were able to make contact with Shindo-sama…”

“…All’s well that ends well.”

“Indeed.”

They seem to be one grade apart, but they interact like close acquaintances.

Did they have some kind of connection, being fellow worshippers of me? An unpleasant connection.

“…The problem is the resurrection method.”

“Yes, exactly. Shindo-sama, is the method you used to resurrect us still usable?”

“Yeah. In principle, I can use it as many times as I want, but is there someone you want resurrected?”

Of course, I am not going to lightly promise to resurrect anyone.

“Yes. We would like you to use it on those who, like us, worship Shindo-sama.”

“Hm? Are you not the only ones who worship me?”

“No. Including us, there are seventeen women who worship Shindo-sama.”

“Seriously…?”

At that point, it is just a religion.

Though the object of worship is completely unaware.

“If resurrected, their Blessings will disappear, and so will their hostility toward Shindo-sama. We feel terrible about relying on Shindo-sama’s power, but if they knew you would resurrect them, they would gladly kill themselves.”

“That is terrifying.”

Even if resurrection is assumed, having people gladly commit suicide is a problem…

“There are lots of Maria-chans…”

Mio muttered, and when I looked at Maria, she silently shook her head.

So not that kind.

“Looking again, it seems there are other people besides Shindo-sama…”

“…True. I did not notice.”

The two finally looked around and noticed Mio, Maria, and the others.

It was clear they had paid attention to no one but me since spotting me.

“Shindo-sama, what is your relationship with these women?”

“Uh, in a word, they are my subordinates. You could say they are a group with me as the leader.”

Though their individual positions differ, what they all have in common is that they are my subordinates.

“Please allow me to join as well.”

“…Me too, please.”

“Huh? You are already in. You have slave crests on your backs, right?”

“”Huh?””

Maria and Mio brought over a mirror so they could see their backs.

As an aside, the two are currently completely naked.

It cannot be helped for resurrection, but what is surprising is that neither of them has mentioned it at all. Even if they are heroes now, they were ordinary high school girls originally, right?

“I-it seems to be true…”

“…”

Becoming a slave must be quite a shock.

Both of them look stunned.

“I am happy! Now I can truly become Shindo-sama’s property in name and reality! Oh! What a wonderful day!”

“…Overwhelming emotion!”

No, they were happy. That is scary.

“We must inform the other members at once. Everyone will surely be happy to die and happy to become slaves!”

“…Without a doubt!”

“What is that, terrifying.”

Scary.

“Ahem. Then, this is the final question. What should we do? Since you resurrected us and enslaved us, there must be something you want us to do. Please tell us. If you say so, we will do anything.”

“Anything?”

“Yes, anything. Sex slaves, meat shields, anything. Please use all of us as you wish.”

That is clearly not a normal Japanese mindset.

Scary.

“By the way, Master, it seems seventeen women currently worship you, but are there no men at all? Do you only save women?”

“Mio, please do not put it in a way that sounds bad. To begin with, I have no memory of doing anything worthy of worship. I only gave a bit of help to those I had connections with.”

“…That was… ‘a bit of help’?”

For some reason, Kino was trembling.

“Just to add, while we formed a group consisting only of women, there are men who were saved by Shindo-sama as well. Those people did not form a group and were rarely at school.”

Shippouin tried to follow up for me. …Probably a follow-up.

As far as I remember, I did not discriminate by gender in my ‘bit of help’.

I also do not think I did anything worthy of worship, but being thought of as someone who only saves women is unpleasant.

Though, considering the gender ratio of my current subordinates, it might be understandable…

“So that is how it is. I do not remember doing anything special or even clearly remember who I helped, but I did help men as well.”

“Vague memories. Also, it looks like there is a difference in perception between the one who helped and the one who was helped.”

Shippouin and Kino nodded in agreement.

“So, for what reasons did the other believers start worshipping me? If I hear it, I might remember.”

I probably would not remember just from faces, but hearing the episodes might help.

“Normally it would be best for them to say it themselves, but if that is what Shindo-sama wishes, none of them would refuse. …For example, there was a girl who was swept away while drowning in a river, fell from a waterfall, and survived because she got caught on a lure Shindo-sama threw.”

“Ah, that happened too. I happened to be lure fishing for once, and I thought I hooked a big one, but it turned out to be a person. In a sense, that was an extra-large catch. I could not exactly take a rubbing, though…”

I cannot exactly ask a half-dead girl to let me take a rubbing.

Oh, right. When I get back, I should take a rubbing of the great sea serpent. I forgot to do it since I was distracted after catching her.

“…If you wish, shall we take a rubbing of that girl? I do not think she would refuse.”

Shippouin made that suggestion, but I shook my head.

“No. That goes against my principles. That was a long time ago. She has probably grown in one way or another since then. Taking a rubbing after catching something and letting it grow is against the rules.”

“There it is. Master’s mysterious principles.”

In Maple’s case, even if she grows in level, she does not grow in size, so that is safe.

“I find it frightening enough that Master even thinks of taking rubbings of girls in the first place.”

“Sera, in my original world, there is a term called ‘pai-rubbing’, which refers to coating a woman’s chest with ink and taking a rubbing. In other words, wanting to take rubbings of women is not such a strange desire for men. At least, in my original world.”

I lectured her while looking at Sera’s chest.

Sera’s chest looks very worthwhile for taking a rubbing.

“A-atrocious culture… Master’s original world is a demonic realm…”

Sera shuddered while covering her chest.

“Sera-chan, Master is joking, okay?”

“…Then that sort of word does not exist?”

“Well… it does exist…”

Even Mio could not deny the existence of something that does exist.

“So it is a demonic realm after all!”

“Well, it exists, but not everyone has that desire. It is a minority fetish, to begin with. Now then, Maria-chan! Shippouin-san! Kino-san! Do not look at your own chests and think about how to take rubbings!”

Mio’s retort was sharp.

For the record, in the order of Mio’s line, it is small, large, wall.

Anyway.

“The conversation went off in a strange direction, so let us return to the original topic.”

“You are the one who derailed it… pi!?”

I silenced Mio and continued.

“Right. We were talking about what to have Shippouin and Kino do.”

“Yes. Please use us as Shindo-sama wishes.”

“…Absolute obedience.”

When told they would obey anything, I almost said, ‘For now, strip’.

If it is absolute obedience, wanting to strip them first is a natural flow.

However, they are already naked, so there is nothing left to strip. Any further would turn this from erotic to horror.

“I want you two to continue being heroes as you have been.”

“But our Blessings were lost at the moment of death. Would it not be difficult to call ourselves heroes without Blessings?”

“That will not be a problem. I will prepare substitutes.”

If I give them skills separated from the remnants of Blessings, they should be able to act much as before on the surface.

“Since Shindo-sama says it is possible, it must be so.”

“…That is certain. Shindo-sama, what is your purpose in having us continue as heroes?”

“Simply put, the heroes are far too incompetent, so I want to reinforce them.”

“We are sorry for being such incompetent heroes.”

“…Sorry.”

Both of them looked dejected.

“If the demon race runs rampant, there will be fewer places to sightsee. They are enemies that must eventually be defeated.”

“As always, Jin-kun looks at things from a tourist’s perspective…”

《I want to go eat tasty food!》

I nodded at Sakura and Dora’s words.

Eating local specialties and visiting famous sites is one of my life’s work.

“But defeating the Demon King is the heroes’ job. I do not intend to become a hero who slays the Demon King. That is why I want you to unite the heroes and accomplish the Demon King’s defeat.”

“Understood. I will defeat the Demon King even at the cost of my life.”

“…Absolute kill.”

“Do not trade your lives. Frankly, that would be a nuisance. Make survival your top priority.”

Achieving the goal at the cost of their lives would not make me happy at all.

“Value your lives” is the basic policy.

“If that is what Shindo-sama wishes, then we shall do so.”

“…Absolute compliance.”

It really feels like Maria has multiplied by two.

Maria having different values due to being from another world is one thing, but having students from the same school be like this is quite shocking.

“That will do. …Oh, right. About what comes next, I want you to cooperate with Scarlet and fight the two monsters. Of course, I will provide support as well.”

“Understood. With Shindo-sama’s cooperation, we are invincible.”

“…Power of hundreds of millions.”

I feel like the idiom and the number of digits do not match…

After that, we explained an overview of our abilities to the two of them.

Since we were keeping Scarlet waiting, we decided to leave detailed explanations for later.

Next, I returned skills based on their Blessings to the two of them.

“These have the same effects as our Blessings… no, they are incomparably stronger.”

“…Hard to use?”

Since the effects would be underwhelming as-is, I enhanced them through \<Expanded Interpretation>.

Since they were no longer Blessings, they would not grow stronger by absorbing other Blessing remnants. An alternative method was necessary.

I also gave them several useful skills and adjusted them so they would become stable fighting forces.

Since most skills only need to be LV3, all the skills I gave them were set to LV3.

Here are the final statuses.

Name: Kino Aichi

LV42

Gender: Female

Age: 16

Race: Human (Otherworlder)

Skills:

Martial:

\<Swordsmanship LV1> \<Throwing LV5> \<Martial Arts LV3>

\<Healing Magic LV3>

Other:

\<Ten People, Ten Colors LV >

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Transmigrator, Hero of Another World

Name: Shippouin Kanna

LV39

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Human (Otherworlder)

Skills:

Martial:

\<Swordsmanship LV5> \<Spearmanship LV5> \<Martial Arts LV3>

Magic:

\<Healing Magic LV3>

Techniques:

\<Command LV3> \<Arithmetic LV3> \<Loyalty LV10>

\<Body Enhancement LV3> \<HP Auto-Recovery LV3> \<MP Auto-Recovery LV3> \<Dignity LV6> \<Guts LV1>

Other:

\<Noble Attraction LV >

I think they turned out quite well-balanced.

…Oh, I am ignoring the fact that \<Loyalty> is maxed. Come to think of it, Maria’s \<Loyalty> maxed out recently too…

My subordinates’ \<Loyalty> skill just keeps rising.

Also, I was a little surprised that the title ‘Hero of Another World’ had not disappeared.

Whether titles are unrelated to Blessings or remain permanently once obtained is unclear. I am not particularly interested, though…

Now, here are the two of their reactions at that time.

“Ah, to receive a gift from Shindo-sama… I am glad to be alive.”

“…Today is an anniversary.”

Once again, it really feels like Maria has increased in number.

## **142: The Hero Emperor and the Tyrant King**

**AN:** As mentioned previously, this chapter is from a perspective other than Jin’s.

I did not want to span multiple chapters with a third-party viewpoint, so it is a bit longer.

---

— Scarlet’s Point of View —

“Tch, they ran back up into the sky again!”

My slash grazed them, and I clicked my tongue as I watched the two flee upward to heal their wounds.

In the end, the battle against the two Final Trials had devolved into a stalemate.

The attacks of the Final Trials are treated as magic, so they have absolutely no effect on me.

On top of that, my attacks are super-effective against them, so purely in terms of compatibility, I should have an overwhelming advantage.

However, they can fly, and I cannot. That difference is enormous.

Their regenerative ability is also troublesome. Even if I deal damage, they just escape into the air and recover.

It truly deserves to be called a drawn-out game. … Come to think of it, I have not played shogi since coming here.

Technically, I could fly if I rode on the black dragon’s daughter, Croa, but aerial combat is impossible.

Because of past trauma, Croa cannot fight in the air. It is pitiful, really. Even though she has lost her memories, the trauma alone remains.

“I hate relying on others, but I guess I will just have to keep repeating this until the Castal guys get here…”

If we can get cooperation from Castal’s people, defeating the Final Trials should not be difficult.

The Queen’s Knight Gene. To be blunt, he was dangerous.

I am not bragging, but I am confident in my ability to judge people.

I have survived my fair share of hellish situations, but the moment I laid eyes on Gene, I felt as though I were facing a star itself. He is absolutely someone you must never make an enemy of.

At least for now, there seems to be no reason for us to be hostile, which is a relief. … There really is not, right? I have a bad feeling about this, though…

If he were serious, Gene could probably instantly kill even a Final Trial.

However, for reasons I do not understand, it seems he has no intention of defeating them. If he wanted to, he would have done so long ago.

That said, every Castal knight besides Gene was also a formidable warrior. If even one of them joined the fight, defeating the Final Trials would become much easier.

-DOOOOOOM!-

While I was thinking about that, a massive sound accompanied by a shockwave echoed from the distance.

In the direction of the sound stood the Grand Cathedral. Judging from the dust rising into the air, it must have been the sound of the cathedral collapsing. If I recall correctly, King Zenon of the Kingdom of Grants was rampaging there.

“… What is that?”

A disgusting presence is approaching from the direction of the Grand Cathedral.

The reaction from the King Sword, Divine Curse is also growing stronger. … Not that it needs to react for me to know.

This sword reacts under three conditions: when a Final Trial is nearby, when someone belonging to demonkind is nearby, and when someone belonging to the gods is nearby.

This time, it is reacting to someone belonging to demonkind.

The troublesome thing about this sword is that it does not react to opponents who are concealing their true nature.

If they reveal their true nature, I can sense them even from some distance away, but if they hide it, I cannot notice them no matter how close they are.

In cases like this, where the presence is obvious even without the sword reacting, the function is pointless.

The ominous presence steadily draws closer.

After a while, its form comes into view.

“That is gross. What kind of form is that…?”

It looked like a spider.

At a height of about five meters was its main body, a boy’s form, and from there extended countless red legs like those of a spider. Unlike an actual spider, the number of legs was far more than eight.

It moved slowly forward, alternately shifting its red legs.

We came close enough to clearly see each other.

I took a stance, ready in case an attack came at any moment.

“So this is where you were. I have been looking for you, Scarlet Crimson!”

The boy, Zenon, wore a confident expression as he looked down at me and shouted.

“You are Zenon of the Kingdom of Grants?”

“Indeed. I am the king who shall rule this world. I am Zenon Grants!”

When I raised my voice to ask, Zenon nodded grandly and declared it.

From what I can see, Zenon does look strong.

However, for someone who claims to want to rule the world, he feels a bit lacking.

At the very least, he should be weaker than the Final Trial, Death God, which took my younger brother and me fighting together to defeat. I do not feel like I would lose to him even now.

“You were looking for me, huh? What, did you come to invite me for tea?”

“Fool. Of course not. I sought you out to kill you and make you my sustenance. Die quietly and offer your blood to me.”

As he said that, Zenon extended one of his red legs like a spear, trying to skewer me.

These red legs seem to be made of blood. And not just the blood of one or two people. From his words, it sounds like he can absorb others blood and turn it into his own power.

That must have been why he was rampaging. His goal was likely to absorb more blood.

-GA!-

I grabbed the red leg and crushed it in my grip.

It was not as durable as I expected, and it collapsed easily.

“You crushed my enhanced spear so easily… As expected, you are the greatest obstacle in this country…”

Zenon stared at me with glittering eyes, but that is not quite right.

“No, there are tons of dangerous people besides me! Like Gene from Castal!”

“What are you talking about? I met that so-called Queen’s Knight Gene of Castal, but I did not feel the same pressure from him that I felt from you. The moment I saw you, I knew you were my equal. I was so compelled that I moved my plan forward to gain power beyond yours.”

It seems Zenon felt a sense of crisis upon my appearance and hastened his original plan.

It is not unpleasant to be taken that seriously, but it bothers me that he is underestimating Gene.

… Could it be that Zenon is bad at measuring others strength?

He can read my strength since I am on a similar level to him, but he cannot grasp Gene’s strength because he is far above him?

I compared Gene to a star earlier, but accurately measuring a star’s size is difficult.

From Zenon’s perspective, perhaps Gene was so overwhelmingly large that he simply fell into the category of “I cannot tell.”

Not “too big to understand”, but simply “cannot tell”, to the point he failed to realize he was far superior. That would be a pretty pathetic conclusion.

“Why did you do all this? If the Hero falls, would that not cause problems for you too?”

Since the boss is willing to talk, I might as well gather as much information as possible.

It is a bit uncool, but it also serves nicely as stalling.

“Whether the Hero falls or not, it does not trouble me in the slightest. The demon race will not attack my country.”

“So you were working with the demon race…”

At the point when Divine Curse reacted to someone belonging to demonkind, that much was already predictable.

I just said I would gather information, but it seems I need to flip the table already.

“Sorry, but I cannot just leave someone who sides with the demon race alone. You will die here.”

“That is my line. I will kill you and gain even greater power.”

I would like to capture him alive and extract information, but that would be difficult against someone like this.

I will fight with the intent to kill, and if I am lucky, maybe I can take him alive.

“I will show no mercy! Take this!”

“That attack is way too slow to hit me!”

Zenon extended many red legs at once, so I ran through the city… or rather, the ruins, to evade them.

There are over two hundred red legs, but only about a hundred are actually being used to attack.

The remaining hundred are likely for defense and movement.

I dodge the legs at high speed, thinking as I run.

A hundred spears attacking at once sounds threatening, but it does not feel that overwhelming.

That is because each individual spear does not move in a particularly complex way.

Naturally, the human brain is not built to control over a hundred objects simultaneously. The more there are, the simpler each movement becomes.

As I grow accustomed to it, I begin landing slashes on the red legs.

Just like before, they are easier to destroy than expected.

The destroyed legs regenerate after some time, but it does take a while.

I destroy many legs, lowering the frequency of his attacks.

“Tch, not only can I not hit you, you are even counterattacking! Just die quietly!”

“Like hell I will, you idiot! Now it is my turn!”

With the attack frequency reduced, now it is my turn.

I close in on Zenon and leap, aiming for his main body. In response, Zenon stacks multiple defensive legs together, forming a massive shield.

“Ugh!”

My slash strikes the shield, instantly reducing its numbers.

This was not a weak slash delivered while running. It was a full-power strike. A shield like that cannot fully absorb the impact.

Zenon staggers from the shock, and his movement legs stumble.

“What power…! You must be killed here for certain! Do it!”

“What!?”

As I attacked Zenon and landed before starting to run again, two shadows approached me.

“GRYAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA!!!!!!”

“BRYUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUU!!!!!!”

They were the two Final Trials, each wielding a weapon in both hands. Both seemed to be long weapons like spears. They probably picked them up somewhere while my attention was focused on Zenon.

If magic does not work, engaging in close combat with weapons is not a bad choice. … Not that it will necessarily work.

I run even faster than before, evading all of Zenon’s legs and the Final Trials’ spears.

I am confident in my stamina, but dealing with all of this at once is rough.

“Tch, you can still go faster?!”

Zenon looks surprised, but in terms of speed, this is pretty much my limit.

If I go any faster, I will not be able to control myself properly. I can use it for momentary acceleration, but then I will not be able to dodge attacks or swing my weapon, making it effectively useless.

“Hit him! Hit him already!”

“GRYAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA!!!!!!”

“BRYUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUUU!!!!!!”

The attacks from Zenon and the Final Trials grow increasingly fierce.

Even if I try to slash the red legs, the Final Trials’ attacks get in the way. If I aim for an opening with the Final Trials, the red legs block me. The regeneration speed of the red legs is now exceeding the destruction rate, leaving me no opening to counterattack.

…This is getting a bit rough.

I probably will not lose immediately, but the lack of a decisive blow is painful.

Do I really have no choice but to adopt an extremely passive strategy, waiting for them to tire out or for reinforcements from Castal?

After continuing this passive battle for a while, a fireball suddenly came flying in from afar.

Is that the Fireball spell?

“Ugh!?”

-DOOOOM!-

The Fireball flew straight toward Zenon and was blocked by the shield he hastily deployed. It exploded violently upon impact, filling the area with smoke. The shock was tremendous, and Zenon’s shield was half-destroyed.

That much power from a beginner spell? Did reinforcements from Castal make it in time?

Thinking that, I turn my face toward the direction of the attack while running. Of course, only for an instant.

“That is… the Hero I knocked out at the training grounds…?”

I have good eyesight, so I could spot the girls about three hundred meters away.

There were four girls there. At the front was the Hero I had knocked unconscious at the training grounds.

There was another black-haired girl who also seemed to be a Hero, but I could not really tell about the remaining two. They were hiding their forms under hoods, and one was wearing a strange mask, so I could not see her face.

… This must be some kind of recognition interference. If I looked carefully, I might be able to tell, but that is impossible in this situation.

Judging from their builds visible through their robes, they are girls. No, one of them is less a girl and more of a child. About seven years old? Or maybe an early-growing five-year-old…

I thought they might be reinforcements from Castal, but instead, it seems the Heroes who can fight have arrived.

I shake off the Final Trials and head toward the girls.

“Yo! Are you reinforcements?”

“Yes. We will fight those monsters on behalf of the Heroes. The two behind us are borrowed forces from Castal.”

When I call out, the Hero I knocked out explains on behalf of the group. I think her name was Shippouin or something like that. Same family name as a wealthy magnate from my previous world. Are they related, I wonder?

And it seems two people from Castal are helping.

That aside…

“You look like a completely different person from when I saw you at the training grounds…”

“What do you mean?”

“No, nothing.”

The two Heroes had become so much stronger compared to when I first saw them that they seemed like completely different people.

And it is also strange that Divine Curse, which reacted to them as beings belonging to the gods when I met them before, is not reacting at all now.

What kind of abnormal situation could have occurred in such a short time?

Still, in terms of combat power, they are a perfect fit to take on Zenon and the two Final Trials.

Well, the biggest problem is that the reinforcements from Castal look far stronger than the strengthened Heroes. Compared to Gene, they are two or three steps below, but even so, they do not seem like opponents I could defeat right now.

I thought I had glimpsed the depths of this world, but ha, the world is still vast indeed.

Hm? I look once more at the child among the Castal reinforcements.

… Could that child be a kin of the black dragon?

Damn it! I am really curious! But now is not the time!

“So, how do we fight?”

“We will handle the two monsters, so could you take on Zenon, Scarlet-sama?”

“I do not mind, but those two are not something Heroes can… No, never mind. Leave those two to you.”

“Yes. Leave it to us.”

Heroes cannot deliver the finishing blow to Final Trials.

That rule is absolute, but with those two in the back, it should not be a problem.

… No, considering that they volunteered to defeat the Final Trials, they might know about the bonus for doing so.

I have already received that bonus, so there is no merit for me to land the finishing blow. I will gladly leave it to them.

By the time the brief exchange ended, the smoke around Zenon had cleared.

We are too far away to hear him, but judging from the movement of his mouth, he is probably saying something like, “Damn you… To wound me like this, I will never forgive you!”

Looking closely, there is a small, scorched mark on Zenon’s cheek. It seems the aftershock of Fireball reached him.

“Alright, I am heading in.”

“Please be careful.”

In the end, only one Hero spoke.

The two in the back seem to have no intention of revealing their identities.

I have no intention of prying either. It is better to avoid danger. Stirring up trouble is something only fools do.

I sense presences behind me as I run.

The four of them must be following me. Even if they are not going all out, this is not a speed an ordinary girl could keep up with. Well, they do not seem ordinary, so I guess that is fine.

“You fools! I will never forgive you!”

As we approach, the enraged Zenon once again extends his red legs.

I was about to intercept them, but a Fireball flew past me from behind even faster.

“Tch!”

Zenon clicks his tongue loudly and leaps away.

With over a hundred movement legs, it must be possible to jump at a level completely impossible for a human.

He leaps dozens of meters into the air, dodging the Fireball. … Is that not a bit overly cautious?

“Leave this to us!”

“Yeah, leave Zenon to me!”

I chase after the airborne Zenon.

The two Final Trials also try to pursue Zenon, but one of the Heroes freely moves through the air to block them. The Fireballs launched by the mage girl also serve as suppression.

“Damn you. One after another, you keep interfering with me… I am the one fit to be king of this world. And yet these ignorant rabble dare to stand in my way…”

Zenon lands safely and mutters with a twisted expression.

“The throne does not suit you. At the very least, selling your soul to the demon race already disqualifies you.”

“What do you know! I am the supreme king! And yet, as a mere human, I would die in a few decades at most. How could such a ridiculous thing be acceptable! Even if I must use the power of the demon race, I will survive and remain the supreme king!”

… I see. So that is Zenon’s secret.

It does not seem like rejuvenation.

Most likely, it is possession. Because Zenon has two souls in one body.

The stronger one is probably the soul of Zenon standing before me now. The other soul feels small and weak, as if it is cowering in a corner.

“Calling yourself the supreme king when you are just surviving like a parasite is pretty rich.”

“You… Say that again…”

In a way, Zenon and I are similar.

Through possession, and in my case, reincarnation, we have both warped the original owner’s life.

I have confirmed that there is only one soul in my body.

There is no doubt that this body is mine. However, without my memories, this person named Scarlet Crimson would have had a different life waiting for him. There is no denying that the original shape of that life was distorted.

“I am saying that a parasite who sold his soul to the demon race, threw away his dignity as a living being, and is merely clinging to life has no right to call himself a king!”

“I will kill you! I will absolutely kill you!”

Zenon’s face twists in rage.

This might be something close to self-loathing.

Even so, I cannot stand someone like Zenon, who willingly steals another person’s life.

That is why I will finish him here.

“Die!”

Zenon once again attacks with his red legs.

Naturally, I run to evade while cutting down the red legs whenever I have spare capacity.

Although the red legs regenerate, they do not seem to be infinite.

Their numbers have dropped significantly. There are only about one hundred fifty left now. He cannot reduce the number allocated to defense, so fewer than fifty are actually attacking me.

“Damn it! Damn youuuuu!!!”

With their numbers reduced, the fifty red legs move more complexly than before.

Even so, I am not so naive as to get caught just because they have improved a bit.

“Hit him! Hit him already!”

“Those slow attacks will never hit me!”

The red legs continue to dwindle in number.

Since they are made of blood, the amount Zenon has absorbed so far must equal his remaining supply. And during this battle, he has not been able to replenish it.

The weakness that was covered by his combination with the two Final Trials has been fully exposed now that it is one-on-one. Time is not on Zenon’s side.

I calmly read each attack and deal with the red legs one by one.

As their numbers decrease, their controllability increases, so I do not assume it will get easier. I do not let my guard down.

As a result of continued calm handling, I reduce Zenon’s red legs to one hundred.

This can be considered the annihilation of all legs except those used for movement and defense. Of course, he could repurpose those for offense, but it is unlikely to change the situation.

“Zenon, this is your loss.”

I say it without lowering my guard, in case he still has a trump card.

“Huff, huff… Do not mock me! I have not lost yet! I cannot lose! I will not lose!”

“Then come at me without hiding behind your defenses. Do you really think you can win just by stretching your legs from a safe zone?”

“Grrr…”

Zenon groans in frustration, but eventually seems to make up his mind and relaxes his posture.

“… Very well. If you insist, I will show you my swordsmanship.”

Zenon draws the sword at his waist.

Oh, that is a surprisingly good sword. And just from his stance, I can tell he is a top-class swordsman. Even if it is the result of possession, he must have honed his skills over many long years.

From what I can tell, Zenon does not look like he has fully mastered the use of his red legs.

Most likely, he either acquired that power recently or has rarely used it until now.

The ability to absorb others blood and grow stronger is undeniably powerful. Zenon is surely stronger than his base state.

However, when facing someone close to your equal in the true sense, an unfamiliar and unwieldy power is of no use at all.

Personally, I find refined human technique more troublesome than a big, strong monster.

Even though he is my enemy, if I am going to fight, I want to fight the human Zenon Grants.

Well, he is still using the red legs, so it is a gray area…

“Come!”

“Now that is better! This will actually be fun!”

Zenon charges straight at me with a leap powered by his red legs.

I charge to meet him, then leap as well.

“Ha!!!”

-ZASH!-

After Zenon and I cross paths, I am the only one left standing.

Zenon lies on the ground, split cleanly in two from the abdomen. The red legs have already vanished.

There is no way he survives this. Or rather, why is he still alive?

“So… I lose… Even after surviving this long…”

Perhaps due to the peculiarity of possession, Zenon’s consciousness remains clear.

With the mark of death on his face, he still mutters as if unable to accept it.

“Not yet… I…”

At that moment, something strange happened.

-DOOOOOOM!!!-

Two large objects came flying in from the distance.

They fell about fifty meters away from us, crashing down with a tremendous impact and sound.

… Those are the two Final Trials, right?

As the dust kicked up by the impact settles, I can see the two Final Trials lying defeated, just as I expected.

One is charred black, and the other is completely battered. It is obvious at a glance that they are dead.

“Kuhahahahahahahahaha!!!”

In the instant I looked away, Zenon extended his red legs toward the fallen Final Trials.

Only two red legs emerged, but they pierced the Final Trials at a speed even faster than before.

“Shit!?”

I had been ready for an attack against me, but this was an action directed at something else entirely, so my reaction was delayed. That single instant of delay proved fatal.

“Hahahahahahahahaha!!!”

Zenon laughs like a madman.

If my suspicion is correct, this is going to be bad.

Countless red legs burst forth from Zenon’s body.

“Tch!”

I hurriedly put distance between us.

The red legs envelop Zenon’s body, rapidly swelling.

“Hahahahahahahahaha!!!”

Zenon absorbed the bodies of the two Final Trials and his own lower half.

The red legs… no, the red flesh continued to expand, eventually forming a giant body over ten meters tall.

Legs sprouted from a massive red mass, and Zenon’s face emerged from its center.

I have seen something like this before…

Ah, that! Ka○nashi (final form)!

Jokes aside, Zenon said he grows stronger the more blood he absorbs.

Just how strong will he become after absorbing two Final Trials?

No more escapism. That thing… is stronger than I am now.

“What omnipotence! It might even surpass Linforce. To absorb Linforce, the Thunder God, and the Wind God all in one day. What a glorious day. If I absorb Scarlet as well, I might even reach the Demon King!”

“Hey, hey, isn’t the Demon King your ally?”

“The Demon King is nothing more than a collaborator. Of course I would steal his power too if I could. I accepted this role because I thought I might be able to absorb those two as well.”

So he was aiming for the two Final Trials from the start.

This is just about the worst possible scenario.

On top of that, in this state, Zenon does not count as a Final Trial, so Divine Curse only reacts to him as someone belonging to demonkind. If he were treated as a Final Trial after absorbing them, things might have been manageable…

More importantly, what did Castal’s side even do? Did they hit the Final Trials with a home run when they defeated them? Those huge bodies? Those girls? Blowing them over a hundred meters away?

Is that not even more monstrous?

… Come to think of it, this Zenon, final form, actually seems weaker than Castal’s reinforcements.

Thinking that way makes me feel a bit more relaxed.

“I do not like this. You look like you are still calm in my presence.”

“Well, you do not seem as impressive as I expected.”

-DOGO!!!-

“Guah!!!”

Before I finished speaking, a red leg swept me away.

I barely saw the attack coming and blocked it with Divine Curse, but I was still blown away along with the defense.

I crashed straight into a pile of rubble.

Ouch, ouch… Man, I am glad I was born sturdy. A normal person would have died from that.

“Lower your head. In my presence, you should be crawling on the ground.”

So arrogant.

Still, this is seriously bad.

What is bad is that I might be forced to use my trump card here.

But if I do not use it, I might actually die…

“Now then, with Scarlet quieting down, I will absorb him… Hmm? Who are you?”

Standing in front of Zenon as he tried to advance toward me was a knight clad in silver armor.

… No way. He just appeared in a place I was watching the entire time.

I could not even catch a trace of his movement with my eyes?

The knight, Gene, looks at Zenon with interest and mutters.

“It is interesting that you can strengthen yourself by absorbing blood even from empty husks of corpses. I panicked when Dora sent them flying, but all is well that ends well.”

That voice sounds familiar.

Even with a monster like Zenon right in front of him, he looks as relaxed as if he were out for a stroll.

“So you are Gene! To appear before me now of all times. Perfect. I will absorb you first!”

-BASHIN!-

“Ow!!!”

The one screaming the next instant was Zenon. … What just happened?

Zenon extended a red leg at high speed toward Gene. So far, so good.

The next instant, Gene produced a wooden sword from nowhere and struck the red leg with it. Even with my eyes, I could barely confirm it. And at this point, nothing is good anymore.

Despite the lack of any visible massive impact, Zenon screams and recoils violently. At that point, it becomes completely incomprehensible.

“It works even better than I expected. As expected of an anti-evil-spirit decisive weapon.”

Gene says that as he raises the wooden sword in his hand.

… What is that wooden sword? It clearly looks like a souvenir with “Nikko” carved into it, yet what presence. I can feel power, intent, and history from it. It is probably on the same level as my King Sword, Divine Curse…

Unlike Divine Curse, which houses a curse, its presence shines like the sun itself. Truly worthy of the name Nikko. … I never thought I would have such thoughts about a souvenir wooden sword.

“W-What is that…?”

Zenon is clearly acting strange.

Only one red leg was struck, yet all the other red legs are trembling slightly.

For some reason, Gene slowly points the tip of the wooden sword toward one of Zenon’s red legs, the movement legs.

“Stop! Do not bring that near me!?”

Zenon lifts the red leg upward to avoid the wooden sword.

Without a word, Gene slides toward another red leg, still pointing the tip at it.

“S-Stop it! Stop!”

Zenon lifts a red leg. Gene approaches another. Zenon lifts a red leg. Gene approaches another. Zenon lifts a red leg. Gene approaches another…

Gene is now directly beneath Zenon, so Zenon should not be able to see him, yet he somehow knows the position of the wooden sword and precisely lifts the targeted leg. One by one, his movement legs disappear.

“I said stop!”

Unable to endure it any longer, Zenon tries to skewer Gene with a red leg…

-PESHIN!-

“Ahun!”

Gene smacks him with the wooden sword, and Zenon writhes in agony.

-DOSUUN!!!-

With many of his movement legs gone, Zenon writhes and can no longer support his weight, causing his main body to crash to the ground.

Even if that red body is made of blood, it must be incredibly heavy. A tremendous impact echoes through the area.

Of course, Gene gracefully evades from directly beneath him. I never thought he would get crushed.

“D-Damn it… I will not forgive you… Ah, no, stop…”

-PESHIN!-

“Ahiiin!”

Thus, Zenon’s dignity is completely destroyed, leaving only Gene smacking him with a wooden sword and Zenon being unable to resist, writhing as he is smacked.

“I do not really like tormenting people…”

Gene mutters dissatisfiedly as he keeps smacking him.

To my eyes, it looks like he is tormenting him quite enthusiastically.

Zenon is no longer even capable of forming words, twitching as he continues to be struck.

Suddenly, as if struck by a thought, Gene approaches Zenon’s main body.

By main body, I mean Zenon’s face, which is barely exposed.

“W-What are you… No… Surely not…!?”

Sensing the ominous atmosphere, Zenon’s face twists in fear.

Gene raises the wooden sword in front of his face.

“Stop… Please stop… Please… I do not want to disappear yet… I do not want to die…”

Seeing Gene’s actions, Zenon begs pathetically for his life.

Gene reassures him.

“Do not worry. This sword cannot kill people. All it can do is send the dead to where they belong.”

Gene did call that wooden sword an anti-evil-spirit decisive weapon earlier. Perhaps it is equipment with what could be called a spirit-body specialty effect.

And Zenon, as a possessor, likely meets the condition of being effective against spirit bodies. … Which means Gene knew Zenon’s true nature all along. He really is unfathomable.

“S-So this is it…”

Zenon’s expression turns hopeless.

Well, as far as (the possessor) Zenon is concerned, this is equivalent to death.

-PESHIN!-

Gene’s strike lands mercilessly on Zenon’s forehead.

“Ahhhh!”

And thus, Zenon Grants, the king who sided with the demon race and laid waste to the capital of the Elgant Theocracy, Elgare, vanished from this world.

Honestly, everything about this was a complete mess…

---

**AN:** Next time, the perspective returns to Jin.

There will be some recap, but the timeline continues directly from here. This episode is also part of the main story.

As mentioned in the comments, the Help function presents the information that “those who possessed the Proof of the Hero died before reaching adulthood”, but to be precise, it should be “everyone who died while possessing the Proof of the Hero was underage.”

Information on those who have not died has not been obtained at this time.
