## **143: The Empty Throne of the Sky and the Torn Vestments of Law**

**AN:** This is the usual results-style chapter.

---

Expanded Interpretation has reached LV8.

A new ability has been unlocked.

[Expanded Interpretation LV8]

The number of valid targets has been expanded to 80.

Multiple Existence has reached LV6.

A new ability has been unlocked.

[Multiple Existence LV6]

Status falsification is now possible.

After using the “Light Blade: Sunshine” to lay Zenon to rest, the familiar announcement for my abnormal abilities leveling up came in.

Probably because he was not all that strong an opponent, unfortunately Expanded Interpretation only went up by one level.

I will test \<Multiple Existence> later.

As for this Zenon and Final Trial battle, I had originally planned to stay strictly behind the scenes.

The plan was to put Shippouin and Kino out front, have Sakura and Dora fight the Final Trial as their support, and then let those two land the finishing blow, granting them the Transcendence skill.

That way, the two Heroes would gain fame for slaying monsters, while we would receive the bonus for defeating the Final Trial. Two birds with one stone.

It was good that we managed to dump Zenon onto Scarlet and get the fight with the Final Trial properly matched up.

Sakura and Dora, whose abilities had been reduced, and Shippouin and Kino, who had gained new power, completely overwhelmed the two Final Trials from start to finish. They were not particularly formidable to begin with, so that was only natural. Halfway through, I was watching Scarlet versus Zenon instead of Sakura’s fight.

The problem was that when Sakura and Dora landed the finishing blow on the Final Trial, Dora swung her combat staff with full force, and by sheer coincidence, sent both of them flying like a home run.

Unluckily, or perhaps luckily, the two landed near Scarlet and the others.

What caught my attention was what would happen if Zenon, after being defeated by Sakura and the others and stripped of his status, absorbed the blood of the Final Trial.

Because the opponent involved a Cursed Mark, even Alta could not fully grasp the information.

Curious, I told Sakura and the others to observe.

The result was that Zenon absorbed the two Final Trials, took in something beyond mere status, and transformed into a provisional final form.

Now, I had decided to stay behind the scenes, but once I saw Zenon in his final form, I could not help feeling itchy.

A boss character that obvious makes you want to defeat it.

Of course, cutting in from the side would not be right. If Scarlet had defeated him, I might have endured it, restrained myself, and held back. But happily, Scarlet was taken out in a single blow.

At that point, it was only natural that I would step in. Scarlet still had another option available, but …it did not seem like something he wanted to use, so I judged it fine.

In any case, I happily stepped forward in my silver knight armor to block Zenon.

Now, deciding to defeat Zenon was fine, but the issue was which weapon to use.

Ordinarily, the Sacred Ultimate Sword: Ultimesia would be the obvious choice. However, when I saw the information that Zenon was a Possessed One, I remembered the “rest in peace” effect of the Light Blade: Sunshine.

In short, I wanted to test whether “rest in peace” would work on a Possessed One.

Conclusion: it worked extremely well.

Moreover, it seemed to neatly erase only the possessing Zenon, leaving the original Zenon alive.

I have no particular feelings toward the remaining Zenon, nor do I feel the need to go out of my way to kill him.

It appears that nearly all the status belonged to the possessor.

After the possessor died and I took the status, what remained was the original personality, with extremely weak status, even lower than that of an ordinary child.

Anyway.

So, I defeated Zenon on a whim, but what now?

My objective was to defeat the Final Trial and take down the boss-like enemy. Frankly, I do not care what happens to this country, and I have no intention of saving it.

All right. There is no benefit to staying here, so I will return to Sakuya like a proper knight.

One unfortunate thing is that because Zenon absorbed the blood of the two Final Trials, I could no longer absorb them via Life and Death Authority.

As a result, the Final Trial-exclusive skills Thunder God and Wind God have become useless trash skills.

That said, they are basically inferior versions of Omnipotence, so if you ask whether I need them, the answer is an immediate no. …I am not even using the superior Omnipotence to begin with.

Before returning to Sakuya, I contacted Sakura and Dora via telepathy.

《Sakura, Dora, I am going back to Sakuya. What will you two do?》

《We will be returning shortly.》

《Go back!》

《As planned, Shippouin-san and the others will remain here to take command.》

This was decided before we headed for the Final Trial, but this time, the credit would go to the Heroes, or rather Shippouin and Kino. Castal would be positioned as a mere collaborator.

Since the two will continue as Heroes, no amount of credit is ever enough.

From here on, they will likely discuss reconstruction together with the Pope, who will eventually revive.

In particular, dealing with Barrier Stones to repel monsters is an urgent matter.

《Understood. Then, see you later.》

《Yes.》

《Bye-bye.》

I cut off the telepathy.

As an aside, we left the rampaging monsters approaching the city of Elgale to the maid corps, including Rico, the Dwarf Hero.

More events are welcome, but having them all pile in at once is annoying.

Given the current situation, it would only throw Elgale into further confusion, and it did not seem interesting, so I gratefully took it as skill points instead. There were not a few rare monsters among the rampaging ones, so it worked out nicely.

Another aside: the maids’ combat training is basically conducted against allies or monsters prepared in labyrinths. When dealing with external monsters, it is done in monster territories far from settlements, after confirming on the map that no people are nearby.

This time, it was a valuable opportunity for real combat for the maids as well, so they were enthusiastic.

…Still, there was no way I could put the maids on the front line against Zenon.

That reminds me, what should I do about Zenon, the original personality?

If things continue like this, he will probably be executed for mass murder.

Even if we say the remaining Zenon is innocent, no one will believe it.

I do not particularly want to save him, but I do feel somewhat sorry.

…Hm? Is not Zenon’s status strange?

Name: Zenon Granz

LV1

Gender: Female

Age: 9

Race: Human

Skill: King’s Authority LV1

Title: King of the Granz Kingdom

Um… what do you mean Zenon is female?

A: It is believed that Zenon Granz was originally born female. Possession via Existence Possession does not simply involve possessing the soul. It appears that the host body is also remodeled to match the possessor.

So, from the moment of possession, the original Zenon was completely overwritten, gender included. …How utterly pitiful.

I turned my gaze toward Zenon.

Zenon was currently buried in the blood that had formed his final body (now gel-like), with only her head barely visible.

Looking closer, her facial structure and hair color were different from when she was possessed.

When he was male, he had silver hair, but now it was a pale cherry-blossom pink. There was a resemblance, but different enough that you would not think they were the same person.

I reached out and pulled Zenon from the mass of blood.

It seems her clothes melted away and disappeared when she transformed.

In other words, a naked young girl emerged.

I stared for a moment. She really is female. …Or rather, returned to female?

There is even a slight swell to her chest. Quite precocious.

A little curiosity arose (not about a nine-year-old girl’s chest).

I wondered how a girl whose entire life, even if only nine years, had been twisted by a possessor would live from here on.

Fortunately, or perhaps unfortunately, her current appearance was far removed from that of a king, so it should be possible to conceal her identity.

Even if she looks nothing like Zenon, if a girl of the same age, bearing traces of Zenon’s features, were captured amid the remains of Zenon’s final form, she would probably be treated horribly.

Better to retrieve her, just in case.

I tucked Zenon under my arm.

Well, there is nothing left to do here, so it is about time I returned to Sakuya…

“Wait!”

My steps were halted by Scarlet, who had recovered enough to move.

He had taken an attack that would have killed a normal human, yet he had already recovered to some extent. Like Sera, those with the Hero’s Proof really are inhuman.

“What do you intend to do with that girl?”

I expected something else, but that was not it.

“That is no longer the Zenon who went on a rampage. She is a victim, manipulated by the one who did the rampaging.”

It seems Scarlet knows a fair bit about Zenon’s background.

A: This is the effect of the Heavenly Eye skill. It is not comparable to Clairvoyance, but it allows the user to obtain information about those they see.

Ah, that Heavenly Eye that got overlooked among all the other oddities in Scarlet’s status. …It is interesting that it resembles Asai’s epithet, the Hero of the Heavenly Eye.

“Yes, I know. I have no intention of charging her with a crime either. But if I leave her here, she will certainly be punished. I deliberately held back so she would not die. It would be a waste if she died, so I am taking her with me.”

“You knew… then that weapon was for that purpose…”

Oh? With so little information, he reached that conclusion?

Just as I thought, Scarlet is an interesting one.

“Do you have any complaints about me taking her?”

When I asked, Scarlet shook his head.

“No, I do not. You are right. And if you are taking her, then you are the only one with the right to do so. I do not care how you treat that girl, but it would be too pitiful for her to be mistaken for Zenon and suffer. If you understand that, then fine.”

From the way Scarlet spoke, he did not intend to interfere with how the girl would be treated, but he wanted to prevent her from being treated as Zenon.

Is that kindness, or cruelty? It is hard to judge.

“Is that all? I do not intend to help rebuild this country, so I am heading back to the camp.”

“Then let me ask you just one thing.”

“If it is something I can answer.”

There are far too many things I cannot answer, so this is my default response.

“Do you… intend to defeat the Demon King?”

“No. That is the Heroes’ job.”

Scarlet looked serious, so I answered seriously.

Is Scarlet truly trying to defeat the Demon King, searching for methods himself and unhesitatingly choosing to support the Heroes if needed?

“I see… Supporting the Heroes really is the shortest route. If those two lead the Heroes as a whole, maybe there is some hope.”

Scarlet must understand the current strength of Shippouin and Kino.

I do not know what will happen to the other hundreds of Heroes, but around fifteen more could potentially reach the same level as Shippouin and Kino.

By then, they will have lost their Blessings, so they will not truly be Heroes… but still.

“There is a mountain of things I want to ask Castal, but that was all I wanted to ask badly enough to stop you here. Sorry for holding you up.”

“I have one question too. What will you do from here? There is no doubt you are the key figure in slaying the monsters. If you play your cards right, you could become this country’s hero.”

This time, I asked.

“I am not interested in such an ironic title as Hero. I will make some use of things for my own objectives, but basically, I intend to let the two Heroes take the credit. At most, it is enough to be known as someone who fought alongside the Heroes.”

With a wry smile at the word Hero, Scarlet said so.

It seems Scarlet plans to maneuver much the same way I do.

With people perfectly suited to be put on a pedestal, it is only natural to want to leave it to them. It is honestly a hassle.

“I see. Then I will act accordingly as well.”

If our stories match, it only adds credibility.

“That would help. Well then… see you.”

“Yeah.”

Thus, I left the ruined Elgale and returned to Sakuya and the others.

I will probably meet Scarlet again someday.

Since carrying her around naked would be awkward, I wrapped the girl in some cloth and ran toward the temporary housing set up away from Elgale.

Once there were no signs of people, I used Ice Magic on the girl to freeze her and stored her in Infinite Storage.

Then I activated the Portal spell and teleported near the temporary housing.

Portal only allows related parties to teleport, so to teleport someone unrelated, they must be placed in Infinite Storage.

Maybe I will have Sakura create a spell that allows teleporting unrelated people next time?

“…So, with the possessor gone, I brought the remaining Zenon with me.”

After returning to the temporary housing, I gave a rough explanation to those present.

Sakura and Dora had already returned.

“I see… So Zenon-kun was actually Zenon-chan… Well, of course you would bring her, Onii-chan. You love royal women. And on top of that, a young girl who lived a life far removed from normality. No way your interest would not be piqued.”

This was Sakuya’s first reaction.

For the record, Zenon is being cared for in another room.

“Stop saying things that sound bad. I have not decided to make her a subordinate. I am just curious what kind of life she will choose from here on.”

“But there is a possibility you will make her a subordinate, right?”

“…It is not zero.”

I cannot lie.

“When Onii-chan says that, she probably will become one, right?”

“Yeah, this really feels like a subordinate route.”

Mio nodded along with Sakuya.

Honestly, I think so too…

“By the way, does she retain her consciousness from when she was possessed…?”

Until Sakura asked, I had not considered that angle. Alta?

A: All memories and sensations while the possessor was active are shared.

“That means she remembers everything Zenon did…”

“And according to Alta, she also shared the sensations. Naturally, that would include the sensation of killing people.”

“That is… awful…”

《Awful!》

“Just how many generations has that been repeated, I wonder.”

“What do they think of their descendants? Truly disgusting.”

Everyone showed discomfort at Alta’s answer.

Like Scarlet said, it would be cruel to treat her as a tyrant king on top of this.

“…If she says she wants to die out of guilt, I will not stop her. I do not intend to force someone who wants to die to live.”

That is one possible choice.

“Yes… that is possible… I understand that feeling, wanting to die because it is so painful… I hope there is at least some salvation for her…”

Sakura said sadly.

Did Sakura ever want to die when she was being bullied? …Of course, I would never ask her. There is no way I could.

That reminds me, how long until Zenon wakes up?

This is not simple unconsciousness, right?

A: It is estimated that she will not awaken for one to two days. The burden on the mind and soul is heavy.

“It seems she will not wake up for a while, so we will need to observe her. At worst, I want to get information about demons and possessors before she commits suicide.”

“I see. If memories are shared, then schemes are shared too. We should prevent impulsive suicide. Better remove anything that could be used as a weapon.”

At Mio’s instruction, the maids removed dangerous items from Zenon’s room.

…Well, there are ways to get memories after death too, but it is best to ask while she is alive.

So, Zenon will be on recovery watch for now.

Next, what should we think about…

A: Master. The Pope, Linforce, is about to revive.

Now that one too. Things never slow down.

“It is only natural, but there are a lot of post-battle events. If we could just skip the results screen, it would be easier…”

“Yeah. There probably is not much important left anyway. Skipping should be fine, right?”

I am a gamer too, so I understand what Mio is getting at.

Skipping non-essential results information is common.

“Normally, this is a national crisis. Of course things are busier after the battle. Honestly, Onii-chan says unbelievable things so casually.”

“Master really has no interest in this country, does he?”

Sakuya and Sera gave wry smiles.

Elgant Theocracy is a country I do not like. On top of that, its major events are already over. Why would I be interested?

“Jin-sama, if you have no interest, shall we leave the response to the maids?”

“No. This is the result of my own choice, so I will at least watch how it plays out.”

I shook my head at Maria’s question.

As for Linforce, I chose to transport her corpse knowing she would revive, so I will see it through.

With Linforce about to revive, I took her from the item box and laid her on the sofa.

She was in terrible condition, having soiled herself and bled, so I used \<Purification>.

\<Purification>, thank you for your continued hard work.

As an aside, time does not stop inside the item box, so if Linforce revived inside it, she would be ejected the moment she revived.

Even if she regained consciousness instantly, she would almost certainly fall to the ground.

If she landed badly, she might die a second time. …That would be interesting in its own way.

About a minute after taking her out, Linforce revived.

Just before reviving, her body shone with light, her wounds gradually closed, and in the end her HP fully recovered.

When the light subsided, Linforce looked like she was simply sleeping.

Soon after, Linforce opened her eyes.

They were vacant, unfocused.

“Hi…”

Now then, what would Linforce say after performing the miracle of revival?

Normally, she would revive before believers and deepen their faith. Unfortunately for her, those around her now had not even a shred of faith in the goddess.

“Hiyaaaaaaaaaa!!! Hyaaaaaaaaaaaa!!! Hii! Hiiiiiiiiiiiiiiii!!! Aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa!!!”

Ah, this is bad.

Linforce fell into a panic, drooling, convulsing, and screaming.

Even though I had just purified her, she was making a mess again. Ruined.

“Hi! Hii! Hiiiiiiiii!!! Hi! Hi! Hyaaaaaa!!!”

“Shut up!”

– Thud! –

“Gehyu!”

My restrained gut punch landed, and Linforce passed out.

Maria caught her and used Purification again.

“She is completely broken… When a beauty breaks, it is quite the sight.”

Mio said with visible discomfort, and the others looked similar.

They are not recoiling because I punched her without hesitation, right?

“There does not seem to be physical damage, but mentally is another story. Did fear break her as she was dying? Zenon killed her while cornering her…”

“Can this be fixed? If the ruler of this country is like that, it is a problem for me too…”

Sakuya has no choice but to worry, since she would be troubled if Elgant Theocracy collapsed.

It is a world-class superpower. With the capital devastated and the nation’s leader in this state, massive chaos is inevitable.

The impact on neighboring countries would be enormous.

A: It cannot be healed without the mental protection of Multiple Existence.

Yeah, I thought so.

So, what to do?

Honestly, I do not need goddess-affiliated people who acted hostile toward me.

“To heal Linforce, I would need Alta’s mental protection. In other words, she would have to become my subordinate.”

“So, business as usual. Since coming to this country, you have taken Ekaterina of the Sanokia Kingdom and Zenon-chan of the Granz Kingdom as subordinates. If you enslave Linforce too, then Queen Sharon of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom is only a matter of time.”

Mio was clearly enjoying herself.

For the record, I have also tamed a mermaid princess in a forest within the Sanokia Kingdom.

Whether that counts is debatable, but just in case…

“I do not even have contact with Queen Sharon.”

“And you did not really have contact with this person either. Things like that work out somehow, do they not?”

Mio muttered softly, “If Master wished it.”

I like cats, and I did not dislike her disposition shown in the fight with Shippouin, so I would like to talk to her, not pet her, but that does not mean I want to make her a subordinate.

Besides, we are not enemies, and I cannot imagine a situation where she would become one.

“Setting Sharon aside, I honestly do not feel like taking Linforce.”

I often add royal women to my subordinates, but I do not add just anyone.

I did not directly add Christia, the former Eldia princess, as a subordinate either. Basically, I do not want to subordinate those who opposed me at an unpleasant level (the Izumo sisters are fine).

“She is the top of a country that took hostile action against Jin-kun…”

《Master’s enemy!》

Dora puffed up adorably. Cute.

“But it is also a problem if you refuse to heal her. Internationally…”

Sakuya said troubled, but this time I cannot grant that request.

“That is something each country should deal with. It is not something I need to take responsibility for. Linforce broke for reasons unrelated to me. I have no reason to make her a subordinate, and no responsibility to heal her. This is different from Eldia.”

With Eldia, I chose to destroy it by my own will, so I helped with the aftermath and honored Sakuya’s wish to keep Christia alive.

This time, regarding Elgant Theocracy and Linforce, I am not involved at all.

As for Linforce, at most I was involved by agreeing to transport her corpse, but I have no obligation to take care of her afterward.

And frankly, none of Linforce’s skills interest me either.

Not every unique skill is desirable.

“Ugh… If Onii-chan says that much, there is no way to change your mind. Mio-chan! Help!”

“Hey, what do you expect me to do… That is unreasonable.”

“Sakura-chan!”

“Sakuya-chan, please do your best…”

Sakuya looked for allies, but Mio and Sakura shook their heads.

After looking around for a while, she seemed to give up and slumped her shoulders.

“No good, huh…”

Not good at all.

I doubt even legendary equipment would sway me.

---

**Side Story**

· **Behind-the-scenes and extra stories.**

The Granz Royal Family

In the Granz Kingdom, the succession of the king is entirely at the discretion of the king. In other words, only the current king can decide the next king.

Furthermore, only male children may become king.

In the Granz Kingdom, the king is an absolute authority and takes precedence in all matters.

It is not strange that there is a royal-only cemetery, but within the Granz royal cemetery, there is a section that only those who became king may enter.

When the previous king dies, the next king places the body into the royal tomb.

Needless to say, these systems are tied to the intent of the first king of Granz, namely the one who possessed Zenon Granz.

By personally selecting the possession target and making that person king, the main objective was to secure the throne.

The first king’s skill does not free the original body simply by moving to a new one. A fragment like a remnant soul remains, and that remnant moves the body until royal succession. Thus, those whose bodies are taken are never freed until death.

Because it is a cemetery only kings may enter, no one knows, but among the coffins holding the remains of successive kings, roughly half contain female remains.

These are the remains of royals who were born female, yet had their bodies taken by the first king and were raised as men, just like Zenon.

---

**AN:** Linforce is apparently not needed.

Not just any royal woman will do.

Next time is the final chapter of this volume. The tenth volume is still not finished…

Before the next chapter, there will be a short story about leveled-up abnormal abilities.

+++

## **143.5: Status Spoofing**

**AN:** This chapter covers the effects of a leveled-up Special Power.

It is essentially part of the main story, but due to page count and chapter break considerations, it ended up as a short chapter.

It differs somewhat from the usual “status spoofing” trope.

---

“Alright, it’s about time to test the new ability of \<Multiple Existence>.”

One of my Special Powers, \<Multiple Existence>, leveled up to LV6 when I defeated Zenon.

Things were hectic at the time, so I put off testing it, but I think it’s time to get to it.

“Come to think of it, Master’s Special Power leveled up again, didn’t it?”

“So what kind of absurd thing can you do this time?”

Before I even start explaining, Sera has already decided it’s something absurd. I don’t understand that.

“Well, it probably is something absurd. It is Master, after all.”

《That’s right-》

“…”

Sakura is left speechless after Mio steals her stock line.

“So, what exactly can this ‘status spoofing’ do?”

Since the others are here as well, I ask Alta out loud.

A: You can spoof the attribute information of items shown in the status display. It is also possible to spoof the items themselves.

That sounds like programming terminology.

“When you say items and attributes, is it fine to think of them like objects and attributes in programming terms?”

A: That is mostly correct.

Thinking of it that way really changes how you look at the status display…

“Master, do you understand programming and stuff?”

“That’s surprising…”

Maria and Sera tilt their heads at the unfamiliar words, but Mio and Sakura probably know them. Dora? Dora is just tuning it out.

“Yeah, back in my original world, a close friend once gave me a ‘Programming Course Even Someone with a Deviation Score of 1 Can Understand,’ so I get the rough idea.”

“Isn’t the target audience level way too low?”

“That just means it’s easy to understand.”

My close friend Azuma has a way of thinking I don’t always understand.

The same goes for my other close friend, Asai. …For some reason, I feel like both of them just said, ‘You’re one to talk’.

“Anyway, thinking of it like that lets me roughly predict what I can do.”

For example, if I do this…

“Done. I spoofed it so my titles include ‘Sword Emperor’.”

Name: Jindou Jin

Titles: Transferee, Esper, Dungeon Master, Transcendent One, Sword Emperor (Spoofed)

“With this, shouldn’t I be able to use the \<Sword Emperor> skill?”

A: You can.

Just as I thought, by spoofing the status, I can spoof what the system references.

That said, it’s only spoofing the reference. I don’t actually gain what’s inside the spoofed thing, meaning the ability itself.

It’s like taking an empty box and writing “Sword Emperor” on it with a marker. You can insist that you have the Sword Emperor title, but the inside is empty.

“Jin-sama, will you try using the \<Sword Emperor> skill?”

“Nah, I wasn’t interested in using it anyway.”

I shake my head in response to Maria’s question.

It’s not like I was interested in the \<Sword Emperor> skill itself. I only tried it because it was a combination of a title and skill I don’t have.

“Huh. That’s interesting. When people talk about status spoofing, I usually imagine something that fakes the status other people can see, but Master’s is different.”

“Of course, I could probably do that too, but in the first place, there aren’t many people in this world who can even recognize status, and there are even fewer who can see someone else’s status in detail.”

If anything, I doubt some half-baked spoofing would work on someone who can thoroughly see other people’s status. Like Orihara, for example…

I try out a few ideas I have for status spoofing.

“I can also spoof an ordinary skill into a Blessing. It might be better to spoof the skills of the Heroes who became my subordinates.”

“Yes. If, for some reason, they end up touching a ‘Blessing Orb’, it would expose that they are not Heroes…”

The “Blessing Orb” is a magical tool that checks Blessings. Sakura and I have both touched it before.

The former Heroes whose Gifts became ordinary skills can no longer act under the assumption that they are Heroes.

Since we’re at it, I’ll spoof their Hero Blessings.

Also, skills like \<Baleful Star>, where damage is reduced unless you have the Hero title, can apparently be fooled with a spoofed title.

In other words, even fake Heroes can defeat the Demon King.

“In that sense, this was another conveniently timed effect, just like always.”

“Well, it is Jin-kun…”

《That’s right-》

This time, Sakura looks like she’s regained her honor. Were you aiming for that?

“That said, for me personally, it’s not that huge of a benefit.”

It’ll be useful, sure, but it’s not something that makes me happy as an individual.

“Why? You can use skills that come as a set with titles, right? That sounds convenient.”

“No, there’s no value in using skills through tricks like that, is there? It’s not even interesting.”

I answer Mio’s question.

It might be amusing as a joke, but being able to use skills through tricks doesn’t make me happy, nor is it something to be proud of. I might try it once or twice, but I’d never make it a core part of my fighting style.

“If it’s not interesting to Master, then it’s not really a merit, is it?”

“That’s right.”

No matter how convenient something is, if it’s not interesting, it gets a low evaluation from me.

“As for other uses, I could erase the slave titles of subordinates, or change Mira’s and the Naruse mother and daughter’s ages back to their original ones, I guess. I don’t think there’s much meaning to it, though…”

It’s a countermeasure in case there’s a magical tool that references slave titles or age.

Do tools like that even exist?

A: They do exist.

They do, huh… Then it’s probably better to do it.

As an aside, when I later explained this to my subordinates, they tearfully begged me not to erase proof that they belonged to me, even if it was just spoofed.

So I made hiding titles basically optional, and only made it mandatory for certain subordinates like Claude who appear on the public stage. Others include the royal group like the Tooru and Kaoru sisters, and Rouge.

“Master not being interested in spoofing titles is clear, but Mio-chan really wants to try using a certain skill. Master, please! Let me use it!”

“Mio, for you to beg that hard, what skill is it?”

“Of course, the ‘Dungeon Master’ title and the \<Labyrinth Domination> skill! I was super curious about it!”

I tell the cruel truth to Mio as she speaks with sparkling eyes.

“Sorry, but \<Labyrinth Domination> can’t be used with a spoofed title.

“”Why!?”

Mio looks so shocked it’s like the word “Gaan” is about to pop out.

“‘Dungeon Master’ and \<Labyrinth Domination> reference each other.”

“???”

“In other words, both have to be real to use them.”

She doesn’t seem to get it, so I explain it a bit more plainly.

“The ‘Dungeon Master’ title checks whether you have the \<Labyrinth Domination> skill, and the skill checks for the title too. On top of that, they also confirm that they’ve been confirmed by the other side. So half-baked tricks don’t work at all. You could say the security is tight.”

“No waaaay…”

As Mio slumps, Maria raises her hand this time.

“Jin-sama, then why can \<Sword Emperor> be used?”

“Oh, \<Sword Emperor> seems to have weak security. Since the \<Sword Emperor> skill and the ‘Sword Emperor’ title are acquired at the same time, it only checks the title once, the first time the skill moves.”

Incidentally, \<Labyrinth Domination> checks every single time you use the ability.

“Only once?”

“That’s right. For example, even if I spoof and erase Maria’s ‘Sword Emperor’ title right now, she can still use the \<Sword Emperor> skill normally.”

“What kind of sloppy security is that…”

Mio says, exasperated.

It seems the nature of skills really differs more than I expected.

“Also, it’s not referencing the exact string ‘Sword Emperor.’ The criterion is that somewhere in the title, there are the characters ‘Sword’ and ‘Emperor.’”

For example, if you had two titles, ‘Emperor’ and ‘Sword Master,’ you’d be able to use the \<Sword Emperor> skill.

“That’s some terrible corner-cutting…”

“This really is sloppy security taken to the extreme.”

“Yeah. The evaluation of the \<Sword Emperor> skill, which was already low, dropped even further.”

And comparatively, the evaluation of \<Labyrinth Domination> goes up.

It was already at limit-up levels to begin with, though.

Sorry, Maria, but that’s why \<Sword Emperor> doesn’t interest me.

“But thanks to this Special Power? Or because of it? Either way, the way we look at skills and titles has changed.”

“Yeah, that part might be worth evaluating. We didn’t find any major uses right now, but it’s surprisingly not bad… cough, I mean, it seems like a power we could make good use of.”

Spoof your gender or race to use exclusive skills.

Fudge your race and skills to play Demon King Army Four Heavenly Kings.

Spoof your age to ride buses and trains at child fare.

The possibilities are endless!

“Alright, everyone, think about ways to use this Special Power too! If you come up with anything interesting, I’ll take suggestions anytime. Anyone whose idea gets adopted will receive a luxurious consolation prize!”

“Who are you talking to? What are you even saying? Is it luxurious? Is it a consolation prize?”

What \<Multiple Existence LV6> can do:

– You can spoof items in the status column.

– There are three types of spoofing: “addition”, “deletion”, and “attribute change.”

– You don’t gain the effects or abilities; it only lets you fool things when they reference it.

---

**AN:** It was a terrifying Special Power that demands imagination from the author.

The reason security was brought up is so that, if some usage the author never imagined becomes possible, they can say, “It’s not possible due to security”, as an excuse. “Currently adjusting.”

+++

## **144: Aftermath in the Divine Capital and the Return**

**AN:** This one is a bit long.

---

Now then, let me give you a digest of the various goings-on after the incident that plunged the divine capital of the Kingdom of Elgant into a state of near-total devastation. Not that I’m particularly interested, mind you!

The mastermind behind the incident, Zenon Grants, is officially considered to have died in battle against the Hero.

As you know, this is not actually true, but based on the testimony of the Hero himself and Scarlet, who fought alongside him, he was declared dead. His body is said to have vanished.

The Pontiff of the Kingdom of Elgant, Linforce, was also thought to have been killed by Zenon, but miraculously survived (or so the story goes). However, due to the shock of the attack, her mind was broken, and it is considered hopeless for her to ever return to the position of Pontiff.

To begin with, the current state of the Kingdom of Elgant itself can only be described as hopeless.

In order to participate in the recent summit conference, influential Goddess Church followers from across the Kingdom of Elgant had gathered. However, in this incident, the Grand Cathedral was destroyed, and those influential figures were slaughtered almost to a man.

As a result, this is no longer something that can be contained within Elgare alone, and the chaos will likely spread across the entire Kingdom of Elgant.

With the linchpin Linforce also broken, there’s no way proper national governance can be maintained.

Rebuilding the city will also take a tremendous amount of time. At present, almost no reconstruction work is actually underway.

With reconstruction crawling along at a snail’s pace, the summit conference was resumed.

After all, with people gathered from every nation, they couldn’t very well keep everyone stuck in Elgare for an extended period.

Yes, the heads of state from each nation, who were thought to have been killed by Zenon, had miraculously survived.

Ah, of course, “miraculously” is a joke.

The heads of state were revived by me and the maids using “Ankh.”

In fact, when Zenon slaughtered all the national leaders in the conference hall, I had Tamo-san secretly collect their bodies.

After the fighting ended, we revived them and laid them near the rubble of the Grand Cathedral, staging it to look as though they had survived by pure chance.

Naturally, reviving them also came bundled with enslaving them.

As a result, the leaders of the nations surrounding the Kingdom of Elgant could no longer oppose me.

From that point on, there were no more disrespectful remarks toward me, Sakuya, or Castal.

As an aside, we didn’t revive everyone who died.

Only the top leaders of each nation, plus a handful of individuals selected by those leaders, were revived.

We didn’t have enough Ankh stock to revive everyone, and frankly, they weren’t worth that much effort. They were basically enemy nations to begin with.

To begin with, the reason we revived them was simply to shut up those annoying countries…

Another aside: not a single person from the Kingdom of Elgant was revived.

Naturally so. There wasn’t anyone I wanted to keep alive. If I wanted to take control of the Kingdom of Elgant, it would be faster to listen to Sakuya’s request and bring Linforce into my fold anyway…

With the leadership of the Kingdom of Elgant completely wiped out, the summit conference was resumed under the leadership of the Kingdom of Sanokia.

One reason for this was that among the nations surrounding the Kingdom of Elgant, Sanokia was practically the only large-scale Hero-supporting kingdom with strong influence.

Scarlet participated in the conference held in a temporary meeting hall set up in place of the Grand Cathedral from the very beginning. In contrast, those who had been participating via the “Paired Farseeing Mirrors” were absent.

Well, that couldn’t be helped, considering all the Paired Farseeing Mirrors had been destroyed.

The biggest topic at the resumed conference was this: “Which country will take custody of the Hero next?”

To be blunt, the current Kingdom of Elgant has no capacity to take in a Hero.

They wouldn’t be able to provide proper support, and any funds given would just end up diverted to reconstruction.

So, a replacement country was needed, but here a major problem reared its head.

Simply put, a jinx had formed: “A country that takes in a Hero will be destroyed.”

Considering Eldia, which was destroyed by Castal, and Elgare, which is now effectively in ruins, that conclusion is understandable.

In other words, each country began trying to shove the Hero off onto someone else.

In the end, it was decided that several Heroes would be entrusted to each of the countries surrounding the Kingdom of Elgant.

One reason was the judgment that concentrating Heroes in a single location was itself a risk.

Since Heroes were now being distributed across multiple nations, the Hero support system also needed to be reworked.

Funds and supplies provided by Hero-supporting nations would be distributed to the countries hosting Heroes in proportion to the number of Heroes they housed.

As discussed before the collapse of the Grand Cathedral, Scarlet of the Crimson Empire and Sharon of the Regalia Beastman Nation chose to become Hero-supporting nations.

The Kingdom of Castal and the Kingdom of Estea remained unchanged in their decision not to become Hero-supporting nations.

At the very least, there are still no achievements attributable to Heroes alone.

In the battle against Zenon, the Kingdom of Castal’s assistance was acknowledged by the Hero representative, Shippouin, as indispensable, and it was decided that Castal would receive credit for 40% of the achievement in defeating Zenon.

The remaining breakdown is 50% credit to the Heroes and 10% to Scarlet. It hurts that Scarlet didn’t defeat a single enemy. He was this close to defeating Zenon, too…

Even so, it seemed to be a satisfactory outcome for Scarlet, who nodded with a satisfied expression.

If there are those who should be rewarded for their achievements, then conversely there are those who should be punished.

Needless to say, that would be the Kingdom of Grants.

As a result of this incident, it was revealed that the Kingdom of Grants had committed one of the greatest taboos among human nations: “Cooperating with the Demon Race.”

It may have been Zenon’s crime alone, but since it was committed by the nation’s leader, it is only natural that it be treated as a crime of the entire state. And the punishment for that crime is severe. In short, the country will perish.

A coalition army of neighboring nations is set to invade the Kingdom of Grants.

You might think, “Another war between humans?” but this time it won’t really be a war.

It will be a one-sided massacre due to the overwhelming difference in force.

Granted, the Castal–Eldia War was also a one-sided massacre, so that hasn’t changed.

Furthermore, part of the spoils from that massacre will serve as rewards for this round of achievements.

Simply put, portions of the Kingdom of Grants will be handed out (with resident enslavement included).

Since the land is an enclave and not needed, Sakuya said they plan to sell it off to neighboring nations and collect the enslaved residents for use.

For the citizens of the Kingdom of Grants, it’s about as unfair as it gets. Not that I feel inclined to go out of my way to save them…

With no one left to pick fights with Castal (since they weren’t revived), the summit conference progressed at an astonishing speed. All agenda items were concluded in just three days.

That’s about all there is to say regarding the Kingdom of Elgant as a whole.

Given the scale of the incident, there’s much more I could talk about, but my interest doesn’t last that long.

More importantly, my own personal, high-density events take precedence.

For example, the matter of the fifteen Heroes who worship me.

That happened on the night we defeated Zenon and his group, after that day’s reconstruction work had ended.

Seventeen Heroes, including Shippouin and Kino, came to Castal’s temporary housing. Their purpose was, of course, to become my slaves.

“Is it really okay for Shippouin, the representative Hero, to come all the way here?”

“Of course. There is nothing in this world more important than serving you, Shindou-sama.”

“…Top priority.”

As always, Shippouin and Kino are Maria (their Japanese is weird).

“So, there are fifteen people riding in that carriage?”

“Yes. All of them are prepared to die at any time.”

Behind Shippouin, who said something terrifying with a smile, I looked to see two rather large carriages parked there.

Inside them were the fifteen Heroes who wished to become my slaves.

“I’ll revive them one by one. If too much time passes after death, memories can be lost. There’s no need to take unnecessary risks.”

“Understood. Then I will call them in order.”

With that, Shippouin brought out one woman from the carriage.

She was wearing something like a bathrobe and had a blindfold on.

She was naked beneath the bathrobe. This was to save the trouble of stripping her during revival. The blindfold was a countermeasure against Blessings. Apparently, if they see me directly, they develop hostility.

“Igarashi-san, I’ll be waiting.”

“Ah. I’ll be there shortly.”

After that brief exchange with Shippouin, I took the woman named Igarashi into the temporary housing.

Inside the room, aside from Igarashi, there was only me and Maria.

“At last, this day has come. Shindou-sama, I humbly ask for your favor.”

Inside the temporary housing, shielded from outside view, Igarashi removed her bathrobe and stood naked.

She was taller than me and had a well-proportioned body. It clearly belonged to someone athletic. This muscle tone… track and field, maybe?

…No good. No matter how much I look, I can’t remember. Who is this?

“Yeah. Leave it to me.”

“Thank you.”

With that, she opened a small vial she had kept in the bathrobe pocket and drank its contents in one gulp.

It was a fast-acting poison.

Igarashi died.

“Ankh.”

Igarashi was revived.

I collected the remnants of her Blessing and cast Slave Art on her.

I removed her blindfold, but since her ego hadn’t returned, her eyes remained vacant.

Now then, it’s hard to ask this while she’s conscious, so I’ll ask now.

“Why do you worship me?”

“When I was in the lower grades of elementary school, I was so poor that I couldn’t even eat properly. You shared your food with me, Shindou-sama, and protected me from malice.”

Uh, who is that?

“You called me Lassie and doted on me. I have no master other than you, Shindou-sama.”

Ah, Lassie! I remember Lassie! My very first pet!

So that Lassie grew up into this, huh. Back then she was scrawny, short, with unkempt hair and a lifeless expression.

With that drastic a before-and-after, no wonder I didn’t recognize her.

When Lassie was in the lower grades of elementary school, she was always hungry, so when I gave her some of my food, she got attached to me.

The way she latched on looked exactly like a dog or cat, so I boldly decided to treat her as a pet. Since she was a pet, I gave her a pet-like name. Since she was a pet, I chased off anyone who bullied her. Since she was a pet, I fed her. Since she was a pet, I taught her various tricks.

Lassie’s pet life continued for several years, but one day she moved away, and we never met again. In hindsight, maybe I should have exchanged phone numbers, but since she was a pet, that thought never really occurred to me. I truly treated her like a pet.

“Ankh.”

Having figured out Igarashi’s true identity, I felt refreshed and cast Ankh again, completing her revival.

The moment ego returned to Lassie’s eyes, I declared:

“Sit!”

“Yes!”

The instant she heard my command, Lassie assumed a pose that no girl her age should ever take. And she was completely naked.

Of course, this wasn’t an order enforced by Slave Art. That reaction proves it. This is definitely Lassie.

“Ah… Shindou-sama’s commands… how nostalgic…”

Lassie wore an enraptured expression while holding the dangerous pose.

“Stay!”

“Yes!”

Lassie snapped to attention. Still naked.

It’s been nearly ten years, but she hasn’t forgotten my commands at all. It’s probably become a conditioned reflex. Truly, Pavlov’s dog.

However, I had to convey a cruel reality to Lassie.

“Sorry, but I already have another pet.”

I was referring to Dora, my pet and body pillow.

“S-such a thing…”

Lassie collapsed to the floor with an expression like the end of the world.

Just how important does she consider the status of “pet”?

“There’s no rule saying I can only have one pet.”

“T-then…!”

“But you once left me for your own reasons. If you want to call yourself my pet again, then first prove your usefulness to me as a slave. We’ll talk after that.”

“Y-yes! I will strive to reclaim the title of pet, no matter what I must sacrifice!”

I think that wanting to become a pet already means you’ve sacrificed something very important: your humanity.

And considering I’m keeping a girl my own age as a pet, there’s a very small chance my own humanity could be questioned as well.

After that, I repeated the process in order: suicide by poison, revival, confirmation of worship reasons, and full revival.

There were a few girls whose identities I remembered before hearing their reasons, but for most of them, I needed the explanation. The fact that I remembered all of them once I heard their reasons was fortunate.

Since they were all from the same school, I assumed they were all girls my age, but surprisingly, there were exceptions.

Two of them were adult women.

One was a newly appointed teacher, and the other was a student teacher. Both chose this high school because I was there. That was surprising.

On the other hand, there was also a ten-year-old girl.

She was a so-called prodigy who skipped grades to enter high school. Of course, she also chose the school because I was there. That was surprising too.

The fact that everyone except those who started worshipping me in high school had chosen their high school solely “because I was there” went beyond surprising and into outright terrifying.

Isn’t my personal information leaking way too much?

I returned their Blessing-based skills and granted each of them a tailored skill set, resulting in a massive boost in combat power.

This should be more than enough to let the Heroes accumulate the achievements they lack.

As for the other Heroes, I couldn’t care less. I just hope they don’t get in the way.

“Leave the rest to you.”

“Yes. We will certainly meet your expectations, Shindou-sama. After all, for that purpose, and that purpose alone, we have strengthened ourselves.”

And so, the seventeen Heroes returned to Elgare.

Ah, wait, they don’t have Blessings anymore, so they’re former Heroes now, right…

There were other memorable events during the summit conference as well, the biggest being Zenon’s awakening.

When you say “awakening”, it sounds cool, but she just woke up normally.

And the first thing Zenon-chan said upon regaining consciousness was this:

“At last… at last I’m free! It was painful… so long… but now I’m free! From here on, I can live my own life!”

She hugged her own body and cried, overwhelmed with emotion.

Given this, it doesn’t seem like guilt-driven suicide is on the table.

After a while, she calmed down and noticed our presence around her.

“Where am I… and who are you…?”

“This is a temporary housing facility set up by the Kingdom of Castal. We’re related to Castal. We rescued you from that monster and have been taking care of you.”

Mio explained on behalf of the group.

“T-then! Is the silver-white knight here too!? I absolutely must thank him! He erased the monster that bound me for so long! He was so cool… I want to be like that someday…”

Zenon-chan looked like a kid admiring a hero, but then immediately noticed something strange about himself.

“…Huh?”

Having realized something, Zenon-chan lifted the sheet covering her and froze.

“U-um… there’s something I’d like to ask…”

“What is it?”

“Where did my penis go…?”

“Pff!?”

Even Mio couldn’t hold it in.

After all, that’s probably the first time in her twenty-four years of life, including her past life, she’s ever been asked something like that.

…No, actually, no one has ever been asked that.

“Well, um… you were actually a girl. So girls shouldn’t say things like ‘penis.’”

Mio said it. Is that really okay?

“Huh? But when I was possessed…”

“The one possessing you was male, so it seems your body was altered into a male form.”

“S-such a thing is possible…?”

“Apparently. I don’t know the details either…”

Zenon-chan wore a blank, stunned expression from the shock.

She couldn’t control the body, but her consciousness thought she was male the whole time.

In the end, it took about ten minutes for Zenon to fully recover.

“I see… so I have nowhere to return to… No, perhaps I never did, even from birth. The me from before wasn’t the real me…”

We introduced ourselves and explained the situation to the revived Zenon.

Even after hearing that it would be effectively impossible to live as Zenon again, she didn’t show much surprise.

If anything, the “actually a girl” revelation seemed to hit harder.

Now then, it’s about time I asked what needed to be asked.

“Sorry, but you need to tell us about your time living as Zenon.”

“I understand. I believe there’s a lot I need to talk about.”

It seems she retained memories even while possessed, so I wanted her to disclose the knowledge gained during that time.

They must be memories she’d rather forget, but she understood there was no helping it.

“After that, though, it’s up to you. How do you want to live?”

“What a cruel question… Freedom… I am free now, that’s true. But that freedom has no future. I have nowhere to go, no one to rely on, no money. My body doesn’t move as I want, and my gender has even changed… Frankly, I’m stuck.”

Her body not moving properly is because her status was taken by the possessor, leaving her with stats no better than a newborn child.

Strictly speaking, I took the stats, but even if I hadn’t, they would have vanished along with Zenon anyway. From the beginning, nothing was left for the current Zenon.

“I don’t want to die. But living as I am now is unimaginably difficult. And I have no choices left. Please, help me. I’ll do anything I can. I don’t need freedom. Please give me a future.”

With that, Zenon-chan bowed deeply.

Mio looked at me with an expression that seemed to say, “I knew it would come to this.”

After that, it followed the usual flow, and Zenon-chan was enslaved.

When told to become a slave, she muttered shyly, “I see… so becoming a woman means that kind of thing too…” but in the end, she agreed.

“I’m prepared. But I only have knowledge as a man, so please don’t expect very feminine reactions.”

That resolve might be a bit too quick.

And after being taught various things, this was her reaction:

“Haha… no wonder that monster was no match. To make enemies of people like you… that monster really was foolish.”

Using the name Zenon as-is would be problematic, so I instructed her to go by “Non.”

“So you’ll still use ‘boku’ as your first-person pronoun?”

“…Yes. I understand I have no choice but to live as a woman. Please consider this my last bit of resistance… no, more like the leftover scraps of Zenon.”

“Well, it has its own flavor, and I don’t really mind.”

Thus, the creation of boku-girl Non-chan was complete.

After that, Non-chan, who had been naked the whole time, was dressed up by the women.

With good base material to begin with, she was put into cute, frilly outfits.

Non-chan’s eyes were dead as the women did as they pleased.

The remnants of masculinity were being ground away with a grinding sound. At that point, it was over for him as a man. Farewell, manhood.

Afterward, Non provided information about the possessor.

Since she only had memories from after being possessed, she didn’t know the circumstances of her initial dealings with the Demon Race, but there were still some results that could properly be called achievements.

For example, the reason Elgare was attacked.

As Zenon had said during the assault, the attack was ordered by the Demon Race, or rather, the Demon King.

The goal was to neutralize Linforce’s “Blessing of the Divine Domain” while annihilating the Heroes.

By sending in Zenon, who wielded overwhelming power, and the Final Trial, which had the trait of being unkillable by Heroes, simultaneously, they aimed to achieve that.

The reason no Demon Race members were sent was because demons cannot enter Elgare while the Blessing of the Divine Domain is active.

Additionally, while Zenon had possessed the “Existence Possession” ability beforehand, the “Creeping Bloodstain” was a curse mark he received from the Demon Race specifically for the Elgare assault.

The one who granted the curse mark was an unidentified demon wearing a black robe. Even the possessor didn’t know the details. However, all instructions given to Zenon came from that “Black Robe.”

Furthermore, it was also Zenon who had ordered the attack on Castal within the Kingdom of Sanokia.

The purpose was to ensure the success of the Elgare assault.

He hadn’t told anyone else about the Demon Race, and even if he brought ordinary soldiers along, it was uncertain whether they would follow orders. Cooperation with the Demon Race is that heavily shunned.

So instead, he decided to clash with Castal, a force that warranted caution.

He also told us about underestimating Queen’s Knight Gene as insignificant, judging Scarlet to be at least his equal, and therefore accelerating the Elgare assault.

Hearing all that, Zenon actually seems surprisingly narrow-minded, or at least sloppy in his planning.

After hearing everything, we also discussed Non-chan’s future treatment.

She has a fair amount of knowledge, but since Zenon deemed her unnecessary, she never received proper education, leaving many gaps in her basic knowledge.

That made things concerning, so I instructed her to redo her studies at the labyrinth orphanage.

I’ve given her stats equivalent to a normal child, so she should be able to live an ordinary life.

Finally, I explained Non-chan’s unique innate skill, which even the possessor didn’t know about.

[King’s Majesty]

Greatly inflicts hindrance effects on inferior opponents. If the gap is large enough, they will be unable to resist the user’s commands.

Debuffs for those below her. And for those even further below, it grants forced command authority.

It’s an extremely powerful unique skill, but Non-chan made a deeply bitter expression…

“At this point, being called a king… I don’t want it, so you can have it.”

She gave it to me.

That aside, here’s something we mustn’t forget.

Meteor Staff: Shooting Star

Category: Long Staff

Rarity: Mythical

Notes: Indestructible, Owner-Bound, MP Charge, Automatic MP Charge, Greatly Enhances All-Attribute Magic, Simultaneous Spellcasting

Charge Rate: 300%

Ruler’s Staff: Alternative

Category: Combat Staff

Rarity: Mythical

Notes: Indestructible, Owner-Bound, Converts Magic Power to Attack Power, Greatly Increases All Stats, MP Boost

Sakura’s “Star Staff: Stardust” evolved into “Meteor Staff: Shooting Star”, and Dora’s “Ruler’s Staff: Replica” evolved into “Ruler’s Staff: Alternative.”

Naturally, both of them gained the “Transcendent” title and the Transcend skill.

The “MP Charge” of Meteor Staff: Shooting Star functions the same as before, storing MP. “Automatic MP Charge” slowly absorbs MP from the atmosphere.

Apparently, it also has a bonus effect of being especially effective when used against spirits, which are masses of MP.

Ruler’s Staff: Alternative’s “Converts Magic Power to Attack Power” works as before, adding magic power (not MP, but magic attack power) to attack power. In addition, “MP Boost” allows for high-powered strikes by consuming MP.

In terms of instant firepower using weapons, Dora’s single strike might now be the strongest.

《I probably won’t get a chance to use it.》

“It’s clearly overkill… If anything, we’re moving toward figuring out how to fight while lowering our stats…”

Yes. Exactly as the two of them say.

Our own stats have skyrocketed so much that we’d have to significantly lower them to have a proper fight.

In this state, even if weapon specs increase, there’s no real opportunity to use them.

We use the convenience effects of Mythical equipment, but almost never the power or performance boosts. It’s overkill…

《But I’m happy it fits my hand better.》

“Yes… it’s become easier to use than before… This must be what owner-bound exclusive equipment means…”

That “Owner-Bound” is the most popular feature is kind of sad.

“But it’s a shame Dora’s shield didn’t get strengthened along with it.”

《Yeah. That’s too bad.》

Since Dora’s staff and shield aren’t a set, only the staff was strengthened, leaving the shield unchanged. We expected it, but it’s still disappointing.

If Dora defeats the next Final Trial, will the shield get strengthened too?

A: It will. However, the Transcend skill and title will be wasted.

That’s the problem. We can’t just lend the weapon to someone else to substitute, either. It’s a tricky situation. I’ll think about it before the next Final Trial.

Let’s talk a bit about Scarlet as well.

Actually, Scarlet bent the rules a bit when attending this conference.

Specifically, he flew freely over other nations territory without permission. Riding a dragonkin, he took the shortest route to the Kingdom of Elgant. That’s an issue.

When we travel as national representatives, we don’t use dragonkin or inferior wind dragons, right?

From what I heard later, Scarlet wasn’t charged with any crime over it.

The reason he rushed to attend the conference was to become a Hero-supporting nation. Given that, the countries he passed over judged it unavoidable.

Additionally, his contributions in the battle against Zenon were also recognized.

He plans to enjoy an unobstructed aerial journey on the way back as well.

He also told Sakuya he would be sending formal documents.

That would be regarding inquiries about dragonkin.

First, she’ll explain things in writing, and if necessary, arrange a direct meeting.

If possible, I’d like to visit the Crimson Empire too (a bit late for that).

It’s about time I’ve run out of things to explain regarding the Kingdom of Elgant.

After concluding our event-packed stay in the Kingdom of Elgant, we returned to the Kingdom of Castal.

The return trip was by carriage as far as the Kingdom of Sanokia, then by inferior flying dragon from there. We obtained permission and had the inferior flying dragons on standby.

…Of course, that was a retroactive setting. Since the top of Sanokia is under my control, I can arrange any story I want.

At present, we’re heading for the Sanokia border alongside the carriages of the Kingdom of Sanokia and the Kingdom of Estea.

…Ah, right. There were others too.

“Is something the matter?”

“…Did you need something?”

Shippouin and Kino tilted their heads at my gaze.

“No, it’s nothing.”

In fact, the seventeen former Heroes who became my slaves are traveling with us as well.

As a result of the summit conference, it was decided that Sanokia would take them in as Heroes.

Sanokia was already a Hero-supporting nation and had friendly relations with the Heroes, so no country objected to Sanokia taking in all seventeen.

Apparently, the remaining Heroes, whose leader figures all disappeared at once, voiced some minor dissatisfaction, but…

As you can probably guess, Sanokia taking in all seventeen was my doing.

I considered distributing them across nations like spies, but I had no expectations for the other Heroes. To ensure the Demon King’s defeat, I decided to keep all seventeen in one place.

And since Queen Ekaterina of Sanokia is under my control, having Sanokia host them would make operations easier.

Partway through Sanokia, we parted ways with Prince Luan of the Kingdom of Estea, Ekaterina of the Kingdom of Sanokia, and the seventeen former Heroes.

“Queen Sakuya, thank you very much for everything. I will repay this debt someday.”

“Mm. I look forward to the day we meet again, Lord Ruan.”

“This is where we part ways as well. From here on, we must proceed with even greater caution.”

Most likely, the Kingdom of Estea will now be the weakest in terms of military power.

While the royals exchanged farewells, we also said goodbye to the former Heroes.

“Shindou-sama, should you require anything, please call upon us at any time.”

“Yeah. I’ll probably be asking for a lot, so count on it.”

“…Top priority.”

“Yes. I will fulfill it, even at the cost of my life.”

As always, Maria-like.

Over there, Dora and Lassie were glaring sparks at each other. …A battle for the pet slot?

After separating from the Sanokia and Estea groups, we continued by carriage for a while, then summoned the inferior wind dragon once we reached an unpopulated area.

From here, it’s a straight shot back to the Kingdom of Castal by inferior flying dragon.

The horses will return at a leisurely pace later.

One week has passed since we returned to Castal.

It was a week of free activity to recover from the long journey.

That said, Sakuya and the others were busy with work that piled up during their absence, so they were even busier than usual. Naturally, the terminals went with them.

Don’t we need at least one more Vega terminal?

As for Rico, the dwarf Hero we took into our fold in the Kingdom of Elgant, she’s currently undergoing maid training and combat training nonstop.

Her immediate goal is to become strong enough to change the results of future sight on her own.

I plan to let her continue training until she’s satisfied, but what comes after that is undecided. Her abilities suit guard duty, but personally, she wants to fight on the front lines.

Why are all local Heroes so violent…?

Around the fifth day, a letter arrived from Scarlet.

It felt rather fast, but there was a reason for that… he used Advance Trading Company’s mail service.

In this world, postal services for letters are astonishingly underdeveloped. The dangers along the roads and the lack of developed land transportation are the main reasons.

In that environment, Advance Trading Company finally entered the postal business.

…No, considering my and Sakura’s abilities, this is an absurdly easy way to make money, right?

With Portal or Infinite Storage, there are countless methods.

You could even just fly on an inferior wind dragon.

And for the destination, you just check the map. Easy?

The price is outrageously high, they only handle letters, identity verification is required, and the conditions are strict. However, since delivery within a few days is guaranteed as long as there’s an Advance Trading Company branch in the destination town, it’s doing very well.

From the perspective of someone who knows the mechanics, it’s a blatant rip-off.

So that’s why Scarlet paid a large sum to send a letter to Sakuya in Castal.

Sakuya is compiling information about dragonkin and will send a reply. Despite already being busy, she looked on the verge of tears at the additional workload.

The maids will help. For a fee.

And so, that leisurely vacation period passed, but unfortunately, it only lasted one week.

On this day, I was engaged in my recently established routine: interacting with the mermaid princess.

Leila has sworn absolute obedience to me, but the reason for that is largely fear.

I want to get along with the monsters I tame, so I’ve been trying to engage in physical contact, but it hasn’t been going well.

Yesterday, I tried holding her, but perhaps the fear exceeded her limit while being held, because she wet herself

Then, crying, she whispered, “I’m sorry… please don’t kill me…”

That’s a problem. So today, to help her get used to me, I was focusing on conversation at a moderate distance.

When the first impression is fear, recovery is hard.

Anyway, back to the point.

While deepening my ties with Leila, I received a telepathic message from Sakuya.

Alta’s reports and Sakuya’s telepathy are triggers for events (game-brain).

《Big Brother. We’ve received an invitation from the Regalia Beastman Nation asking to host us as state guests… What should we do?》

---

Crimson Empire? Scarlet already appeared, so that’s enough, right?
