## **144.5 Advance Trading Company**

**AN:** This time, I will introduce the reputation of the Advance Trading Company mentioned in the main story, from a slightly unusual perspective.

---

My name is Jennifer. I am a highly skilled female spy. I am 19 years old and single.

At present, I have been commissioned by a certain trading company to investigate the Advance Trading Company.

The Advance Trading Company is the name of a trading company that has developed rapidly over the past few months.

Its main branch is located in a prime area of Quindam, the royal capital of the Kingdom of Castal. The head of the company is a woman named Lucea. Shortly before the establishment of the Advance Trading Company, a female Queen’s knight with the same name went missing, but whether the two are connected is unknown. There is also no definitive proof that they are the same person.

At first, I thought the purpose might be to dispatch merchants under the influence of the Castal royal family to various regions to gather information on other countries, but even so, it is unclear why a Queen’s knight would be used. She hardly seems suitable for the role.

Since the background of the company’s owner is not a particularly high priority for the investigation, I decided to put that aside for now.

No, let me be honest.

At this point, the investigation into the Advance Trading Company has made almost no progress at all.

There are virtually no channels through which to obtain information.

I cannot speak with employees. The company is not registered with the merchants guild, and its applications to the city are kept to the bare minimum. Infiltrating the interior of the building is impossible, to put it lightly.

In the first place, neither the stores nor the employees reveal their origins.

One day, seemingly out of nowhere, an Advance Trading Company store is constructed, and it is already staffed with a sufficient number of employees. From what I have heard, not a single one of them is a local.

And all employees are extremely tight-lipped, leaking absolutely no unnecessary information.

One of my colleagues attempted to infiltrate the company by becoming an employee, but was reportedly rejected outright, without even being given a chance.

This was not because her identity as a spy had been exposed. Rather, the Advance Trading Company does not recruit employees at all. Even local residents cannot become employees.

It is practically the only complaint that can be raised against the otherwise well-regarded Advance Trading Company.

Yes, the Advance Trading Company has an extremely good reputation.

In particular, it enjoys overwhelming support from the residents of the cities where it operates.

So much so that there are many people who want to become employees, as mentioned earlier.

There are many reasons why the Advance Trading Company is so well regarded.

It is often said that they rarely run out of stock, that their product selection is excellent, and that their quality is stable and consistent.

And yet, they do not forget to be considerate toward other shops.

Specifically, for goods that are already sold in that city, they set their prices slightly higher. In other words, the items are not unavailable at the Advance Trading Company, but it is more economical to buy them elsewhere.

Basically, the Advance Trading Company focuses on goods that are difficult to obtain in that particular region. Moreover, those main products are sold at the “appropriate price of the region where the goods originate.”

Considering transportation costs, it seems like they would be operating at a loss, but this appears to be a core principle of the Advance Trading Company, and it is strictly upheld at all of their locations.

The fact that items normally hard to obtain in that region can be purchased more cheaply than the local market price is one of the reasons the Advance Trading Company is so well supported.

Incidentally, even after investigating, the routes by which they procure their goods remain unknown. This is the single biggest reason the investigation has stalled.

As an aside, although I mentioned that items available at other shops are priced higher, there are still plenty of customers who choose to buy them at the Advance Trading Company.

Because the quality of their products is consistently high, many people are willing to pay a little extra.

On the other hand, they show no consideration at all toward shops whose quality is significantly inferior. They seem quite strict when it comes to a lack of corporate effort.

This request comes from one of the country’s leading trading companies, which lost many customers to the Advance Trading Company due to such a lack of effort.

They want some leverage to threaten the Advance Trading Company.

To be honest, it is a rather pathetic request, but since they pay well, I accepted it. Still, after only one week, I am already completely stuck.

Now then, once again today, I am investigating the Advance Trading Company.

I noticed a banner standing in front of the store I frequent.

I approached and read it. …What? “We have started a postal service”, it says?

And not just within the city. As long as there is an Advance Trading Company store, you can send items across cities and even across national borders? That is impossible…

Upon checking more closely, the price is quite high. However, it is not so expensive as to be completely out of reach.

There are many restrictions: both the sender and recipient must have verified identities, and items other than letters cannot be sent. Still, if the conditions are met, delivery will be completed within a few days.

This makes that rumor seem far more plausible.

Because the Advance Trading Company’s product selection is simply too good, a certain rumor has been circulating.

That rumor is that “the Advance Trading Company possesses a teleportation-type magical tool.”

When it comes to teleportation-type magical tools, the Kingdom of Estea’s labyrinth-exclusive item, the “Phase Transition Stone”, is famous. …In fact, I have never heard of any others.

The rumor spread from the idea that the Advance Trading Company owns some unknown teleportation-type magical tool, allowing them to achieve their astonishing inventory.

No one in my line of work has obtained proof, but otherwise their selection is impossible to explain.

Normally, if it were known that such a magical tool existed, the country would not stay silent. It would undoubtedly be a national-treasure-class magical tool.

And yet, there is no country that has demanded the Advance Trading Company hand over such a tool.

This is not just a rumor, but an actual incident.

A certain country within the At Confederation reportedly demanded that the rumored magical tool be handed over.

The very next day, all Advance Trading Company stores in that country vanished without a trace.

Since then, I have not heard of the Advance Trading Company building any stores in that country.

Because the Advance Trading Company had already established a firm position by that point, the country that was abandoned by them suffered a severe loss of trust from surrounding nations.

The Advance Trading Company has an extreme aversion to interference from those in power, and if influential figures in a country or city attempt to use their authority against them, the company will withdraw from that land without hesitation. Without leaving a single trace.

I have also never heard of any interference from other trading companies, for example, achieving any success.

For instance, there was a trading company that hired thugs to obstruct their business. Those thugs were thrown around by a company employee wearing a maid outfit, suffered broken bones, and were then handed over to the military police after the entire incident was recorded with a magical recording device.

After some time, that trading company was exposed for wrongdoing and shut down. It is said that someone provided information, though the truth has not been revealed. Still, people have their suspicions.

Company employees live in residences attached to the stores, and for some reason, they are said to be absurdly strong, making attacks impossible. Since the distribution routes of goods are unknown, ambushing shipments is impossible to begin with.

Conversely, there are cases where the Advance Trading Company is completely ignored.

There was a trading company that succeeded in spreading bad rumors about the Advance Trading Company and driving away customers.

It worked because the city was poorly informed about outside matters. However, that Advance Trading Company store never closed.

Over time, the company interacted with the townspeople, and before anyone realized it, that trading company had lost its customers.

Additionally, the product that trading company had monopolized was sold by the Advance Trading Company not at an inflated price, but at a fair price, roughly the same as before, and the difference in quality completely turned the tables.

Moreover, they apparently maintain their own blacklist, and anyone who causes trouble related to trading companies is refused entry at their stores even in other cities.

What is terrifying is that this blacklist is openly published.

Being publicly labeled as a person of concern by a trading company famous for honest business practices has an influence that cannot be underestimated. It is, quite literally, a public execution. I phrased that pretty well just now.

Furthermore, once someone is placed on the blacklist, there is no mercy. I have never heard of the Advance Trading Company accepting anyone back, no matter how sincerely they apologize.

…When I think about it calmly, am I not doing something extremely dangerous right now?

All right. Once I report the investigation results up to today, I will withdraw from this job.

I will have to pay a penalty, but I have a bad feeling about this. In this line of work, it is better not to ignore your instincts.

“Oh my, is that Jennifer over there?”

I was startled when someone suddenly called out to me, but I recognized the voice and felt relieved as I turned around.

“So it is you, Clara. …What is with that outfit?”

She is Clara. A colleague of the same generation as me, and someone I have competed with many times.

However, her clothing is strange. Because Clara is wearing the maid uniform worn by Advance Trading Company employees.

On top of that, she is holding shopping bags filled to the brim with groceries.

“Did you manage to get into the Advance Trading Company?”

Clara was the colleague who previously tried to infiltrate the Advance Trading Company as an employee.

I had not seen her recently, but since she is wearing the company’s maid uniform, did she succeed?

However, this area should not have been within her usual range of activity.

“Well, yes. You could say I got in. But I have already washed my hands of my previous line of work, so it does not really matter anymore.”

“You always said it was your calling, just like me. And that way of speaking, too…”

She used to be a spy just like me, speaking bluntly and without a trace of charm. She said she would live as a spy and die as a spy.

She was definitely not the kind of woman who would smile brightly, carry shopping bags, and speak to acquaintances in a feminine tone.

“Well, it is customer service, so of course I fix the way I speak. And besides, even though I am not one to talk, you should not call that kind of job your calling.”

Clara scolded me.

This woman is not the Clara I know.

“People who do work in the shadows have no human rights…”

She looked like she was smiling, but there was deep darkness in her eyes.

What happened to Clara!?

“I-I have somewhere to be, so excuse me!”

“Oh, that is too bad. Well then, see you.”

I was frightened and ran away from the scene.

The mornings at the Advance Trading Company start early.

For someone like me who is nocturnal, working from early morning was hard, but after continuing for a week, I got used to it.

“Jennifer, please arrange those products over there.”

“Yes! Understood, Clara-senpai!”

Following Clara-senpai’s instructions, I swish my skirt and head toward the potion display shelves.

At first, I was not used to the maid uniform, but after wearing the skirt for two weeks straight, I have grown accustomed to it.

Thanks to relentless practice, I can now serve customers with a smile, and I have learned how to deal with improper customers. Getting used to a gentle, feminine demeanor and manner of speech was the hardest part.

After one week of conditioning and one week of training, I finally became a true Advance Trading Company employee yesterday, even if I am at the very bottom.

I cannot thank Clara-senpai enough for putting my punishment on hold by becoming my instructor.

I can never return to spy-like work again. A “no-human-rights” job like that is far too terrifying to continue. I have had enough of seeing hell.

“Clara-senpai, I am finished over here.”

“Whew, that means we are done preparing to open.”

We will open in just a few minutes.

We had to prepare some new products at the last minute, but I am glad everything worked out.

We wait in front of the doors.

At the Advance Trading Company, there are quite a few customers who come first thing in the morning to see the merchandise.

-Garan garan-

The time comes, and the shop doors open.

“Welcome. Welcome to the Advance Trading Company.”

Now then, let us work honestly again today.

---

**AN:** Next, I will post another short story on the 24th.

That one will be a side story.

After that, I will post the character list and settings, and if I can manage the writing schedule, I will post a longer short story.

## **Side Story 11: Recollections of the Dungeon Master (2)**

**AN:** The East short stories are planned to proceed roughly in this format.

---

“Cheers!” x3

At the call for a toast, Shindo, Azuma, and Asai clink their glasses filled with juice.

Today is Christmas.

With the town bustling, the three of them are having a Christmas party at the Shindo household.

“Hey, why are three guys having a Christmas party anyway…”

“Asai, are you really making that comment now?”

At Asai’s entirely reasonable question, Azuma looks at him with an exasperated expression.

“We had nothing else to do, so the three of us got together to do something Christmas-like and kill time. That was the idea, right? And you didn’t object either, did you, Asai?”

“Yeah, I get that, but it’s even less glamorous than I expected. Or rather, it’s kind of bleak…”

On the table are cake, drinks, chicken, and the like.

Neither Shindo nor Azuma can cook at all, and Asai cannot make anything serious either, so everything was store-bought.

Shindo, riding the mood, had needlessly decorated the room, so the atmosphere itself was flashy. Because of that, the oppressiveness of it being three guys only stood out even more.

“If so, why not make use of your specialty network and gather some women right now, Asai?”

“No, calling people over on Christmas Day itself is pushing it.”

Asai shakes his head in response to Azuma’s light jab.

“But you’re popular, Asai. Even if you suddenly called them over, it feels like you could gather one or two.”

“If girls showed up just for me, the atmosphere would freeze instantly… If anything, each of us would have to bring a girl for the balance to work.”

Even Asai does not have the courage to be the only one bringing a girl to a gathering of guys.

“I refuse. I do not have a girlfriend, and the only ones who approach me are honey traps backed by overseas corporations. Yes, it is unpleasant!”

“Even geniuses have it rough…”

Shindo can only give a wry smile at that.

“I keep saying I want to live a normal student life, but no one ever listens. Really, I wish they would knock it off already.”

“Well, I’ve heard from all over that technology development is being delayed because Tomei is living the student life. For people like that, your current situation is hard to overlook.”

If Azuma were to get serious, there is no doubt that progress in the technological field would accelerate. Quite a few people would like him to quit being a student and work at his own company instead.

And to add to that, this tendency is stronger overseas than in Japan, and Azuma’s route to school has an unnaturally high number of foreign women with great bodies.

“I suspect this house is being watched as well.”

“Yeah, they are. I saw a few.”

“So you noticed. If you called them, they would probably come, you know? Absolutely not that I would call them, though.”

“I am also a bit reluctant to let unknown foreign women into my house…”

Shindo, the homeowner, also shows reluctance. Naturally so.

“If we are talking about someone else we could invite, perhaps Asai’s little sister, Hijiri-chan?”

“…Do you understand how I would feel if you invited my own sister as the centerpiece of the party? Besides, she is at a different Christmas party, so it is impossible.”

“That is unfortunate. She would have been perfect for teasing Asai.”

“You bastard, Tomei…”

Azuma mutters, “It would have been perfect with Hijiri on Holy Night.”

“Still, that would mean I am the only one with no prospect of inviting a woman. How sad.”

Since Asai and Azuma could invite women if they did not choose, Shindo was feeling a sense of being left out.

“Huh, Jin is saying that?”

“Being oblivious is truly frightening…”

Shindo is looked at by the two as if he were something strange.

“Hm? What do you mean?”

Not understanding at all, Shindo tilts his head.

“As far as I know, within the school alone there are seventeen… no, eighteen. And that is not even counting outside of school, yet you have not noticed at all…”

“Even I noticed… Sensitive to hostility, but dull to affection. What kind of protagonist is that…”

“Well, whether it is pure affection is debatable.”

“Indeed. If anything, what those girls have is almost fai… no, perhaps it is better left unsaid.”

“What are you even talking about!”

Even though it is about him, Shindo cannot understand at all and raises his voice.

“Jin, for example, what would you do if a woman confessed to you? A female classmate, or even an upperclassman, underclassman, or teacher would do.”

Without answering Shindo’s question, Asai throws one back at him.

“Why out of the blue? …Well, I would probably turn her down. If I got a girlfriend, the time the three of us hang out would decrease. At least until we graduate high school, having fun comes first.”

“…For me, being able to have fun properly probably only lasts through high school.”

“Yeah. There is no way they would wait until university.”

Azuma’s excellence is at a level that affects the development of the world itself.

Asking to add another four years of a mere hobby like student life would be difficult.

In the worst case, they might resort to force. And that could lead to a bloody conflict after a counterattack.

Azuma understands this as well, which is why he is enjoying the student life he can only have now, and his time with Shindo and Asai, to the fullest.

It is not that Shindo has no interest in women, but having fun with Asai and Azuma is even more enjoyable, and combined with the time limit, his priorities have been decided.

“If Azuma’s situation were not a thing, and we could keep hanging out after graduating high school, maybe I would have made a girlfriend or something. No, even then I might have put fun first and postponed romance…”

“How much do you like having fun, Jin… I feel sorry for the romance being postponed.”

“At least until I cannot hang out with you two anymore, it comes later.”

“That could easily be ten years or so, right?”

The two smile wryly at Shindo’s outrageous statement.

“But it is also hard to imagine Jin growing old and becoming unable to move.”

“If anything, I cannot imagine Shindo dying.”

“Ah, I kind of get that.”

“You are making me sound inhuman… Speaking of which, Azuma, you seem like you would live on endlessly as just a brain. Inside a glass tube, soaked in preservative.”

“Who are you calling the final boss?”

“Ah, I get that too.”

“On the other hand, Asai seems like he would die happily surrounded by his grandchildren.”

“So I am the only normal one!?”

“Yes. You seem like you would have the most ordinary death.”

“Should I be happy about that!? Or sad!?”

No one knows the answer.

“From overseas corporations to being the president of an otherworld labyrinth. You never know what will happen in life.”

“Azuma-sama, what is shacho?”

“Kyui?”

At Azuma’s murmur after having a dream of his original world for the first time in a while, Kana, the labyrinth caretaker beside him, and Shiro, the horned rabbit, voice their questions.

“Sorry. I just had a dream about my original world for the first time in a while.”

“Azuma-sama, whenever you dream of your original world, you always make a comment first thing in the morning, do you not?”

“Is that so? Perhaps it leaves that strong an impression.”

“Kyui!”

This kind of thing had happened many times before, and Kana had gradually gotten used to it.

Toward Azuma, who happily talks about his original world, she harbors complicated feelings, yet because Azuma looks happy, she cannot say anything. It is a rather touching situation.

“So, what kind of dream was it this time?”

“Well… if I had to say, it was a story about talking over the future. Come to think of it, the content was hardly what one would call sensible…”

“Kyui?”

Is talking about living eternally after removing one’s brain really something that can be considered a discussion of future dreams?

“Future dreams, you say. Is that shacho you mentioned earlier your dream, Azuma-sama?”

“No, being a president is not really a dream. Also, could you stop saying shacho in broken speech? It reminds me of honey traps…”

“? …Understood. I will not say it anymore.”

Even without understanding, Kana seems to have sensed something.

They have been together for quite a long time now, so she can roughly read Azuma’s emotions from his expression.

Azuma seemed to be suppressing a very, very sad emotion.

What kind of honey trap could make Azuma this sad?

Kana was very curious, but could not bring herself to ask.

“In the end, I never had time for romance, but perhaps I should think that it was good I could at least play at raising children.”

“You mean the Estea royal family? Speaking of which, why did you decide to entrust the governance of this country to someone not even related to you by blood? And on top of that, you went out of your way to raise an orphan…”

The first king of the Kingdom of Estea was originally an orphan.

He deliberately did not make him a labyrinth caretaker, but raised him normally and made him the king of the country built atop the labyrinth.

“I cannot have children, so it is like a substitute.”

Due to something like a side effect of being transported to another world, Azuma can no longer have children.

He cannot leave behind his blood, but at least wanted to leave behind a child-like existence to future generations.

“(That is truly regrettable…)”

“Did you say something?”

“No, nothing at all.”

Kana, who remains in the young appearance she had when she became a labyrinth caretaker, but is already mentally beyond an adult, seems to have various thoughts regarding Azuma.

“That said, in that sense, Kana is also like a daughter to me.”

“(That is really, truly regrettable!)”

“Did you say something…”

“No! Nothing at all!”

“I-I see… If you say so…”

“Kyuu…”

Shiro lets out a small cry, as if to comfort Kana.

“…Kana, what is the meaning of this?”

To Azuma, Kana is a labyrinth caretaker he has been with for a long time and an irreplaceable presence, but from time to time she does things so outlandish that even Azuma cannot understand them.

“B-baby.”

How should one react when a woman you have known for a long time is waiting in your room dressed as a baby and sitting in a cradle?

Incidentally, Kana’s apparent age is around ten, and she had already experienced menarche before becoming a labyrinth caretaker.

“Could this be because of that recent child-rearing conversation…”

“!?” B-baby. Kana is a baby, so she does not know what you are talking about, baby.”

As a woman, Kana has already given up on being seen as one.

If so, she resolved to at least try to soothe Azuma’s boredom. It truly was an outlandish decision.

“Kana, how old are you this year?”

“…Baby. I am a newborn zero-year-old baby.”

“…”

She became a labyrinth caretaker at the apparent age of ten.

And from there, they have been together for fifty years.

Azuma approaches Kana, pats her on the shoulder, and shakes his head.

“Kana, I appreciate the sentiment, but that is not what I meant. …You must be tired too. I am sorry I did not notice.”

“Eh?”

“I saw nothing. I am going out for a walk for a bit, so while I am gone…”

“Eh…?”

Saying that, Azuma leaves the room.

Left behind, Kana turns red, then pale, and then makes up her mind.

“(Shindo-sama, Asai-sama. It is because of you two that I ended up dressed like this! Someday, please let me punch you once!)”

If Kana ever met those two while she was alive, she would punch them once, at least.

Kana strongly swore so in her heart.

…Is this really Shindo and Asai’s fault?

“Kyui…”

---

**AN:** Exactly half a year away from Christmas today.

This could already be called Christmas without exaggeration, right? That is why it contains a bit of Christmas material.

## **Characters Appearing in Volume 9**

**AN:** Yes, yes, don’t say “Is this a character introduction?”

Tomorrow I’ll be posting the settings, or rather a summary/list.

Can settings be posted separately?

---

Basically, only characters whose names actually appeared in the main story. Skills are excluded.

Information that was not explicitly stated is excluded.

**Protagonist Side**

Name: Leila

Gender: Female

Age: 3

Race: Mermaid

Titles: Jin’s Familiar of Benevolence, Mermaid Princess

Notes: A mermaid girl tamed in a forest within the Kingdom of Sanokia. Her appearance resembles a girl in her mid-teens, but her speech and behavior match her actual age, creating a very mismatched impression. After being subjected to Jin’s pranks, her fear exceeded its limit, and she chose submission and being tamed. As a result, unlike Jin’s other familiars, fear occupies the highest position in her feelings toward him. She has no dissatisfaction with being kept by Jin, but whenever Jin approaches, her heart will not stop pounding. …Is this love?

Name: Rico

Gender: Female

Age: 15

Race: Dwarf

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Dwarf Hero

Notes: A local Hero possessing precognitive abilities. Heroes are already prone to misfortune, and she ended up acquiring an extra, unnecessary skill on top of that. Learning that power could change the future she foresaw, she developed an intense craving for strength. As a concrete form of that strength, she chose to prioritize speed. She works as a maid, and her main weapons are concealed tools. She has various items hidden under her skirt. For now, she is the oldest among the Heroes, but because she is a dwarf, she looks the youngest.

Name: Ekaterina

Gender: Female

Age: 15

Race: Human

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Queen of the Kingdom of Sanokia, Emissary of Saki

Notes: First appearance was in Volume 3, “Side Story Episode 4: The Sword Saintess.” At the time of the side story, she was referred to as a “priest.” She is a companion of Mizuhara Saki, Jin’s childhood friend, and became queen of the Kingdom of Sanokia through a coup. She was the king’s illegitimate child and raised in a temple, but when she was about to be caught up in a noble conspiracy, she was saved by Saki. Since then, she has devotedly adored her as “Big Sister.” Her purpose in attending the summit was to offer herself to Jin in accordance with Saki’s instructions. She does not harbor even the slightest doubt about this.

Name: Unknown (Ekaterina’s Bodyguard)

Gender: Female

Notes: Like Ekaterina, her first appearance was in Volume 3, “Side Story Episode 4: The Sword Saintess.” In the side story, she was referred to as a “knight”, “scout”, “mage”, and “hunter.” In the end, her name never appeared here either. Originally a member of Saki’s party, she now serves as Ekaterina’s bodyguard. She came together with Ekaterina to offer herself to Jin.

Name: Aichi Kino

Gender: Female

Age: 16

Race: Human (Otherworlder)

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Transferee, Hero of Another World

Notes: First appearance was in Volume 6, “Side Story Episode 8: Behind the Start of the War.” A girl who was saved by Jin in her original world and has believed in him ever since. Also known as one of “Earth’s Marias.” Codename: “No-Pan.” Her Blessing as a Hero was \<Ten People, Ten Colors>. She died during the Elgare assault and safely became Jin’s slave. A Japanese-doll-like, traditional-style beauty, and because of her high support capabilities, she is popular among the Heroes. However, she has no interest in anyone other than Jin, so it is meaningless. Taciturn.

Name: Kanna Shippouin

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Human (Otherworlder)

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Transferee, Hero of Another World

Notes: Her basic setup is almost the same as Aichi Kino’s. Codename: “Omorashi.” Her Blessing is \<Noble Attraction>. She also becomes Jin’s slave after dying. A young lady from a prestigious family, a versatile character who can do anything. With charisma as well, she is truly queen-like. She is packed with traits that could be called mandatory in a school harem story. However, she has no interest in the queen’s seat; rather, she wants to kneel before Jin. She would not mind being stepped on. She would even lick his feet.

Name: Zenon Granz

Gender: Female

Age: 9

Race: Human

Titles: Jin’s Slave, King of the Kingdom of Granz

Notes: One of the heavily loaded characters. Born female, but immediately after birth, her body was taken over by the first emperor, who possessed a possession ability. The first emperor was connected to the demon race and became the perpetrator of the Elgare assault. After being forcibly exorcised by Jin, she returned to her original personality, but since she had believed herself to be male, she is confused by the sudden change in sex. In a sense, she can be described as a girl who was raised as a boy. Not particularly fond of TS, but this one is fairly likable.

Name: Mei Igarashi

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Human (Otherworlder)

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Transferee, Hero of Another World

Notes: Her basic setup is almost the same as Aichi Kino’s. Codename: “Lassie.” Her Blessing has not been disclosed, but it is a physical ability enhancement type. After dying, she becomes Jin’s slave, or rather, pet. In her original world, she was a high school girl athlete who set high school records in track and field. She grew up poor and was supported by Jin, being treated as a pet. Unlike the other believer Heroes, she did not choose her school to follow Jin; she was scouted, and Jin happened to be there. During her pet days, Jin saw every inch of her body.

Name: Unknown (Hero Believers of Jin)

Gender: Female

Notes: Fourteen female Heroes who were saved by Jin in their original world and came to believe in him. Their backgrounds vary widely, including a female teacher, a student teacher, and a ten-year-old child prodigy who skipped grades, but since they are essentially padding, their names do not appear unless there is a strong demand.

**Kingdom of Castal**

Name: Rudolf

Gender: Male

Race: Human

Notes: Commonly known as the “Gut-Punch Minister” (listed as “The minister who threw the gut-punch” in the Volume 2 character introduction). A loyal retainer of Sakuya and the finance minister of Castal. A highly capable individual who has also grasped Jin’s true nature. He has known Sakuya since she was young and thinks of her like a daughter. For Sakuya’s happiness, he wants Jin to take her as his wife. Pro-marriage faction.

Name: Unknown (Castal Elder)

Notes: Elders who accompanied the delegation from Castal. Three men and one woman. They have almost no screen time, and their names never appear. This is because Rudolf worked too hard.

**Elgant Theocracy**

Name: Ann

Alias: Linforth May Elgant

Gender: Female

Age: 1803

Race: High Elf

Titles: Pope of the Elgant Theocracy

Notes: The pope of the Elgant Theocracy and a high elf who has lived for an eternal span of time. Within Elgare, she possesses the skill of immortality and basically never goes outside. She strongly believes in the Goddess and will lose her temper if the Goddess’s actions are insulted. However, during the Elgare assault, her mind breaks due to fear of death.

Name: Kiene

Gender: Female

Age: 201

Race: Elf

Titles: Sword Emperor, S-Rank Adventurer

Notes: An elven swordswoman who inherited the skill \<Sword Emperor>. She relies on tricks, and her actual combat ability is not that high. A friend of the priest, she attempts to kill Jin and the others at the priest’s request. However, Jin shows no interest at all, and she is killed by a proxy Maria.

Name: Salt

Notes: Salt.

Name: Unknown (Priest)

Gender: Male

Race: Elf

Notes: A priest of the Grand Cathedral of Elgare. A fervent worshipper of the Goddess who harbors hatred toward those who killed the Heroes. He repeatedly sends assassins after Jin and the others, but fails every time. In the end, he is killed by Jin as “travel expenses.”

**Kingdom of Estea**

Name: Luan

Gender: Male

Age: 12

Race: Human

Titles: Prince of the Kingdom of Estea

Notes: A prince who came to the summit as the representative of the Kingdom of Estea. The younger brother of Cattleya, one of Jin’s subordinates. He is evaluated highly by Jin, and Luan himself also evaluates Jin. In his heart, he thinks of Jin as his sister’s husband. He vaguely senses his sister’s suspicious behavior, such as going to Jin’s mansion to eat.

**Beastman Nation of Regalia**

Name: Sharon

Gender: Female

Notes: The queen of the Nation of Regalia. Since information has not been released, there is no status display, but it has been stated that she is a beastman with an appearance of roughly the same age as Jin and the others. She overlaps slightly with Kino as a taciturn character, but is fairly muscle-brained. Her mentality matches Jin’s preferences, and she is highly evaluated by him. She has many unrevealed skills, and during her duel with Shippouin, she fought under restrictions. If she were to fight seriously, she could even fight Scarlet… apparently. Attacking Scarlet while restricted was a small mistake.

**Crimson Empire**

Name: Scarlet Crimson

Gender: Male

Age: 38

Race: Human (Reincarnator)

Titles: Transcendent One, Emperor of the Crimson Empire

Notes: Since Jin did not go to the Crimson Empire, a representative came from the Crimson Empire instead. A man who frequently comes up in conversation within the story. His existence was hinted at in Volume 3, Episode 53, meaning he did not appear for 85 episodes. Confident in his eyes, he can see through various things. He has also cleared the final trial and even holds the title of Transcendent One. He is also one of the key characters going forward. However, the next volume is not the Crimson Empire arc.

Name: Kuroa (Real Name: Yoiyami)

Gender: Female

Race: Dragonkin

Titles: A dragonkin who came to the Divine Nation of Elgant together with Scarlet. She was injured in a battle with a dragon and was forced out of the “Dragon Gate”, at which time she lost her memories. She was picked up by Scarlet and harbors feelings for him, but Scarlet refuses to deepen their relationship. “If you act on emotion while you’ve lost your memories, you might regret it once you regain them. If you still say you love me after you get your memories back, then I’ll accept you.”

**Others**

Name: Wind God Tornado

Titles: Demon King’s Familiar

Notes: Mob Final Trial No. 1.

Name: Thunder God Lightning

Titles: Demon King’s Familiar

Notes: Mob Final Trial No. 2.

**AN:** It was a volume where short-story characters kept appearing one after another in the main story.

This kind of thing is fun to do.

I wonder where Kudo-kun went… (from Side Story Episodes 1 and 2). But even so, Kudo.

## **Setting: Jin’s Power Base**

**AN:** This is the first of two consecutive setting posts.

It is a memorandum that can be skipped without any problem.

---

Jin’s sphere of influence as of Volume 9

National Section

Kingdom of Castal

Influence: 99%

– Queen Sakuya is under Jin’s command.

– There are many maids in the royal castle who are under Jin’s command.

– The head office of the Advance Trading Company is located here.

– The A-rank adventurer clan “Saviors” is stationed here.

Kingdom of Estea

Influence: 80%

– Princess Cattleya is under Jin’s command.

- The top authority, the king, is not under his command.

– The labyrinth, which is Estea’s main industry, is under Jin’s control.

– The normally inaccessible areas below the 50th floor of the labyrinth are being privatized.

- In effect, this means he owns land equivalent to more than ten times the territory of the Kingdom of Estea.

– He manages the party of Cynthia, the holder of the labyrinth floor records.

– The Advance Trading Company is expanding into the kingdom.

Kingdom of Narunka (Atto Confederation)

Influence: 100%

– A centrally governed nation, with all royal family members and nobles who were in the capital brought under Jin’s command.

– Villages where Unique Skill holders are likely to be born are protected as important strongholds.

– The Advance Trading Company is expanding into the kingdom.

Dragonkin Hidden Region

Influence: 90%

– Three next-generation chieftain candidates (Dora, Blue, and Leaf) are under Jin’s command.

- The current chieftain, who is the top authority, is not under his command.

– The labyrinth that serves as the hidden region’s “other face” is under Jin’s control.

– The barrier protecting the hidden region is maintained by Jin.

– More than 90 dragonkin are under Jin’s command.

Izumo Wa Kingdom

Influence: 50%

– Princesses Tooru and Kaoru are under Jin’s command.

- The top authority, the king, is not under his command.

– The Advance Trading Company is expanding into the country.

- It is handling the reconstruction after the Oni God incident almost single-handedly.

- As a result, the country has incurred a massive debt.

Former Kingdom of Eldia

Influence: 100%

– The royal family has already been wiped out.

– It has become territory of Castal.

- Management is handled by Jin’s subordinates.

Brown Wall Kingdom

Influence: 100%

– The Advance Trading Company is expanding into the kingdom.

- It greened the desert that had occupied the center of the kingdom and obtained full authority over it.

- Due to prior contracts, it does not even have to pay taxes.

- Ten thousand former citizens of the Kingdom of Eldia are participating in development as slaves of the Advance Trading Company.

– The kingdom depends on the Advance Trading Company for most transportation, food, and other necessities.

– Although not a single member of the royal family has been brought under Jin’s command, the kingdom is effectively under Jin’s control.

Kingdom of Sanokia

Influence: 60%

– Queen Ekaterina is under Jin’s command.

- Her five bodyguards are as well.

– Former Heroes who have become affiliated with the Kingdom of Sanokia are under Jin’s command.

Countries Participating in the Leaders Conference

Influence: 20%

– The top leaders of countries that participated in the leaders’ conference are under Jin’s command.

- Excluding the Elgant Theocracy, the Beastman Kingdom of Regalia, and the Crimson Empire.

– The status of Advance Trading Company expansion differs by country.

Individual Power Section

Advance Trading Company Group

– Belongs to a trading company organized by Jin’s subordinates.

– The company head is nominally Lucea.

– Total membership is approximately ten thousand.

– Stores have been opened in many countries.

Estea Labyrinth Group

– Belongs to the Labyrinth Guardians who maintain and manage the Kingdom of Estea’s labyrinth.

– The person with authority second only to Jin is the Chief Labyrinth Guardian, Caro.

– Total number of Labyrinth Guardians is approximately one thousand.

– Excludes children belonging to the orphanage.

Saviors Group

– Adventurers belonging to the A-rank adventurer clan “Saviors.”

– The clan’s base of operations is the Kingdom of Castal.

– The clan leader is Claude.

– Many members are also explorers of the Estea labyrinth.

Mercenary Group

– Belongs to mercenary bands active mainly in the Atto Confederation.

– Includes many monsters who cannot become adventurers.

– Primarily makes a living by subjugating monsters.

- Among the monsters they defeat, those that are suitable may be tamed and join the mercenary bands.

Mansion Group

– Maids and butlers entrusted with the maintenance and management of Jin’s mansions.

– Many also serve concurrently as members of the Advance Trading Company.

Confidential Group

– Subordinates of Jin who do not act openly and live in the mansions or labyrinths.

– Includes harpies that lay eggs, dragonkin who have come from the hidden region to study, and others.

– Also includes the spirit Rain, the ash person Aya, and the Primordial Divine Dragon El.

Music Troupe

– A music troupe organized by one of the maids, Fille.

– Many members serve concurrently. Aya from the Confidential Group is also a member.

– Their main area of activity is the Kingdom of Estea, but as their popularity has grown, they have increasingly gone on tour.

– Officially, they are treated as an organization related to the Advance Trading Company.

---

**AN:** There are probably others I have not written down.

In some cases, they are omitted because they are not significant enough to be called a power, and in other cases, I simply forgot.
