## **Settings: Special Powers List**

**AN:** This is the second of two consecutive settings posts.

These are memo notes that you can skip without any problems.

Tomorrow’s update is still undecided. If the short story is finished, it will be the short story (progress 95%).

---

Special Powers list as of Volume 9

\<Life and Death Authority>

Level: Yes

– Can take or grant skills and statuses.

– Skills and statuses are treated as points.

– If you take skills and then defeat an opponent in a weakened state, the experience gained is reduced by that amount.

– Skills that are taken but cannot be used become disabled.

– They can also be intentionally disabled (can be toggled on and off).

– LV1: Base state.

- Effective range is 2 meters.

- Gradually takes statuses and skills.

– LV2: Robbery Murder

- Limited to targets killed by the owner, statuses and skills can be taken even from corpses.

- It is impossible to grant statuses to corpses.

– LV3: Point Conversion

- Can convert skill points into other skill points.

- Normal skills can be converted at a rate of 5 points into 1 unconverted point.

- 1 unconverted skill point can be converted into 1 normal skill point.

- Cannot be used on skills that are not possessed.

– LV4: Limited Release

- Power range is permanently extended to 10 meters.

- Once per day, the effect can be expanded when taking abilities.

- After expansion, range becomes 30 meters, and abilities can be taken at ten times the normal speed.

– LV5: Base Enhancement

- Power range is permanently extended to 30 meters, and abilities can be taken at ten times the speed of LV4.

- Can take abilities simultaneously from all targets within range.

- Once per day, range can be extended to 100 meters and speed to 100 times.

– LV6: Skill Integration

- Can integrate skills of the same category.

- Unique skills, drawback skills, racial or other inherent skills cannot be integrated.

- Integration is performed by absorbing 1 point.

- Skill point acquisition is only possible through conversion (10:1).

- Skills can be integrated by categories such as \<Martial Arts> or \<Magic>.

- Integrating martial arts skills creates a skill called \<Martial Arts>.

- Inherent skills are skills that can only be learned by limited targets based on gender, race, etc.

- Integrated skills cannot obtain skill points.

- Integrated skills cannot be separated.

– LV7: Special Skill Nullification

- Can nullify the target’s skills, Blessings, and curse marks.

- Effective range is the same as normal skill transfer.

– LV8: Soul Absorption

- By absorbing corpses and souls, it becomes possible to use race-limited skills and the like.

- Absorption of both the corpse and the soul (generally identical to the corpse) is required.

- Allows use of the absorbed target’s exclusive skills.

\<Clairvoyance>

Level: No

– Includes Appraisal, Map, Status Viewing, and Help functions (glossary and Q&A).

– Displayed over the field of vision (similar to AR).

– Visibility can be toggled on or off at will.

– Does not interfere with normal vision.

– Appraisal

- Allows visual confirmation of statuses such as HP and MP.

- Appraisal can be performed on oneself and others alike.

– Map

- A map that looks down over the surrounding area from above.

- Statuses can be checked from the map.

- Mental states are classified by color.

- Blue: Subordinates, allies (best friend, lover class)

- Red: Enemies

- Green: Indifferent, neutral

- Yellow: Believers

- The map has conditional search and alert functions.

- The map can display only the current area and adjacent areas.

- Areas where subordinates are present can also be checked.

- After expansion, four areas including the current area can be checked.

– Help

- A combination of a glossary and Q&A.

– You can vaguely tell if the other party is lying.

\<Infinite Storage>

Level: No

– Sends touched objects (more precisely, objects close enough to be considered touched) into an invisible storage space.

– Capacity is unlimited.

– Living beings cannot be stored, but petrified or frozen states are possible.

Corpses can be stored unconditionally.

– Stored items can be sorted into folders, searched by conditions, etc.

– You can choose whether to stop or not stop time for stored items.

– Even spells immediately before activation can be stored.

– Stored items can be processed through disassembly, synthesis, or item-use operations.

\<Bond of Contract>

Level: No

– Can form a master-servant contract with beings that become subordinates of the Power holder (subordinates, slaves, familiars, etc.).

– Contracted parties are connected by invisible lines.

- Through the invisible lines, various things can be shared.

- Skills and abilities can be used by others.

- Allows “telepathy”, conveying thoughts without speaking.

– Only the owner can determine the details of the Power.

- A network where the owner is the master, and all others are slaves.

– Activation condition is connecting the owner’s little finger to a part of the other party’s body.

- If the other party accepts becoming a subordinate at that time, application is complete.

- The other party not using a little finger is because they may not have an organ corresponding to a little finger.

\<Multiple Existence>

Level: Yes

– A power that acts on things such as information and the mind.

– The abilities gained through leveling do not have much unifying consistency.

LV1: An external interface for abilities called “Alta” is generated.

– Pseudo-personification of \<Clairvoyance>.

– Constantly monitors the map and statuses.

– Unlimited parallel thinking and high-speed thinking.

LV2: Enables preservation and protection of the mind and memories. Restoration is possible under certain conditions.

– Mental-type attacks are nullified.

LV3: Adds dungeon management functions.

– Relocates dungeon core functions directly under \<Multiple Existence>.

LV4: Can reconstruct absorbed corpses and souls as new pseudo-personalities.

LV5: Can grant owned personalities temporary bodies and manifest them.

– MP consumption is required.

– These bodies have no statuses.

– Based on half of the user’s maximum status values, arbitrary temporary statuses can be set.

– The farther the body moves away from the user, the more the statuses decrease.

– Shares any skills possessed by the user.

– Even if the temporary body dies, the pseudo-personality is not lost.

– A cooldown is required before re-manifestation, depending on the power.

LV6: Enables status falsification.

– Items listed in the status window can be falsified.

– The types of falsification are “addition”, “deletion”, and “attribute change.”

– No effects or abilities are gained; it only deceives when referenced.

\<Expanded Interpretation>

Level: Yes

– Can strengthen or expand the effects of possessed skills, abilities, and items.

– By removing the enhancement or expansion, other targets can be strengthened.

– When used on \<Short-Range Movement>, movement up to 150 meters becomes possible.

– Applied magic can be used even in the gray world.

- Only power increases; MP consumption does not change.

– For \<Clairvoyance>, the map range expands and more detailed information can be confirmed.

– For \<Multiple Existence>, the precision of temporary bodies given to pseudo-personalities increases.

- Can even reproduce the traits of Void Beasts and Archangels.

– When used on weapons, rarity increases by one to two levels.

- When the effect is removed, the item collapses.

– When used on the \<Chantless Casting> skill, even Unique magic can be activated without chanting.

– The map of \<Clairvoyance> can grasp four areas.

– When used on \<Monster Taming>, targets whose HP has been reduced to the brink can be forcibly tamed.

– When used on \<Labyrinth Domination>, death no longer occurs even if authority is revoked.

– LV1: Effect target count is 10.

– LV2: Effect target count expands to 20.

– LV3: Effect target count expands to 30.

– LV4: Effect target count expands to 40.

– LV5: Effect target count expands to 50.

– LV6: Effect target count expands to 60.

– LV7: Effect target count expands to 70.

– LV8: Effect target count expands to 80.

\<Magic Creation>

Level: No

– Can create magic that does not exist in this world within the bounds of the user’s imagination.

– Creating magic requires a large amount of MP.

- This can be resolved by sharing MP with the protagonist.

– The MP cost of imagined magic becomes greater than the MP assumed from its effect.

– On the status screen, it is labeled as \<Unique Magic>.

Revive: Heals missing body parts. Does not restore HP.

Warp: Instantly move within visible range.

Portal: Set up at any location to freely teleport.

Room: Create a room in a subspace.

Energy Ball: Convert MP into spherical pills of condensed nutrients.

Ankh: Resurrect the dead.

Summon: Summon subordinates.

Vacuum: Collect nearby magic stones and valuable items.

Ant Trap: Destroy nearby traps.

Connect: Translate monster language. Can also be applied to non-monsters.

Boost: Increase the effect of the next spell used. Effective for attack, recovery, and support magic.

Refresh: Alleviate physiological discomfort.

Float: Reduce the weight of objects.

Reverse: Reincarnate demons or monsters as humans.

---

**AN:** I was careful not to write any hidden settings here that should not be written.

+++

## **Chronicle 4: The Heroic Saga of Claude, an A-Rank Adventurer (Part 1)**

**AN:** Since I made it in time, I am posting a short side story.

I apologize to those who are waiting for the main story.

As you can tell from the title, there will be two more installments of roughly the same length.

I plan to post all of them by the 10th, when the next main story update is scheduled.

---

My name is Claude.

I used to be a completely unremarkable slave with nothing going for me, but now, through some twist of fate, I am an A-rank adventurer.

We have been ordered by our master, Jin-sama, to become S-rank adventurers.

There are two major conditions to becoming an S-rank adventurer.

The first is to receive recommendations certifying that you are worthy of S-rank from at least three countries.

The second is to leave behind achievements worthy of S-rank.

We have already received recommendations from the Kingdom of Castal and the Kingdom of Gashas.

And just the other day, we also received a recommendation from the Kingdom of Estea, where we currently reside.

All that remains now is an achievement worthy of an S-rank adventurer, in most cases the subjugation of a powerful monster, and then we will finally obtain the title of S-rank adventurer.

That day, an emergency summons was issued to our clan “Saviors”, by the Adventurers Guild of the Kingdom of Estea.

“Recently, the small southeastern country neighboring the Kingdom of Estea, the Duchy of Rifer, was occupied by monsters. We would like to ask Claude-san and his group to help reclaim it.”

“Reclaim a country, you say…?”

The eight of us core members were listening to the explanation from the receptionist in a reception room at the Adventurers Guild in the capital of the Kingdom of Estea.

“Yes. According to those who fled from the Duchy of Rifer, a horde of undead attacked. The ducal knight order attempted to respond, but they were completely overwhelmed, and it seems the capital city was occupied in the blink of an eye.”

“What happened to the citizens?”

“Fortunately, the undead themselves move slowly, so most of the residents were able to escape. However, several villages that were slow to receive word were wiped out, and the knight order also suffered many casualties.”

…It seems there were not a few victims.

To the east of the Kingdom of Estea lies the Crimson Empire, a country Jin-sama refuses to go to. Because of that, Jin-sama has almost no presence there, and incidents like this can happen.

Whether or not a place falls within Jin-sama’s sphere of activity greatly changes the likelihood of tragedies occurring.

I know it is not my place to complain, but I wish Jin-sama would travel the world as quickly as possible.

“The undead horde does not seem inclined to leave the central region of the Duchy of Rifer, so the likelihood of this country being affected is low for now. However, we cannot leave a monster-occupied country alone indefinitely. We would very much like Claude-san and the others to join the reclamation effort.”

“You say ‘join’, so that means you are not asking us to handle everything on our own, correct?”

“Yes. Ordinarily, something of this magnitude would be led by the country itself. However, there is a reason it cannot be handled so easily.”

The receptionist continued with a serious expression.

“It appears that anyone who dies within the undead’s area of activity becomes undead themselves and begins attacking the living. Furthermore, even if undead are defeated, they revive after some time. We suspect that someone is using large-scale necromancy.”

“If someone with only half-baked ability goes in, it would only make the situation worse.”

You cannot reduce the number of undead, and those who die become undead and bare their fangs.

If handled poorly, it would turn into a negative cycle.

“Yes, that is our assessment as well. Unless the user of necromancy is defeated, eliminating the surrounding undead would be pointless. That is the role we would like to ask of Claude-san and his group.”

“You want us to take down the necromancer?”

“Yes. We are well aware of Claude-san and the others’ abilities, so we do not believe you would be outmatched by a necromancer. More importantly, you have a means of aerial movement. Being able to ignore the undead along the way is an enormous advantage.”

We have been given inferior wind dragons by our master, Jin-sama.

Being able to move through the air is, by itself, an overwhelming advantage.

“The Kingdom of Estea and the surrounding countries will gather personnel to draw the surrounding undead away. Once the undead numbers decrease in the center, we would like Claude-san and the others to strike at the source. Attempting to reach the center by land alone would be unwise.”

According to the receptionist, the number of undead exceeds ten thousand at minimum.

Each individual undead is, frankly speaking, weak, but when faced with an immortal army of that size, it would not be easy.

“We also considered requesting the dragon knight order of the Kingdom of Castal, but Her Majesty the Queen is currently out of the country attending a summit. Under those circumstances, we cannot ask them to dispatch their main force to a distant location. We have no choice but to manage with the surrounding countries.”

The inferior flying dragons we received from Jin-sama are publicly said to have been granted by the Kingdom of Castal.

More precisely, they are said to have come from Gene-sama, a Queen’s Knight. Well, Gene-sama is actually Jin-sama in disguise.

“Additionally, this request will be a named request from the Kingdom of Estea and the Duchy of Rifer.”

“So it is not a compulsory request?”

When a city or country is in crisis, a compulsory request can be issued, forcibly summoning adventurers in that city.

Moreover, the reward for compulsory requests is low, making them one of the most disliked things among adventurers.

In contrast, named requests carry no coercive force, and the reward scales with adventurer rank, making them something of a privilege for high-rank adventurers.

…Well, they often come with plenty of troublesome strings attached, so there are those who dislike them as well. Jin-sama, for example…

“Yes. Several conditions could not be met, so we were unable to designate the reclamation operation as a compulsory request. The role of drawing in the surrounding undead will primarily be handled by the national knight orders and volunteers of goodwill. Naturally, they will be compensated, but…”

It is an undead horde large enough to occupy a country.

If there is no direct damage, it is understandable that people would not want to get involved.

This country in particular has few adventurers, and explorers tend to dislike fighting outside labyrinths, making it even more so.

However, from a national perspective, it is not a problem that can be left alone.

“If Claude-san and the others were to refuse, the only remaining option would be to wait for Queen Sakuya of Castal to return and request the dispatch of the dragon knight order, including Queen’s Knight Gene-sama. We can only hope nothing happens until then…”

If we refuse, the matter will reach Sakuya-sama and Jin-sama.

We cannot allow the two of them to be burdened with something we can handle ourselves.

I look around at my companions.

They nod or smile back at me.

Only Iris, who fears Jin-sama, was nodding repeatedly with a glaring expression, terrified of causing Jin-sama any trouble.

“Understood. If we are acceptable, we will cooperate in the reclamation operation.”

“Really? Thank you very much!”

Thus, we decided to take on a central role in the Duchy of Rifer reclamation operation.

After discussions, it was decided that the operation would begin in one week.

Because it was such a sudden development, the surrounding countries rushed about preparing.

In the midst of that, what proved useful were the inferior wind dragons given to the Kingdom of Estea.

Previously, when we were given inferior wind dragons, Lady Cattleya of the Kingdom of Estea had apparently wanted some as well.

After being given conditions by Jin-sama, Lady Cattleya managed to fulfill them, and the kingdom was granted fifty-one inferior wind dragons.

One might think that means the Kingdom of Estea should use those inferior wind dragons to strike the necromancer, but that is difficult.

The reason is that, in the Kingdom of Estea, the inferior wind dragons are considered gifts.

They were never intended to be the main fighting force, and were prioritized for communication and transport, assigning them to knights who could ride them well rather than those who were strongest.

Simply put, the dragon knights of the Kingdom of Estea are weak.

Even so, having means of movement and communication is significant, and if they can coordinate with the surrounding countries and prepare for the reclamation operation within just one week, that is more than satisfactory.

During that time, we were not asked to serve as messengers using our inferior wind dragons.

They wanted us to focus on preparation and raise the success rate of the operation as much as possible.

“We will also participate in the reclamation operation.”

“We will participate.”

《We will be drawing in the surrounding monsters, though.》

While we were eating at Jin-sama’s residence, four members of “Saviors” who were active in Estea, Cynthia-san, Karen-san, Soura-san, and Kate-san, spoke to us.

Like us, they are Jin-sama’s slaves and explorers ordered to conquer labyrinths.

“That would help a lot, but is it really okay? Won’t it interfere with labyrinth conquest?”

“It is absolutely unacceptable to interfere with Jin-sama’s orders. I will never allow it. If you want to die so badly, then go die somewhere that has nothing to do with Jin-sama’s orders.”

The one who asked them was Nott.

And when Jin-sama is involved, Iris breaks. She is usually calm, but…

《Iris-san, do you really think I would do something that goes against Jin-sama’s orders? Of course, labyrinth conquest is proceeding smoothly, and reaching the 50th floor is not far off. However, we have no intention of conquering it during a period when Jin-sama is rarely present. We want to report the conquest of the 50th floor directly to Jin-sama.》

“I understand! I want Jin-sama to praise me directly too!”

《Yes, if he would even pat my head, that would be the ultimate joy!》

“I understand that too!”

Kate-san is one of those who worship Jin-sama as a god. Sometimes, her words send a chill down my spine.

On the other hand, Roro, who agreed with her, harbors pure affection for Jin-sama. Pure…yes, let us call it pure. That is what makes everyone happiest.

The two seem to be having a conversation, but in reality, the content does not line up at all.

“Both of you, stop there. This conversation is going nowhere. Well, if you are not going against Jin-sama’s orders, then it is not my place to interfere. …Sorry for doubting you.”

《Please do not worry. If our positions were reversed, I would have questioned it as well.》

See? Chilling.

“We are on the 47th floor right now! Once we conquer the 50th floor, inferior wind dragons will be granted to Cynthia and the others as well. If possible, we wanted the reclamation operation to be after that!”

The labyrinth has fifty floors…well, actually sixty, but ordinary explorers can only go to the fiftieth.

No one has conquered them all…except Jin-sama.

Once Cynthia-san and the others conquer the labyrinth, they will be granted inferior wind dragons just like Lady Cattleya.

“I think that would be impossible…”

As Adel says, they would not postpone the operation for such a reason.

“If you want, you could ride on our inferior wind dragons?”

“We would welcome Cynthia-chan and the others~”

At Coco and Cicely’s suggestion, Kate-san shook her head.

《I appreciate the offer, but it would be better to avoid that in order to clearly define our achievements.》

“Yes. Though it may sound inappropriate, this situation is an opportunity. We should reduce uncertain factors as much as possible.”

Yuria-san nodded at Kate-san’s words.

“An opportunity? What do you mean?”

“Huh?”

“Oh, I see…”

Nott and Cicely do not seem to understand, but Coco seems to have realized at the last moment.

“This battle should be more than sufficient as an achievement for us to become S-rank. In order not to dilute that achievement, I think it would be best for us to handle it ourselves.”

“Ah, I see. When you put it that way, you are right. Alright! Now I am really fired up!”

Having understood, Nott’s motivation ignites.

Yes. This operation is one we cannot afford to fail, in many ways.

“How could you not notice? Considering Jin-sama’s orders, you should have realized immediately!”

“Hehehe~”

Iris, it would be cruel to expect that from Cicely.

“Leave thinning out the undead to us! We hunted undead to death on the thirtieth floors, so we are used to it!”

“It was rough, wasn’t it, Karen-chan?”

“It was harsh, wasn’t it, Soura-chan?”

《On the thirtieth floors, there was hardly any time to rest. Without learning how to recover stamina during short breaks, we would never have been able to fight through it.》

I have heard that on the labyrinth’s thirtieth floors, countless undead spawn and swarm relentlessly.

The four who overcame that are perfectly suited for this reclamation operation.

Except that, aside from Cynthia-san, they seem to have taken some mental damage…

《Leave the rear to us, and please fight without worry in the center.》

“Thank you very much. That is truly reassuring.”

I know Cynthia-san and the others’ abilities well.

If they are drawing in monsters around the perimeter, we need not worry about that side.

That was not the only welcome reinforcement.

“Tira-chan, joining in♪”

“For this reclamation operation, the Atto Confederation will also be dispatching personnel. As capable individuals of the Atto Confederation, requests were sent to us as well. We are not adventurers, so we could have declined, but with family participating, we could hardly refuse.”

“Leave it to us!”

“Thank you for your help.”

The three mercenaries from the Atto Confederation, Tiramisu-san, Chocolat-san, and Maple-san, will be joining us.

The reason they work as mercenaries rather than adventurers is because they are monsters and cannot register as adventurers. That said, they are exclusive mercenaries of the Advance Trading Company, which is family, so to speak…

To be honest, we have had less interaction with them than with Cynthia-san’s explorer group, but I know their strength well. I have seen them use powerful magic many times at social gatherings.

“One of our objectives is to subjugate evil monsters lurking around the Confederation. They do not appear to be monsters that fled from the Confederation, but there is no proof they are unrelated either.”

“I do not think any monsters I know could pull this off, but you never know what might happen…”

“That description fits Honey perfectly, right♪”

Tiramisu-san calls Jin-sama Honey.

Indeed, around Jin-sama, you never know what might happen. And there is no guarantee that Jin-sama is the only such mysterious existence.

“Chocolat-san and Maple-san can fly, right? Do you plan to accompany us to the center?”

“No. I heard the plan from Kate, so we will be thinning out the undead around the perimeter. With our magic, we can reduce their numbers from long range, so we should be quite useful.”

“Tira-chan will just be throwing rocks though♪”

Yuria-san’s question is answered by Chocolat-san and Tiramisu-san.

Tiramisu-san is apparently a monster called a dinosaur, completely incapable of using magic.

However, she is terrifyingly tough and strong, a pure power fighter.

“We will leave the spotlight to you, so make sure you finish it properly.”

“Do your best♪ Do your best♪”

“I am counting on you.”

“Yes. Leave it to us.”

Two groups under Jin-sama’s command are participating.

We absolutely cannot show anything pathetic now.

This is becoming a battle we cannot lose.

During the one week before the operation began, we devoted ourselves solely to preparations for the Duchy of Rifer reclamation operation, without taking on any other requests.

We procured necessary supplies such as potions at the stores of the Advance Trading Company.

The Advance Trading Company is run by Jin-sama’s subordinates, so they are essentially family, but since that relationship is not public, we have to purchase things normally.

They do give us secret discounts, though…

We buy in bulk and store everything in an item box.

It is an ultra-high-capacity, ultra-luxury item box obtained during our adventures.

With just this one, you could build a mansion in a prime district of the capital…or so they say. We are not adventurers for money, so no matter how much we are offered, we would never sell items essential for our adventures.

And that ultra-luxury item box…is actually a disguise for our master’s Infinite Storage. It is truly laughable.

Next, we prepare our weapons and armor.

That said, it is impossible to prepare new weapons at this point, so we just have Nott perform maintenance.

“There…does not seem to be much time…so I will…help as well…”

“If Mimi-san helps, that is like having a hundred extra people.”

The dwarf Mimi-san is one of Nott’s masters.

With only one week for preparation, she decided to help with weapon maintenance to reduce Nott’s burden.

Mimi-san herself is a master swordswoman, but she has stepped away from the battlefield.

She said she only fought out of necessity, and now that there is no longer a need, she wants to devote herself solely to forging weapons for Jin-sama.

We equip the weapons and armor they maintained.

They fit our bodies naturally, as we are accustomed to them, yet they feel as good as new.

“Come to think of it, you made anti-undead equipment the other day, right? If we were going to use something anyway, maybe that would have been better.”

In fact, Nott had previously crafted anti-undead weapons for all of us.

The motivation was that we competed to see who could defeat undead monsters the fastest at a social gathering.

This time, we will likely face many undead, so having anti-undead weapons would make the fight much easier.

However, I shake my head in refusal.

“Those weapons were not made from materials we obtained through our adventures, were they? We should not use them when we are trying to become S-rank through our own ability.”

“…That is true. Sorry, I said something strange.”

“Besides, our target is the necromancer. There is no guarantee that person is undead, right?”

While undead that use \<necromancy> are common enough, humans can use \<necromancy> as well.

“Yeah, there is a strong possibility the mastermind is human.”

“Rather than gambling everything on one assumption, I think it is better to use weapons we are familiar with so we can handle any opponent.”

“Agreed.”

Finally, we review our techniques.

It would not be an exaggeration to say that we devoted most of the ten days to this.

First, we confirm coordination within the group.

We focus primarily on coordination as two four-person parties.

We split into my group of Coco, Cicely, and Yuria-san, and Adel’s group of Nott, Roro, and Iris, and recheck formations against monsters and humanoids.

Next is coordination as an eight-person party.

This time, without focusing on the four-person units, we adjust our movements so that each of the eight fulfills their role.

I am the party leader, but when operating as an eight-person party, we entrust overall command to Yuria-san in the rear.

Then we adjust coordination in pairs, trios, and with different combinations of party members in sequence.

We make sure we can coordinate with anyone.

After that, we conduct training to resolve individual issues.

These vary for each person, so they are done as independent training.

My weakness is my lack of finishing power.

If I borrow Yuria-san’s cooperation and use Spiritization, it is a different story, but my individual attack power is on the low side.

A shield-bearing one-handed sword user is not expected to have overwhelming attack power, but to call oneself S-rank, it is lacking. At the very least, I want one or two finishing moves.

“Haa, haa…”

“You are at it again. Why do you not stop such reckless training?”

When I am lying flat on my back in the training ground, exhausted, Coco, who was training nearby, calls out to me with an exasperated look.

“I cannot…haa…stop that easily…haa…”

“Here, water.”

“Thanks…haa…”

I sit up halfway and gulp down the water she hands me.

The burden seems greater than I expected.

“I am not talented. If I do the same things as everyone else, I will never become stronger than an ordinary person.”

“…I understand how you feel, but there is no need to deliberately take such a bad gamble. Manifesting a unique-class skill is not something that happens so easily.”

Yes. My goal is the manifestation of a skill.

And not just any skill, but an overwhelmingly powerful one that Jin-sama classifies as unique-class.

“Is \<Shikuchi> not enough for you?”

“It is not. It is not enough. \<Shikuchi> alone does not have finishing power.”

I have already succeeded in manifesting one unique-class skill.

However, even that is no longer enough for me.

“You just have to endure until you become S-rank, right?”

“I want to obtain it by my own power.”

“You are so selfish…”

Coco smiles wryly, but this is one thing I cannot compromise on.

“This is my last chance…”

“Well, if you insist that much, I will not stop you. Do your best for the remaining six days.”

“I will.”

It seems Coco was also on a break.

After saying that, she returned to her own training.

Alright, time for one more push.

The long yet short week passed.

We arrived near the border between the Kingdom of Estea and the Duchy of Rifer.

Currently, knight orders and adventurers from the surrounding countries are deployed in a ring around the Duchy of Rifer.

It is impossible to completely surround it, so they are divided into roughly thirty groups, drawing in undead and defeating them individually.

Because undead revive over time, prolonged fighting is considered difficult, and the time limit is set at two hours. If that is exceeded, forces will withdraw and the operation will be deemed a failure.

In that case, our survival would be considered hopeless.

“How are the undead movements?”

At the operation headquarters, I ask a guild official of the Kingdom of Estea.

“There are still no major movements. Having occupied a country so brazenly, yet doing nothing, is extremely unsettling.”

For over a week now, the undead have shown no major movements whatsoever.

With the undead continuing to occupy the country without clear purpose, tension among the surrounding countries had risen.

We review unit placement and the geography of the Duchy of Rifer once more.

It is believed the mastermind is likely in the ducal capital.

“It is almost time for the operation to begin.”

The start time draws near in the blink of an eye.

“Then we will begin our preparations as well.”

“We are counting on you.”

Shortly after that, the Duchy of Rifer reclamation operation began.

First, the surrounding units advance into the Duchy of Rifer and draw in the undead.

After drawing them in for a while and repeatedly defeating them in detail, we will head for the center riding our inferior wind dragons.

Even as we make our final adjustments, multiple rapid reports come in.

One says that large undead have appeared in various locations and are sweeping aside adventurers and knights.

One says that a large undead was pulverized by a stone thrown by a frilly-dressed young girl.

One says that a large undead was smashed to pieces by a girl wearing a maid outfit.

One says that people wearing maid outfits are generally strong.

One says that undead defeated by some adventurers, mercenaries, and those in maid outfits do not revive, allowing the front line to be pushed forward little by little.

One says that since the objective is to draw them in, pushing the front line forward is undesirable.

More than half of this sounds familiar…

There are a lot of inside jokes, but at least the battle situation does not seem bad.

And then, as the battle situation begins to stagnate, it is finally time for us to sortie.

“Alright, let us go.”

“Yeah!” x7

---

Character Introductions

Name: Claude  

Gender: Male  

Race: Human  

Equipment: Sword and shield  

Notes: Leader of the adventurer group and protagonist of this biographical chronicle. For his personality, read the chronicle.

Name: Adel  

Gender: Male  

Race: Human  

Equipment: Spear  

Notes: A quiet, soft-spoken, gentle boy. In some ways, it would not be an exaggeration to say he has grown the most among the adventurer group. His former timid demeanor is completely gone, refined into calmness. His quiet voice is something he was born with, so it cannot be helped.

Name: Nott  

Gender: Male  

Race: Dwarf  

Equipment: Hammer  

Notes: A dwarf boy aspiring to be a blacksmith. Despite calling himself an aspiring blacksmith, he already possesses respectable skill. Juggling both adventuring and smithing is quite demanding, but he finds it rewarding. Many of the adventurer group’s weapons are drops, but some are forged by Nott.

Name: Coco  

Gender: Female  

Race: Beastkin (Dog)  

Equipment: Two daggers  

Notes: An energetic, loyal-dog-type girl. Her dream is to become Jin’s knight, but she hates heavy armor. Speed is her strength, so equipment that does not hinder movement suits her. One of her worries is that her chest has grown since her diet improved. Another worry is that her voluminous blonde hair explodes when she wakes up, so she currently hides it in a ponytail. A dog beastkin with a ponytail…tease her about it and she will get angry.

Name: Cicely  

Gender: Female  

Race: Human  

Equipment: Spear  

Notes: A laid-back, gentle girl with wavy brown hair. Despite her relaxed demeanor, she moves quite nimbly in combat. She loves Coco and was always with her when they first became adventurers. Lately, their individual activities have increased, making her a little lonely. Unable to help it, she carries around a handmade Coco-chan doll. She gets so nervous around Jin that her laid-back nature disappears. She still is not used to it.

Name: Roro  

Gender: Female  

Race: Human  

Equipment: Greatsword  

Notes: A red-haired girl with braided hair hanging down on both sides. She is quite voluptuous for her age. Even before her diet improved, she had a chest comparable to Coco’s. She is relatively calm when Jin is not involved. One of the few girls who is genuinely in love with Jin. She has received various lectures about nighttime activities from close female adventurers and has resolved to make Jin turn her way someday. However, those depictions are cut from the main story.

Name: Iris  

Gender: Female  

Race: Half-elf  

Equipment: Sword and shield  

Notes: A bespectacled half-elf girl. Her long green hair, which once reached the ground, was cut short after she became an adventurer. She used to be taciturn, but that is in the past, and she now talks quite a lot with her companions. She does not hesitate to hurl barbs at her friends. She is one of those whose personality changed significantly within the adventurer group. While she still becomes hysterical regarding Jin, actually speaking with him has made her slightly better.

Name: Yuria  

Gender: Female  

Race: High elf  

Equipment: Whip and dagger  

Notes: The oldest of the adventurer group (approximately 400 years old), an amnesiac silver-haired loli granny (apologies). She has many intriguing titles such as Elf Princess Priestess and Elf Royalty, but despite being introduced over a hundred chapters ago, they have been left untouched. She possesses high-level Spirit Arts and is the cornerstone of the adventurer group’s trump card, Spiritization. Her current concern is that, unlike the other members, her body does not grow (a racial trait).

---

**AN:** I called it a short side story, but it has the volume of one main story episode (three main story episodes total).

I am prepared to be told to get on with the main story, but if I do not write this now…

+++

## **Chronicle 4: The Heroic Saga of Claude, an A-Rank Adventurer (Middle)**

**AN:** This is the middle part. If things continue at this pace, the next update is expected in about four days.

---

After leaving the operations headquarters, we were flying over the Principality of Rifel on inferior wind dragons.

The Principality of Rifel is small, so with inferior wind dragons, we should be able to reach the central district in about twenty minutes.

The inferior wind dragons were given to us one per person by Jin-sama.

Since conversation is difficult when riding separate inferior wind dragons, we speak using telepathy.

《It really does not seem to be a mistake, no matter how many times I look. Those are not undead. They are spirits…》

Yuria-san, who has learned \<Spirit Arts>, says this while looking down at the horde of undead below.

《Eh? They just look like zombies and skeletons to me.》

《But Yuria-san would not misidentify them, right?》

Just as Coco says, the ones that took control of the Principality of Rifel were hordes of zombies and skeletons.

What is beneath us right now looks exactly the same.

However, since Yuria-san is a specialist when it comes to spirits, it is hard to believe she is mistaken. In that sense, I agree with Cicely.

《Those are corpses and bones possessed by corrupted spirits.》

《Corrupted spirits… those are spirits that have absorbed too much miasma, right?》

Adel says this uncertainly, but that understanding should be correct.

Corrupted spirits are masses of magical power like normal spirits, but most of their composition is stagnant mana, miasma.

They are gluttonous beings, and their existence deviates from the natural laws of spirits. Contracts through Spirit Arts are impossible with them.

《Yes. Even I have never seen such a large number of corrupted spirits.》

《Wait a moment! Does that mean the mastermind is not using Necromancy!?》

《Most likely… I believe it is something closer to Spirit Arts, though not quite the same.》

When Roro speaks in a flustered manner, Yuria-san quietly nods.

If the opponent is spirits, then Necromancy, which controls undead, is unrelated.

However, as mentioned earlier, corrupted spirits cannot be contracted through Spirit Arts, so there must be some other mechanism related to Spirit Arts at work.

《Let’s save the analysis for later. It looks like a large-scale welcome.》

In the direction we are heading, giant undead… no, corpses possessed by corrupted spirits are waiting for us.

They are clearly aware of our presence and are staring at us with lifeless eyes.

Giants are monsters not found in this area. They are grotesque giants standing five to seven meters tall. They have silhouettes similar to humans, but language does not work on them, and they have neither intelligence nor reason. They are dangerous monsters.

《No matter how big they are, if they cannot reach us up here, they are not scary.》

Since we are flying several dozen meters above the ground, even giants should not be able to attack us… or so we thought.

《Nott, could you please stop tempting fate?》

I have a bad feeling about this…

Is this what Mio-san often calls a flag?

The possessed giant slowly grabbed a nearby skeleton.

《Ah…》

All of us instantly realized what the possessed giant was about to do.

《Idiot! Nott, you idiot! This is because you said something unnecessary!》

《Hey, Iris! This is not my fault! Even if I had not said anything, it would have done the same thing… Here it comes! Evade!》

Just as expected, the possessed giant swung the skeleton back and threw it at us.

We maneuver our inferior wind dragons and evade the flying skeleton.

《Claude, what should we do? Considering our objective, we could ignore it and keep going.》

《If we are in a hurry, maybe we should ignore it?》

《We are clearly being targeted, and if it follows us, it will be troublesome. I would like to defeat it here.》

We have already passed beyond the Adventurers battle line, and it will take about ten more minutes to reach the center.

At this point, the adventurers drawing attention away no longer seems effective.

The remaining time worries me, but it is better to eliminate potential dangers.

《Claude, take a look… it seems it is not going to be that easy…》

《There are over twenty possessed giants. Ten dragon zombies… no, possessed dragons. Even I did not imagine such a welcome.》

For reasons unknown, more than twenty possessed giants and ten pseudo dragon zombies, dragons possessed by corrupted spirits, are approaching us.

To make matters worse, three of the pseudo dragon zombies were originally wind dragons and can fly. The others include fire dragons, earth dragons, and water dragons, two or three of each. All of them are threats.

Still, the absence of higher-ranking dragons is a small mercy.

《Just having numbers does not always mean strength, but this is still troublesome. What will you do, leader?》

Iris asks provocatively, but the answer is already decided.

《Let us eliminate the large ones here. Yuria-san, please take command.》

《Understood. Dispersed combat. Prepare two-person teams!》

《Yes!》 x7

Considering the number and strength of the enemies, we adopt a tactic of pairing up to individually eliminate the large targets.

《It took longer than I expected…》

Because we chose a fighting style that suppressed exhaustion, we ended up using more time than anticipated.

As expected, our lack of decisive finishing power is an issue. Against large enemies, half-hearted attacks sometimes do not work at all.

《There is still over an hour left, right? Do not worry about it.》

《That is correct. Moreover, large enemies were not originally factored in. Considering that we fought them, I believe we are still progressing smoothly.》

Nott and Yuria-san try to reassure me.

《That is true. We still have time. We are almost at the center, so let us pull ourselves together and go!》

《Exactly. You are the leader, so straighten up. Do not show such a pathetic side in front of your companions!》

《Haha… Iris is as strict as ever…》

Because they are my companions… no, more like family, there are parts where I let my guard down.

We advance further, and finally reach the central area of the Principality of Rifel.

《Where do you think the mastermind is?》

《Over there.》

In response to my muttering, Yuria-san points with her finger.

What lies beyond is the royal castle of the capital of the Principality of Rifel.

《Yuria-san, can you tell?》

《Yes. Corrupted spirits are still spirits. Now that we are this close, I can tell where the presence is strongest.》

Yuria-san nods in response to Roro’s question.

《It seems there is more to it than that.》

《There are no other corrupted spirits around.》

《You are right. Only that area has none.》

As we move in the direction Yuria-san indicated, the number of pseudo undead strangely decreases.

The closer we got to the center, the denser the pseudo undead became, yet at the true center, there are fewer of them instead.

《Claude, what do you think?》

《I have no idea what the objective is. It could be a trap, but I cannot think of a reason to deliberately not place pseudo undead in the center. If it is meant to lure us into complacency, it is too obvious… I think we have no choice but to proceed carefully. Coco, what do you think?》

《I think we should move forward as well. I am uneasy, though.》

Not advancing is not an option, but this unnatural feeling without an explanation is unsettling.

“?!”

The next moment, an overwhelming chill runs through us.

《W-What is this ominous presence!?》

《A massive corrupted spirit. And it is separate from the mastermind…》

– GOGOGOGOGO –

A sound like an earthquake echoes, and a gigantic magic circle unfolds in the air.

The magic circle opens like a gate, and the source of the chill emerges from within.

《The highest-ranked dragon…》

What appears is a dragon called a Gigantic Rock Dragon, which ranks even higher among the upper dragon species.

As its name suggests, the Gigantic Rock Dragon is especially massive among dragons, boasting a total length of nearly fifty meters.

Generally, dragons capable of using Dragon Arts are called upper dragon species.

The fire dragons we fought earlier are also upper dragon species, but they rank lower. The difference in strength compared to the Gigantic Rock Dragon is obvious.

Even though it is a pseudo dragon possessed by a corrupted spirit, its strength cannot be underestimated.

As we stop advancing on our inferior wind dragons and cautiously observe the Gigantic Rock Dragon, we notice that there is a man and a woman riding on its head.

Since the Gigantic Rock Dragon is an earth dragon type and cannot fly, it trudges forward on foot.

It stops at some distance from us, and the man speaks up.

“You there. What business do you have with my country?”

It seems he is using Amplify from \<Daily-Life Spells LV2>, since his voice carries clearly despite the distance. I should use it as well.

The man looks to be in his twenties, wearing flamboyant clothes like a noble. He does not look trained, is slender, and tall.

The woman appears to be about the same age, a beautiful woman clad in a pure white dress. However, there is no life in her eyes.

The man holds the woman by the waist, clinging to her like a close married couple.

“The Principality of Rifel is not your country, is it?”

“The Principality of Rifel? …Ah, are you talking about the country that used to be here? No. This is no longer the Principality of Rifel. This is now a country for just me and Louis.”

Of course, a country taken by such violent means would never be recognized as a nation.

However, the man’s expression does not look like he is joking.

He is clearly the mastermind, but I confirm just in case.

“Was this your doing?”

“My doing? What are you talking about?”

When I ask, the man tilts his head as if he truly does not understand.

“Occupying the Principality of Rifel using undead… no, corrupted spirits.”

“Occupying sounds unpleasant. They were a bit in the way, so I had them move aside. This country is rich in greenery and has beautiful scenery. It was perfect for the two of us to live peacefully together. Right, Louis?”

He says this while gazing at the woman.

What should I do… The words are getting through, but it feels like the conversation itself is not.

I have to force things forward somehow… Leaving it to the flow will not get us anywhere.

“…I will answer your first question. We are here as adventurers to reclaim the occupied Principality of Rifel.”

“I see. Thank you for your hard work. Then could you go back and report that reclaiming it was impossible? As you can see, I have this Gigantic Rock Dragon. I will praise you for making it this far, but surely you cannot handle this, can you?”

This is bad… I was trying to provoke him into starting a fight, but it is not getting through at all.

On the contrary, he seems intent on sending us back.

“We only need this country. We have no intention of advancing troops elsewhere. Just a few decades is fine. Could you not leave us alone to live peacefully?”

The man says this with a gentle expression.

There is no ambition in his eyes. Despite taking over a country, his sole objective is to live peacefully.

“That is impossible.”

“Why? I have no intention of harming anyone unless I am threatened.”

As long as you do not approach, the pseudo undead do not attack.

It is eerie, but leaving it alone might seem acceptable at a glance.

…That cannot be right.

“Do you know? When you occupied this country, people died. You have already killed villagers who posed no threat to you. How can we trust the words of someone who has already done what he claimed he would not do?”

If his goal was to live peacefully and he strictly never attacked unless attacked, we might have considered it.

But this man has already harmed innocent civilians who did nothing.

Attacking and killing innocent people who lived peacefully, then claiming you want to live peacefully yourselves… that is unforgivable. I will not forgive it.

“Believe or not is up to you. Then what will you do? Do you intend to defeat this Gigantic Rock Dragon?”

“Yes. We will defeat that dragon, and… you. We will take this country back.”

“Hahaha, you say interesting things. Then try if you wish.”

With that, the man jumps down from the dragon’s head.

Immediately after, something like black mist bursts from the woman’s back and forms wings.

Just like that, the man and woman fly back toward the castle.

《That woman, like the pseudo undead, is possessed by a corrupted spirit.》

Yuria-san explains, but we had already guessed as much.

《More importantly, we should get down to the ground quickly! Otherwise we will end up fighting while riding inferior wind dragons!》

《That is true… that would be far too disadvantageous…》

We immediately land the inferior wind dragons and dismount.

If the opponent is an earth dragon, it is easier to fight on the ground than while riding. Inferior wind dragons are excellent, but they are not that strong in combat.

…And I do not want to needlessly put the inferior wind dragons Jin-sama gave us in danger.

We have the inferior wind dragons fly high enough that attacks cannot reach them, and face the Gigantic Rock Dragon.

Once the man and woman return to the castle, the Gigantic Rock Dragon begins moving its massive body again.

“No holding back! Full power! Call Element, all!”

Yuria-san activates Spirit Arts and summons all the spirits she has contracts with.

Seven differently colored lights appear and fly toward the seven of us besides Yuria-san.

An earth spirit goes to Nott, an ice spirit to Adel, a wind spirit to Coco, a water spirit to Cicely, a fire spirit to Roro, and a dark spirit to Iris.

And to me comes a mass of light, Akari-san, the light-attribute spirit.

《Claude-kun, do you need your big sister’s power again?》

“Yes, please.”

By cloaking ourselves in spirits matching our attributes, we can greatly increase our combat power.

That is one of our trump cards. Spiritization.

《Okay, leave it to your big sister! Boom!》

Akari-san says this and rams into me. Just before colliding, she turns into particles of light and is absorbed into me.

At that moment, power wells up from deep within my body.

And I deliberately suppress it.

Up until now, ‘Spiritization’ greatly enhanced our abilities for a limited time.

However, being unable to fight properly after the time limit expires is a problem. It is too short-sighted for an S-rank adventurer who needs to achieve results continuously.

As a result, we came up with ‘Spiritization LV2’.

‘Spiritization LV2’ involves suppressing the spirit’s power after activating Spiritization, preventing excessive boosts. During battle, the power is released momentarily to increase abilities, then suppressed again.

In other words, by repeatedly applying short bursts of enhancement, we reduce mana and stamina consumption.

Of course, it was not as simple as it sounds, and there were many issues, but by verifying and resolving them one by one, we refined it to a level fully usable in real combat.

Naturally, all seven of us except Yuria-san can use ‘Spiritization LV2’.

“Gooooo…”

Just as we finish preparing, the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon raises one leg while groaning.

It is definitely a stomp.

“Prepare for anti-giant monster combat!”

“Yeah!” x7

Under Yuria-san’s command, we spread out widely.

We have fought monsters many times before.

Even against ultra-large monsters, we do not fight without a plan.

When facing large monsters, there is no advantage to clustering together, so we first spread out and secure favorable distances.

– DOOOOOON –

The (pseudo) Gigantic Rock Dragon’s stomp causes a tremendous shock, but it is in vain.

“Cicely, let’s go!”

“Okaaay!”

First, Coco and Cicely approach the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon with spears.

Cicely normally uses a spear, but Coco usually fights with dual daggers.

However, daggers are ineffective against large monsters, so she equips a spear instead.

Coco prefers daggers for their maneuverability, but for someone as fast as her, a spear that converts speed into power is not a bad match.

“Hah!”

“Eii!”

The two thrust their spears into the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon’s legs, but no blood gushes out.

“That was shallow!”

“No! That thing has no blood flowing through it!”

Iris denies Coco’s frustrated remark.

“That is just a corpse of a Gigantic Rock Dragon. They must have drained the blood to prevent decay!”

That is right. It looks like a Gigantic Rock Dragon, but it is nothing more than a corpse possessed by a corrupted spirit.

I do not know the details, but even a Gigantic Rock Dragon’s corpse would decay if left alone.

If you are going to use corpses as trump cards, it would not be strange to take measures to prevent decay.

《Tactical change! Anti-giant monster combined with anti-control-type combat!》

Since we are spread out, Yuria-san gives instructions via telepathy.

Normal monsters can be damaged by continuous attacks anywhere.

However, corpses controlled by possession often cannot be defeated just by damaging the body. To defeat them, you must destroy them to the point they can no longer be controlled.

Destroying a monster of Gigantic Rock Dragon class to that extent with normal weapons would take too long.

“‘Ice Shot’…”

Adel, who was at a distance, fires ‘Ice Shot’ from \<Ice Magic LV3>.

A large ice projectile strikes the massive body of the Gigantic Rock Dragon.

Following Adel, the other members begin chanting spells one after another.

If you want to destroy a giant monster, magical attacks are the most effective by common sense.

“Gooooo…”

《Another stomp is coming! Evade!》

The pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon launches another stomp.

We evade while continuing our spell chants.

A normal adventurer party would have the vanguard buy time while the mages chant in the rear.

However, all of us can use magic and are trained to fight as vanguards.

Even Yuria-san, who provides overall buffs with \<Spirit Magic>, has enough skill to fight on the front lines.

That means we can act as decoys while dealing heavy damage with magic.

“‘Fire Shot’!”

“‘Aqua Shot’!”

“‘Wind Shot’!”

“‘Stone Shot’!”

“Eat ‘Dark Shot’!”

Everyone’s magic strikes the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon.

Since we all started chanting almost simultaneously, it is natural that the spells activate at nearly the same time.

Incidentally, Shot-type spells have a good balance of chant time and power among LV3 spells and are effective against single targets, so all party members favor them.

“‘Light Shot’!”

Of course, I do as well.

“Gooooo…”

Even though it is massive, taking repeated mid-level spells will cause damage.

Even if the corrupted spirit itself is unharmed, the body begins to crumble.

“Gooooo…”

The pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon spins around and launches a wide-area tail attack.

The tail, over five meters long, sweeps across a wide area, but because it is slow to execute, we can evade it with ease.

…In fact, the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon has no truly effective attacks against us.

The difference in size is simply too great, making precise attacks difficult.

Originally, a dragon’s trump card is \<Dragon Arts>, namely breath attacks.

Breath attacks would have allowed wide-area, high-power attacks compared to stomps or tail swings.

However, a Gigantic Rock Dragon that has become a corpse cannot use \<Dragon Arts>.

It would be sufficient combat power against large numbers, but against a small elite force, its attacks are too crude and easily avoided.

“‘Light Shot’!”

“Gooooo…”

We continue to land magic attacks while evading.

《It is going well. I will go reduce its offensive power a bit.》

Roro says this and runs toward the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon.

The pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon is in the middle of a tail attack.

Roro crouches at the point where the tail’s tip, which is somewhat thinner, will pass, and raises her greatsword.

“Gu!”

– ZUGAGAGAGAGA! –

Roro’s greatsword grinds through the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon’s tail.

She intends to use the dragon’s own force to sever its tail.

Rather than blocking it head-on, she lets it slide, so it is somewhat better, but the impact on Roro is still tremendous, and she lets out a cry of pain.

“Ei!”

With Roro’s shout, the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon’s tail is severed and flies off somewhere due to centrifugal force.

With its reach greatly shortened, the threat of tail attacks is significantly reduced.

Since it is a corpse, it may be more fragile than when it was alive.

《It was easier to cut than I expected. We might be able to sever other parts as well.》

《Claude-kun, Coco-san, please see if you can sever upper parts. Roro-san and Cicely-san, lower parts. Iris-san, Adel-kun, Nott-kun, continue magic attacks. Be careful not to hit allies.》

《Roger.》 x7

After hearing Roro’s report, Yuria-san gives instructions.

Coco and I, the two lightest and fastest, run up the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon.

“It is big, so it is easy to climb.”

“Be careful not to get careless and fall.”

“As if I would make such a mistake! I can fly!”

While ‘Spiritized’, we can fly for a short time.

Originally, ‘Spiritization’ has no such effect, but we achieved it using various tricks.

That said, this idea itself would not have been born without Jin-sama, so it is hard to call it purely our own power.

“Hah!”

“Eiya!”

“Gooooo…”

Using short bursts of flight, we climb the massive body and sever its relatively small arms, or rather forelegs.

Below, Roro and Cicely are cutting off the toes of its feet.

《It is going smoothly! At this rate, it will be an easy win!》

Does Nott feel uneasy unless he tempts fate?

“Gooooo… GAAAAAAAAAAAA!”

The moment its groan changes, the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon collapses onto the ground.

《Idiot, Nott! You said something unnecessary again!》

《I told you, it is not my fault!》

Iris scolds Nott.

Even if Nott had said nothing, it probably would have done the same thing… but the timing…

“GAAAAAA…”

While lying prone, the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon drives its hands, feet, and tail into the ground.

They are the very parts we severed.

“What is it doing… Eh!?”

“No way…”

The ground writhes as if being sucked into the severed parts, and in an instant, arms, toes, and the tip of the tail regenerate.

This is bad. Very bad.

《If this regeneration can be repeated indefinitely, we have no chance of winning. Therefore…》

Yuria-san analyzes calmly.

Looking closely, even the areas damaged by magic are recovering.

To defeat the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon, we must either whittle it down without giving it time to regenerate, or destroy it in one blow to an irreparable level…

《We should defeat the man controlling the corrupted spirit first.》

That is the only option.

《Claude-kun, Coco-san, may I ask you?》

《Yes, that is fine.》

《Leave it to us!》

We cannot send too many people to defeat the man, since the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon still needs to be handled. Someone must hold it back.

It is also important to go with at least two people, since the opponent may not be alone.

In that case, Coco and I, who are fast, are the best choice.

《Please be careful. The effects of Spiritization will weaken as your distance from me increases.》

《Yes!》 x2

We slip past the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon and run toward the royal castle where the man is.

“GAAAAAA…”

The pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon notices our movement and tries to attack.

– DOGAGAGAGA! –

Shot-type spells fired by our companions strike the pseudo Gigantic Rock Dragon.

“Your opponent is us.”

“Do not look away.”

“Claude, we are counting on you.”

“Coco-chan, good luck!”

“Defeat them quickly and come back!”

“We entrust this to you both.”

Seen off by our companions, Coco and I continue running.

---

Spiritization Attributes

Name: Claude

Attribute: Light

Notes: He is the protagonist, so light is fine.

Name: Adel

Attribute: Ice

Notes: Quiet, meaning low temperature, therefore ice.

Name: Nott

Attribute: Earth

Notes: He is a dwarf, so earth. He also uses a hammer.

Name: Coco

Attribute: Wind

Notes: Energetic. Fast. Wind.

Name: Cicely

Attribute: Water

Notes: Gentle and laid-back, that is water.

Name: Roro

Attribute: Fire

Notes: Romance-brained, red hair, passionate. It has to be fire.

Name: Iris

Attribute: Dark

Notes: Hysterical, so dark. It cannot be helped.

Name: Yuria

Attribute: None

Notes: Since she is required to activate ‘Spiritization’, she does not ‘Spiritize’ herself. Therefore, no attribute.

Lightning attribute spirit “?!”

**AN:** Since this is a serious battle, Claude-kun’s heroine does not appear this time.

In the first place, since the stage is Estea, there is no room for her to appear.

Of course, Estea probably has its own heroine.

To be meta about it, if we tried to include the heroine position, the story would spiral out of control…
