## **Chronicle 4: The Heroic Saga of Claude, an A-Rank Adventurer (Part 2)**

**AN:** The titles of these biographical tales have been getting progressively more extravagant.

That was something I decided from the very first post of the series.

---

Because there were no fake undead around the royal castle, Coco and I were able to approach it without much trouble.

“This is anticlimactic. I thought at least one more giant rock dragon might show up.”

“No, that would actually be a problem.”

If another fake giant rock dragon appeared, things would get really rough.

When we got close enough, we noticed that familiar man and woman standing in front of the castle.

I thought they would be inside the castle, but they were just standing there out in the open…

We approached them cautiously.

“Oh, you made it. Did you manage to defeat the giant rock dragon?”

Even though he should know our objective, the man spoke in a calm voice.

“It seems we need to defeat you first, so we will leave that for later.”

“You pushed us that far, did you? That is surprising.”

I could not understand how the man could look genuinely surprised.

“…Why are you so relaxed? We are declaring that we are about to kill you. And yet you do not even ready a weapon, nor do you show any sign of caution. Are you prepared to die?”

I could not understand his thinking at all, and ended up asking.

Trying to understand the person you are about to kill does nothing but weigh on your conscience, with no real benefit…

“The reason I am not cautious? That is simple. I have Luis. With that alone, there is no reason for me to be cautious. I will show you proof. Luis, please.”

The moment he said that, the woman’s body blurred.

-DOGH!-

“Guh!”

I barely managed to see her kick and block it with my shield, but the impact was far stronger than expected, and I was blown back.

“Claude!”

“Incredible. You can react to Luis’ attack?”

I see. Because he fully trusts in the woman’s power, he can maintain such a relaxed attitude.

“So that woman’s corpse is your trump card. She certainly is a powerful bodyguard.”

“DO NOT CALL LUIS A CORPSEEEEEEEEEEEE!!!”

The man overreacted to my words, screaming with bloodshot eyes. So much for his calm demeanor…

Also, that was so sudden that it really startled me.

“L-Luis is not dead. Luis is alive. Look, she is so beautiful. There is no way she is dead. Luis protects me. Luis will live together with me. Luis will never betray me. I will never betray Luis either. Until the day I die. Even after I die. Forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever forever…”

The man broke.

No, he was probably broken to begin with. I never thought calling her a corpse would be the final blow.

“We do not need anyone else in our country. Anything that threatens our peace must be killed. Yes, we knew that from the beginning. There is no one who would ever understand us. We will live together, just the two of us. Anyone who approaches us will be killed. We do not need people who do not understand us. I do not want to see ugly things. We want to live seeing only beautiful scenery. Humans are ugly, so… disappear!”

Once again, Luis’ body blurred.

But once you recognize it, it is not an impossible speed to react to.

“There!”

I blocked her kick with my shield and redirected the force.

Her physical abilities were terrifying, but she seemed to lack a warrior’s instincts, and I was able to easily throw off her balance.

“Coco!”

“I know!”

My role is to be the shield.

The opening I create will be used by my allies.

“Shi!”

Returning to her original dual-dagger style, Coco displayed unmatched strength in close-quarters combat against people.

There was no way the unbalanced woman could evade Coco’s attack.

-GARIGARIGARIGARI-

“What is this woman!? She is insanely hard!”

Coco’s slash should have cut her body clean in half, but all it did was make a sound like striking metal.

There was only the faintest scratch, and it did not look like any real damage was done.

If Coco’s attack did that little, my own attacks would not be much different.

“LUISSSSSSSSSSSS!!!!!!!!”

Despite our situation not being favorable, the man’s reaction was completely different.

“Luis! Come here!”

When he shouted, the woman instantly returned to his side.

“Ah, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis. You have gotten hurt this much… Ah, ahhh, ahhhh, ahhhh, Luis, Luis…”

Saying that, the man touched her wounds over and over again.

We did not know how to react and could only stare.

What should we do? Should we attack?

After a while, all emotion drained from the man’s face.

“…Enough.”

The now expressionless man muttered.

“I planned to spend the rest of our lives together, but that is over. I never thought only Luis would get hurt. I cannot endure this. If we are to be hurt, then we will be hurt together. We swore to be together in sickness and in health. Ah, Luis! Let us become one!”

The man pulled out a small bottle from his pocket, opened the lid, and drank its contents in one gulp.

“Ah, my beloved Luis…”

When he embraced the woman, miasma and evil spirits burst forth from his body, enveloping them both.

From within the miasma came sounds like ‘crack!’, ‘squelch!’, and ‘squish…’, noises that should never come from a human body.

“Ugh… what is that? That is disgusting…”

It was understandable for Coco to say that.

When the miasma cleared, what stood there was a truly grotesque existence.

Simply put, the man’s body was growing out of the woman’s body in multiple places.

“Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis, Luis.”

From the man’s mouth near the woman’s waist, only her name was repeated over and over.

The woman remained expressionless.

“Claude, I do not really get it, but we have to defeat that thing, right?”

“Yeah… probably.”

I did not understand either.

“Then I will try attacking once. When the fight restarts, back me up.”

“Got it.”

Since I did not know whether to call it a woman or a man, I would tentatively call it ‘the woman’.

Since the woman did not move, Coco decided to test an attack.

“Hah!”

She ran in and swung her dagger…

“Gah!”

“Coco!?”

She was kicked away before she could land the blow.

The woman’s movements were clearly faster than before.

“This is bad… that was a solid hit…”

She managed to stand up and take a stance, but the damage was heavy.

She seemed to be slowly healing with \<Healing Magic>, but it would take some time to fully recover.

Then buying time was my job as the shield.

The woman did not pursue Coco, but kept staring at her.

And the moment Coco stood up, I felt power gather in the woman’s legs.

I moved between Coco and the woman using \<Shukuchi>.

“I will not let you touch Coco.”

The moment I said that, the woman’s body blurred.

“Guh!”

I blocked the heavier kick with my shield.

I tried to redirect it, but the kick was too heavy to fully deflect.

My hands tingled violently from the impact.

I worried about the damage Coco took from receiving this kick directly.

Having been stopped, the woman stood still and looked around restlessly.

This was bad. My hands were numb, and another attack would be disastrous.

Why was she stopping?

“Claude, are you okay?”

Coco asked worriedly. She seemed mostly recovered.

“Yeah, I am fine. But she suddenly stopped moving.”

“Huh? Why?”

The moment Coco looked at the woman.

“Kyaa!”

The woman rushed her and kicked.

Before, Coco could not dodge because it happened at the moment of attack, but if she could anticipate it, she could evade it.

The woman launched a barrage of kicks at Coco.

“Hey! Why!? Why are you only targeting me!?”

Barely, Coco continued dodging.

Even though I was right there, the woman kept focusing only on Coco.

Until Coco attacked first, the woman did not move at all.

…Does she only target those who attack her?

When I stood between Coco and the woman, Coco was not in her line of sight.

At that time, the woman did not attack Coco.

…Does she only attack targets she can see?

《Coco! Hide behind me!》

To avoid sound-based detection, I sent the instruction via telepathy.

《Got it!》

Coco dodged and immediately ran behind me.

Just as I thought, the woman stopped moving and looked around.

《Wh-what is going on?》

《I think once someone attacks her, she will try to kill that person as long as she can see them.》

《I see. That is why if I stay in your shadow, she does not attack.》

《Do not show your face. I cannot fully block that attack.》

For now, the fact that I have not attacked yet is our lifeline.

《Yeah, I know. That attack is brutal.》

At worst, we might have to retreat.

It is not an obvious threat like the fake giant rock dragon, but a single humanoid being this strong is terrifying in its own way.

《…Which means, Claude, you have exactly one chance to attack, right?》

《After that, we will be hit with a storm of attacks…》

And she will probably react even then, so there is no guarantee the attack will land.

I could not help but wish Yuria-san were nearby, with Spiritization in perfect condition.

《Why do not we try that technique?》

《…Are you serious?》

She meant the technique we practiced during training.

The big move that never became a skill.

If it lands, it is a one-hit kill. If it fails, then I am the one…

《Before I even land the hit, I will get kicked away by a counter.》

《It will be fine. I will act as bait and create an opening so you can attack.》

《That does not sound fine at all.》

As the shield, I did not want to use someone else as bait, and the risk to Coco was far too high.

On top of that, the success rate of the technique without it being a skill was less than ten percent.

That is far too dangerous a gamble.

《Claude, sorry. It looks like we do not have much time…》

《…Yeah.》

The woman stopped looking around and began sniffing the air.

She first searched with her eyes, and now she was using her nose?

If her sense of smell was strong, it would only be a matter of time.

《It looks like we have no choice.》

《Alright. But I think I can last only one minute as bait.》

《Please. Stay as far away as you can. I need as much time as possible.》

Coco slowly backed away behind me, staying out of the woman’s sight.

This should buy us some time.

The big move takes time to activate.

If it were a skill, it would be different, but as it is, the charge time is long. It is almost unusable in real combat.

I began chanting a spell.

My specialty, ‘Light Shot’.

The woman’s face turned in our direction.

She probably had a general idea of our position and was going to investigate further.

After the 15 seconds required to chant an LV3 spell passed, the spell was ready to be fired by declaring its name or focusing strongly.

But I deliberately maintained that state.

《She found me!》

At last, the woman noticed Coco.

She relentlessly targeted Coco, kicking again and again.

《Claude! I am counting on you!》

Coco barely continued to dodge.

I imagined transferring the ready spell into my sword.

But the mana did not move as I envisioned.

Activating \<Magic Sword> really was difficult.

If it worked, I could unleash a powerful blow combining physical and magical damage…

I repeated the image over and over.

The one-minute limit approached.

It was not working.

The mana would not move.

Finally, one minute passed.

Coco did not rush me. She trusted me and kept dodging.

-DOGH!-

“Gah!”

“Coco!?”

A dull sound rang out as Coco was blown away.

The woman’s kick hit her directly.

“Do not worry! Keep going, Claude!”

Coco landed skillfully despite being blown away, and encouraged me even as she staggered.

The woman attacked Coco again.

She was barely dodging, but her movements had lost their sharpness.

Another hit was only a matter of time.

…No. I cannot allow my companion to be hurt in front of me.

If we attacked together, we might land hits.

But for now, I had to draw the woman’s attention to myself and buy time for Coco to recover.

I did not have much strength left, but I would increase the output of Spiritization to boost my reaction speed.

If I could make her see me as the greater threat, that would be ideal.

“…Huh?”

The moment I increased ‘Spiritization’ output, I could clearly feel the flow of mana gathered in my hands.

I transferred that mana into my sword.

“It is this easy…”

Thus, I finally acquired the Unique-class skill \<Magic Sword> that I had trained for so long.

Come to think of it, spirits are masses of mana.

It made sense that moving mana would be easier while ‘Spiritized’.

Until now, I avoided practicing \<Magic Sword> during ‘Spiritization’ training because I did not want to burden Yuria-san.

To think I could learn it just like this…

No, now was not the time to think about that.

I had to end this fight.

《Coco! Here I go!》

《I have been waiting!》

-DOGH!-

“Guh!”

Coco deliberately took the woman’s kick with her arm.

She grabbed the leg.

The woman violently swung her leg, blowing Coco away and breaking free.

Just as Coco intended, that created a huge opening.

I stepped in with all my ‘Spiritization’-enhanced strength and activated \<Shukuchi>.

“Raaah!!!”

I closed in and swung down with all my might.

The woman barely reacted and tried to kick me, but my attack was faster.

-ZUBASH!-

“Gyaaaaaaaaaaaaaah!!!!!!!”

The power of \<Magic Sword> was overwhelming.

The woman, who shrugged off Coco’s slashes, was cut down easily.

Her body was split cleanly in two vertically, and a scream burst from the man’s face.

“Ah, ahh… Lui… s…”

Those were the man’s last words.

The woman’s body turned into black mist and vanished.

Because I activated ‘Spiritization’ and \<Magic Sword> simultaneously, my MP was completely drained, and I collapsed.

Ah, I am exhausted…

“Coco, are you okay?”

“Somehow… ouch, ‘Heal’…”

It seemed we both survived.

I drank an MP potion and focused on recovery.

《Claude-kun, are you okay?》

“Yes, somehow…”

《Good. Then I will return to Yuria-chan first.》

“Thank you very much.”

Because my MP was depleted, Spiritization was forcibly cancelled.

After thanking Akari-san, she returned to Yuria-san.

The wind spirit that had been Spiritized with Coco also returned.

“Yuria-san and the others will probably arrive soon. Let us rest a bit…”

“Agreed…”

We collapsed together in front of the royal castle.

Now, let me tell you what happened after.

Coco and I were retrieved by our companions and left the capital.

The countless fake undead in the Duchy of Rifel lost their power and turned to ash the moment the mastermind was defeated.

Thankfully, the corpses of tens of thousands of fake undead did not remain across the country.

Just to be safe, they planned to stay away from the country for a few days to observe the situation.

Our request was considered completed the moment we defeated the man, and we were not required to help with the cleanup.

Fortunately, there were no deaths among the adventurers and knights, with even the worst cases being serious injuries.

Naturally, all of Jin-sama’s associates were almost unharmed. Coco probably took the most damage.

And then, we officially became S-rank adventurers.

Apparently, we were the first to be certified as S-rank by the Adventurers Guild of Estea.

Estea’s adventurers are not exactly top-tier, after all…

Incidentally, all eight of us were recognized as S-rank.

Normally, high-rank adventurers do not often form parties. Because of that, even grouping several S-rank adventurers does not necessarily make a strong party.

However, each of us individually possessed strength worthy of S-rank.

Simply put, we could handle situations that a normal single S-rank adventurer could not. That also gave us a major advantage even against other S-rank adventurers.

We also had the chance to meet the Grand Duke of Rifel during the evacuation.

He personally thanked us and even asked us to move our base of operations to the Duchy of Rifel if possible.

He even said he would be willing to marry one of his daughters to me.

I declined, since I could not enter an engagement without Jin-sama’s instructions or permission. Besides, the only unengaged princess was currently two years old, so please do not make unreasonable requests.

We came to the Kingdom of Estea to obtain recommendations to become S-rank adventurers.

After receiving recommendations, achieving a great feat, and becoming S-rank adventurers, we returned to the Kingdom of Castal, our home, one week later.

What stuck with me was how incredibly disappointed the Adventurers Guild of Estea looked.

Estea’s adventurers are not exactly top-tier, after all…

Two more days later, Jin-sama and the others returned from the Elgant Theocracy.

“You did well. Congratulations.”

Jin-sama praised us for becoming S-rank adventurers.

“Roro is happy…”

“I am happy too…”

Coco and Roro, who adored Jin-sama, asked him to pat their heads and were thoroughly satisfied.

Iris, who greatly feared Jin-sama, looked deeply relieved.

That night was the customary promotion celebration party.

We enjoyed the dishes that the mansion’s maids prepared with all their skill.

Mio-san’s cooking seemed to have become even better.

As high-rank adventurers, we sometimes eat expensive food, but we have never found anything that surpassed the meals at Jin-sama’s mansion.

“Ah, but if this is the last promotion party, that is a bit sad.”

“Yeah. I want to have more parties.”

“Roro agrees. If we want to hold a party, would it not be best to ask Jin-sama?”

“Then, Claude, ask him for us, okay?”

“Coco, why does it have to be me?”

“Huh? You are the leader, right? Or Adel could do it.”

“Adel, if you ask in a way that upsets Jin-sama, I will punch you.”

“Coco-chan and Iris-chan are so cruel…”

“Then I will go instead.”

“See, because Adel said he would not go, Yuria-san is volunteering. You idiot, Adel!”

“Iris-chan, that is cruel…”

In the end, when we all asked Jin-sama together, he agreed to hold parties regularly.

The maids also told us ‘good job’, since it meant more chances to interact with Jin-sama. They rarely ask him for anything themselves…

After the party, Jin-sama summoned us.

Iris, who feared him excessively, and Cicely, who feared him a little, were extremely tense.

The rest of us were also nervous, though not to the same degree.

“I called you here to ask about your future plans. This is not a scolding, so relax.”

Those words put everyone at ease.

“What do you mean by future plans?”

As the leader, I asked.

“I told you to become S-rank adventurers. But I did not give detailed instructions for after that. The original idea was that having the influence of S-rank adventurers would make things easier.”

To be honest, looking at Jin-sama now, I sometimes wondered if he really needed even S-rank-level influence.

“Now that you are S-rank, I will not tell you to desperately rack up adventurer achievements anymore. So I want you to find your own goals and hobbies. Nott is a good example. Being a blacksmith is half a hobby, right?”

“Y-yes! That is correct. It strengthens the party as well, so it is both hobby and practical.”

Even Nott could not joke around with Jin-sama.

“I am saying I will allow hobbies with no practical benefit as well. …Well, they were never forbidden, but except for Nott, you were all nothing but adventurers. So I decided to formally permit it.”

That was true. We focused entirely on fulfilling Jin-sama’s orders and paid little attention to anything else.

“I would like to seriously study cooking, if possible. Is that acceptable?”

“Yes, of course.”

Jin-sama nodded to Roro.

“I am not saying you must decide right away. I just want you to think about how you want to live going forward, as a milestone. Of course, you will receive named requests as S-rank adventurers, so you will have to balance things.”

With that, Jin-sama dismissed us.

Becoming an S-rank adventurer does not mean my life is over.

As Jin-sama said, it is just a milestone.

“My future path…”

Until now, all I had to do was follow Jin-sama’s instructions and aim for S-rank.

But now, we have to decide our own path.

It is confusing to be told so suddenly, but thankfully, I have reliable companions and family.

Let us discuss our future together.

---

Summary

Name: Claude

Gender: Male

Race: Human

Equipment: Sword + Shield

Attribute: Light

Notes: His future dream is to expand the scale of his clan. Believing that being an adventurer suits him best, he plans to continue actively adventuring for now while also exploring other paths.

Name: Adel

Gender: Male

Race: Human

Equipment: Spear

Attribute: Ice

Notes: His future dream is to become a scholar or a teacher. Through learning many things under Jin, he realized that he does not dislike learning and thinking. Fortunately, he has many connections.

Name: Nott

Gender: Male

Race: Dwarf

Equipment: Hammer

Attribute: Earth

Notes: His future dream is to become a blacksmith. This has been his consistent goal since becoming an adventurer, and in a sense, he is the closest to realizing his dream.

Name: Coco

Gender: Female

Race: Beastkin (Dog)

Equipment: Daggers x2

Attribute: Wind

Notes: Her future dream is to become Jin’s knight or attendant. Since adventurers and knights differ in fundamental mindset, she has begun learning the mindset of a knight from Lucia.

Name: Cicely

Gender: Female

Race: Human

Equipment: Spear

Attribute: Water

Notes: Her future dream is undecided. She was never good at thinking deeply and lived life going with the flow. After being admonished by her companions, she decided to try a little harder to think about it.

Name: Roro

Gender: Female

Race: Human

Equipment: Greatsword

Attribute: Fire

Notes: Her future dream is to become a bride. Judging maid training to be similar to bridal training, she began maid training. Spending more time in the mansion increased her encounter rate with Jin, which is a plus.

Name: Iris

Gender: Female

Race: Half-Elf

Equipment: Sword + Shield

Attribute: Dark

Notes: Her future dream is to become a librarian. She has always been a bookworm, which is also why her eyesight worsened. In fact, before becoming a slave, she was raised in a fairly well-off household.

Name: Yuria

Gender: Female

Race: High Elf

Equipment: Whip + Dagger

Attribute: None

Notes: Her future dream is undecided. As a long-lived high elf with amnesia, she has more time than others to think things through, and she believes she must do so carefully to avoid regret later.

**AN:** The purpose of these biographical tales is to depict the path until Claude and the others become S-rank adventurers, so this concludes the arc.

The main story resumes on 7/10.

## **Chronicle 4: The Heroic Saga of Claude, an A-Rank Adventurer (Latter Half)**

**AN:** It is a bonus, it is the truth, and depending on the person, it may even be unnecessary.

This is the true final chapter of the side story.

---

One week had passed since the recapture of the Duchy of Rifel.

After adventurers and knights finished confirming conditions throughout the country, the citizens of the Duchy of Rifel began returning home.

Meanwhile, in the forest where fake undead had first overflowed during the occupation of the Duchy of Rifel, someone was letting out a laugh.

‘Kukukuku, well now, that was quite an entertaining spectacle. It was worth granting my power.’

That presence shook its body of black miasma while scattering foul energy around it.

‘Ahh, playing with humans truly is fun. Now then, shall we begin a new game to the west from here next? In time, I would like to devour that troublesome Spirit Sanctuary as well.’

“Unfortunately, there is no next time for you.”

‘Who are you?’

Until just moments ago, there had been no one in the forest other than the black miasma.

And yet, in the blink of an eye, the presences of eight people had approached.

“We call ourselves the Saviors. Naturally, you know who we are, correct?”

‘Ahh, the ones who slew my servant. Why were you able to come here? Did you know in advance that I was here?’

“Yes. We also know that you were watching us through the fake undead and through that man.”

That being… the aggregate of evil spirits that had lodged fragments of itself within the fake undead, had been watching the battle in the Duchy of Rifel through all of the fake undead and the spirit arts user who had been under its control.

The evil spirit had lamented the death of the woman it loved, tempted the man whose heart had broken, and made him place an evil spirit into the woman’s corpse. Yes, the evil spirit had been watching the rampage of the broken man from a front-row seat.

‘Oh? You know that much? Then you understand, do you not? That you cannot do anything to me. It goes without saying, but I possess far greater power than my servant. Why did you show yourselves before me?’

The evil spirit did not abandon its air of composure toward the ‘Saviors’.

It had been watching the battle in the Duchy of Rifel from the best seat.

To the evil spirit, the ‘Saviors’, who had struggled against the servant it had empowered, did not seem threatening in the slightest.

Knowing that they could not win, why would they take the risk of appearing before it?

That was what puzzled the evil spirit.

‘Could it be that you desire my power? Certainly, for humans, you are rather strong. If you were to gain my power, there would be none among humans who could rival you. Hmm, interesting. Very well… if you accept my dominion and become new toys, I shall grant you this power.’

After thinking for a moment, the evil spirit mistakenly concluded that the ‘Saviors’ were after its power.

“No. Our objective is the subjugation of you, evil spirit.”

However, the evil spirit’s misunderstanding was immediately denied.

‘…Are you fools who cannot even measure your own strength?’

Because the battle with its servant had been entertaining, the evil spirit had been in a good mood before the ‘Saviors’.

But when the ‘Saviors’ made a statement without knowing their place, its mood instantly soured.

‘You defeated my servant only a few days ago. What could you possibly have accomplished in such a short time? Just because you beat someone on the level of my servant, do you truly believe you can face me?’

“Yes. As we are now, we can defeat you.”

Though the evil spirit applied light pressure, not a single member of the ‘Saviors’ showed a frightened expression.

‘…Very well. If you intend to defy me, I shall make you understand that foolishness with your own bodies.’

In that instant, the evil spirit’s presence rapidly swelled.

Then, the black miasma condensed, taking on a demonic form.

When the evil spirit set its feet upon the ground, the grass around it withered.

The overwhelming miasma of the evil spirit was enough to affect the surrounding ecosystem.

‘Consider me now to be a hundred times stronger than the woman you struggled to defeat.’

In truth, the power the evil spirit had given to the woman was only about one hundredth of its total.

Whether the amount of power is directly proportional to strength is unclear, but there is no doubt that the difference approaches a factor of one hundred.

Even so, the ‘Saviors’ showed no sign of agitation.

Because they understood well what they could and could not do, they did not view the present evil spirit as such an overwhelming threat.

“Earlier, you asked what we could do in just a few days after defeating your servant, didn’t you?”

‘I did. And what of it?’

Perhaps out of interest in the ‘Saviors’ thinking, the evil spirit did not attack immediately and instead listened.

“In those few days, we became S-rank adventurers.”

‘Kuhahaha, and what of it? Have you been promoted within some framework created by humans and convinced yourselves that you have grown stronger? Do you think that alone has given you the power to stand against me?’

The evil spirit laughed scornfully.

To mistake an increase in authority for an increase in actual strength looked nothing but ridiculous to it.

“Yes. Because we became S-rank, permission was granted to use the power we had been saving up all this time. If we use that, defeating you will not be difficult.”

‘?’

The evil spirit could not understand what the ‘Saviors’ were saying.

“We were told that those without knowledge and experience were unnecessary, so we have been fighting with only the bare minimum of support this entire time. Telling mere orphans to become S-rank adventurers through ability alone is quite an unreasonable demand, don’t you think?”

‘…What are you talking about?’

“Simply put, we had sealed our true strength until we became S-rank. Think of us now as being more than a hundred times stronger than when we defeated your servant.”

Hearing words that seemed to mock its own earlier statement, the evil spirit realized it was being provoked.

‘You insolent humans… Very well. Then I shall personally correct that misconception. And once you are dead, I will grant your corpses fragments of myself and use you as servants. Even in death, you will be together with your companions. Be grateful for my mercy. Kuhahahahaha!!!’

The evil spirit further increased its presence and lunged at the ‘Saviors’.

Jin, master of the ‘Saviors’, returns a portion of the status of monsters defeated by his subordinates to the one who slew them.

Through this, Jin’s subordinates grow stronger each time they defeat a monster.

Here, there is something I want you to notice.

That Claude and the others struggling against something like a fake giant rock dragon is extremely unnatural.

As you know, among Jin’s subordinates, the ‘Saviors’ are considered veterans.

They are also the ones who have been fighting the longest among Jin’s subordinates.

Naturally, they have slain a considerable number of monsters.

In other words, the ‘Saviors’ should not find it strange to possess far greater power than they had shown.

The reason that power was sealed lies solely in Jin’s policy.

While Jin favors solving problems through brute force, he also places great importance on fundamentals and base strength.

When turning his subordinates into S-rank adventurers, he wanted them to be individuals with the knowledge and experience befitting S-rank, not adventurers who simply bulldozed through with skills, stats, or special powers.

For that reason, after granting the ‘Saviors’ only the minimum skills and stats necessary to function as adventurers, he sent them out with almost no additional benefits.

Although they were permitted to use certain abilities such as telepathy and \<Infinite Storage>, during normal adventuring and requests they were not even allowed to view their own status or maps.

Naturally, almost no status or skill feedback was being returned to them.

However, Jin particularly despises unjust discrimination.

Having returned status to his other subordinates, there was no way he would return nothing to the ‘Saviors’ alone.

Thus, the status the ‘Saviors’ should have received remained unused and accumulated.

And that status would be released after they became S-rank.

Once they were recognized as top-class adventurers, Jin judged that there would be no problem with them wielding overwhelmingly high stats.

For the ‘Saviors’, the difference between before and after becoming S-rank adventurers was absolute.

To the extent that their claim of being more than a hundred times stronger was no exaggeration at all.

Even so, just because they had become S-rank adventurers, the ‘Saviors’ had no intention of frequently using that immense power.

Great power easily leads to arrogance, and more than anything, they felt more attachment to the strength they had built up through their own efforts.

For that reason, the ‘Saviors’ decided that they would only use that power against opponents they could not possibly handle on their own, enemies they could never reach with their base stats alone, such as an evil spirit.

“Guboaaaaa!!!”

And so, the dying scream of the evil spirit echoed.

---

**AN:** While writing side stories, the main story is not progressing.

Everything is backwards.
